<pb n="b625"/>
<head>bṛhatī</head>
<head>(śābarabhāṣyavyākhyā)</head>
<head>tṛtīyādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pādaḥ</head>
<ab type="sutra" n="1">athātaśśeṣalakṣaṇam ।। 1 ।।</ab>
<p>1<quote>nānākarmalakṣaṇaṃ vṛttamiti</quote> । karmānubandhabhedācchāstrabhedaḥ, ataḥ śāstra-
bhedalakṣaṇaṃ vṛttamityarthaḥ । nanu ca śāstrabhede satyaidamarthyaṃ na
siddha‍yati aṅgapradhānānām । viniyogataḥ karmabhedaḥ uktaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b626"/>
nanu cedānīmeva viniyogaścintyate । kathaṃ viniyogato bhedaḥ, bhede
sati viniyogaḥ । ata eva na bhedalakṣaṇaṃ vṛttamiti hetvarthatayaiva
bhedalakṣaṇopanyāsaḥ śeṣalakṣaṇasya । satyaṃ, hetvarthatayaiva upanyāsaḥ
satyaṃ ca bhedādviniyogaḥ । tathāpi śāstrabhedo'pi viniyogata
eva । kintvasau viniyogaḥ padanimittakaḥ ।</p>
<p>kimidaṃ padanimittaka iti ? pratipattau hetuḥ padanimittakaḥ
padārthānāṃ saṃbandhapratipattinimittaka ityarthaḥ । yastvayaṃ tṛtīye
cintyate sa kāryanimittakaḥ । ato vākyārthabhedena śāstrabhede
sati vākyārthānāṃ parasparaṃ śeṣaśeṣicintā śeṣalakṣaṇamityucyate
lakṣyate hi śeṣaśeṣipratipattau na pratipādyate1 । nanu vrīhīn
﻿<pb n="b627"/>
prokṣatīti padārthānāṃ śeṣaśiṣicintā । aśravaṇamatrāparādhyate
bhavataḥ । vrīhibhiryajetetyanena sahāsya śeṣaśeṣicintā na puna-
rvrīhipadārthamātratayaiva । kimiti tarhi śeṣalakṣaṇaṃ ? viniyojyo
hi śeṣaḥ tadviṣayāṇi śrutyādīni tasmāccheṣalakṣaṇamityucyate ।
śeṣiparijñānaṃ tarhi kinnimittaṃ ? pramāṇāntaranimittakaṃ tat ।
﻿<pb n="b628"/>
lakṣyate hi śeṣī śeṣapratipattau, na pratipādyate । ato yuk‍taṃ
śeṣalakṣaṇam ।</p>
<p>yadyevaṃ viniyojyaḥ śeṣa iti vaktavyam । kimidaṃ śeṣaḥ parārtha-
tvāditi ? uktamasmābhiḥ padanimittako'pi viniyogo vidyata iti ।
ataḥ kārye viniyojyaḥ śeṣaḥ kathaṃ syāditi śeṣaḥ parārthatvādityu-
ktam । yasya kārye viniyogaḥ sa tadartha eva bhavati । ataḥ
parārthatvāditi lakṣitam । na ca kāryaṃ parārthaṃ bhavitumarhati kāryameva
hi tanna syāt yadyanyārtham ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b629"/>
<p>ata eva garbhadāsadṛṣṭānto bhāṣye । nanu ca parārthatāmātraṃ parārtha-
śabdenocyate । kimidaṃ atyantaparārtha iti । ucyate । ata evā-
tyantaparārthaḥ yasmāt parārthatāmātrataivocyate । ataḥ sādhu vivṛtam ।
﻿<pb n="b630"/>
<quote>kaḥ śeṣaḥ kena hetunā śeṣaḥ1 iti</quote> । kimidaṃ praśnadvayaṃ ? kena hetunā śeṣa
ityetāvadvaktavyam । siddha‍yati hi parārthatvāccheṣa iti । ucyate,
syādetadevaṃ yadi siddhavadabhidhānaṃ hetoḥ syāt । heturapyatra kathanīya
evetyadoṣaḥ ।</p>
<p>ata eva ko dharmaḥ kathaṃlakṣaṇaṃ ityuktam । kiṃ punaḥ siddhasya
kathane prayojanaṃ ? upayuktādanyaḥ śeṣa ityevamādinivṛttyartham ।
<quote>kathaṃ ca viniyujyata 2iti ?</quote> ko'yaṃ praśnaḥ ? kena viniyujyata iti
vaktavyam, kimidaṃ kathaṃ ca viniyujyata iti ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b631"/>
<p>atrābhidhīyate । kena viniyujyata ityucyamāne śrutyādivyā-
pāra eva kevalaṃ pṛṣṭaḥ kathitaśca bhavati । na punaḥ saviniyogānāṃ
śrutyādīnāṃ, na ca niyogaśūnyāni śrutyādīni śeṣatāmāpādayituṃ
śak‍nuvanti । kāryābhāvāt । kāryanimittaṃ ca parārthamityuktam । ataḥ
kathaṃ ca viniyujyata ityuktaṃ sahetukaviniyogasiddha‍yartham । ata eva
ca śrutyādīni viniyoge kāraṇānītyuktam । na punaḥ śrutyādibhiriti ।
kathamityanuṣaṅgaḥ । teṣāṃ balavadabalavattetyanenāpi kathaṃ cetyanuṣak‍tavyam ।
﻿<pb n="b632"/>
eṣa tāvat lakṣaṇārthaḥ । naitāvatā vinā śeṣaparijñānasiddhiḥ । ata
evānyadapi sādhanasiddha‍yarthaṃ kiñcidupoddhātādinā śeṣaḥ parārtha-
tvāditi sūtraṃ sabhāṣyaṃ vyākhyātam ।</p>
<p>1<quote>atha tatra kiṃ bṛttam ? yaistu dravyaṃ cikīrṣyate guṇastatra pratīyeteti</quote> ।
uk‍taṃ taccheṣalakṣaṇaṃ manvānasyaitaccodyam । uttaraṃ tu niyoga-
viṣayatā tatrāpanītā śeṣatvaṃ tu ihaiva sarveṣāṃ pratipādyate ।
ko'yaṃ viniyogaviṣayatvāpanhavaḥ ? na ca viniyogaśūnyāni
śrūtyādīni śeṣatayā viniyok‍tuṃ śak‍nuvantītyuktam ।
﻿<pb n="b633"/>
tasmāccheṣatvaṃ viniyogāpahnavaśceti vipratiṣiddham । ataḥ śeṣatvaṃ
vā nāstyapūrvaviṣayatā vā nāpahnotuṃ śakyate । ucyate---anabhijño
bhavān viṣayaniyojyānām । na brūmo guṇabhūteṣu pusāṃ niyojyatā
nāstīti । kiṃ tarhi ? viṣayastu na bhavatīti। kāryāntarasya darśanāt।
yasya punarniyogasiddhireva kāryaḥ sa viṣayaḥ <q>‘teṣāmarthena’</q> ityatna prakaṭa-
tarameva vakṣyāmaḥ । ato yuktamuk‍taṃ tatrāpūrvārthatā vyāvartiteti ।1</p>
﻿<pb n="b634"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="3">dravyaguṇasaṃskāreṣu bādariḥ ।। 3 ।।1</ab>
<p>kaḥ punaratrāsyābhiprāyo dravyaguṇasaṃskāreṣveva pārārthyaṃ vadataḥ ?
ayamabhiprāyaḥ---vibhaktibhiḥ tādarthyaṃ prātipadikārthasya pratipādyate ।
tacca dravyaguṇayorupalabhyate ekahāyanyā krīṇātīti aruṇayeti
ca । saṃskārasya tu kathaṃ ? tatrāpi vibhaktyaiva vrīhin prokṣati
vrīhīnavahanti iti । nanu ca prātipadikārthasya prādhānyaṃ
dvitīyā pratipādayati na karmaṇo guṇabhāvam । akārakajño bhavān ।
kārakavibhak‍tayo hi kathaṃ kriyānirapekṣāḥ । tasmāt kriyā-
nirapekṣameva prātipadikārthasya prādhānyaṃ guṇatvaṃ vā । ata
eva ca vibhaktividhāne bhagavataḥ pāṇineḥ kārakoddeśaḥ ।
<pb n="b635"/>
kathaṃ tarhi taddhitādiṣu tādarthyāvagatiḥ kathaṃ copapadavibhaktayaḥ ।
ato'nyadapi vibhaktivyatirik‍taṃ pārārthye pramāṇaṃ dravyaguṇasaṃskāreṣu
vaktavyam ।</p>
<p>nanu copakāradarśanameva dravyaguṇasaṃskārāṇāṃ pārārthye heturiti
bādarermatam । kimatra vibhaktyādibhi kriyate । ucyate---yadyu-
pakāradarśanaṃ pārārthye hetuḥ brīhayo'pi prokṣaṇasyopakārakāḥ syuḥ । atha
prayojanaṃ prati upakāradarśanaṃ hetuḥ, prayojanavattājñānamidānīṃ kutaḥ ?
﻿<pb n="b636"/>
niyogata iti cet । evaṃ tarhi niyoganirvṛtireva pārārthye
hetuḥ kimidaṃ upakāradarśanaṃ kariṣyati । ata eva ca
vibhak‍tivyatyayo'pi prayājaśeṣeṇetyevamādiṣu siddho bhavati ।
kṛttaddhitasamāsāśca tadvaśenaiva aidamarthyapratipādakā bhavanti । eva-
mapyupapadavibhak‍terasaṅkaraḥ siddho bhavati ।</p>
<p>kimiti tarhi bādariḥ dravyaguṇasaṃskāreṣveva śeṣabhāvaṃ
manyate yadi niyoganirvṛttiḥ pārārthye hetuḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b637"/>
<p>na niyogaṃ phale puruṣe ca manyate yāga eva niyogaḥ
tannirvṛttyā ca niyoganirvṛttiḥ । dravyaguṇasaṃskāraiśca yāgo
nirvartyate । ataḥ teṣāmeva pārārthyaṃ evaṃ manyate bādarirā-
cāryaḥ । nanu svargaṃ yāgena kuryāṃdātmārthaṃ iti niyogaḥ ।
ātmanepadaprayogāt । naivaṃ śabdāt pratipat‍tuṃ śakyate dvitīyā hi
kārakasya prādhānyaṃ pratipādayati । yasyāḥ kriyāyāḥ tatkārakam ।

﻿<pb n="b638"/>
na ca svarge yāgasya kārakamiti siddham । na ca
vedāt kriyākārakasaṃbandhāvagatiḥ । siddhasya hi anuṣṭhānaṃ
codyate । kathaṃ tarhi yadāhavanīye juhvatīti ? yuk‍taṃ
pramāṇāntareṇa saṃbhavadarśanāt । svarge punarnaitadupapadyate vedasyā-
prāmāṇyaprasaṅgāt । kiñca kartṛviśeṣaṇaṃ cātra svarga(kāma)śabdaḥ
na kartṛviśeṣaṇamīpsitatamaṃ bhavati rājapuruṣaṃ paśyetivat ।
﻿<pb n="b639"/>
ato na svargaṃ kuryāditi niyogaviṣayatā śakyate pratipat‍tum ।
kathaṃ tarhi svargakāmapadasaṃbandhāt svargaṃ bhāvayediti bhāṣyam । eva-
metadbhāṣyaṃ anyathā hi svargamiti śravaṇāt svargaṃ bhāvayediti syāt ।
﻿<pb n="b640"/>
ata eva svayameva tadbhavatītyetadabhiprāyaṃ tat । nimittamātra-
kathanaṃ hi tat karmaṇaḥ । ataḥ prayojanaṃ svargo yāgasya na
karma pākasyeva grāsaḥ । ato dravyaguṇasaṃskārāṇāmeva sādhya-
sādhanabhāvāvagateḥ prayojanavattayā śeṣabhāvaḥ । na punaḥ karmatve-
nāpratīyamānayoḥ phalapuruṣayorapi syāt । tasmāt sūk‍taṃ
dravyaguṇasaṃskāreṣu bādariḥ iti । <quote>1na cet phalayāgau guṇabhāvena codyete
kasya puruṣaḥ pradhānabhūto bhaviṣyatīti</quote> । ko'yaṃ prādhānyapratiṣedhaḥ
śeṣatā hi puruṣasya pratiṣedhyā <q>“na yāgaphalapuruṣeṣu”</q> iti
pratijñānāt । ucyate । śeṣatānivṛttyarthameva prādhānyaṃ
pratiṣidhyate । kathaṃ ? sati hi prādhānye puruṣaḥ śeṣa iti
﻿<pb n="b641"/>
śakyate vak‍tum । kimiti ? puruṣaśabdo hyayaṃ svargakāme prayuktaḥ
yadi tadarthaḥ svargaṃ syāt tadā tadviśiṣṭasya śeṣatā syāt ।
svadravyaviśiṣṭasyeva prayājādeḥ । atādarthye punaḥ svargasya kevalaṃ
kartṛtayaiva śeṣabhāvaḥ dravyamātratayetyarthaḥ na puruṣaśeṣatayā । na
svargakāmapadavācyatayetyabhiprāyaḥ । tasmādanavadyam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="4">karmāṇyapi jaiminiḥ phalārthatvāt1 ।। 4 ।।</ab>
<p>kathaṃ phalārthatā karmaṇaḥ ? kāmino hi adhikāro yāge । sa
ca phalasādhanatāṃ yāgasyānāpādayan na siddha‍yatīti ṣaṣṭhe vakṣyāmaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b642"/>
yadi punarayaṃ yāgaḥ phale sādhanabhāvaṃ na pratipadyate tatra ko doṣaḥ ।
na khalu kaścit । pratīyate tu tathā । nanu śeṣalakṣaṇe śeṣatā
pratipādayituṃ nyāyyā, kimidamucyate 1<quote>enamevārthaṃ ṣaṣṭhe sūtraireva sādhayiṣyati</quote>
iti, kiṃ vā śrutyādivyatirik‍taṃ kiñcidanyat śeṣatve pramāṇamasti ।
atha śrutyādīnāmanyatamaṃ tadihaivopanyasanīyaṃ kimiti sānyāsikaṃ
kriyate । atrocyate---adhikārāpekṣiṇī hi sā na śrutyapekṣo'dhikāra
iti sānyāsikaṃ yāgaphalaśeṣatvaṃ yuktam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b643"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="5">phalaṃ ca puruṣārthatvāt ।। 5 ।।1</ab>
<p>phalamapi puruṣaṃ pratyupadiśyate yaḥ svargo me syādityevaṃ
kāmayate tasya, niyogaḥ na svargaḥ ātmānaṃ labheteti । kutaḥ
ātmanepadaprayogāt ।2</p>
<p>nanu ca svargakāmaśabdādevedamavagamyate svargo me bhavediti ।
kimidamātmanepadaprayogāditi । athāyamabhiprāyaḥ parasya duḥkhaṃ
kāmayata ityatrāpi kameḥ prayogenānātmasaṃbandhitvenāpi dṛṣṭa iti
tadayuktam, tatra paraśabdaprayogāt duḥ khasya ca parasambandhitve-
nābhīṣṭatvāt । yatra punaḥ paraśabdo na śrūyate nāpyaniṣṭaṃ duḥ khaṃ tatra
kenānyena kāmyamānasya saṃbandho'nyatra kāmayituḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b644"/>
<p>atha manyase kāmyamānenaiva kāmaḥ saṃbadhyate svargo bhavatviti ।
na hi; tannibandhanasukhāsmaraṇāt । na kasyacit (kāmamātreṇa)
sadbhāvamātre kasyacitkāmo bhavati । tasmādātmanepadopanyāso
liṅgatayā pratipattavyaḥ na punaḥ prāpte pramāṇatayā ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="6">puruṣaśca karmārthatvāt1 ।। 6 ।।</ab>
<p>svargaścetpuruṣārthaḥ svargakāmapadavācyatayaiva <q>‘yajamānena saṃmitau-
dumbarī bhavati’</q> ityādiṣu kartuḥ śeṣatvaṃ kathaṃ ? adhikṛtasya kartṛtvāt ।
﻿<pb n="b645"/>
kartuśca yajamānaśabdavācyatvāt । tasmāt sūk‍taṃ sūtratrayaṃ
jaimineḥ vṛttikāramatopanyāsaḥ pūrvapakṣāparījñānārthaḥ । kimiti
kalpāntaraṃ na bhavati । na hi āpekṣikaṃ śeṣatvamasti । viniyo-
jyanibandhanaṃ hi tat । viniyoga evāpekṣika iti । satyam । śeṣaḥ
viniyojyaṃ śeṣiṇaṃ cāpekṣite na punarekasya śeṣaśeṣitāmāpādayati ।
﻿<pb n="b646"/>
vrīhyādīnāṃ ca svaśeṣāpekṣatayā tulyatvāt । tasmāt svakauśala-
pradarśanārthaṃ paramatamupanyastaṃ bhāṣyakāreṇa ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="7">teṣāmarthena saṃbandhaḥ1 ।। 7 ।।</ab>
<p>uktaṃ niyogasavyapekṣāṇi śrutyādīni viniyojakāni
śāstrāntaravihitasaṃbandhitayā ca kāryalābha ityuktam । śāstrā-
ntaravihitaṃ(yuktaṃ) hi śeṣi bhavati na śeṣaśāstrādeva prādhānyamava-
gamyata iti sak‍tuṣu darśitam । śāstrāntaravihitāni ca vrīhyādīni
﻿<pb n="b647"/>
kathaṃ tatsuṃyuk‍teṣu saṃśayaḥ । kāryaśūnye hi śeṣaśās‍traṃ kalpyaṃ kārya-
pamekṣate । pratyakṣaśrutakāryaṃ tu sandihyata ityayuktam । ucyate ।
niyogādanyat viniyogagamyaṃ kāryamastīti na śakyate vak‍tum ।</p>
<p>nanu ca <q>‘yaistu dravyaṃ cikīrṣyate’</q> iti nāpūrvaṃ
kāryamityuktam । satyam । sthite etasmin śeṣatve tat । śeṣa-
tvamevedānīṃ niyoganirvṛttyā vinā nāvagamyate ityākṣepaḥ ।
kimiti vā na niyogoniṣpādyate vrīhīn prokṣatīti ।
yadyatra niyogārthaniṣpattiḥ, darśapūrṇamāsābhyāmityanena na
﻿<pb n="b648"/>
saṃbadhyeta । atha <q>‘phalavatsannidhau’</q> iti saṃbandhaḥ sa tu niyogaikya-
lakṣaṇa iti pratipādayiṣyāmaḥ । atrāpicet sa eva saṃbandhaḥ
na tarhi vrīhīn prokṣatītyetāvataiva niyogasiddhiḥ । ataḥ
tuṣakaṇavipramocanaṃ na svargāvāptivat nāntarīyako niyogasya ।</p>
<p>evaṃ tarhi ko'yamupanyāsaḥ <q>‘auṣadhe sānnāyye ca karmavyā’1</q>
iti । naiva hi padārthānāṃ prādhānyamasmin pakṣe । ucyate---naiva hi
﻿<pb n="b649"/>
padārthānāṃ prādhānyaparo'yaṃ granthaḥ kiṃ tarhi sarveśeṣatābhiprāyaparaḥ ।
nanu cāsminnapi pakṣe śeṣaśeṣitaiva nopapadyate aṅgapradhānām ।
sarvaśeṣāṇāṃ niyogārthaśeṣatvāt । prakaraṇapramāṇasvarūpanirūpaṇe'sya
codyasya parihāraṃ vakṣyāmaḥ । iha tu kāryāntarāsaṃbhavāta
pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ darśapūrṇamāsābhyāmityanena asaṃbandhādityuktam ।
tasmāt prayājādīnāmeva niyogo hyetallakṣaṇaḥ sarveṣā-
mabhisaṃbandhaḥ । kathaṃ tarhi vrīhīn ājyaṃ iti ca । asmin
pakṣe sak‍tuvadetadbhaviṣyati । gāṃ dadāti itivadvā ।
﻿<pb n="b650"/>
ata idamuktam । 1<quote>avadhātādayastu padārthāḥ śrutyā vidhīyanta</quote> iti ।
bhāvārthānāṃ śrutyā niyogasaṃbandhaścetyarthaḥ । vākyenaiṣāṃ vrīhyādi-
saṃbandha iti bhāvārthānupraveśena dravyādīnāṃ tu niyogasaṃbandha
ityarthaḥ na pradhānabhūtānāṃ, na hi dravyaparyanto niyogaḥ
svaya2mevasādhyatvāt tasmāt sūk‍taṃ sarve sarvārthā iti ।
﻿<pb n="b651"/>
kimidamadṛṣṭaṃ bhavatīti । adṛṣṭamapūrvaṃ niyoga ityekamida-
mityuk‍taṃ <q>‘ato'pūrvaṃ kṛtvā’</q>iti ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="10">phalaṃ tu saha ceṣṭayā śabdārtho'bhāvādviprayoge syāt ।। 10 ।।</ab>
<p>atrocyate । syāt sarvārthatā yadi hi kāryārthe virodho
niyogasya syāt । na tvatra virodho vidyate । kathaṃ na vidyate
virodhaḥ ? kathaṃ vā vidyate virodhaḥ । uktaṃ kāryāntaratvāt tuṣakaṇa-
vipramokasyeti । na ca kāryaṃ kāryāntare saṃbadhyate yathā svargaḥ
paśubhiḥ evaṃ niyogaḥ kāryaṃ tuṣakaṇavipramokaśceti viprati-
ṣiddham । anabhijño bhavān viṣayaniyojyānāmityuktam ।
﻿<pb n="b652"/>
kathaṃ anabhijñaḥ ? viṣayo hi 1nāmādhikārasaṃbandhī svargakāmo
yajeta iti । tasya ca niyogasiddhireva prayojanam । dṛṣṭe'rthe
saṃbhavatyapi yathā godohanena paśukāmasya praṇayediti ।</p>
<p>nanu cātrāpi phalasiddhiḥ; niyogasiddha‍yarthā phalasiddhiḥ
iti ṣaṣṭhe vakṣyāmaḥ । ata eva ca <q>‘karmāṇyapi jaiminiḥ phalārthatvāt’</q>
﻿<pb n="b653"/>
<q>‘phalaṃ ca puruṣārthatvāt’</q> <q>‘puruṣaśca karmārthatvāt’</q> iti viṣaya-
niyoga1 eva upasaṃhṛtaṃ sakalasya padārthajātasya śeṣatvam ।
niyojyaḥ idānīṃ kaḥ ? akārakabhūtapadārthaviśiṣṭa iti ṣaṣṭhe
vakṣyāmaḥ । kaḥ punarasau ? adhikṛtaḥ karmaṇi ? kimidaṃ adhikṛtaṃ
iti ? nanu ca kartaivādhikṛtaḥ । yathā na karturadhikāro'dhi-
kṛtasya kartṛtvamiti ṣaṣṭhe vakṣyāmaḥ । yadyevaṃ kimāyātaṃ vrīhīn
prokṣatītyatra । kāryāntarepi niyogāvirodha itīdamevāyātam ।
﻿<pb n="b654"/>
vrīhīnprokṣatīti pradhānabhūtaviṣayasaṃsparśānniyogasya na niyogāntarā-
vagatiḥ samidādīnāmiva । nanu kāryāntaramityuktam । kāryā-
ntaratve ca niyogāntarāvagatiḥ someṣṭīnāmiva । satyaṃ
yadi kāryāntaraṃ syāt । kathaṃ na kāryāntaraṃ ? adhikāra-
niyogākṣepāt taṇḍulaniṣpatteḥ svargasiddhivanna kāryāntaram ।
﻿<pb n="b655"/>
tasmādadhikāraniyoga evāyaṃ vrīhīn prokṣati iti prayājādī-
nāmiva । iyān viśeṣaḥ dṛṣṭakāryadvārakastvayaṃ sākṣānniyoga-
kārya eva prayājādiḥ na ca dvārameva pratibandhakaṃ bhavitumarhati ।
viśeṣato dṛṣṭasākṣānniyogasaṃbandhānāmapi dvāraṃ kalpyam । idaṃ ca
klṛptamiti viśeṣaḥ । tathā ca dvārakalpanāmantareṇa pradhāneti-
kartavyatāsiddhirna bhavati tathā prakaraṇapramāṇa eva vakṣyāmaḥ । tadida-
muktaṃ pramāṇābhāvānna sarvārthateti । na hi dṛṣṭe saṃbhavati
saṃbandhahetau kalpyaṃ hetvantaramātmānaṃ labhate ityarthaḥ ।
nanu ca viniyogataḥ kāryaṃ, na kāryato viniyogaḥ
﻿<pb n="b656"/>
parihṛtametat śāstrāntaradṛṣṭaviṣayatvāditi । ata eva bhedā-
bhedalakṣaṇaṃ heturiti । tasmāt sūk‍taṃ phalaṃ tu saha ceṣṭayeti ।
kāryānurodhī niyoga ityarthaḥ । ato ye yatra śrūyanta
iti siddham ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="11">dravyaṃ cotpattisaṃyogāt tadarthameva codyeta ।। 11 ।। a. 5 ।।</ab>
<p>idaṃ cintyate spha‍yaśca kapālāni ceti sannidhāpanavidhayaḥ
saṃyogato'viśeṣāt prakaraṇāviśeṣācceti kiṃ sarvārthatayā'vagamyante
uta <q>‘spha‍yenoddhanti’</q> ityevamādibhiḥ upasaṃhriyanta iti । kiṃ
tāvada‍yuk‍taṃ ? nopasaṃhriyanta iti । kutaḥ ? aśak‍teḥ । kathamaśaktiḥ ?
﻿<pb n="b657"/>
sannidhāne hi viniyogaikyāt dvāramātrānujñānācca dṛṣṭadvāra-
katvameva śakyate vak‍tum । kalpyapratipakṣatvāt । na punaḥ
dṛṣṭaviśeṣadvāramapi । tasmāt śaktito vyavasthāḥ । atrābhidhīyate ।
syādetadevaṃ yadi dvāramātramevānurudhyate niyogena (tataḥ) saṃbandhānu-
sārī hi niyogaḥ । (kathaṃ tarhi aruṇād‍yupanyāsena nirākaraṇaṃ
āsthite guṇavacanatve aruṇādivadbhaviṣyati vākye niyoga
iti ।) uktaṃ śāstrāntaravihitaviṣayatvānniyogasyeti । ataḥ
sannidhāpanavidhayo na saṃbandhavidheḥ pratipakṣāḥ bhavitumarhanti tanmūla-
tvāt iti । ataḥ siddhamatrāpi ye yatra śrūyanta iti ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b658"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="12">arthaikatve dravyaguṇayoraikakarmyānniyamaḥ syāta1 ।। 12 ।। a. 6 ।।</ab>
<p>saṃskāradravyavidhayo ye yatra śrūyante te tatraivetyuktam । guṇe
idānīṃ cintyate---kiṃ ye yatra śrūyante tatraiva uta kṛts‍ne prakaraṇe
niveśa iti । nanu ca anvitapadārthakatvāt padānāṃ naiva kevalaguṇa-
vacanatā saṃbhavati yathā na kevalākṛtivacanatā <q>‘ālabheta’</q> iti na
kevalaguṇavacanatā śakyate vak‍tuṃ yathā <q>‘vāyavyaṃ ś‍vetamālabheta’</q> iti ।
satyaṃ aparityaktadravyasyaivānvayo yatra dṛśyate amūrtasya naiva
tadudāharaṇam । yatra punaḥ parityaktadravyābhiprāye kevalaguṇavacana-
syānvayaḥ yathā paṭasya śukla iti bhavati tatra saṃśayaḥ । kāraka-
vibhak‍tau satyāmapi kiṃ kriyānvayī guṇavacana uta kevaladravyā-
nvayyeveti ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b659"/>
<p>nanu ca kevalaguṇavacanatā asyāsmin vākye naiva pratīyate
paṭasya śukla iti(vat) ṣaṣṭhīnirdeśāt dravyasya tena saṃbandhāvagateśca
śuklaśabdasya yuktaṃ kevalaguṇavacanasyānvayitvam । iha punaḥ
aruṇayeti kārakanirdeśāt kriyāsaṃbandhāvagatiḥ । tadava-
gateśca guṇamātrasyāśak‍teḥ aparityaktadravyasyaivānvayo yuktaḥ
ś‍vetamālabheteti vat । ucyate । na dravyasambandhā-
vagatireva tatra guṇavacanatve hetuḥ dravyāntarānavagatirapi
dravyāntarāvagatau hi paṭasya śuklo bhāga itivat guṇaguṇinoḥ
saṃbandho na syāt । yadyevaṃ kimāyātaṃ aruṇayeti ?
﻿<pb n="b660"/>
idamāyātam । atrāpi ekahāyanyā na dravyāntaraṃ pratīyate ।
ataḥ ekahāyanīśabdopāttatvāt dravyasya nāruṇāśabdaḥ dravyā-
ntaropaniviṣṭaṃ guṇamabhidhātuṃ śaknoti । ekahāyanyupaniveśe ca
na krayasambandha ityupariṣṭādvakṣyate । tasmāt padāntaropāttadravyake
vākye kevalaguṇavacanānvayitaiveti sthitam । ata upapadyate
saṃśayaḥ । kiṃ vākyaṃ bhitvā prakaraṇe niveśo guṇasya dravyayogitvāt
uta karaṇanirdeśāt krayaṇa eveti । kathamevaṃ sthite guṇavacanatve <quote>“1nanu
naivāyaṃ guṇavacanaḥ, kiṃ tarhi ? dravyavacanaḥ</quote> ityākṣepaḥ upapadyate । ucyate---s‍trī-
liṅganirdeśāt, dravyāśritatvāt । prātipadikārthagatatvācca liṅgasya ।
﻿<pb n="b661"/>
kimaruṇayetyevamādidarśanaṃ nāstyākṣepavādinaḥ । na nāstidarśanaṃ,
kintu aruṇayetyevamādiṣu netyabhiprāyaḥ । kathaṃ tarhi aruṇāda‍yu-
panyāsena nirākaraṇaṇam ? aruṇādiṣu prayogasādhuteti । kathamaruṇā-
valliṅgamiti dravyavacanatānirākaraṇam । sthite guṇavacanatve
dṛḍhatareṇa kāraṇena aruṇāvalliṅgaṃ bhaviṣyatītyabhiprāyaḥ <quote><q>“atha krīṇātinā
na sambadhyeta tasminneva vākye ekahāyanīśabdena sambhantsyate na bhaviṣyati vākyabheda”</q></quote>
iti vadataḥ ko'bhiprāyaḥ । ayamabhiprāyaḥ---yadā dvayoḥ kriyā-
sambandhaḥ tadā dravyāntaranirodhāt kevalaguṇavacanatā aruṇayeti ।
yadā punaḥ kriyāsambandho nāsti tadā āśritatvāda‍guṇānāṃ 
dravyāṇāṃ ca tadāśrayatvena guṇānāṃ ko nāma dravyasaṃbandhaṃ
niruṇāddhi yathā nīlotpalamiti । atrottaram---prātipadikāttā-
﻿<pb n="b662"/> 
vata guṇa eva pratīyate padāntarasaṃbandhāt‍tu aparityaktadravya-
ko'nvayaḥ । liṅgaṃ ca vākyādbalīyaḥ । kimidaṃ vākyālliṅgaṃ
balīya iti । aidamarthye hi balābalamuktam na punaranvayayo-
ge'pi । ucyate । anvayayoge ca anvayāvagatau satyāṃ kena
balābalaṃ nivāryate । uktaṃ cāsmābhiḥ । padāntareṇa dravyopādānāt
kriyāsaṃbandhācca padadva‍yasya kevalaguṇānvayitā na śakyā vākyena
bādhitum । atredānīmuttaram---kriyāyogitve'nanvayamālocya
ananvayādvaraṃ dravyānvayaḥ dravyānvayitvepi kriyānvayo nātidūraṃ
parityakto bhavati ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b663"/>
<p>avaśyaṃ caitadevābhyupagantavyam । anyathā hi prakaraṇasaṃbandho-
'pi na syāt prakaraṇe hi kriyayā dravyeṇa vā anvayaḥ । kriyayā
tāvannasaṃbandha ityuktam । atha liṅgāt dravyeṇāpi na saṃbadhyate
hanta ananvayitā'bhyupagatābhavati । na ca ananvayitā abhi-
dhānasya dharmo loke dṛṣṭaḥ । tasmādvaramasminneva vākye dravya-
saṃbandhābhyupagamaḥ । ata eva nīlotpalādiṣvapyanvayo(na)
dṛśyate । anyathā hi saṃbandhābhidhānavibhaktiśūnyānāmapi kathaṃ
vānvayaḥ syāt 1<quote><q>“naitadevamiti”</q></quote> । satyameva vaibhaktiko'pi
saṃbandhaḥ abhidhānalakṣaṇo bhavati yadyapratipakṣo bhavet
ayaṃ tu sapratipakṣaḥ । ataḥ tṛtīyānuguṇamevāsyānvayitvaṃ
﻿<pb n="b664"/>
kalpayitavyam, na punaḥ kevalābhidhānānuguṇam । tasmāt na
nīlotpalavat saṃbandha upapadyate । ucyate । yadi tṛtīyārthaḥ
prātipadikārthānvayavirodhī syāt syādetadevam । sa punaḥ prāptatvānnaiva
virudhyate । ato yāvadaprāptamekahāyanyā saṃbadhyata iti na doṣaḥ ।
bhavedetadevaṃ yadyekahāyanī nānyārthā, sāpi tvanyārthaiva । na ca
dvayoranyārthayoḥ mithaḥ saṃbandhaḥ saṃbhavati । kimarthā punarekāhayanī ?
krayārtheti brūmaḥ । kiṃ punaḥ kāraṇaṃ tulye samabhivyāhāre krayārthā
ekahāyanī na punaḥ guṇasaṃbandhārthā । atra bhāṣyaṃ <q>“abhihitamapi
punaḥ paryanuyujyata”</q> iti । yadyabhihitaṃ kimiti paryanuyujyate ।
anyārthasyānyeva saṃbandhaḥ virodhapradarśanārthaṃ tadarthamevottaraṃ tṛtīyā-
﻿<pb n="b665"/>
saṃbandhāt krayārthateti । anyārthamapyanyena saṃbadhyata iti na
doṣaḥ । śaknoti hi ākāṅkṣāvataḥ anyārthamapi sannihitamā-
kāṅkṣāṃ pūrayitum sannidhānāviśeṣāt । satyaṃ, śak‍noti na puna
ryadarthaṃ tatsaṃbandhitayaiva । nanu ca tatsaṃbandhinyapi sannidhānama-
viśiṣṭam itarasya cākāṅkṣā । bhavedetadevaṃ yadi sannidhānamaviśiṣṭaṃ
iha tu sannidhānamapyanyārtham । na cānyārthaṃ sannidhānamākāṅkṣati
svārthasiddhaye । satyamevam । tasyāvaśyānvayabhāvitvāt ।
abhidhānasya cānyasyāsannidhānāt anyārthatāmavakṛṣya
sannidhānamātraṃ parigṛhyate । tathā ca rātrisatrādiṣu dṛṣṭam ।
﻿<pb n="b666"/>
yuktamuktam, kintvatra prakaraṇāt sannidhānamananyārthaṃ vidyate ।
tasmādvākyabhedādevānvayo yuktaḥ ananyārthasya saṃbandhino'vagamāt
ataḥ prakaraṇe sarvasmin‍niveśa ityevaṃ prāpte brūmaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="12">arthaikatve dravyaguṇayoraikakarmyānniyamaḥ syāt ।। 12 ।।</ab>
<p>kraya evāruṇimā niviśate । kathaṃ ? tatsaṃbandhapratipatteḥ tṛtī-
yātaḥ । nanu kevalaguṇavacanatvāt na kriyayā saṃbadhyata ityuktam ।
duruktaṃ tat । kathaṃ duruktam ? yasya hi yādṛśaṃ kriyāsādhanatvaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ
﻿<pb n="b667"/>
tasya tathāvidhasyaiva vibhaktayaḥ saṃbandhamāpādayanti । dravyaviśeṣaṇa-
tayā ca guṇaḥ kriyāṃ niṣpādayati । aviśiṣṭasya kāraṇatvānu-
papatteḥ । nanu cānupāttadravyaka evāyaṃ prayogaḥ paṭasya śukla
iti vadityuktam । tatsatyamuktaṃ na punaranupāttadravyatayā kriyā-
saṃbandho'pahnotuṃ śakyate । svavyāpārāpekṣitvāt kriyāyogasya ।
na cānupāttadravyatayā vyāpārahāniḥ śakyate vak‍tum । svavyā-
pārāpekṣāṇi kārakāṇi kriyayā saṃbadhyante iti na kārakāntara-
vyāpāramapekṣante । nāpyarthāntaragataṃ hānamupādānaṃ vā'bhidhānasya ।
﻿<pb n="b668"/>
tasmādbhinnavyāpārakatvādekahāyanīdvāraka eva krayasaṃbandha upapannaḥ ।
ata eva ca na vikalpaḥ prayojanavada‍dravyāntara---
saṃbandhārthaṃ kriyāyāḥ prādhānyam । tatprādhānye tu na pratyekaṃ
vākyaparisamāptiḥ । tasmādekavākyatvātsiddhaṃ dravyaguṇayoraikakarmyā-
nniyama iti ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="13">ekatvayuktamekasya śrutisaṃyogāt1 ।। 3-4-13 ।। (a. 7)</ab>
<p>ukto dravyaguṇasaṃskārāṇāṃ viniyogaḥ । idānīṃ viniyojya-
viṣayagatā cintā kriyate । evaṃ śrūyate <q>‘grahaṃ saṃmārṣṭi’</q> iti ।
﻿<pb n="b669"/>
tatra saṃśayaḥ---kiṃ śoṣiṇo viśeṣaṇaṃ śoṣitve ādriyate śeṣasyeva śeṣa-
tve uta neti । kathaṃ punaratra saṃśayaḥ ? yuktaṃ nāvaccheṣaḥ upādīyamāna-
tvāt tadupayogiviśeṣaṇam । śeṣiṇaḥ punaḥ kāryāntare nirjñātaśeṣa-
bhāvasyaiva svaśeṣayogo yukta iti na saṃśayaṃ manyāmahe । ucyate ।
śrutitaḥ sarvaṃ kalpate nopādeyatvāt paśorekatvam, kiṃ tarhi ?
śruteḥ । śrutiścennādriyate dvitvaṃ bahutvaṃ vā kimiti śoṣitayā nopā-
dīyate । ataḥ śeṣiṇyapi yathaiva grahaśrutirādriyate evamekatvaśrutirapi
aviśeṣāt । tadidamuk‍taṃ---<q>‘ekatvayuktamekasya śrutisaṃyogādi’</q>ti ।
﻿<pb n="b670"/>
ata eva ca <q>‘agnīnādadhīta’</q> iti bahutvasiddhiḥ yūpaṃ chinatti’
iti ca ekatvam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="14">sarveṣāṃ vā lakṣaṇatvādaviśiṣṭaṃ hi lakṣaṇam ।। 14 ।।</ab>
<p>atrocyate---naitadevaṃ yadekasya saṃskāra iti । saṃskāro hi nāma
vyāpārāntarayogyatā । yasya saṃskāro vyāpārāntarayogyatālakṣaṇaḥ
saṃbhavati sa eva saṃbandhitāmāpadyate । nanu ca sasaṅkhyāka
eva saṃskāreṇa vyāpārāntarayogyaḥ kriyate । kutaḥ ? vyāpārāntaraṃ
upādānaśeṣatvāt saṅakhyāyā liṅgasya ca । yathābhūtaścāsau śeṣaḥ
tathābhūtasyaiva saṃskārasaṃbandhaḥ kāryārthatvāt । aindravāyavādi-
﻿<pb n="b671"/>
vākyeṣu ca ekatvayuktā eva grahāḥ śeṣatvena śrūyante । ato-
'vivakṣitamityayuktam । na ca grahamātraṃ śeṣaḥ ekaikasya
viniyogāt ।</p>
<p>nanu viniyuktasyopādānaśeṣatvaṃ saṅkhyādayaḥ pratipadyante yathā
ca śeṣabhāve prādhānyaṃ tathā śeṣibhāvepi । bhavatu prādhānyaṃ na
kaścidvirodhaḥ saṅkhyādyaparityāgena tu yathaiva śeṣatāṃ pratipadyate tathaiva
saṃskāryatāmapīti vadamāḥ । atrocyate---satyaṃ śeṣabhūtasyaiva saṃskāraḥ
tathāpi saṅkhyādayo na saṃbadhyante । kutaḥ ? sarvatra hi padārthāntara-
saṃbandhaḥ pradhānasyaiva rājapuruṣamānayetivat । tatra hi rājārthaḥ
﻿<pb n="b672"/>
kevalamupalakṣaṇatayaiva bhāti । evamatrāpi dravyameva pradhānaṃ, yadanyatta-
dupalakṣaṇaṃ jātyādi । na ca upalakṣaṇasya kāryasaṃbandhaḥ । ata
idamuktaṃ aviśiṣṭaṃ hi lakṣaṇamiti । nahyekatvadīnāṃ vilakṣaṇatve
grahāntaranivṛttau sāmarthyamasti saṃbandhī hi saṃbandhyantaraṃ nivartayati ।
nanu coktaṃ na saṃbandhimātraṃ(tā) saṃbandhī hetuḥ kastarhi ? śrutyādi-
pratipādyateti । atra caikatvaviśiṣṭaḥ śrutyā pratipādyate śeṣī ।
kathaṃ ca śakyate vak‍tum śrutipramāṇake vastuni ekatvamaviva-
kṣitamiti । na coddiśyamānatvaṃ vidhīyamānatvaṃ vā śrutiṃ vihanti ।
śrutividhāte hi grahepyaprāptiḥ syāt । athāyamabhiprāyaḥ uddiśya-
mānasya viśeṣaṇamavivakṣitamiti । asyaivārthasyāsminnadhikaraṇe
heturvaktavyaḥ na cāsāvastītyuktamiti । ucyeta---ayamasti hetuḥ
﻿<pb n="b673"/>
kāryavaduddiśyamānaṃ pradhānībhavati । pradhānasya vidheyena saṃbandho'tra
na pradhānasya guṇānāṃ, yasmāt guṇānāṃ pradhānopādānanimittaṃ
tadupādānaśeṣatvam ।</p>
<p>ke punaramī guṇāḥ ye vibhaktyabhidheyāḥ prātipadikārthasya ।
kathaṃ guṇatā vibhaktyarthānāṃ ? prātipadikārthaṃ pratyavacchedakatvāt ।
vibhaktyartho hi prātipādikārthamavacchinatti । avacchedakatayā ca
upādānaśeṣatā । tasmāt siddhaṃ saṅkhyādeḥ dravyaṃ prati guṇatvaṃ
vibhaktyabhidheyasya । na ca guṇānāṃ guṇaiḥ saha saṃbandho
vidyate guṇaścāyaṃ saṃskāro nāma । uk‍taṃ ca guṇānāṃ ca
parārthatvāt” iti । athāpi nāma prātipādikābhidheya
evāyamartho jātyādiḥ viniyojyaśca । tathāpyanuddiśyamāno
naiva pradhānatāṃ śaknoti pratipat‍tum । kimiti ? uddeśohi nāma
﻿<pb n="b674"/>
kāryāvacchinnasya vastuno bhavati na padārthamātrāvacchinnasya । ato
jātyādibhiḥ dravyamevopalakṣayitavyam । na hi dravyaviśeṣādṛte
kāryaviśeṣaparyavasānaṃ bhavati । tasmādupalakṣaṇatayaiva tatra jātyā-
deranvayaḥ na punaḥ kārakatayā । nanu caivaṃ sati upādeyatvepi kārya-
viśeṣānavagāt jātyādīnāmupalakṣaṇataiva । na caivamiṣyate jātirevāṅga-
miti mīmāṃsakāḥ । anabhijño bhavān upāttopādeyayoḥ upātta-
dravyalakṣaṇaṃ hyuddiśyamānapadārtho bhavati । vidheyaṃ punaḥ kamupalakṣa-
yati ? vihitatvāddhi kāryasidhyarthaṃ svāśrayaṃ dravyamākṣipati nopalakṣa-
yati । ata uddiśyamānasya upalakṣaṇatvāt dravye saṃpratyayo bhavati
﻿<pb n="b675"/>
na punaḥ svasaṃbandhinyabhidheye । tasmāt kāryamātramevāpekṣate'vacche-
dakatayā na punaḥ śrutyā'bhihitamekatvādikam । (tarhi) upāttataiva
tatra viśeṣāvagame hetuḥ । yatpunarupādeyaṃ tat śrutita eva viśiṣṭa-
mavagantavyam, nānyata iti viśeṣaḥ । so'yamukto hetuḥ uddiśya-
mānasya viśeṣaṇamavivakṣitamityatrārthe । upāttatvādityuk‍to hetuḥ ।
kā vārtā agnīnādadhīta yūpaṃ cchinattīti ? vivakṣitā saṅkhyā, atra
hīdamevopādānavākyam । nanu cāgnipadabhuddeśakam । pradhānabhūtāścā-
gnayaḥ । satyaṃ yathā bhavānāha । kintu dvividho hyuddeśaḥ upāttasyānu-
pāttasya ca । grahaṃ saṃmārṣṭītyupāttoddeśaḥ ag‍nīnādadhītetyanupāttoddeśaḥ
﻿<pb n="b676"/>
anupāttañcoddiśyata iti kathamidaṃ ? vidheyaviṣayo hyuddeśa ityucyate,
nopāttatvamanupāttatvaṃ ca uddeśyatve hetuḥ । ataḥ pramāṇāntarasiddha-
viśeṣaṇaṃ uddiśyamānamavivakṣitaviśeṣaṇaṃ bhavati । yatpunaravijñāta-
viśeṣaṇamevoddiṣṭaṃ tat vidheyavat śrutita eva viśiṣṭamavagantavyam ।
tasmāt suṣṭhūcyate upāttoddeśe'vivakṣitaṃ viśeṣaṇamiti । nanu
ca grahaṃ saṃmārṣṭīti dvitīyeyaṃ kārakavibhaktiḥ kārakaṃ
ca kriyārthaṃ bhavatīti śābdāḥ । nanu īpsitatame dvitīye-
yam । satyaṃ, sā tu kārake । nanu ca vipratiṣiddhaṃ
﻿<pb n="b677"/>
īpsitatamaṃ kārakaṃ ceti ? kathaṃ vipratiṣiddhaṃ ? kimidaṃ
īpsitatamaṃ nāma ? yadi tāvat yataḥ kriyāsiddhiḥ
tadīpsitatamaṃ evaṃ tarhi kārakamātre prasaṅgaḥ tataśca viśeṣā-
bhidhānamanarthakamidaṃ karma idaṃ karaṇamiti । atha yatkriyayā āpyate
utpādyate saṃskriyate vā tatkarmetyucyate । na tarhi kārakaṃ kriyā-
paryavasānāpekṣo hyāptyādiko guṇaḥ । paryavasite hi vyāpāre phalaṃ
niṣpadyate na punaḥ phala[sya]sādhyaiva kriyā bhavati । ataḥ īpsitaṃ
kārakaṃ ceti vipratiṣiddham । atrābhidhīyate---na viprati-
ṣiddham । āptyādiko guṇaḥ kārakasthaścākārakasthaśca yadā kārakasthaḥ
﻿<pb n="b678"/>
tadā kārakameva phalam । kimidaṃ kārakameva phalamiti ? ।
yadā hi kārakameva kayācidvikārāpattyā vyāpyamutpādyaṃ
saṃskāryaṃ vikāryaṃ ceṣṭaṃ tadā tadeva phalamityucyate tāmevāvasthā-
maṅgīkṛtya īpsitatamavyapadeśaṃ labhata iti । kriyāsiddha‍yarthaṃ
phalasiddha‍yarthaṃ vā । ataḥ kārakamīpsitatamamiti na viruddham ।
vidyate hi kārakaṃ na phalasamavāyi yathā karaṇādi । vidyate
ca phalaṃ na kārakasamavāyi yathā svargādi । nanu
svargādyapi kārakasamavāyyeva kartṛgāmi kriyāphalamiti vaca-
nāt । na kārakatayā phalasamavāyo vidyata iti ।
adhikāralakṣaṇavyāpāro'yaṃ adhikāralakṣaṇe uktaḥ । kathaṃ
tarhi bhagavataḥ pāṇineḥ sūtraṃ kartrabhiprāye kriyāphale
﻿<pb n="b679"/>
iti ? asyāpi tatraivārtho nirūpyate । ato grahaṃ
saṃmārṣṭīti yadyapi grahaḥ saṃmārgaṃ niṣpādayati tathāpi na tasyāṃ-
śasya vācikā vibhaktiḥ īpsitatamatvabhācaṣṭe phalāṃśaṃmityarthaḥ kriyā-
niṣpādyamiti yāvat । tasmāt śrutito viśeṣāvagama iti
siddham । ataḥ upāttaviṣayaḥ saṃskāra iti sthitam । nanu ca
vyabhicāryetaddarśanam । anīpsitatame'pi dvitīyā bhavatyeva । tataḥ
kim ? idaṃ tato bhavati kārakāṃśābhidhāyinī na phalāṃśābhidhā-
yinī । evaṃ grahamityapi kārakamevācaṣṭe । tataścaikatvamaviva-
kṣitamimi na śakyate vak‍tum । kathaṃ tarhi grahārthaḥ saṃmārgaḥ
pramāṇābhāvāt । prayojanavatvāt yathā paśupuroḍāśo'g‍nīṣoma-
devatārthaḥ । atrābhidhīyate---karmepsitatamatvaṃ tāvat dvitīyā'bhidhatte ।
tathā yuk‍taṃ cānīpsitamiti tu kriyānirbāhyamevetyarthaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b680"/>
iyān viśeṣaḥ kriyāntarasaṃbandhitayā ekasyopādānaṃ ekasya neti ।
evaṃ tarhi gāṃ dadātītyavivakṣitatvaṃ saṅkhyāyāḥ । bhavatviti cenna;
prayojanāntarakalpanāprasaṅgāt । kimiti kalpanā neṣyate ? pramāṇā-
bhāvāt । nanu ca dvitīyaiva pramāṇaṃ; satyaṃ, kāryāpekṣāyāṃ viśeṣaṃ
samarpayāti na punaḥ kāryāntaramavagamayituṃ kṣamā, viniyogaparyava-
sāyinyo hi vibhakta‍yaḥ na kāryaparyavasāyinyaḥ navā'dhikāra-
śūnyo niyogo'stīti <q>‘phalavatsannidhau’</q> ityatra vakṣyāmaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b681"/>
saṃskāravidhayastūktāḥ teṣāmarthena ityatra । uktottaramapi kimiti
bhavatā paricoditaṃ ? (bhāvikārya)vismaraṇāparādhāditi manyāmahe
tadidaṃ smāryate anupātaviṣayamidaṃ prādhānyamiti yūpavat siddhaṃ
vivakṣitatvaṃ saṅkhyāyāḥ । amunā ca viśeṣeṇa sūtrāntarapraṇayanaṃ
bhagavataḥ pāṇineḥ akathitamiti । tatrāpi tathāyuktamityanuvartate
tasmāt dvitīyāprādhānyaṃ na vyabhicaratīti sthitam । upātte tu
viṣaye viśeṣaṇamavivakṣitamiti siddham । 1<quote>grahādiṣvekatvaṃ
brūyāt na dvitīyādīn pratiṣedhet”</quote> iti । upāttaviṣayatvāt tu grahaśruteḥ
upādeye hyekatvādayo viśeṣaṇam । iha punaḥ upāttataiva viśeṣā-
vargatau heturityuktam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b682"/>
<p>nanu ca <q>‘parisañcaṣṭa’</q> iti ko'bhiprāyaḥ ? ayamabhiprāyaḥ---eka-
tvamananvitaṃ syāt nānanvitānāmabhidhānamastītyuk‍taṃ tadbhūtā-
dhikaraṇe । naitadasti satyamananvitābhidhānamekavacanasya prāpnoti na
punaḥ parisaṅkhyā saṃbhavati aprāptatvāt । grahasaṃbhārgādeḥ saṃbandhasya
prāptau satyāmanyanivṛttau niyogaḥ prabhavati । aprāpte punaḥ yathā
ś‍veti śrutiḥ na kākādīn nivartayituṃ kṣamā । na cānanvitā-
bhidhānam tasyāpi prāp‍tyavagamāt । nanu ca yuktaṃ śvādiṣu । ekatvaṃ
punaḥ bahuṣūpādīyamāneṣu pakṣepi na prāp‍noti । ato'nanvitā-
bhidhānaṃ duṣpariharamiti । parihṛtamidaṃ bhāṣyakāreṇa na vibhak‍terva-
canamevaikaṃ prayojanamiti । kathaṃ punaranena parihṛtamidaṃ bhavati ?
itthamanena parihṛtaṃ bhavati-saṅkhyāyā ananvaye'pi karmamātre prayoga-
darśanāt yathā brāhmaṇo na hantavya iti । atrāpi sādhyamiti cet,
﻿<pb n="b683"/>
na nañarthe vadhena saṃbadhyamāne ekatvamanvetuṃ kṣamam । anyataḥ
pravṛttyavagamāt । tasmādekatvābhidhānaṃ karmamātre sādhviti
draṣṭavyam ।</p>
<p>1<quote>ayaṃ cāparo doṣaḥ iti</quote> । ekatvānvitābhidhāne āśrīyamāṇe
grahatvaṃ nopāttaviṣayaṃ syāt anupāttaviṣayatve ca grahatvasyānanvayaḥ
prāp‍noti । ananvīyamāne ca saṃsargavidhānaṃ nirviṣayatvādanarthakam ।
﻿<pb n="b684"/>
<q>“athaikatvasaṃmārgasaṃbandho vidhīyeta”</q> tatrāpi dvayī gatiḥ syāt anena
guṇaphalasaṃbandhavadvidhānaṃ na saṃbhavatīti darśayati । anyatra syāditi
kathaṃ ? ekatvaṃ tāvannopāttasyopalakṣaṇāya alaṃ bhavati ।
sammārgeṇa hi saṃbadhyamānaṃ pradhānaṃ vā bhavati guṇo vā
nānyaḥ saṃbandho'sti । kathaṃ nāsti ? prātipadikāśritaṃ hi
saṅkhyābhidhānaṃ vibhak‍tīnāmityuktam । kasmānna viṣayatayā
uddeśyatayā vidheyatayā vā saṃbandhaḥ saṃbhavati paratantratvāt ।
﻿<pb n="b685"/>
abhyupagamyāpyaruṇāvanna saṃbhavatītyuktaṃ grahasya pradhānatvāt ।
nanu ca pradhānepi saṃbhavatyeva viśeṣaṇaṃ nimittabhūtaṃ kārakatva-
māśritya । kena cok‍taṃ na saṃbhavatīti ? iha punarvidhānāsaṃbhavaḥ
pradarśita pradhānatvāda‍grahasya । athocyeta grahādi lakṣayitvā tasyaika-
tvasaṃbandho vidhīyate na saṃmārgasaṃbandha iti । ko'bhiprāyaḥ ? ayamabhi-
prāyaḥ---kaḥ punaḥ pakṣapātaḥ saṃmārgo'nvayī na punarekatvamiti ।
uttaraṃ---kriyāśūnyo'pyanvayo na saṅkhyādeḥ saṃbhavati । asati
tu vidheye saṃbhavatyapi na ca śrutyānvayaḥ ekatvasyāstītyuktam ।
﻿<pb n="b686"/>
yadyavivakṣitamekatvamiti1 lakṣaṇavirodhaṃ darśayati । bahuṣu bahuvacana-
miti śābdāḥ । na vayametadvicārayāmaḥ2 iti pramāṇataḥ sthite lakṣye
kiṃ lakṣaṇaṃ kariṣyatītyabhiprāyaḥ । na cātra lakṣaṇavirodhaḥ na
vibhak‍tervacanamevaikaṃ prayojanamiti vyākhyātam । api ca grahaḥ
prātipadikārthaḥ ekatvaṃ vibhaktyarthaḥ । kimato yadyevam ? etadato bhavati
prātipadikārthagataṃ hi vibhaktiḥ svamarthaṃ śrutyaiva vadatīti vibhaktya-
bhihitasya pāratantryaṃ darśayati । tacca vyākhyātam । atha yaduktaṃ
paśumālabheteti upādeyānāṃ śrutito viśeṣa ityuktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="16">3saṃskārādvā guṇānāmavyavasthā syāt ।। 3-1.16 ।। a. 8.</ab>
<p>yadi kāryata upādānāṃ upāttasya ca lakṣaṇaṃ
﻿<pb n="b687"/>
śeṣitayaiveti tato grahaśrutirapi hi somarasādhāre pātre lakṣaṇaiva ।
ekakāryatvāt । saṃmārgasya ca somarasāvasekanirharaṇameva prayo-
janamityupapannaṃ camasānāmapi saṃmārjanam । darśitaṃ caitadbhāṣya-
kāreṇa । sāmarthyataśca kāryasiddhau kevalasammārgavidhānalābhaḥ
prakaraṇe mantropadeśavat । uktaṃ caitadbhāṣyakāreṇa ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="17">1vyavasthā vā'rthasya śrutisaṃyogāt tasya śabdapramāṇatvāt ।। 3-1.17 ।।</ab>
<p>atrābhidhīyate---śrutitaḥ upāttaparijñānaṃ nopādā-
nāt śrutiḥ । śrutiśca grahaṃ saṃmārṣṭīti । nanu ca
somāvasiktaparimārjanaṃ tulyaṃ kāryamityuktam । satyamuktam ।
﻿<pb n="b688"/>
na śrutibādhe tatsamarthamityuktamasmābhiḥ । śrute yadeva kāryaṃ tadeva
cet kāryaṃ kimityaśrute'pi na bhavati । na hi kāryaṃ śrūyate ।
śrūyate hi kāryamityuktam । kāryaṃ cenna kriyate kathaṃ yaveṣu prokṣaṇam ?
yathā tat tathā navame vakṣyāmaḥ । yaduk‍taṃ saṃsargamātra-
vidhānaṃ lābho labhyata iti । tadayuktam । niyogaviṣayatvāta
niyogasya darśitaṃ ca bhāṣyakāreṇa । viniyoge sati na
﻿<pb n="b688"/>
kaścidvirodho niyogasya syāt sannikarṣasyāpi viśeṣāt । sa ca
virodhe । iha tu virodhābhāvādatantraṃ viprakarṣa iti siddham ।
ekatvaṃ punaryathā nānveti tathoktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="18">1ānarthakyāttadaṅgeṣu ।। 3-1-18 ।। a. 9</ab>
<p><q>‘saptadaśāratnirvājapeyasya yūpo bhavati’</q> ityatroddeśakaṃ padaṃ kiṃ
vājapeyasya saptadaśeti uta yūpasya saptadaśeti । pūrvapakṣavādino'bhi-
prāyaḥ । yadi yūpa ityuddeśakaṃ padaṃ vājapeyasyetyananvitābhidhānaṃ
﻿<pb n="b690"/>
prāp‍noti yūpena vājapeyasyāsaṃbandhāt । tasmāt vājapeyasaṃbandhini
yūpaśabdo draṣṭavyaḥ । evamanvitapadārthako vākyārthaḥ samarthito bhavati ।
atrābhidhīyate । yadi yūpaśabde śrautānvayini vājapeyasyetyananvitaṃ
syāt syādetadevam । atra punaḥ saptadaśārat‍niryūpa ityapi saṃbandhe
vājapeyaśabdo'nvita eva । kathaṃ ? saṃbandhasaṃbandhinyapi ṣaṣṭhyantasyā-
nvayadarśanāt devadattasya nap‍tetyevamādiṣu । tasmādyūpaśabdasya
lākṣaṇikatve nāsti pramāṇamiti yūpenaiva saṃbandhaḥ । kimiti punaratra
vājapeyasyetyanena kṛtam ? kimasmākamanena kṛtaṃ na kṛtamiti ?
﻿<pb n="b691"/> 
anvayastāvadvidyate । vidyamānānvaye tu vākyārthe kiñcitkāryayogi
bhavati kiñcit prāptārthaṃ sadanūdyata iti na doṣaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="19">1kartṛguṇe tu karmasamavāyādvākyabhedaḥ syāt ।। 3-1-19 ।। a. 10</ab>
<p>abhikrāmaṃ juhotīti kiṃ karmaṇaḥ karmānvayo vidyate uta neti
cintyate । kathaṃ punaranvayo vidyate kathaṃ vā na ? tatra pūrvapakṣavādino-
'bhiprāyaḥ na karma karmasādhyaṃ bhavati । tasmādyaḥ prakaraṇe kartā'bhi-
krāmatītyanvayaḥ । nanu ca prayājeṣvapi yaḥ kartā tatrāpyanvayo bhavatyeva ।
﻿<pb n="b692"/>
satyaṃ bhavati yadi juhotītyabhidhāyakaḥ syāt । anabhidhāya-
katve tasmin na karturuddeśyatvaṃ saṃbhavati nānṛtaṃ vadeditivat ।
tasmāt saṃyogato'viśeṣāt prakaraṇāviśeṣācca vākyabhedaḥ । juhoti-
rodānīṃ kimarthaḥ ? yadarthastadartho bhaviṣyatīti ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="20">1sākāṅkṣaṃ tvekavākyaṃ syādasamāptaṃ hi pūrveṇa ।। 20 ।।</ab>
<p>satyamananvayaḥ karmaṇaḥ karmaṇā । kartṛsaṃbandhāt tu
aruṇāvat saṃbhavatīti । nanu ca karturupādānaṃ
nāsti yathā ekahāyanyāḥ, juhotītyasyānabhidhāyakatvādi-
﻿<pb n="b693"/>
tyuktam । na brūmaḥ karturuddeśo'stīti । tannimittakastu karmodde-
śe'pyanvayo na virudhyata iti, tatra tasya saṃbhavāt aruṇādhikaraṇa-
vaiṣamyam । tatra dvayorapyanvayinorupādānaṃ iha tu saṃbhavamātreṇaiveti
viśeṣaḥ । yaduk‍taṃ bhāṣyakāreṇa pūrvapakṣe saṃbandhamātraparijñānāt
prayogavacanāt kartavyatāsiddhiḥ iti tatraiva karturuddeśyatvaṃ na
virudhyata ityabhiprāyaḥ । rāddhāntavādī tu saṃbhavamātreṇānvaya-
siddherna karturuddeśena prayojanamastīti manyate । ataḥ siddhaṃ karmāpi
karmaṇāmuddeśyatāṃ pratipadyata iti ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b694"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="21">1sandigdhe tu vyavāyādvākyabhedaḥ syāt ।। 3-1-21 ।। a. 11</ab>
<p>upavyayata ityatra sandihyate---kiṃ sāmidhenyanuvacanasya kartā
upavyānena saṃbadhyate uta kṛts‍ne prakaraṇa iti । nanu naivātroddeśyaṃ
padaṃ kiñcicchrūyate । anuddiṣṭapadārthaṃ ca yattat prakaraṇenaiva saṃbadhyate
saṃyogato'viśeṣāt prakaraṇāviśeṣāccetyuktam । ucyate---ādhastye
tāvadadhikaraṇe anuddiṣṭenāpi kartrā'nvayo'pi na virudhyata
ityuktam । evamatrāpi sāmidhenīnāṃ kartuḥ sannidhānāt
kriyāntarasādhanatayā upavyānasya loke'vagatatvāt anuddi-
ṣṭo'pi kartā sannihitaḥ kāryaparipūraṇāyālaṃ bhavitumarhati ।
﻿<pb n="b695"/> 
<quote>1nanu darśapūrṇamāsayoreva prakaraṇamidam । paraprakaraṇe sāmidhenyaḥ śrūyanta
iti ।</quote> ko'sya bhāṣyasyārthaḥ ? varṇito'smābhiruddeśyapadā-
bhāvāt prakaraṇāviśeṣaḥ । <quote><q>“satyaṃ, paraprakaraṇe śrūyante । tathāpi
tāsāmavāntaraprakaraṇamasti”</q></quote> iti । kimidamavāntaraprakaraṇam । ekasya
hi adhikāravidheḥ prakaraṇam । na hi aṅgavidhīnāmapi prakaraṇamasti ।
pradhānavidhyabhedāt । pradhānavidhīnāṃ ca abhedaṃ caturthe vakṣyāmaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b696"/>
saṃskāravidhīnāṃ ca teṣāmarthena saṃbandha ityatrānuvādaḥ pradarśitaḥ ।
tasmādavāntaraprakaraṇaṃ grāhakaviniyojakatayā nopapadyate ।
ataḥ sannidhānamātramavaśiṣvate । ucyate---sannidhāna evāyaṃ
prakaraṇaśabdaḥ prayuktaḥ । kathamavagamyate । yena tatsannidhā-
vabhidhīyamānaṃ tasyeti jñāyate iti vacanāt । nanu ca
viniyojake'pi prakaraṇe sannidhānaśrutiśabdaḥ upapadyate ।
kena cok‍taṃ nopapadyata iti । kintu tanna saṃbhavatī-
tyuktam । vākyabhedaśravaṇācca, vyavadhānaṃ ca darśayati ।
﻿<pb n="b697"/>
parārthena vyavadhānamānantaryaṃ vihantiṃ na punaḥ viniyogam । anyathā
svāhākārasyāviniyogaḥ syāt samidādibhirvyavadhānāt । atha
nivitpadānāmanyārthatvāt grāhakasyāpi vyavadhānamiti dvādaśāhīna-
syetyapi vyavadhānaṃ syāt । kiñca kāmyairavyavadhānaṃ nivitpadānāṃ
syāt । tataśca nividarthatā prāpnoti । satyaṃ yadyanuvacanavyavadhāna-
mabhipretam । iha tu sannihitakartṛvyavadhānamabhipretaṃ tacca guṇaphala-
saṃbandhābhidhāne sati karmaṇo vyavadhānādupapannaṃ karturvyavadhānam ।
﻿<pb n="b698"/>
evaṃ sthite pūrvapakṣavādino'bhiprāyaḥ---guṇaphalasaṃbandhepyanuvacana-
śrutau kartā sannihita eveti sāmidhenyarthaṃ upavyānam
rāddhāntavādī tu nāvidhīyamānaṃ sannihitaṃ bhavati svasthānasthitamanu-
vadanīyamanūdyate, na punaḥ sannidhāpyate । anūdyamānavaśavartitvā-
danuvādānām । ataḥ sannidhānāviśeṣāt kṛts‍ne prakaraṇe niveśa
iti siddham ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="22">guṇānāṃ ca parārthatvādasaṃbandhaḥ samatvāt syāta1 ।। (3, 1. 22. a. 12) ।।</ab>
<p>vāraṇo yajñāvacara iti yajñasaṃbandhitvena pātraṃ śrūyate ānartha-
kyāttadaṅgoṣviti sthito nyāyaḥ । tadidānīṃ pavamāna-
﻿<pb n="b699"/>
haviṣāṃ yadyādhānāṅgatā tataḥ pavamānahaviṣṣveva pātravidhānametat ।
yadi nāṅgatā tadā sarvayajñārthamiti । kiṃ tāvad‍yuktam ? pavamāna-
haviṣṣu vidhānam । ādhānāṅgaṃ hi pavamānahavīṃṣi prakaraṇe caitacchrūyate
pradhāne cāsaṃbhavat dharmaḥ aṅgeṣu vidheya ityuktam । nanu ca
pavamānahavīṃṣi agnyarthāni yadāhavanīye juhotīti vacanāt ।
anārabhyavādo'yaṃ sarvahomānāṃ guṇatvenāhavanīyaṃ vidadhāti na
prādhānyaṃ saṃbhavati । tasmādānarthakyāttadaṅgeṣviti pavamānahaviṣṣu
vidhānam । atrābhidhīyate---naivādhānaprakaraṇe pavamānahavīṃṣi śrūyante
nāpyagnyarthānyeva । kathaṃ ? yadāhavanīye juhotīti vacanāt ।
﻿<pb n="b700"/>
nanu ca guṇatayā vidadhātyanārabhyavādo'yamityuktam । na brūmo na guṇa-
tayā vidadhātīti । kintvatra prakṛtitaḥ prāptipradarśanārthaṃ evaṃ vacana-
mupanyastaṃ nopadeśārtham । kathaṃ punaḥ prakṛtiprīptau prādhānyaṃ bhavatīti
nanu ca guṇatayaiva prakṛtito'pi prāp‍noti । satyamevam । ādhāno-
pakārakatvamagniniṣpattyā bhavati । agniniṣpattiścetprayojanaṃ kimi-
tyādhānopakārakatayā na punaḥ sākṣātprakṛtitaḥ saṃbandhāt । nanu ca
guṇatayā prāptirityuktam । satyamuktaṃ sā punarādhānāṅgatve na saṃbhavati
aniṣpannatvādag‍neḥ । niṣpādayatīti cet tarhi sākṣānniṣpādakatvam ।
﻿<pb n="b701"/>
na hi sākṣātsaṃbandhe saṃbhavati parapṛṣṭhena saṃbandho yuktaḥ ।
tasmātsarvārthatā vāraṇādeḥ yuk‍teti ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="13">mithaścānarthasaṃbandhāt ।।3-1-23 a. 13 ।।</ab>
<p>tadeva punarudāharaṇāntare cintyate kenacit viśeṣeṇāna-
rthakyāttadaṅgeṣviti । kaḥ punarasau viśeṣaḥ । ayamasau viśeṣaḥ ।
tatra yūpaśabdaḥ śrūyate । iha punaḥ nājyabhāgābhidhānam । ataḥ
pūrvapakṣavādī manyate । yuk‍taṃ vājapeye yūpaśabdābhidhānāt vyava-
dhāne'pi vājapeyetyanvayaḥ । iha punaḥ saṃbandhisaṃbandhyanvaye na
kiñcit pramāṇamasti । katha tarhi dvivacanam । dvayordvivacanam । nanu
caikatvāt prādhānyasyaikaivānuvākyā । kimidaṃ ekatvātpradhānasyeti ।
﻿<pb n="b702"/>
nanu caikaikatra pradhānatrayamasti । na brūmaḥ ekameva pradhānamiti । ekai-
kasyetikartavyatāsaṃbandha iti vadāmaḥ tataḥ kiṃ dvayorasaṃbandhaḥ ।
nanu cājyabhāgayorekena saṃbandhaḥ । satyameva, śrutyā tu dvayotpatteḥ
dvandvābhidhānamaviruddham । iha punaḥ pradhāne svataḥ ekatvāt anu-
vākyāyā ekaikasyāścotpatteḥ pradhānānāṃ dvandvavirodhaḥ । ucyate---na
virodhaḥ । kimiva vacanaṃ na kuryāt nāstivacanasyātibhāra iti ।
tatra dvitvamayathārthatvaṃ ca mantrasya bhaviṣyati, vyavadhāne pramāṇā-
bhāvādityuktam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b703"/>
<p>atrocyate---tadidamayuktamabhihitamiti vadāmaḥ । kasmāt ? na
tatrāpi yūpaśabdābhidhānaṃ hetuḥ । kiṃ tarhi vidheyasya yogyatā ।
saṃbhavati ca yogyatayāpyanvayo vājapeyasyetyuktam । evamatrāpi
saṃbhavati yathāyogyavidhāne yathārthatvadvitvayoḥ pramāṇamasti ।
tasmādājyabhāgayoreva mantravidhānamiti siddham ।</p>
<p>yatpunaridamuktaṃ bhāṣyakāreṇa1 nanu pradhānagāmitvepi dvayoḥ
pradhānayordve anuvākye āgneyasya ag‍nīṣomīyasya ceti tatkathaṃ ?
dvitvotpattervirodhāt । abhyupagamyāpi yuktyantaravirodhapradarśa-
nārtham ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b704"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="14">ānantaryamacodanā ।।1 3. 1. 24-a. 14 ।।</ab>
<p>yadi yogyatā niyamahetuḥ ihāpi tarhi staraṇe dīkṣitāvedane ca
parisamāptā yogyatā ityatraivaidamarthyaparisamāptiḥ ।</p>
<p>atrocyate---satyaṃ yadyatraiva yogyatā kṛts‍nepi prakaraṇe sā ।
tathaiva yadi paramekavākyatāṃ niyantuṃ kṣamā । sā ca nāsti dvayo-
rākhyātayorasaṃbandhāta kriyāyāṃ kriyārthāyāṃ tumun‌ṇvulauḥ tau ca
na staḥ ataḥ kṛts‍ne prakaraṇe niveśaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="15">śeṣastu guṇasaṃyuktaḥ ।। 3-1-25-a. 15 ।।</ab>
<p>kaḥ punaratra pūrvapakṣavādino'bhiprāyaḥ āgneyepi
saṃbhavati aindrāgnepi saṃbhavatīti । ayamabhi-
﻿<pb n="b705"/>
prāyaḥ---uddeśye hi padārthamātrarayaiva upalakṣaṇatvam । saṃbandhimātra-
tayaiva siddherna viśeṣo'pekṣaṇīyaḥ । vidheye punaḥ viśeṣaniṣṭhatvātkāryasya
yuktaṃ viśeṣāpekṣaṇam । tasmādāgneyavidhau naindrāgnavidhiḥ upalakṣaṇe
punaḥ padārthānugamānna virodhaḥ । ata eva cāvyāsajyasaṃbandhi-
ḍitthaḍavitthadarśanam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="27">vyavasthā vā'pyarthasaṃyogāt ।। 27 ।।</ab>
<p>atrābhidhīyate---yathā bhavānāha tathāpi tu yathā'bhidheyaṃ
lakṣaṇāsaṃbhave nāyathārthatvaṃ bhavati । pūrvaprasiddhaṃ hi lakṣaṇatve(na)
hetuḥ । ato nāprasiddhalakṣaṇā bhavitumarhati yathāprasiddhāsaṃbhave ca
﻿<pb n="b706"/>
aprasiddhanimittatāpi gṛhyate । tasmādāgneyasyaiva caturdhākaraṇamiti
sthitam । ḍitthaḍabitthādīnāṃ tu pratyekameva siddhiḥ āgneyastu
pratyuktaḥ ।</p>
<trailer>iti bṛhatyāṃ tṛtīyādhyāyasya
prathamaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>
﻿<pb n="b707"/>
<head>atha tṛtīyādhyāyasya
dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ ।।</head>
<ab type="sutra" n="1">arthābhidhānasaṃyogānmantreṣu śeṣabhāvaḥ syāt tasmādutpatti-
saṃbandho'rthena nityasaṃyogāt1 ।। 3-2-1 a. 1 ।।</ab>
<p>yuktaṃ tāvat 2 kiṃ mukhya evābhidheye mantrāṇāṃ viniyogaḥ
uta gauṇe'pīti । idantvayuk‍taṃ kaḥ punarmukhyaḥ ko vā gauṇa iti ।
kathamivāyuktam ? yaḥ paraśabdaḥ paratra vartate sa gauṇa iti sthitam
tathā ca darśitam---3kathaṃ punaḥ paraśabdaḥ paratra vartate ? svārthābhi-
dhāneneti । tasmādayukto'yaṃ praśnaḥ ।</p>
<p>athāyamabhiprāyaḥ, lakṣaṇāyāmapi paraśabdaḥ paratra vartate
tadva‍yāvṛttyartho'yaṃ praśnaḥ iti ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b708"/>
<p>tannopapadyate । yadeva gauṇatve lakṣaṇaṃ vakṣyati---1anā-
dṛtyaiva māṇavakapratyayaṃ jvalanaṃ agniśabdāt pratiyanto
dṛśyante na tvanādṛtya jvalanapratyayaṃ māṇavakaṃ pratiyanti iti ।
lakṣaṇāyāmapyevameva । nahyanādṛtya gaṅgāpratyayaṃ gaṅgāsamīpaṃ pratiyanti
tasmānna tannivṛttyarthamiti śakyate vak‍tum ।</p>
<p>atha mataṃ lakṣaṇāyāmanveti lakṣaṇāpadaṃ gauṇe punaḥ nānveti
iti । tadayuktam । pratītau tāvat dvayamapyanveti । kārye punarnaikamapi ।
ato'nenāpi viśeṣaṇena na viśeṣaḥ । atha vākyārthanivṛttaye yatnaḥ,
﻿<pb n="b709"/>
tanna; naivārthāntare vākyaṃ vartate anvitābhidhāyīni padā-
nyeva hi vākyam । anvitāśca padārthāḥ vākyārthaḥ । na
cānanvitābhidhānamasti iti pradarśitam । evaṃ tarhi praśnārtho-
vyākhyeyaḥ । evaṃ ca sopapada---suṣṭhuprasiddha bahuśaḥ prayogāśca
pratyuktā bhāṣye atastannirākaraṇārtho'pyayaṃ praśnaḥ nopapadyata eva ।
﻿<pb n="b710"/>
ucyate । ayaṃ praśnasya arthaḥ vākyārthavagamāddhi nimittatayā
padārthavibhāgo'vagamyate । sa cāyaṃ māṇavake'gnau ca tulyaḥ
agnirmāṇavaka ityuk‍te māṇavakaḥ piṅgalatā ca nimittam । agnirjva-
latītyuk‍te jvalano jvalanakriyā ca । tasmānna viśeṣaṃ paśyāmaḥ
asya śābdo nimittabhāvo'sya gauṇo nimittabhāva iti । nanu
cāgnipratyayapurassarā māṇavake pratītiḥ paiṅgalyasya; naivaṃ śakyate
﻿<pb n="b711"/>
vak‍tum । uktamidaṃ vākyānnimittabhāvāvagatiriti । agnirmāṇa-
vaka iti piṅgalataiva kevalaṃ nimittatayā'vagamyate yathā piṅgalo
māṇavaka iti । tasmād‌durnirūpamidaṃ gauṇo'yaṃ mukhyo'yamiti manvā-
nasya praśnaḥ । na copapadādibhiḥ saṃbhavatīti pradarśidaṃ bhāṣye । agni-
rivāyaṃ māṇavaka ityatra yuktamagnisādṛśyam ivādīnāṃ sādṛśye prayoga-
﻿<pb n="b712"/>
darśanāt । ag‍nirmāṇavaka iti tu ivārthaśūnyo'rthaḥ vākyārthaḥ
yathā piṅgalo māṇavaka iti ca tulyo nimittabhāvaḥ । ato niṣprayo-
janamevedamadhikaraṇaṃ manyāmahe । kathaṃ tarhi gaṅgāyāṃ ghoṣaḥ kūpe garga-
kulamiti । yuktaṃ prativasatītyasya sāmarthyaṃ na bhavatīti samīpānva-
yitā । ag‍nirmāṇavaka iti tu piṅgalaguṇāvagamo na kathañcinnopa-
padyate । tasmāt bhavatu lakṣaṇā । gauṇatve punaḥ na kiñcit
pramāṇamasti । kathaṃ cāg‍nipratyayo loke paiṅgalyādapyupapadyate
﻿<pb n="b713"/>
pūrvādivāparapratyayaḥ । atrābhidhīyate---ivārthanibandhana evāyaṃ pratyayaḥ
kutaḥ ? tathā'vagateḥ । kathaṃ punarivaśabdamantareṇevārthaḥ pratīyate । iva-
śabdo'pi tāvadivārthaḥ kimiti kalpyate । prayogadarśanāditi cet
atrāpi tulyam । nanu ca paiṅgalye'vagate jvalanasādṛśyamavagamyate apara-
śabdavadityuktam । naitadupapadyate । māṇavakasadṛśo'g‍nirityapi pratyayaḥ
﻿<pb n="b714"/>
syāt । iha punarviparītamiti । atipaiṅgalyāt jvala-
nasyopamānamiti cet nāsyāṃ kalpanāyāṃ pramāṇamasti । yathāvagamaṃ
nimittakalpanā nyāyyā tanmūlatvāt nimittāvagateḥ । ato yadyapi
viparītaḥ saṃbhavati tathāpi prasiddhapratipakṣatvāt nātmānaṃ labhate ।
apratipakṣo hi saṃbhavaḥ saṃbhavaḥ । tasmādupapannaṃ prayogapratyayābhyāṃ
gauṇamukhyābhidhānam । kiṃ mukhya evābhidheye mantrāṇāṃ viniyogaḥ,
uta gauṇe'pīti । tasmāta yukto vicāraḥ ।</p>
<p>kiṃ tāvatprāptaṃ ? aviśeṣādubhayābhidhānaṃ; ag‍nirjvalatītyapi
prayogo dṛṣṭaḥ ag‍nirmāṇavaka iti ca । tasmānna vinigamanāyāṃ
﻿<pb n="b715"/>
heturasti । atrābhidhīyate---ayamasti mukhyābhidhānaśūnyaṃ nāsti
gauṇābhidhānamiti pradarśitam । tasmānmukhya eva śabdasya
vyāpāraḥ । abhidhānena mantrā upakurvanti mukhye cābhidhānaṃ
na gauṇe । kutastarhi gauṇapratyayaḥ ? sādṛśyāditi । satya-
muktam, tat‍tu upāyātvena na punarnimittanirākaraṇatayāpi ।
kena cok‍taṃ nimittatā nirākriyata iti । mukhye saṃbhavati
na gauṇe viniyogaḥ kṣama iti etāvaducyate । yatra puna-
rmukhye na saṃbhavati tatra gauṇe'bhyupāyatvamiṣyata eva । na tarhi
pūṣādyanumantraṇādīnāṃ utkarṣaḥ । samākhyayā viniyuktānāṃ
﻿<pb n="b716"/>
mukhya eva saṃbhavatītyutkarṣaḥ । tasmāt mukhye yatra saṃpratyayo na tatra
gauṇe'pi mantraniyame pramāṇamasti । kimarthaṃ mukhyaṃ pratyāyayatītyeva-
mādinā pradarśitam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="2">1vacanāttvayathārthamaindrī syāt ।।3-2-3 a. 2 ।।</ab>
<p>aindna‍yā gārhapatyamupatiṣṭhate ityatra saṃśayaḥ kimaindreṇa mantreṇa
gārhapatyasyābhidhānaṃ utendrasyeti । kathaṃ punaḥ gārhapatyamupatiṣṭhata
iti spaṣṭāyāṃ śrutau saṃśayaḥ ? mukhye'rthe mantro viniyujyata iti
sthitamādhastye'dhikaraṇe । nanu ca mukhyāsaṃbhave gauṇepi ca vini-
yujyata eva । etadeva na vijānīmaḥ saṃbhavo vidyate neti । [nanu]
gārhapatyamupatiṣṭhata iti spaṣṭaiva śrutiḥ । viniyojyasāmarthyānu-
sārī viniyoga iti anīpsitārthā dvitīyā bhavatīti brūmaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b717"/>
tathā ca smaryate <q>‘tathā yuk‍taṃ cānīpsitaṃ’</q> iti । ayameva cāsya viṣayaḥ
viniyojyavaśāt kārakaparyavasāyyeva । yadvā gārhapatyamupetyābhi-
dhatta iti dvitīyopapadyata eva । tasmādindrābhidhānam । yuk‍taṃ caitadevaṃ
anyathā alaukikī abhidhānaśaktiḥ kalpanīyā । nanu gauṇamabhidhānaṃ
bhaviṣyati । nāsti gauṇamabhidhānam । siddhe hi prayoge goṇamabhidhānaṃ,
na punargauṇāt prayogasiddhiḥ । na cātra gārhapatye indraśabdaprayogo-
'nyataḥ siddhiḥ kartavyatopadeśāt । ato yathābhidhānaṃ viniyogaḥ
atrābhidhīyate । gārhapatyābhidhānaṃ mantreṇa kartavyam । kutaḥ ?
yathopadeśaṃ hi kāryaṃ na yathākāryamupadeśaḥ । atideśo hi saḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b718"/>
nanu ca yathākāryamupadeśo'pīti saptamādye uktam । niyogārthaḥ
tatra kāryaśabdenoktaḥ na punarāp‍tyādayaḥ । nanu ca viniyoge eva
sandihyata ityuktam । kimiti na niścita iti cet । anīpsite-
'pi dvitīyādarśanāt । kimidamanīpsitamiti ? tathā yuk‍taṃ cānī-
psitamiti । sutarāṃ tarhi dhātvarthaṃ prati prādhānyam । anyathā hi
tathāyogo na syāt । tarabarthaḥ idānīṃ kimarthaḥ ? anīpsitamapi
pradhānamiti ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b719"/>
<p>nanu cok‍taṃ nādṛṣṭā śabdaśaktiḥ kalpayituṃ śakyata iti ?
kimatrādṛṣṭaṃ vacanād dṛśyata eva । na vacanāt padārthānāṃ
śaktiḥ śakyā avagantum । kathaṃ tarhi yogādeḥ niyogārthasiddhau
śaktiḥ ? kāryāvagamyatvāt । iha tu viparītam । yadyatrāpi
pratipattavyamiti vacanaṃ syāt bhavet kāryadarśanam । idantvanya-
parameva vacanaṃ endra‏‍yā gārhapatyamupatiṣṭhata iti । tadidamuk‍taṃ-saṃbandha-
syāśāstrahetutvāt1 iti । gauṇaṃ tarhyabhidhānaṃ bhaviṣyati ।
nanu prayogasiddhe gauṇamabhidhānamityuktam । atrāpi kārya-
﻿<pb n="b720"/>
tayā siddha ityaviśeṣaḥ । guṇaśravaṇaṃ pradarśanārthaṃ sūtra iti matvā
yogāccetyuktaṃ bhāṣyakāreṇa ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="3">tathohvānamapīti cet1 ।। 3-2-5 a. 3 ।।</ab>
<p>atrāpi <q>‘avaghnannāhvayati’</q> ityāhvānena avaghātaṃ kuryādityarthaḥ
guṇādvā'bhidhānaṃ bhaviṣyati yogādvā āhnayatītyanuvādaḥ । yo hye-
hīti brūte sa āhvayatyeva । tririti kathaṃ ? śākhāntare pāṭhāt
﻿<pb n="b721"/>
trirityapyayamanuvāda eva । atrābhidhīyate---trirityetāvadvidhīyate ।
anyat sarvamanūdyate । nanu ca trirityapi prāptaṃ, na, aniyamāt
kvacit dviḥ paṭhyate । tasmādavaghnanniti lakṣaṇaiṣā । nāyaṃ doṣaḥ, anyataḥ
prāpteḥ । nanu ca pravṛttāvaghātasya naiṣa mantraḥ prāpnoti । idamapyanyataḥ
pnāptatvādevācodyam । tasmānna gauṇe viniyoge pramāṇamasti ।
﻿<pb n="b722"/>
yadi punarayaṃ mantro'vaghāte mukhyārthaḥ syāt nāvaghāte lakṣaṇā kalpitā
bhavet । śakyate ca haviṣkṛcchabdenāvaghāto vak‍tuṃ patnīvat । satyam
śakyate, āhvānantu ananvitārthaṃ prāp‍noti । tribhiriti
ca aniyataṃ syāt । tasmādvaraṃ lakṣaṇaiva । tayā ca liṅgamai-
kāntikam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="4">1 tathotthānavisarjane ।। 3-2-10, a. 4 ।।</ab>
<p>nanu codāharaṇamevedaṃ, kimatrātidiśyate । na hi anyatvā-
dṛte sādṛśyamupapadyata eva । idamastyanyatvaṃ pūrvasminnadhikaraṇe
﻿<pb n="b723"/>
trirityevadvidhīyate । anyatsarvamanūdyate । iha punaḥ kālasaṃyogo
vidhātavyaḥ aprāpte sayogavidhāne lakṣaṇā na nyāyyeti pūrvapakṣavādī
adhikaraṇavaiṣamyaṃ manyate । rāddhāntavādī tu praiṣārthānanvayatulyatvāt
tathetyuktavān ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="5">1sūktavāke ca kālavidhiḥ parārthatvāt ।। 3-2-11 a. 5 ।।</ab>
﻿<pb n="b724"/>
<p>atrābhidhīyate, neyaṃ kālakṣaṇā । kiṃ tarhi ? mantropade-
śo'yam । nanu cānyārtho mantra ityuktam na haraterabhidhāteti ।
mābhūt haratervācakaḥ haratidevatāvācako bhaviṣyati । nanu ca
nirvṛttayāgadevatāvacano'yam । na ca haratiryajatiḥ । ucyate-nirvṛtta-
devatāvacanatve'pi tatsaṃskāro yāgo bhaviṣyati । paśupuroḍāśavat ।
nanu cāyaṃ haratirna yajatirityuktam । haratiryajatiḥ mantrasaṃbandhāt ।
﻿<pb n="b725"/>
nanu caivaṃ sati saiva lakṣaṇā prāp‍noti । na lakṣaṇā, yāge
sati haratyarthasya prāptatvāt । ālabhetetivat । anyathā hi vṛtta-
midamā nirdeśyaṃ syāt । āśāsta iti ca bhūtanirdeśaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b726"/>
tasmātsuṣṭūcyate haratiryajatiriti । yaduk‍taṃ pratipattau sabhavantyāṃ
nārthakarma nyāyyamiti । sviṣṭakṛdvadavirodho bhaviṣyatītyuktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="6">1kṛtsnopadeśādubhayatra sarvavacanam ।। 3-2-16 a. 6 ।।</ab>
<p>haratiryajatiḥ sūktavākamantrastheti sthitam । idamidānīṃ
cintyate । kiṃ sakalasya sūktavākasya paurṇamāsyāmamāvāsyāyāṃ ca
prayoga uta devatāpadavibhāgeneti ।</p>
<p>nanu cintaiveyaṃ nopapadyate । sthitamarthaikatvādeka-
vākyatvam । śliṣṭapaṭhitānāṃ pradhānadevatāpadānāṃ na cātrai-
kārthatvaṃ saṃbhavati । nāpi vibhajyamānasākāṅkṣatvam ।
﻿<pb n="b727"/>
tasmādbhinnānyetāni । bhinnānāṃ tvekavacananirdeśe sati kathaṃ
kṛts‍naprayoga āśaṅkyate । yathā āg‍neyyetyuk‍te na kṛts‍nā āgneyyaḥ
prayoktavyā ityāśaṅkā bhavati । mukhye ca saṃbhavati na gauṇe
viniyoga ityapi sthitam । ucyate । yathā bhavānāha । kintu
pūrvapakṣavādī manyate sūk‍tavāko vartata iti vākyasamūhe eka-
vacanamidaṃ, evamatrāpi sūktavākeneti samūhagatamevedamekavacanaṃ,
ataḥ samudāya evātra karaṇam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b728"/>
<p>nanu samūhasyaikārthatā na saṃbhavati । vacanāt kalpyate
yathā uttamaprayāje । imāmāśaṅkāṃ nivartayituṃ idamadhikaraṇam । kṛtaḥ
pūrvapakṣaḥ । idānīṃ rāddhānto'bhidhīyate---nātra samūhaviniyoge
pramāṇamasti sūktavāko vartata iti anyathāpyekavacanopapatteḥ । ekā-
bhidhānāddhi pāṭhakānāṃ sūktavāko vartata iti yujyate'bhidhānam । iha
punaḥ sūktavākena prastaraṃ praharatīti na liṅgabādhenaikavākyatvaṃ śakyate
kalpayitum, yathāliṅgaṃ viniyogopapatteḥ । tasmādviśeṣāgrahaṇāt yena
﻿<pb n="b729"/>
kenacit sūktavākena prahṛte prahṛtaṃ bhavati sūktavākena prastaraṃ
praharatīti । samudāyābhiprāyastu heyatayopanyastaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="7">1liṅgakramasamākhyānāt kāmyayuktaṃ samāmnānam ।। 7 ।।</ab>
<p>ādhastye'dhikaraṇe uk‍taṃ prakaraṇāt pratyekaṃ śeṣatve prāpte liṅgā-
dvibhāga iti । ihedānīṃ prakaraṇādyat balīyaḥ tatkramasamākhyābhyāṃ
nitarāṃ balīya iti pūrvapakṣavādī manyate । liṅgāccheṣatve atantre
kramasamākhye ।</p>
<p>nanu naiva liṅgaṃ kevalaṃ viniyojakaṃ rāddhānte vakṣyati viniyo-
jakatve tu balābalam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b730"/>
<p>kimarthaṃ vā prāk śrutiliṅgādhikaraṇāt balābalacintā ।
atrābhidhīyate । naiveyaṃ balābalacintā । sāpekṣaṃ liṅgaṃ
viniyojakamityatra pratipādyate । kathaṃ tarhi pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ?
liṅgamapi śrutyādivat pramāṇāntaranirapekṣamiti balābalasūtre
anukramaṇāt pūrvapakṣo'yam । rāddhāntastu---sāmānyasaṃbandhe sati
śeṣiviśeṣe liṅgaṃ viniyojakamiti । yathā liṅgaṃ na kevalaṃ
viniyojakaṃ tathā śrutiliṅgādhikaraṇe nipuṇataramupapāda-
yiṣyāmaḥ । ataḥ kramasahitaṃ ca liṅgaṃ viniyojakam ।
﻿<pb n="b731"/>
ubhayaliṅgapramāṇasāhitye ca prayojanamuk‍taṃ bhāṣye ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="1">1adhikāre ca mantravidhiratadokhyāteṣu śiṣṭatvāt ।। 8 ।।</ab>
﻿<pb n="b732"/>
<p>āgneyyā''gnīdhramupatiṣṭhata ityevamādiṣu liṅganirdeśeṣu kiṃ
yāvalliṅgā grahītavyāḥ uta prakṛtānāṃ grahaṇamātramiti । pūrvapakṣavādī
tu vidheyasya prakṛtābhidhānasāmarthyaṃ na saṃbhavati iti manvāno
yāvalliṅgaṃ grahaṇamityāha । uddeśyapadaṃ hi prakṛtāpekṣaṃ bhavati na
punarvidheyārthasamarpakamapi । uddeśyatvaṃ hi nāma prayojanavadarthatā । na ca
sāmānyaṃ prayojanavadbhavati upāttaviṣayatvāt prayojanavattāyāḥ । nanu
ca sāmānyamevopādīyate । nāparimitasyopādānaṃ saṃbhavati । tasmā-
llakṣaṇatayaiva tatra sāmānyam । yathok‍taṃ grahādhikaraṇe vidheyaṃ punaḥ sapa
rimāṇaṃ śabdādevāvagantavyam । anyato'navagamāditi pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b733"/>
prakṛtamaprakṛtaṃ vā yāvalliṅgaṃ vidheyam । kiṃ prakṛtābhirliṅgavatī-
bhirupasthātavyaṃ uta dāśatayībhya evaṃliṅgā āgamayitavyā
iti dāśatayīgrahaṇaṃ na prakṛtapratipakṣatayā । etaduk‍taṃ bhavati ।
kiṃ yāvalliṅgā grahītavyā uta prakṛtā evaivaṃliṅgā āgamayitavyā
iti ।</p>
<p><q>‘kimidaṃ 1upadiṣṭopadeśo na nyāyyaḥ’</q> ? idamidam । upadiṣṭa-
taiva hi tasya viśeṣaḥ । na cāsau vidheyāṅgamityuktam । prakṛtvaṃ
punarabhidhānāt‍tulyam । atrāha-2virodhe sati liṅgena prakaraṇaṃ bādhyate
﻿<pb n="b734"/>
na caitayorvirodha" iti । ko'bhiprāyaḥ ? ayamabhiprāyaḥ prakṛte'pi
gṛhyamāṇe'bhihita evārtho gṛhīto bhavati । yathaikasyāmapi gavyupā-
dīyamāne caritārthaiva gāmālabheteti śratiḥ । naitadevamiti । nātra
liṅgavattā śabdārtha iti manyate । ucyate, talliṅgavattā'neneti
heyatayā'sya pakṣasyopanyāsaḥ । dāśatayyāṃ punaḥ mantravyaktāviti
prakṛta eva saṃpanne liṅgārthe niṣpramāṇakaḥ prakṛtabādha iti
manyate ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b735"/>
<p><quote>1liṅgajanitastu pratyayaḥ kaścinmithyeti</quote> । liṅgārthasaṃpattau satyāṃ ko'yaṃ
mithyābhāvaḥ । ayamabhiprāyaḥ---nāyaṃ sāmānyopasaṃhāraḥ śabdārtha
iti । <q>‘svargakāmo yajeta’</q> iti na sampatyā anyaprayogārhopi
śāstrārthaḥ paryavasita iti śakyate vak‍tum । nanu ca vyaktirapadārtha
iti sāmānyopasaṃhṛtirevopanyastā1 । etadeva na vijānīma
iti pratyayārthapradhānatvāt taddhitāntānāṃ na tadvattā'ṅgamiti
﻿<pb n="b736"/>
manyate । tasmānna sāmānyopasaṃhārārthamidaṃ śāstram । nanvetataduk‍taṃ
kāryāntare prakṛtasyopadeśo nāsāvarthāntara upadekṣyata iti
upadiṣṭopadeśaparihārāyāyamupanyāsaḥ । kimiti ? liṅgavanmātra-
grahaṇāditi darśitam । nātropadiṣṭatā hetuḥ । nanu caivaṃ
sati prakṛtabādhaḥ । bhavatvabhidhānāt prakṛtabādho na doṣaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b737"/>
api ca na liṅgaṃ prakaraṇaṃ vā'nugrahītavyamiti nānugrahārthā
śāstrārthopasaṃhṛtiriti yaduk‍taṃ tadidam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="8">1tadākhyo vā prakaraṇopapattibhyām ।। 3-1-22 a. 8 ।।</ab>
<p>atrocyate---rāddhāntī tu prakṛte'pi vidheyapratyayo naiva na ghaṭata
iti manvānaḥ prakṛtasyaiva grahaṇamityuktavān । kathaṃ ? uddeśyatvaṃ hi
nāma prayojanavato bhavati ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b738"/>
<p>prakṛtatvaṃ punaḥ vidheyepi prakṛtapratyayaṃ naiva bādhate । na hi
sannihite viśeṣe sāmānyaśabdaḥ tamativartate । nīlotpalamitivat
gāmānayetivadvā । tasmāt prakṛtapratyarthī na sāmānyaśabdo bhavitu-
marhati । prakṛtā evaivaṃ liṅgavyaktayaḥ parigṛhyanta iti siddham । sarveṣāṃ
copadiṣṭatvāditi । yaduktaṃ tadidam । yadyupadeśamātraṃ sarvatrāsti
prakṛtagrahaṇe'pyupadeśo na viśeṣaṇamityuktam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b739"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="1">1liṅgasamākhyābhyāṃ bhakṣārthatānuvākasya ।। 3-1-25 a. 9 ।।</ab>
<p>idamidānīṃ cintyate---yathā prakṛtatayā liṅgamupasaṃhṛtaṃ kimevaṃ
samākhyāpi svanimitta evopasaṃharati uta yathāliṅgaṃ viniyoga
iti । kiṃ tāvad‌yuktam ? samākhyāpi prakṛtavanniyamayatyeva
viśeṣe liṅgam । nanu liṅgāntaravirodhaḥ prāpnoti । na, viśeṣaṇa-
tayāpi liṅgāntarasyāvirodhāt । yataḥ svārthe parārthe vā'bhidhāna-
maviśiṣṭam । nanu ca pārārthye lakṣaṇā prāpnoti । tathāpya-
bhidhānamaviśiṣṭaṃ idaṃparatāviśeṣo'yaṃ nābhidhānaviśeṣaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b740"/>
tasmānniyantumarhati samākhyā ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="1">1tasya rūpopadeśābhyāmapakarṣo'rthasya coditvāt ।। 3-2-16 ।।</ab>
<p>satyamavirodhi liṅgāntaram---kintu anidaṃparatāyāḥ pramāṇaṃ
na vidyate । bhakṣaṇavalliṅgāntaraviṣayasyāpi smaraṇārha-
tvāt । prayogo hi smaraṇīyaḥ । grahaṇādyapi ca prayogaṃ eva ।
tasmādyathāliṅgaṃ vyavasthā । nanu ca samākhyāśūnyaṃ liṅgaṃ
viniyojakatāmeva na pratipadyate । naiva samākhyā-
śūnyaṃ bhakṣanimittāpi samākhyā kratusaṃbandhitāmāpādayatyeva ।
﻿<pb n="b741"/>
laukikī lakṣaṇetyasyoktaḥ parihāraḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="10">1guṇābhidhānānmandrādirekamantraḥ syāt tayorekārthasaṃyogāt ।। 10 ।।</ab>
<p>pūrvādhikaraṇāpavādo'yam । aprayogābhidhāno mantraḥ prayo-
gābhidhānena saha ekavākyataṃ nīyate samākhyayā । liṅgaṃ hi
dṛṣṭārthatayā samākhyāyopasaṃhṛtam । yatra punaḥ dṛṣṭārthatā nāsti
tatrādṛṣṭakalpanāyāṃ pramāṇaṃ nāsti iti samākhyaiva viniyoktrī ।
sā ca svanimittaiveti siddhaṃ lakṣaṇenaikavākyatvamityekamantratvam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b742"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="11">1liṅgaviśeṣanirdeśāt samānavidhāneṣvanaindrāṇāmamantratvam ।। 11 ।।</ab>
<p>iha pānopalakṣaṇaprakaraṇe samānavidhāne sthite <q>‘anuṣṭu-
p‌chandasa’</q> iti namanadarśanāt <q>‘‘aindraḥ somo
﻿<pb n="b743"/>
gṛhyate mīyate ca”</q> iti prakṛtivikāraśaṅkāyāṃ kṛtvācintā ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="1">1punarabhyannīteṣu sarveṣāmupalakṣaṇaṃ dviśeṣatvāt ।। 12 ।।</ab>
<p>atra āśrāvaṇādapanayaḥ prasthitadevatāyā iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।
agrahaṇānneti siddhāntaḥ ।</p>
<p><quote>2pāt‍nīvate tu pūrvavat । 3tvaṣṭāraṃ tūpalakṣayet । triṃśacca ।।</quote></p>
<p>āgrayaṇāt punaranāgrayaṇasyāpi taduddeśena grahaṇamityayanaya
eva । tvaṣṭari sahavacanāt pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । nācoditatvāditi rāddhāntaḥ
﻿<pb n="b744"/>
trayastriṃśati tvag‍neḥ mādayitṛtvadarśanāt punarāśaṅkā । mādayitṛtaiva
tatprādhānyāt devatābhāvamāpādayati iti rāddhāntaḥ । evamanuva-
ṣaṭkāradevatāpi taduddeśenāgrahaṇānnopalakṣyā ।</p>
<p>sthitāduttaram---ekayāgatvāttu samānavidhānam । tasmādaindra-
meva samantrakam itaradanāmnānādamantrakameva ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b745"/>
<p>aindrāgne punaḥ pānamevopalakṣyate na devateti । āg‍neyaṃ
caturdhā karotīti sthite pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ devataivopalakṣaṇaṃ pānābhāvāditi
rāddhāntaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="18">1chandaśca devatāvat ।। 3-2-42 a. 18 ।।</ab>
<p>devatayā tulyaṃ cchanda iti manvānasya pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ
ekachandaso na vidyata iti rāddhāntaḥ । anuṣ‍ṭup‌chandasa iti chando-
ntaravidhānāt namatītyasya parihāraḥ । aindraḥ somo mīyate gṛhyate
ca iti samānavidhāne sthite yathāliṅgaṃ mantra iti sthitam ।
tasmādidamapyakāraṇaṃ prakṛtivikārabhāvasya ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b746"/>
<p>idānīmindrapītasya iti sthite savanasāmānādhikaraṇyāt
sarve mantravanta iti rāddhānta ।</p>
<trailer>iti bṛhatyāṃ tṛtīyādhyāyasya
dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>
﻿<pb n="b747"/>
<head>atha tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ ।।</head>
<ab type="sutra" n="1">1śruterjātādhikāraḥ syāt ।। 3-3-1 a. 1 ।।</ab>
<p>1<quote>śruterjātādhikāraḥ syāt</quote> । <q>‘uccairṛcā kriyate’</q> iti kimayaṃ vedadharmaḥ
uta ṛgdharma iti saṃśayaḥ । ko'yaṃ vedo nāma ? nanu cargapi veda
eveti । ucyate---vidhāyakaṃ vedaśabdenocyate । etaduk‍taṃ bhavati
---yadṛgvedaśabdavācyaṃ vidhāyakaṃ tadvidheyadharmaḥ uta yatra pādavyavasthā
tasmin mantra iti ।</p>
﻿<page n="b748"/>
<p>kiṃ tāvad‍yuktam---uccaiḥ ṛcā kriyata iti vacanādṛgdharmo'ya-
miti । nanu vedopakramametadvākyam । ko doṣaḥ ? ṛkṣvapyayaṃ veda-
śabdo vartata eva । evaṃ ca na vikalpo bhaviṣyati vedāntarapaṭhi-
tasya ṛgjātasya ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="2">1vedo vā prāyadarśanāt ।। 3-3-2 ।।</ab>
<p>atrocyate---vedadharmo'yam । kutaḥ ? vedaśabdopakrama-
tvādvākyasya । nanu ca upakramopasaṃhāravaśāt ṛkṣu vartata
ityuktam । satyamuktam । tattu nopapadyate । kathaṃ nopa-
padyate ? evaṃ nopapadyate । upakrame yaḥ padārthaḥ parijñāto
﻿<pb n="b749"/>
bhavati tadviśeṣapratipattireva kevalamupasaṃhārādapekṣyate । na
punastadvirodhyarthāntaram । ato'virodhidharmavidhānameva kevalaṃ
vedena saṃbadhyate । ṛk‌cchabdastadānuguṇyādanuvādaḥ । kathaṃ
punarnargvedaśabdenocyate ? kena cok‍taṃ nocyata iti ?
kintu vidheyatayā na vidhāyakavat । dṛṣṭaścāyaṃ ṛk-
śabdo vede---ṛgbhiḥ prātardivi deva rhayate’ iti । kuta
etat ? yajurvede tiṣṭhati madhye ahna iti sahayogāt ।
﻿<pb n="b750"/>
dharmopadeśaśca sāmnāṃ pṛthaktvenaivamevedamupapadyate । anyathā hi
ṛgvidhānātsiddheḥ pṛthagvacanamanarthakam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="1">1trayīvidyākhyā ca tadvidi-iti ।।</ab>
<p>trayīvidyaśabdaśca vedatrayavidi vartate । tataḥ kiṃ ? idaṃ tato
bhavati । vede ṛgādiśabdānāṃ prayogo dṛṣṭa iti । yatpunarvedāntaroktasya
svarāntarāpattiriti । vidhānānna doṣaḥ । prakaraṇabādhaśca vākyādiṣyata
eva । kiṃ punaḥ kāraṇaṃ vedasaṃyogepi prakaraṇaṃ nānugṛhyate, ṛg‌dharma-
vidhānavat । ucyate-ṛcāmaṅgatvāttaddharmaḥ prakaraṇena gṛhyata iti yuk‍taṃ;
﻿<pb n="b751"/>
vedadharmatve punaḥ vidhānamupalakṣaṇam । na ca tadaṅgamiti yāva-
dvidhānaṃ dharmavidhiḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="2">1guṇamukhyavyatikrame tadarthatvānmukhyena vedasaṃyogaḥ ।। 2 ।।</ab>
<p><q>“ya evaṃ vidvānagnimādhatte”</q> iti yājurvaidiko vidhiḥ । <q>“ya 
evaṃ vidvān vāravantīyaṃ gāyati”</q> iti ādhānaprakaraṇe sāmavaidika
iti kṛtvā cintyate । yājurvaidike bhavatūpāṃśutvaṃ, sāmavaidike
coccaiṣṭvaṃ, satyamevaṃ yadyaṅgapradhānavidhī bhidyete yathātvabhedaḥ tathā
phalavatsannidhau aphalaṃ tadaṅgamityatra vakṣyati । abhede cobhayaveda-
vidhānāt bhavati saṃśayaḥ । ubhayavedavidhānāt vikalpo
bhavatu । na vikalpaḥ saṃbhavati । evaṃ sati aṅgavidhiranuvāda
﻿<pb n="b752"/>
ityaṅgavidheḥ pradhānavidhitantratvaṃ darśayati । tathāpi kaḥ saṃśayaḥ ? aya-
masti saṃśayaḥ kimaṅgavidhirākṣiptasvavidheya eva pradhānavidhitantro
bhavati, uta pradhānenaikībhūto vidheyaṃ vidhatta iti । pūrvapakṣavādī
manyate । svārthaṃ vidhāya prayojanavaśāt pradhānenaikībhavati vāravantīya
gāyatītyasya yaḥ svārthaḥ । ataḥ sāmavaidikasvarayuktasyaivāṅgabhāvaḥ ।
atrābhidhīyate---vihitasvārtha eva pradhānenaikībhavati । na punaraṅga-
tāmapi vidhāya । pradhānavidhiraṅgatāṃ vidhatta iti saptamādye vakṣyāmaḥ
﻿<pb n="b753"/>
aṅgatayā ca vāravantīyasya prayogaḥ na vāravantīyaṃ gāyatītyasya
vidherviṣayatayā । ato na svārthavidhiḥ pradhānavidhiṃ bādhitumarhati
svārthasya prayogārthatvāt । tadidamuktam---<q>“1guṇasyānuṣṭhānena mukhyaḥ
saguṇaḥ kathaṃ syāditi guṇe pravartate । guṇapravṛttyā cenmukhyayya
guṇahānirbhavati guṇapravṛttau phalameva nāvāptaṃ bhavati । atha pradhānaṃ
saguṇaṃ kariṣyāmīti guṇe pravartamāno guṇasya guṇaṃ vinipātayati nāsya
svārtho hīyate nāsau guṇaṃ saguṇaṃ kartuṃ pravartata”</q> iti na guṇavidhau
svārthe pravṛttirītyuk‍taṃ bhavati । prayogāṅgatvācca guṇavidheḥ pradhāna-
guṇena bhavitavyamityuktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="3">2bhūyastvenomayaśruti ।। 3-3-10 a. 3 ।।</ab>
<p>sthitaṃ tāvat pradhānavidhinibandhano guṇaḥ guṇavidhi-
﻿<pb n="b754"/>
nibandhanaṃ guṇaṃ bādhata iti । idamidānīṃ cintyate---yatrobhayatra
pradhānaśrutiḥ tatra kva pradhānacodaneti । yatra pradhānacodanā
tannibandhanena guṇena bhavitavyam । tatsidhyartheṣācintā tatrā-
gṛhyamāṇaviśeṣatvādubhayatretyuktvā bhūyastvenaikatra nirūpitaṃ
vālavyajanādinā bahupu rājapratimeṣūpaviṣṭeṣu rājā'vagamyata iti
dṛṣṭāntābhidhānam । tadidamubhayamayuktam । kva bhūyastvena pradhānasya
prayogābhidhānaṃ dṛṣṭam । na ca bālavyajanaṃ ś‍vetacchatraṃ vā bhūyastvenā-
vagamayati । kiṃ tarhi ? asādhāraṇatayā । tasmādasaṃbaddhamevedaṃ
bhāṣyaṃ manyāmahe ।</p>
<p>atrābhidhīyate---nedamasaṃbaddham । bhūyastvena hi prayogā-
vagamassūcyate sakalaprayogo'vagamyata ityarthaḥ । alpāṅgā-
﻿<pb n="b755"/>
bhidhāne punaḥ na sakalaprayogāvagatirbhavati । sakale ca prayoge'vagamya-
māne prayogābhidhānamatirbhavati । prayeyāddhi pramāṇānumānamiti
sthitam । yadapi ca vālavyajanamupanyastaṃ tadgamakasāmānyatayā
bhūyastveneti sūktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="4">asaṃyuk‍taṃ prakaraṇāt iti kartavyatārthatvāt ।। a. 4 ।।</ab>
<p>1 kimetāvantyeva pramāṇāni ? ke'yaṃ praśnaḥ ? yadi tāvata
sūtrārtha eva na śakyate vyākhyātuṃ praś‍nena vinetyabhiprāyaḥ । tada-
yuktam । praś‍nena kimatra; yadasaṃyuk‍taṃ tatprakaraṇena viniyujyata iti
﻿<pb n="b756"/>
nanu kenāsaṃyuktamiti na vidmaḥ । evaṃ tarhi etadeva
praṣṭavyam । kenāsaṃyuktamiti । k‍vedamupayujyate kimetāvantyeva
pramāṇānīti ? athāyamabhiprāyaḥ । kimiti śrutyā liṅgena
vākyena vā yadasaṃyukteṃ tatprakaraṇena viniyujyata iti । kimetā-
cantyeva pramāṇātīti, tathāpyuttaraṃ tāvadasaṃbaddhaṃ anyadapyastīti ।
yadyanyadapyasti kimiti tarhi śrutyā liṅgena vākyena vā'saṃyukta-
mityucyate । athājñānameva naiva śrutiliṅgavākyebhyaḥ pramāṇamanya-
dvijñāyata iti tathāpi svarūpaṃ vaktavyam । nāsaṃyuktaṃ prakaraṇāditi
yujyate kartavyasya itikartavyatākāṅkṣasyeti vakṣyamāṇavadvaktavyam ।
﻿<pb n="b757"/>
ataḥ praś‍no'rthe'naupayika iva dṛśyate । atrābhidhīyate---ayamabhi-
prāyo bhāṣyakārasya । lakṣaṇādāvuk‍taṃ <q>“1śeṣalakṣaṇamucyate ।
śrutyādīni viniyoge kāraṇāni”</q> iti । tatra tāvat śrutiliṅga-
vākyaiḥ viniyojyaṃ śeṣatvamuktaṃ prakaraṇena viniyojyaṃ punaḥ kimatra
bhaviṣyati । nanu ca prayājādayaḥ santyeva kimiti praśnaḥ ।
bāḍhaṃ praśnārthaḥ vidyate prayājādīnāṃ hi ekaniyogalakṣaṇasaṃbandhaṃ
caturthe vakṣyati darśapūrṇamāsādibhiḥ kimatrānyatsaṃbandhe pramāṇaṃ
mṛgyate । evaṃ ca tadbhūtādhikaraṇa evoktaḥ saṃbandhaḥ anvitā-
midhāyibhiḥ padaiḥ sarvatra śabdārthāvagame heturiti vyāpakaṃ
bhavati । pramāṇāntare punaranviṣyamāṇe nānvitābhidhānanibandhanaḥ
﻿<pb n="b758"/>
śakyate pradarśayitum । prakaraṇādibhirhi vākyārthānāṃ saṃbandhāvagatiḥ ।
na ca vākyārthasya vākyārthasya ca saṃbandhe padābhidhānalakṣaṇaḥ saṃbandha
upapadyate । anvitaṃ hi padārthāntareṇa padārthamācaṣṭe padaṃ, na
vākyārthaṃ vākyārthāntareṇa । ato darśapūrṇamāsārthatayā prayājādi-
vākyārthānvayaṃ aśābdaṃ manyamānasya praśnaḥ ।</p>
<p>nanu caitānyeva pramāṇātīti aśābdaṃ manvānasya praś‍nenaiva
bhavitavyam na punaḥ kimetāvantyeva pramāṇānīva । ucyate---eta-
devok‍taṃ yadyasaṃyuk‍taṃ na tarhi viniyojyam । ato'saṃyuktamiti
vadatā etāvantyeva pramāṇānītyuk‍taṃ bhavati । tasmāt yukto'yaṃ praśnaḥ
﻿<pb n="b759"/>
---kimetāvantyeva pramāṇānīti । itarastu nāvaśyaṃ padārthā-
ntarānvitameva śābdam । aidamarthyenāpi śabdaḥ saṃbandhaṃ
pratipādayatyeveti manvāno netyuktavān । itarastu pṛcchati 1kimaparaṃ
kāraṇamiti praśnenaivopakramaḥ pūrvapakṣa iti, pūrvoktapraśnārthavivaraṇaṃ
﻿<pb n="b760"/>
kā nāmeyaṃ nadīti ca । na cānirjñātanadyarthasyaivopapadyate praśna iti 
prakaṭīkṛtaḥ praśnārthaḥ <q>‘kathaṃ punarasaṃyuktasyaiva viniyogaḥ’</q> । tadi-
damaidamarthyailakṣaṇaṃ kathayati iti kartavyatārthitvāditi । aidamarthyenāpi
śabdaḥ sabandhaṃ pratipādayatyeveti ।</p>
<p>nanu caikaniyogalakṣaṇasaṃbandho'yamityuktam । kimidamiti-
kartavyatārthitvaṃ nāma ? ucyate---ekaniyogalakṣaṇa eva saṃbandho
nopapadyate yadītikartavyatā lakṣaṇaḥ saṃbandho na syāt । na
hyasaṃbandhavidheyasya ekaniyogatā upapadyate vidheyanānātvāt ।
﻿<pb n="b761"/>
upapadyate ca karaṇetikartavyatayā saṃbandhaḥ । anyatrāpi sādhye
darśanāt । sādhyaścāyaṃ niyogārthaḥ । tasmādupapannaṃ itikartavya-
tārthitvāditi vidheyasaṃbandhakāraṇam । kimiti tadbhūtādhikaraṇe
vākyasyaivārthenautpattikaḥ saṃbandho darśitaḥ । ucyate---asūtrārthajño
bhavān । kriyārtheneti vadatā sarvasyaivāsya prāmāṇyaṃ darśitam ।
tasmādaidamarthyalakṣaṇameva saṃbandhaṃ vede vedavido manyante । tatsidhyarthaṃ
tu padārthānāmapi anvitābhidhānaṃ darśitam । aidamarthyameva hi
﻿<pb n="b762"/>
pramāṇāntaratve hetuḥ । anvitābhidhānaṃ tu pramāṇāntarapūrvakeṣvapi
tulyam devadattaḥ kāṣṭhaiḥ sthālyāmodanaṃ pacatītyevamādiṣu laukikeṣu
vākyeṣu । ataḥ prakaraṇaviniyojyamapi śeṣatvamastīti siddham ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="6">1kramaśca deśasāmānyāt ।। sū. 12. a. 5 ।।</ab>
<p>atredānīṃ kaḥ praśnārthaḥ aidamarthyalakṣaṇameva hi saṃbandhaṃ vedavido
manyanta ityuktam । nanu caitāvantyeva pramāṇānītyākṣepeṇa bhavitavyaṃ
kimidaṃ <q>‘kimetāvantyeva pramāṇānī’</q>ti । atrocyate-atrāpyasaṃyukta-
﻿<pb n="b763"/>
grahaṇaṃ viṣayāntarapradarśanārtham । satyamaidamarthyavyatirekeṇa saṃbandho
nāsti, tathāpi pramāṇāntaramasti aidamarthyaviśeṣāvagatau sthāna-
sāmānyaṃ nāma tadidamuk‍taṃ---kramaśca deśasāmānyāditi । prayojanaṃ tu
darśitameva ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="6">1ākhyā caivaṃ tadarthatvāta ।। sū. 13. a. 6 ।।</ab>
<p>atredānīṃ praśnārtho nopapadyate aidamarthye sati sthānavat
viśeṣāvagame hetutvāt samākhyāyāḥ । ucyate---astyatra
viśeṣaḥ yuk‍taṃ tāvatsthānasya viśeṣāvagahetutvaṃ vaidikatvāt ।
﻿<pb n="b764"/>
samākhyā punaḥ laukikī । na ca laukikamabhidhānaṃ vedārthāvagame
heturbhavati । yathā <q>‘pacati’</q> ityevamādipu । ata idaṃ kimetāvantyeva
pramāṇānīti । atrocyate । samākhyāyā laukikatvepi vaidi-
kasyārthasya viśeṣāvagame hetutvaṃ pratipadyate । kutaḥ ? abhidhānaṃ
hi kṛttaddhitasamāsānāṃ saṃbandhini prasiddhaṃ vaidikasyārthasya cedama-
bhidhānaṃ yadyapi svayaṃ laukikam । ato viśeṣamavagamayati । na
cedaṃ smṛtivat pramāṇāntarāpekṣaṃ autpattikatvāt śabdārtha-

﻿<pb n="b765"/>
saṃbandhasya । tasmādyuktaṃ ākhyā caivaṃ tadarthatvāta iti yato
viśeṣāvagame hetuḥ । prayojanamuktam ।</p>
<p>śrutiliṅgavākyaprakaraṇasthānasamākhyānāṃ samavāye pāradaurbalyamartha-
viprakarṣāt ।। 7 ।।</p>
<p><quote>1kā punaratra śrutiḥ ? kiṃ liṅgamiti</quote> । nanu cāyaṃ praśno nopapadyate ।
kimiti nopapadyate ? yasmāt uktāni viniyoge kāraṇāni
iyuktam । na cānirjñātasya uktatā saṃbhavati । tasmādvipratiṣiddhaṃ
<q>“uktāni viniyoge kāraṇānīti । kā punaratra śrutiḥ rkiṃ liṅgaṃ”</q>
iti ca ।</p>

﻿<pb n="b766"/>
<p>athāyamabhiprāyaḥ viniyoga eva śrutyādibhiruk‍to, na
punaḥ śrutyādīnāṃ svarūpamiti । yadyevaṃ tarhi vaktavyaṃ uk‍taḥ
śrutyādibhirviniyoga iti । na viniyoge kāraṇānyuktānīti ।
kiñca viniyogoktyā viniyogakāraṇānyuktāni bhavantyeva । kāryataḥ
kāraṇaparijñānāt । arthāvacchedyameva hi śābdaṃ viśeṣato bhavati ।
svarūpato varṇamātragrahaṇāt । ato viniyogoktyāpi1 naiva praśno
na ghaṭate । śrutiliṅgayośca svarūpamabhidhāya punarvākyapraśne ko'bhi-
prāyo na vidmaḥ । athāyamabhiprāyaḥ saṃhatyārthamabhidhati padāni vākyaṃ

﻿<pb n="b767"/>
miti spaṣṭamevānyatvamupalabhāmahe । tasmādasaṃbaddhamevedaṃ bhāṣyamiti
arthajñānamānino manyate ।</p>
<p>atrābhidhīyate---satyamarthāt pramāṇāvagatistathāpi upapadyata
evāyaṃ praśnaḥ kā punaratra śrutiriti । kathamupapadyate ? satyaṃ gārhapatya-
śravaṇaṃ śrutiḥ satyaṃ ca indrābhidhānasāmarthyaṃ liṅgaṃ tathāpi padāntara-
nirapekṣaṃ naivobhayaṃ śakyate'vagantum । aindrayā gārhapatyaḥ upasthā-
tavya iti । nāpīndraparatā mantrasya । tulye padāntarasavyapekṣatve
﻿<pb n="b768"/>
viśeṣaṃ ajānan pṛcchati---<quote>kā punaratra śrutiḥ kiṃ liṅgamiti</quote> । atha
kimityādāveva etanna nirūpitaṃ <quote>śrutyādīni viniyoge kāraṇānī</quote>tyāsmin bhāṣya
eva । atrocyate---tatrāpyetat utsūtrameva vaktavyam । iyāṃstu atra
viśeṣaḥ <q>‘śrutiliṅga’</q> ityasya sūtrasya vyākhyātavyatayā aupoddhāti-
katayā saṃbaddhamabhidhānaṃ bhavati । kathaṃ punaridānīṃ tulye padāntara-
saṃbandhe gārhapatyaśabdasya śrutitocyate ? iyamucyate padāntara-
saṃbandhastu indrābhidhāne gārhapatyābhidhāne vā aviśiṣṭaḥ । gārhaṃ-
patyaśravaṇameva gārhapatyābhidhāne vyāpriyate । nanu dvitīyā vyāpriyata
ityuktam । satyamuktam gārhapatyaśravaṇe sati । ataḥ padasyaiva
﻿<pb n="b769"/>
nidarśitaṃ na prātipadikamātrasya । evamindrābhidhānepi mantre
padāntaramudāste । evaṃ ca sati vākye praśnottarametadvivekāye-
tyupapannameva । ato'sādhāraṇapratipattinimittatayā saṃhatyārthā-
bhidhāne satyapi śrutirliṅgamiti cocyate । tasmādupapannaṃ śruti-
liṅga‍yorvirodhe kimubhayaṃ viniyojakaṃ uta śrutireveti । prakaraṇa-
praśnābhiprāyaṃ tu svasthāne vakṣyāmaḥ, kramasamākhyayośca ।</p>
<p>nanu caivaṃ sati vaktavyaṃ śrutiḥ liṅgaṃ cobhayaṃ pramāṇaṃ ata śruti-
rbalīyasīti । iha punaḥ śrutiliṅagayoḥ kiṃ śrutirbalīyasī āho-
svit liṅgamiti na ghaṭate । yasmādidamapi kāraṇaṃ śrutiḥ liṅgamapīti ।
﻿<pb n="b770"/>
tasmādyathaivopanyastamasmābhiḥ tathaivopanyasanīyam, na tu kiṃ
śrutirbalīyasī āhosvit liṅgamiti । tulyabale ete
kāraṇe iti ca pūrvaṣakṣahetudarśanāt । tasmādanyathaivopanyā-
so'nyathaivopasaṃhāra iti । viruddhaṃ phalamapyevamevopanyastam
kimindrasya gārhapatyasya copasthānaṃ kartavyaṃ, uta gārhapatyasyaiveti ।
tasmādupakramopasaṃhārayoḥ sāmyaṃ vaktavyam ।</p>
<p>yadapi ca evaṃ tarhi liṅgavākye virudhyamāne iha saṃpradhāryete na
śrutiliṅge iti tadapyayuktamiva, sarvatra samavetaṃ vivik‍taṃ ca dṛśyata
ityuktatvāt vivekasya । yā śrutiḥ sā liṅgena viruddha‍yata iti vākyaṃ
punaḥ lakṣaṇayāpyupapadyata evetyuktvā athaveti śrutyantaropanyāsaḥ
kimaparitoṣāt uta vikalpārtha ityetadapi naiva jñāyate ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b771"/>
<p>ucyate---yastāvadupanyāsaḥ kiṃ balīyasī śrutiḥ āho---
svilliṅgamiti tatrāyabhiprāyaḥ । kiṃ liṅgonmardanenaiva yathā śrutiḥ pramāṇa
tathā liṅgamapi । yadi ca ubhayamubhayopamardanenaiva pramāṇaṃ tadopapadyata
evāyamupanyāsaḥ kiṃ balīyasī śrutiḥ āhosvilliṅgamiti ।</p>
<p>etaduk‍taṃ bhavati---na vidmaḥ kiṃ balīya iti । tasmādubhayaṃ
pramāṇaṃ ubhayaprāmāṇye cobhayorabhidhānam । ata eva cāniyama
ityuktam <q>“yadi tulyabale ete kāraṇe”</q> iti ca viśeṣāgrahaṇāt ।
<q>“tato vikalpa”</q>1 iti । ko'yaṃ vikalpaḥ ? nanu cāsmin pakṣe
samuccaya eva । abhidhānavikalpamaṅgīkṛtyaitaduktaṃ na prayogavikalpam
﻿<pb n="b772"/>
yadi tu liṅgaṃ balīyaḥ’ ityetadapi bhāṣyamupanyāsavat draṣṭavyam ।
evaṃ tarhotyuk‍te viśeṣe punaḥ praśnaḥ kenābhiprāyeṇa ? na kevalāt
gārhapatyaśravaṇāta tadupasthānāvagatiḥ । tāvanmātrasya ca śratitva-
mupadarśitam । tadidānīṃ rāddhāntavādyabhiprāyaṃ vivṛṇoti---satyaṃ
vākyādṛte nāyamavagamaḥ gārhapatyaśravaṇāt tadupasthānāvagatiriti ।
yā'tra śrutirityuktam indrābhidhānepi tulyatvāt । kathaṃ ? balīya-
syapi hi liṅge aindrayopatiṣṭhata ityetat gārhapatyaśabdena sahaika-
vākyatāmupetyaiva । yadi hi nopeyāt tato liṅgena virudhyeta
tasmāt śrutiliṅgayorvirodhaḥ । atha vā nātra ekavākyatvāditi
﻿<pb n="b773"/>
pakṣāntaropanyāsaḥ sakalapadapradarśanārtha iti vyākhyātam । kiṃ
punaratra yuktam ? ubhayatra svārthāvagamāt । liṅgādapi liṅgārtho'vagamyate
śruterapi hi śrutyarthaḥ । vākyasya caudāsīnyāt ubhayatrābhidhānamātraṃ
virudhyate । na cābhidhāne kaścidviśeṣo'vagaṃmyata ityataḥ tulyabale ete
kāraṇe ityuktam । 1<quote><q>“nanu liṅgasya bhaṅgurasyeva rūpaṃ savicikitso hi liṅgātpratyaya”</q></quote> iti ।
keyaṃ vicikitsā nāma ? asamyak pratyayaḥ । kimatrāsamyaktvam ।
nahīndrābhidhānāt indro'bhidhātavya iti pratyayo bhavatītyarthaḥ ।
bhavati tu gārhapatyaśravaṇāt vidhāyakavākyagatatvāta gārhapatya-
śabdasya । nanu cāvidhāyakatvāt liṅgasya prāmāṇyameva nāsti, kathaṃ
﻿<pb n="b774"/>
virodha iti । satyaṃ---abhidhānasāmarthyamātraṃ naiva pramāṇam-iti-
kartavyatāvagame satyanyato viśeṣāvagame pramāṇaṃ, kartavyatāvagamāt
prakaraṇādibhiḥ । karmavyatāvagame cābhidhānamātramavaśiṣyata ityuktam ।
tasmāta tulyabale ete kāraṇe iti । <q>“1balīyānapi hi hetuḥ”</q> iti
na ca tāvat balīyān, anvāruhyāpi na virodho'stīti manyate ।
<quote>nanvayameva virodhaḥ sakṛt upasthānaṃ coditam asakṛdabhinirvartyata iti । naivam---upastheya-
bhedāt pratipradhānamāvartante guṇā iti nyāya evaiṣaḥ na virodho'rthaḥ</quote> । nanu cedaṃ avi-
rodhottaraṃ na ghaṭate । nahyatropastheyadvayaṃ śrūyate aindrayā
gārhapatyamupatiṣṭata iti gārhapatya evaikaḥ upastheyatayā
śrūyate nendro'pīti । tasmādanuttaramidam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b775"/>
<p>ucyate---prakaraṇāt kartavyatāvagamāt indrapadāt indrā-
bhidhānaṃ pratīyata iti manvānena <q>‘upastheyabhedāt’</q> ityuktam ।
vākyasāmānyāt । evaṃ tarhi gauṇamukhyatā nopapadyata iti
punarvirodhopanyāsaḥ । nanu ca pratipradhānaṃ guṇāvṛttau satyāṃ
naivāsau virodho ghaṭate । aviniyuktamantrāpekṣo'yaṃ virodhaḥ ।
viniyoge tvavirodhaḥ iti siddho'tra pūrvapakṣaḥ ।</p>
<p>atrocyate---<quote>śrutiliṅgayorvirodhe śrutirbalīyasī iti । kutaḥ ? arthaviprakarṣāt ।
