kimidaṃ arthaviprakarṣāditi arthasya viprakarṣaḥ arthaviprakarṣaḥ । kaḥ punararthaḥ ? śrutyarthaḥ
﻿<pb n="b776"/>
gārhapatyamupatiṣṭhata iti sannikṛṣṭaḥ śrutyarthaḥ । indraḥ upastheya iti viprakṛṣṭaḥ । kathaṃ ?
<q>‘kadācana starī:’</q> ityanena mantreṇendra upasthātavya iti na śrūyate । satyapīndrābhidhānasāmarthye
vacanābhāvat anupasthānīyaḥ indra ityavagamyate</quote> । nanu pūrvamevoktaṃ satyāṃ kartavya-
tāyāṃ indrābhidhānaṃ pramāṇaṃ, tataścobhayatrābhidhāne tulyataiva । ato
dvayoḥ prāmāṇyamiti । kimidaṃ punarākṣiptam samāhitaṃ ca ?
<quote><q>“dharmasya śabdamūlatvādaśabdamanapekṣaṃ syāt iti । yadetat prakaraṇaṃ liṅgaṃ ca ubhyamapyeta-
daśābdam । na cātikrāntapratyakṣa eva evaṃlakṣaṇake'rthe śabdamantareṇa paricchedo'vakalpate ।
ato manyāmahe viprakṛṣṭaṃ śrutyarthālliṅgamiti”</q></quote> ucyate---aśābdametaditi viśeṣaṃ
pradarśayitum । nanu caivaṃ sati prāmāṇyamevāsya hīyate । kuto
﻿<pb n="b777"/>
virodhaḥ । adhāyamabhiprāyaḥ asati virodhe smṛtivalliṅgasya prāmāṇya-
miti । tadayuktam । kutaḥ ? smṛterhi arthamavagamya virodhādviparyayaḥ
kalpyate । iha punaḥ upasthānaṃ naivāvagamyata ityuktam । kathamana-
vagamyamāne'rthe'numānam । tasmāddurgṛhītastenasaṃbhāṣitavadasaṃbandhaṃ
pratibhāti । punarapi kartavyatāpekṣālliṅgādevārthāvagatiṃ darśayati ।
śrutisaṃbhave vā avagativākyasādhāraṇye sati kathamayaṃ viśeṣa
iti vaktavyam । atrābhidhīyate---kartavyasyetikartavyatākāṅkṣasya
vacanaṃ prakaraṇamiti prakaraṇādaidamarthyalakṣaṇa eva saṃbandhaḥ na punaḥ
anvitapadārthalakṣaṇa ityuktam । tataḥ kim ? anvitapadārtha-
﻿<pb n="b778"/>
lakṣaṇaḥ saṃbandhaḥ padārthebhya evāvasīyate । aidamarthyalakṣaṇastu kevalaṃ
kāryata eveti na padārthānvaye vyāpāro'vagamyate । evamapi ko
viśeṣaḥ ? ayamasti viśeṣaḥ---1padārthānvitalakṣaṇaḥ tasmin
sati paścātkāryayogaḥ pada rthānvayalakṣaṇastu prathamata eva । so'yamartha-
viprakarṣaḥ । anvayapradarśanārthaṃ ca tārtīyaṃ pramāṇaṣaṭkaṃ śeṣaśeṣivido
manyante । sa cānvayaḥ śrutau prathamataramavagamyata iti na kāryataḥ
pāścātyāyāṃ padārthānvayāvagatau pramāṇamasti । nahyanvitasyānvayo
dṛśyate yataḥ । tasyāt sūktaṃ liṅgāt śrutirbalīyasīti ।
ānumānikamabhidhānaṃ ca padārthānvayāpekṣameva draṣṭavyam ।
﻿<pb n="b779"/>
1vikalpasya cānyāyyatvāditi mantravākyāpekṣam । nendraśabdasyā-
bhidhānadvayaṃ nyāyyamityabhiprāyaḥ । ato na viniyuktasya viniyogo
ghaṭata iti pradarśito hetuḥ । yaduktamavirodha iti; evamuk‍to virodhaḥ
yadutendraśabdasya mantravākyāpekṣayā nābhidhānadvayamupapadyata
iti । aidamarthyasyānvayalabhyatvāt śrutāvuparatā kartavyatāpekṣeti
nākāṅkṣādvayamupapadyata iti virodhaḥ । tadidamakṛtasāmarthyatvaṃ
mantravākyasya niyogasya coktaṃ vākyaprakaraṇaśabdābhyām ।
﻿<pb n="b780"/>
ata upapanno'rthaviprakarṣaḥ । 1<q>“liṅgavākyayorvirodhe kimudāharaṇam ?
syonaṃ te sadanaṃ kṛṇomi ghṛtasya dhārayā suśevaṃ kalpayāmi
tasmin sīda amṛte pratitiṣṭha vrīhīṇāṃ medha sumanasyamānaḥ iti”</q> ।</p>
<p>nanu cārthaviprakarṣādityukto hetuḥ sāpekṣanirapekṣatvaṃ ca liṅga-
vākyayoḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b781"/>
<p>ataḥ prakaṭa evārthaviprakarṣaḥ kimityadhikaraṇāntaramāra-
bhyate । na kevalamidamadhikaraṇaṃ, sarvādhikaraṇākṣepa evāyam ।
sujñāno hyarthaviprakarṣaḥ । kathaṃ? liṅgaṃ tāvaduktaṃ nirapekṣatvāditi ।
vākyamapi padārthānvayāvagamyamānasaṃbandhaṃ aidamarthyalakṣaṇāt balīya
iti pradarśitam । prakaraṇamapi tadapekṣitvāt kramasya kramādūlīyaḥ।
evaṃ kramo'pi saṃbandhakṛttayā vedāvagamyatvācca samākhyāyā balīyā-
neva । ato nārambhaṇīyānyevaitāni adhikaraṇānītyarthaviprakarṣajñānā-
bhimānino manyate । atrocyate---yattāvadidamuktaṃ nirapekṣatvālliṅgaṃ
balīya iti । tadayuktam । kasmāt ? sakalasya hi mantrasya kartavya-
tāvagamāt na kevalāt padāt kartavyatāvagamo bhavati ।
﻿<pb n="b782"/>
ato vākyameva prathamataraṃ padānāṃ parasparasaṃbandhāvagame hetuḥ । saṃba-
ndhasya ca kāryāvagatiḥ । tasmādvākyameva balīya iti bhavati matiḥ ।
avaśyaṃ caitadevamabhyupagantavyam । anyathā hi avirodhisyonādi-
padāntarasaṃbandho'pi nirapekṣatvālliṅgasya viniyoge na syāt ।
ato durjñāno'yaṃ vākyaliṅgayoḥ viprakarṣa iti prārabdhamidamadhikaraṇam ।
ayameva ca pūrvapakṣavādino'bhiprāyaḥ padāntarasavyapekṣaṃ liṅgaṃ viniyo-
jakamityubhayatra viniyogaḥ । yatpunaridamuk‍taṃ1 liṅgasya śrutyāpi bādhi-
tatvāditi । ko'yaṃ hetuḥ ? na hi śrutyā bādhitasyānyenāpi bādhyatā ।
﻿<pb n="b783"/>
tasmāt bāliśabhāṣitamevedaṃ pratibhāti । nedaṃ bāliśabhāṣitam ।
anyo'bhiprāyaścodakasya । yathaiva śrutyā padārthānvayasaṃbandhajñānakāraṇa-
tvena liṅgaṃ bādhitaṃ kāryaikyaviniyojyatvādevaṃ vākyenāpīti pūrvapakṣi-
tam । atrābhidhīyate---yajuṣastāvadviniyogaḥ pratipadam । kāryataḥ
punaraikyaṃ padānāṃ, yāvadekaṃ kāryaṃ tāvadaviruddhaḥ padāntarasaṃbandhaḥ ।
kāryāntare tu pratyarthini na kāryāntarasaṃbandhitā śakyate pratipat‍tuṃ
pratipadavidhānādeva । atra hi kāryato mantratvam । na mantrataḥ kāryaṃ
<pb n="b784"/>
yathā ṛkṣu sāmasu ca । ataḥ kāryanirapekṣakevalapadārthānvaya-
saṃbandhitāṃ vākyanibandhinīṃ bādhate liṅgam ।</p>
<p>nanu ca śrutāvapyevameva prāpnoti । satyaṃ prāpnoti yadīdaṃ yajuḥ
syāt tat‍tu śrutiviniyojyatvaṃ ṛkṣu pradarśitam । ṛcāṃ tu
mantrataḥ kāryamityuktam । yajuṣāṃ punaḥ yatrāpi iṣe tveti viniyogaḥ
tatrāpyupādānavaśādvicchedaḥ na punaḥ kāryopādānābhyāṃ anyo
yajuṣṭve heturasti । tasmādyukto vākyabhedaḥ । yatpunaridaṃ bhāṣya-
kāreṇa pradarśitaṃ---1<q>“nanu caikavākyatvepi liṅgameva vyāpriyata”</q> iti ।
tadayuktamiva pratibhāti । kimiti, kāryato'trārthanirṇayaḥ । kutaḥ ?
﻿<pb n="b785"/>
na sāmarthyamātrāt, kāryasavyapekṣaṃ hi sāmarthyaṃ liṅgamiti
nirūpitam । yadapi ca parihṛtaṃ---<q>“arthaviprakarṣo'tra bādhyatve hetuḥ ।
asti caikavākyabhūtasya liṅgasyābhidhānālliṅgāt viprakarṣaḥ”</q>
iti । tadapyayuktamiva । ekavākyatāhetorliṅgasyāliṅgatvā-
dityuk‍tam । atrocyate---pratipadaṃ viniyogāt ekavākya-
tayāpi ca kāryopapatteḥ yuktā liṅgatāśaṅkā । parihāraścārtha-
viprakarṣāt । tasmānnātra śrutirliṅgaṃ vākyamiti tantraṃ, viprakṛṣṭaṃ
aprāpakamiti sūtrārthaḥ । ataḥ siddhaṃ kāryabhedādvākyabheda iti । tarhi
tasmin sīdeti kimālambanamidaṃ ? pūrvaprakṛtālambanamevevati brūmaḥ ।
nanu caivaṃ sati parārthataiva pūrvasya prāpnoti tataśca vākyaṃ
balavadityuktaṃ bhavati । nāvaśyaṃ parāmarśe tādarthyameva
﻿<pb n="b786"/>
bhavati । anyārthamapyanyārthenāvamṛśyate eva sarvanām‍netyadoṣaḥ । yathā
tatprayojako heturiti, yathā ca vede etasyaiva revatīṣviti ।
tasmādvalīyo'bhidhānamiti siddham । aya 1vākyaprakaraṇayoḥ
kathamiti । kiṃ punaḥ prakaraṇaṃ nāmeti । ko'yaṃ praśnaḥ ? itikartavya-
tārthitvādityevaṃ nirjñāte prakaraṇe na vidmaḥ kimartho'yaṃ praśna iti ।
atrocyate---iti kartavyatārthitvādityuktam । na vidmaḥ kasyeyamiti
kartavyatārthiteti । yasyeyamitikartavyatākāṅkṣā tadatrocyate
---kartavyasyeti niyogārthasyetyarthaḥ । tasyetikartavyatākāṅkṣasya
yeyaṃ tṛtīyākāṅkṣā tatprakaraṇaṃ tena biniyogaḥ । tadviniyoge kāraṇaṃ
na kartavyatāmātraṃ nāpyanyat । ta smādupapannaḥpraśnārthaḥ, uttaraṃ ca ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b787"/>
<p>idānīṃ vākyaprakaraṇayoḥvirodhe <q>“1tulyabale ete kāraṇe”</q> iti
ko'bhiprāyaḥ ? kāryārthatvādanvayasya ubhayaṃ kāryeṇa viniyujyata
iti । yadvā kāryādṛte'nvayasya bādhitatvāt prakaraṇameva balīyaḥ ।
tatpratyayatvādvākyasya । evaṃ manyānenoktaṃ vākyasya bādhitatvāditi ।
﻿<pb n="b788"/>
atrocyate---atrāpyarthaviprakarṣādityukto hetuḥ । kathamartha-
viprakarṣaḥ uktaḥ? kāryārthatayānvayaḥ kalpyaḥ । na ca klṛptānva-
yasya kāryārthatve siddhe'nvayāntaraṃ viniyuktaviniyogavirodhāt
liṅgavacchakyate pratipat‍tum । tasmādvākyaṃ balīyaḥ । durjñānaviprakarṣa-
jñāpanāyādhikaraṇaprapañco'yaṃ liṅgavat sarvatra draṣṭavyaḥ । udāharaṇa-
muktam । <q>“1 atha prakaraṇasya kramasya ca virodhe kimudāharam”</q> iti ।
atrāpi pūrvapakṣavādī manyate kramaprakaraṇayostulyabalatvamiti ।
﻿<pb n="b789"/>
kathaṃ ? bhāṣyakārastāvat ajñānameva vyapadiśati1 । kimajñānāt‍tulya-
balatvaṃ sidhyati ? jñānasya hi tulyabalatvaṃ atulyabalatvaṃ vā viṣayaḥ
nājñānasya । nanu cājñānamapi pramāṇatayopanyastameva । na, vyavahāra-
mātraṃ tadityuk‍tam । pramāṇāntaraprameyābhāvamātraṃ prameyam । iha
tulyabalatvaṃ atulyabalatvaṃ ca na pramāṇāntaraprameyabhāvamātraṃ
śakyate vak‍tum । kathaṃ tarhyetadbhāṣyaṃ <q>“na tāvadviśeṣamupalabhāmaha”</q>
iti । bhāṣyakāra evātra praṣṭavyaḥ ।</p>
<p>atrocyate---durvidagdhavacanamātramidam । ayamabhi-
prāyo bhāṣyakārasya । nātrānayorviśeṣo jñāyata iti
﻿<pb n="b790"/>
sarvatra prakaraṇānusyūteḥ kramo'pi kāryavānavagamyate eva । kāryataśca
sannidhiranvitamavagamayatīti । pratyuta prakaraṇamevātra bādhyatayāva-
gamyate । viśeṣopasaṃhārāt sannidheḥ । na hi klṛptasya sannidheḥ
kalpanā śakyate vak‍tum । anvayasyeva । tatpunaridamanvāruhya-
vacanamityuktamādhastye'dhikaraṇe । sarvatra caivaṃ draṣṭavyam ।
﻿<pb n="b791"/>
atrocyate---kramātprakaraṇaṃ balīyaḥ । kutaḥ ? na hyanā-
kāṅkṣitasya kramaḥ saṃbandhe hetuḥ । sannidhimātraṃ hi kramaḥ ।
na ca sannidhimātrāt saṃbandho bhāryā rājñaḥ puruṣo devadattasyetivata ।
ākāṅkṣā ca prakaraṇavatāṃ tulyeti sarvapradhānasaṃbandho videvanādīnām
kramāddhi ākāṅkṣā, ākāṅkṣāto'nvayaḥ anvayācca tādarthyamiti ।
so'yamarthaviprakarṣaḥ । yaduktaṃ kramādākāṅkṣopasaṃhāra iti tadayuktam ।
sarvārthatvepi kasyacitsannidhānabhavaśyaṃbhāvīti pāṭhārthameva tat ।
﻿<pb n="b792"/>
bādhitasya hyanugraho nyāyya ityuktam । “prakaraṇavataḥ sākāṅkṣatvāt
sannidhāne cāmnātena paripūrṇenāpyavakalpata ekavākyatvaṃ iti । kimidaṃ
paripūrṇenāpi iti ? etaduktaṃ bhavati---na cetkramaḥ prakaraṇaṃ
ekavākyataiva nāsti । nanu ākāṅkṣā sannidhiryogyatvamiti
caikavākyatve hetuḥ । satyaṃ vākyārthāvagatau, iha punarvā-
kyārthasya vākyārthasya ca saṃbandhaḥ । sa cetikartavyatārthitayaiva
saṃbadhyata ityuktam । kramaḥ punaḥ vākyārthasya ca sannidhāna-
mityuktam । yathā bhāryārājñaḥ puruṣo devadattasyetyatra pradarśitam ।
﻿<pb n="b793"/>
<q>“atha kramasamākhyayoḥ kathaṃ ?”</q> kramo hyākāṅkṣāvataḥ sannidhaubhavati
viśeṣāvagatau hetuḥ । samākhyā punaḥ viśeṣanimittaiveti tulyabale
ete kāraṇe iti । tasmādubhayaṃ viniyojakam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b794"/>
<p>atrābhidhīyate---kramo balīyān vaidiko hyasau sannidhiḥ ।
samākhyāpunarlaukikī । nanu caivaṃ vadatā samākhyā naiva pramāṇamityuktaṃ
bhavati । maibaṃ vocaḥ arthaviprakarṣa evānena prakāreṇocyate । kathaṃ ?
samākhyā hi saṃbandhanimittā satī sannidhānādyavagamayati ।
kramaḥ punaḥ svayameva sannidhiḥ । na ca pratyakṣasya sannidheḥ punaḥ
sannidhānāntarakalpanāṃ ghaṭate iti so'yamarthaviprakarṣaḥ । kathaṃ tarhi
samākhyā ? samavāyādibhiḥ upapadyate brāhmaṇagrāmavat ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b795"/>
<p>1<q>“atha yat tatra tatrābhidhīyate idamanena bādhyaṃ idamanena
bādhyamiti tatra yadbādhyate kiṃ tadbādhakaviṣayaṃ prāptaṃ utāprāptamiti”</q> ।
kasya vyākhyānametat ? na kasyacidapīti brūmaḥ । kiṃ tarhi anena
atra kriyate । bhāṣyakāra evātra praṣṭavyaḥ । atrābhidhīyate
---śrutyādīnāṃ balābalacintāśeṣabhūtamidaṃ bhāṣyam । kathaṃ kṛtvā ?
balābalacintā hi bādhyāpekṣiṇī । tadidānīṃ bādhyaṃ kiṃ
bādhakaviṣayaṃ prāptaṃ sat bādhyate utāprāptamiti । ubhayathā'bhi-
hito doṣaḥ । nanu ca prāptabādho daśame darśita eva । kimiti
prāptau satyāṃ virodho darśitaḥ । ucyate---kāryataḥ prāptau na doṣaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b796"/>
<p>ihopadeśaścintyate । upadeśena ca prāptiḥ durbādheti tatraiva
daśame pradarśayiṣyāmaḥ । iha kasmāttanna pradarśyate ? pradarśita-
meva <q>“pratipradhānamāvartante guṇā”</q> iti । kathaṃ pratipradhānāvṛttyabhidhāne-
nābādhaḥ pradarśito bhavati । dvayoḥ prāmāṇyābhyupagamena
pratipradhānābhidhānāt । prāpteścāviśeṣāt । tasmāt ayuktamida-
manena bādhyamiti aprāpte'pi । atredānīmupadeśabādhavido
'bhidadhati । sāmānyataḥ prāptiṃ manvānā viśeṣamapaśyantaḥ smṛti---
pramoṣanimittaṃ prāptijñānaṃ vyapadiśanti śuktikāyāmiva rajata-
jñānam । viśeṣāvagamāt‍tu tatteṣāṃ nivartata iti bādhaśabdaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b797"/>
nanu cāyamuk‍to bādhaḥ prathamapāda eva <q>‘yasya ca duṣṭaṃ
karaṇaṃ’</q> ityatra kimiti punarupanyastaḥ ? ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b798"/>
<p>astyatra viśeṣaḥ tatra hi śuk‍tikārthasyāgrahaṇāt rajate
ca smarāmīti pramoṣāt vyapadeśasiddhiḥ । iha punarāga-
mikatvena dvayasyāpi tulyatāpattirbhavatyeveti punarārabdham ।
kiṃ punarāgamikatve dvayasyāpi tulyatāpattiḥ । tulyatāpattau
vā bādhaḥ । atrocyate---svato viparyayābhāvāt । na śuk‍tikādi-
ṣviva svayameva viyarpayo bhavati aparīkṣitakāraṇasvabhāvasyāpi ।
<pb n="b799"/>
iha punaḥ kāraṇaparīkṣādvārako viparyaya iti prārabdhamidama-
dhikaraṇam । tadviśudhyarthaṃ cedaṃ bhāṣyam । so'yaṃ aprāptabādha
iti sūktam ।। 8 ।।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="15">।। 6 ।। ahīno vā prakaraṇādnauṇaḥ ।। 15 ।।</ab>
<p>idamidānīṃ cintyate---kiṃ niyogasannidhirbalīyān
﻿<pb n="b800"/>
uta viniyogasannidhiriti । pūrvapakṣavādī kāryārthatvādviniyogasya
prakṛtakāryasaṃbhave prakṛtakāryasaṃbandho yukta iti manyate । kathaṃ tarhi
viniyogaḥ ? kāryārthatvāt, tadanuguṇo vyākhyāyate । evaṃ tarhi prakara-
ṇādvākyaṃ durbalamityuk‍tam, na, san‍nidhānāviśeṣe hi vākyaṃ balīyaḥ ।
yatra punaḥ kāryasan‍nidhireva nāsti kiṃ tatra vākyaṃ kariṣyati ।
﻿<pb n="b801"/>
tasmāt kāryānuguṇaiva padārthavyākhyeti yuk‍taṃ na hīyata
ityahīnaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="16">1asaṃyogāt‍tu mukhyasya tasmādapakṛṣyate ।। 16 ।।</ab>
<p>atra bhaṇyate---uk‍tamasmābhiḥ padārthānvayaḥ saṃbandhakāraṇaṃ
kāryato'pyanvaya evāvagamyate । na cānvayāvagame pratītānvayatyāgo
yuktaḥ । na ca dṛṣṭe hastini tatpādenānumānaṃ saṃbhavati । tasmāda-
pratipakṣameva padārthavyākhyānaṃ yuktam । padārtha eva hi padārthaprati-
pakṣo bhavati na punaḥ kāryam । anyathā hi arthavādapadānāmapi
kartavyatābhidhānataiva syāt । tasmādahīnasyeti kratvantarārthataiva
nyāyyā ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b802"/>
<p>nanu ca tulyamevātra śrautatvaṃ ekatra na hīyata ityahītaḥ anya---
trānhāṃ samūha iti । kimasmākamanayā cintayā । ekatra śrauto'nyatra
gauṇa iti kṛtvā cintitam । na cedatra saṃbhavati udāharaṇāntaraṃ
saṃbhaviṣyati । yadvā rūḍhiṃ manyate bhāṣyakāraḥ satreṣvadarśanāt ।
﻿<pb n="b803"/>
vyutpattimātraṃ taddhitavidhiḥ śunaśśepādiṣu samāsavidhiriva ।
tasyādidamapyupapadyata evodāharaṇam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="17">।। 9 ।। dvibahutvayuktaṃ codanāttasya ।। 17 ।।</ab>
<p>nanu caiva pūrveṇaivādhikaraṇena gatamidam । na hi pratīyamānānva-
yatyāgo yuktaḥ kāryānurodheneti । satyam---kintu astyatrādhikā-
śaṅkā । yathāśaktiprayoge nitye karmaṇi yajamānāntarapraveśamapi
manyate pūrvapakṣavādī । pat‍nyabhiprāyaṃ caikaśeṣābhidhānam
tasmādanutkarṣaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b804"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="19">na prakṛterekasaṃyogāt ।। 19 ।।</ab>
<p>atrābhidhīyate---yajamānāntarapraveśastāvanna saṃbhavati । kutaḥ ?
yajamānasya hi yathā śak‍nuyādityucyate । tatra yanna saṃbhavati
tasyaiva gauṇārthatā, tyāgo vā, na punaryajamānāntaropādānena saṃpat ।
sati caivaṃ na yajamānādvitvaṃ bahutvaṃ vā bhavati prakṛtau । yadapyuk‍taṃ
pat‍nyabhiprāyā dvayoryajamānayoḥ bahubhya iti cābhidhānopapattiriti ।
tadapyayuktam । tasmānna pat‍nyabhiprāya iti itaretarayogo ghaṭate ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b805"/>
<p>ādhāne tu lakṣaṇayā, asaṃbhavāt śrautasya yathā ca pat‍nyā
sahetaretarayogo nāsti yāge tathā ṣaṣṭhe vakṣyāmaḥ । satriṇāmeva
hi saḥ । tasmādatrāpi pūrvavadutkarṣaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="20">।। 10 ।। jāghanī caikadeśatvāt ।। 20 ।।</ab>
<p>kena punaḥ prasaṅgenedamadhikaraṇamāyātam ? anena prasaṅgena ।
sthitaṃ tāvat prakaraṇāt vākyaṃ balīyaḥ sannidhāne
﻿<pb n="b806"/>
cāsannidhāne ca kāryasya । atredaṃ sandihyate---kimayaṃ vākyārtha
utāyaṃ iti vākyārtha eva saṃśayaḥ । kiṃ jāghanyuddeśena pat‍nīsaṃyājā
vidhīyante uta viparītamiti । pūrvapakṣī tāvat jāghanyuddeśena
pat‍nīsaṃyājavidhānaṃ manyate । kutaḥ ? evaṃ śrauto'rtho-
vihito bhavati । anyathā hi vākyārthavidhānaṃ syāt ।
nanu cāsmin pakṣe vākyārtha eva vihito bhavati anyadanya-
smin‍nucyate । anabhijño bhavān vacanavyaktīnām । na brūmo
vākyārthasya vidhisaṃbandho nāsti iti kiṃ tu vidheyo vākyārthaḥ ।
etaduk‍taṃ bhavati---na sannikṛṣṭatyāgena viprakṛṣṭārthavidhānaṃ yuktamiti ।
ayaṃ cāparo lābhaḥ jāghanyā paśupādānakalpanā na kṛtā bhavati ।
tasmādatrāpyutkarṣaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b807"/>
<p>codanā vā'pūrvatvāt ।।</p>
<p>atrābhidhīyate---jāghanyevātra pat‍nīsaṃyājeṣu vidhīyate ।
kutaḥ ? yāgavidhāne hi pat‍nyartho vidhātavyo bhavati । nanu cātra
pat‍nīsaṃyājāścodakena saṃnihitā eva । satyam---vidhīyamānatvena tu
prakaraṇāntare prayojanānyatvamiti karmāntarāpattiḥ । nanu cāsannidhānaṃ
tatra karmāntaratve hetuḥ na vidhīyamānatā, na cānanyārthatvamatra, jāgha-
nīyasaṃbandhārthatvādvākyasya । tasmānnāyaṃ vākyabhedaparihāra upa-
labhyate । ucyate---anabhijño devānāṃ priyaḥ śāstra-
bhedasya । vidhānasannidhirhi vihitavidhāne bhedamuparuṇaddhi,
﻿<pb n="b808"/>
na padārthamātrasannidhiḥ । uddeśyatve hi bhavati padārthamātrasannidhirapya-
vagamahetuḥ, padārthamātrasavyapekṣatvāt uddeśya bhāvasya । tasmāda‍yukto
vākyabhedaḥ । yatpunaridaṃ bhāṣyakāreṇobhayathā saṃbandhividhāna-
mupanyastaṃ tatkimartham ? ucyate । nāntarīyakasākṣādvidhānaviveka-
pradarśanārtham । pradarśanamidānīṃ kimarthaṃ ? anyatarāprāp‍tyarthaṃ
neha prakaraṇe ubhayasyāvāptirupapadyate । tasmāt anyatara-
dvidheyam । sā ca jāghanyeva, pat‍nīsaṃyājānāṃ prāptatvāttasmādanutkarṣaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b809"/>
yatpunaridamuk‍taṃ na paśuṃ prayuṅk‍ta iti asmadīyepi pakṣe laukikyāḥ
prayuk‍tervidyamānatvāt‍tulyam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="24">।। 11 ।। 1santardanaṃ prakṛtau krayaṇavadanarthalopāt syāt ।। 24 ।।</ab>
<p>atrāpyutkarṣāśaṅkā dīrghaśacdasyānanvayāt । dhṛtyā ityartha-
vādānupapatteśca । anutkarṣavādī tu latādairdhyeṇāpyanuvādaṃ manvānaḥ
dīrghasya vā somasya iti prakṛtāvevaitadvidhānamiti manyate । rāddhānta-
vādī punaḥ somāpekṣaivātra dīrghatā mantavyā na latāpekṣeti
ca nātirekādvinā'rthavādopapattiḥ iti saṃsthāsvityuktavān ।
nanu cāsminnapi pakṣe prakaraṇādutkarṣa eva । saṃsthā hi vikārāḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b810"/>
yāgābhiprāyo'yamutkarṣaḥ kāryāpekṣayā tūtkarṣa evetyadoṣaḥ । yatpuna-
ridamuk‍taṃ sīsena krīṇātītivadvikalpa iti । nanu ca tatra
samuccayo'nayoḥ na vikalpaḥ daśabhireva krīṇātīti । bidhānavikalpa-
maṅgīkṛtyaitannidarśanam, na prayogavikalpam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="32">।। 12 ।। 1saṅkhyāyuk‍taṃ kratoḥ prakaraṇāt syāt ।। 32 ।।</ab>
<p>vākyārthasamavāyāpekṣiṇī prakaraṇādutkarṣacintā gatā, idānī-
mabhidhānavipratipattirvākya eva cintyate---kimayaṃ prathama-
śabdo jyotiṣṭoma eva vartate uta jyotiṣṭomaprayoga iti ।
﻿<pb n="b811"/>
<q>‘eṣa vāva prathamo yajño yajñānāṃ’</q> iti śravaṇāddhi spaṣṭaiva yajñavacanatā
gamyate <q>“1evaṃ ca prakaraṇamanugrahīṣyate”</q> iti pratiṣedhavidhyabhiprāyaṃ
tat ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="33">2naimittikaṃ vā kartṛsaṃyogāt liṅgasya tannimittatvāt ।। 33 ।।</ab>
<p>atrābhidhīyate---satyamasmāt prayogāt avagamyate kintu
ya etenāniṣ‍ṭvā'thānyena yajeteti prayogādapi prāthamyamavagamyate
﻿<pb n="b812"/>
nāniṣ‍ṭvā'thānyena yajeteti । kathaṃ ? kartṛsaṃbandhitayā śrūya-
māṇatvāt । kartuśca prayogeṇa saṃbandho na prayojyena । prayogapare
ca vākye eṣa vāva prathamo yajño yajñānāṃ yajjyotiṣṭoma iti śrutiḥ
na punaḥ prayojyaniṣṭhā । kvacidasya prayogo'vagamyate jyotiṣṭoma-
śabdasyaiva । ataḥ prayoga evāyaṃ iti na prathame prayoge pravṛñj‍yā-
dityarthaḥ । yajñaśabdaśca prayojyaviṣayatvāt prayoge'pyupapadyata eva ।
﻿<pb n="b813"/>
prathamaprayojyo yajñānāmityarthaḥ । evaṃ ca prakaraṇa eva pravargya-
vidhirupapanno bhavati ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="34">।। 12 ।। 1pauṣṇaṃ peṣaṇaṃ vikṛtau pratīyetācodanātprakṛtau ।। 34 ।।</ab>
<p>pauṣṇaṃ peṣaṇaṃ uttaravivakṣayetyuk‍tam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="35">।। 13 ।। 2tatsarvārthamaviśeṣāt ।। 35 ।।</ab>
<p>idamidānīṃ cintyate kiṃ yāvatpauṣṇaṃ tatsarvaṃ prapiṣṭaṃ kartavyaṃ uta
carureveti । tatra pūrvapakṣavādī viśeṣāgrahaṇāt sarvārthamiti manyate ।
nanu ca puroḍāśe prāptatvāt na śakyate vidhātuṃ; na, pauṣṇatayā aprāpteḥ
﻿<pb n="b814"/>
tasmāt sarvārtham । nanu hṛdayādyākṛtivināśaḥ paśau bhavatu,
vacanāt । kimiva vacanaṃ na kuryāt । atrocyate---puroḍāśe
tāvat prāptatvānna vidhiḥ । nanu pauṣṇatayā'prāptirityuktam । kāryata
eva prāptiriṣyate na saṃbandhitayā anyathā hyarthavādapadānāmapi
kāryārthataiva syādityuktam । nanu caivaṃ sati prakaraṇādvākyaṃ durbala-
mityuktam । kārye satyanvayakalpanā ato balavattā uktā vākyasya ।
﻿<pb n="b815"/>
tasmānna vidhānaṃ puroḍāśe saṃbhavati । paśau tarhi saṃbhavati । na
hi । tarhi sāpekṣatvaprasaṅgāt śāstrasya । na ca nirapekṣe saṃbhavati
sāpekṣāśrayaṇaṃ yuktamityuktaṃ śabdavidbhiḥ । tasmāt carāveva peṣaṇaṃ
śabdāt pratīmaḥ । yatpunaridamuk‍taṃ 1yadyapītyevamādinā bhāṣya-
kāreṇa evamapi sāpekṣatvaṃ naiva parihartuṃ śakyata ityabhiprāyaḥ ।
anvārohamātraṃ caitata । pūrvameva hyukto hetuḥ । nanu ca carāvapi
carutaiva hīyeta viśadasiddhaudane prayogadarśanāt । na, piṣṭakacarāvapi
pak‍tisāmānyāt ityabhihitaḥ caruśabdaprayoga iti carāveva
peṣaṇamiti siddham ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b816"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="39">।। 15 ।। 1ekasminnekasaṃyogāt ।। 39 ।।</ab>
<p>atra bhāṣyakāreṇa indrapītāgneyaśabdābhyāṃ viśeṣo darśitaḥ
pūṣā prapiṣṭabhāgo bhavatīti । tathā adantako hīti hetuvacanaṃ somā-
pauṣṇe nemapiṣṭaścaruriti । somāpauṣṇe nemapiṣṭa ityanuvādo yuktaḥ ।
nemapiṣṭavidhāne hi pauṣṇopalakṣaṇāt carurityavivakṣitaṃ syādityeva-
mādyadhikāśaṅkānirākaraṇārthamidamadhikaraṇam । atrocyate---katha-
māsāmāśaṅkānāṃ nirākaraṇaṃ ? kāryaprayuktatvāddharmāṇāmityuk‍to
hetuḥ । kathaṃ punaḥ kāryeṇa saṃbandho devatāpadayuktānāṃ bhavatīti
﻿<pb n="b817"/>
niṣprayojanatvāddevatāyāḥ kāryārthatvācca yāgasyeti lakṣaṇopapadyate ।
devatā cedupalakṣaṇaṃ na dvidevatākeṣūpalakṣayituṃ kṣamaḥ । adevatā hi
sā tatra । adantakatvādīnāṃ tu hetuvannigadatvenārthavādatvamuktam ।
arthavādāśca guṇavādena vyākhyeyāḥ । nemapiṣṭaśabdasya nyāyā-
petatvāt dvidevatākeṣu viśiṣṭavidhānaṃ bhaviṣyati । tasmādeka-
devatākeṣu peṣaṇamiti siddham ।</p>
<trailer>iti bṛhatyāṃ tṛtīyādhyāyasya
tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>
﻿<pb n="b818"/>
<head>tṛtīyādhyāyasya caturthaḥ pādaḥ ।।</head>
<ab type="sutra" n="1">।। 1 ।। 1nivītamiti manuṣyadharmaḥ śabdasya tatpradhānatvāt 3-4-1 ।।</ab>
<p>kathaṃ punaḥ vidhinā tvekavākyatvāditi sthite'rthavādatve puna-
rvidhānāśaṅkā । ekavākyatve hi na vidhidvayamavakalpata iti na nivī-
tatvādividhisaṃbhavaḥ । pākṣikīṃ prāptiṃ manvāno vidhiṃ manyata iti cet ।
tadapyayuktam । tasyāpi vacanāntareṇa prāptatvāt upapadyata evārtha-
vādaḥ । ucyate---prakaraṇāṅgatayā'prāptiṃ manvānenedamadhikaraṇaṃ cinti-
tam । vidhānepi prakaraṇāṅgatā na saṃbhavatīti sthitamarthavādatvam ।
﻿<pb n="b819"/>
nanu cātithyādāvaprāptirvidyata iti yuk‍tam । na । tadanvayāna-
vagamāt । manuṣyamātrasaṃbandhitāyāṃ tu prāyādibhirupapannatvāt
arthavādataiveti siddham ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="10">।। 2 ।। 1digvibhāgaśca tadvatsambandhasyārthahetutvāt ।। 3-4-10 ।।</ab>
<ab type="sutra" n="11">।। 3 ।। paruṣiditadhṛtapūrṇavidagdhaṃ ca tadvat ।। 3-4-11 ।।</ab>
<p>tadvadityayamatideśaḥ kimabhyadhikaṃ paśyataḥ ? anyathā
hyupavīte prāptiḥ, anyathā dikṣu, anyathā paruṣi dinādiṣviti
viśeṣapradarśanārtho'yamatideśaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b820"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="12">।। 4 ।। 1akarmakratusaṃyuktaṃ saṃyogānnityānuvādaḥ syāt ।। 3-4-12 ।।</ab>
<p>uk‍taṃ nivītādhikaraṇena kratudharmatayā nivītādi pratīyate manu-
ṣyaśravaṇāditi । prāyeṇa ca prāptatvādanuvāda iti । atrāpīdānīṃ
tadvadevānuvādaṃ manvānasya pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । nanu ca tatra manuṣyaśabda-
śravaṇādyuk‍to'nuvādaḥ prāyikīṃ ca prāptimāśritya arthavādaḥ । ucyate ।
atrāpi pūrvaprāptapratiṣedhāt gamyata eva pumān yasyāsau pratiṣedhaḥ ।
pratiṣedhaśās‍tre hi sarvatra pratiṣidhyamānakriyākarturevādhikāraḥ
﻿<pb n="b821"/>
ataḥ pūrvaprāptasyaivāyamanuvādaḥ । vidyate ca prāptiḥ arthataḥ ।
prāptimātratayā ca pratiṣedhopapatteḥ na prakaraṇārthatā । nanu cāyamanu-
vādaḥ kasya vidheḥ śeṣaḥ ? na kasyacidapīti brūmaḥ । prāp‍tiranuvādatve
hetuḥ nārthavādatā ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b822"/>
<p>ekavākyatvena hi arthavādo bhavati na prāp‍timapekṣate
yathā jārtilayavāgvā juhuyāditi । tasmānnānuvādaḥ । nanu cedaṃ
śrutivākyaṃ tasyāḥ smṛtermūlaṃ bhaviṣyati । na bhavitu-
marhati । atra hi śrūyamāṇasya prakaraṇārthatā'vasīyate na puruṣārthatā
anuvādapakṣe punaḥ puruṣārthatayaiva prāp‍teḥ siddhā puruṣārthatā । nanu ca
﻿<pb n="b823"/>
kratvarthatayāvagamyamānasya kathaṃ puruṣārthatayā'nuvādo yuktaḥ kalpa-
yitum । ucyate---kraturapi hi puruṣārtha eva । atastatsaṃbandhi-
tayāpi puruṣasyecchātaḥ prāpnotyevānṛtavadanamiti na doṣaḥ tatsaṃbandhā-
vagateḥ । upanayottarakālabhāvitvācca kratūnāṃ siddho'nuvādaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="13">1vidhirvā saṃyogāntarāt ।। 3-4-13 ।।</ab>
<p>atrābhidhīyate । āyuṣmataivok‍taṃ na smṛtivākyasyedaṃ mūlatāṃ
pratipadyata iti । evaṃ cet tvayaivedaṃ saṃyogāntaramabhyupagataṃ saṃyogā-
﻿<pb n="b824"/>
ntaratve ca nānuvādaḥ śakyate vak‍tum । nanu ca pratiṣedhe
pratiṣidhyamānakriyākarturevādhikāra ityuktam । satyamuktam । na tu
tat prakaraṇe śakyate vak‍tum । kimiti ? padārthamātra eva
pratiṣedhopapatteḥ laukikeṣu punaḥ puruṣecchāta eva pravṛttirviṣayatāṃ
pratipadyate pratiṣedhasyeti tatkriyākarturevādhikāro yuktaḥ । iha
punaḥ kratvarthatayaiva pravṛttirgamyate padārthasyeti na tasya karturadhikāraḥ
śakyate vak‍tum । nanu ca kartaivākhyāteṣu pradhānatayāvagamyate ।</p>
<pb n="b825"/>
niyogābhedāt‍tu prayājādīnāmaṅgatvabhavagamyate । saveṣāmekaphalānu-
bandhatvāt । saṃskārakarmaṇāmapi kratvarthasya saṃskāryatayā'vagateḥ
yuk‍taivāṅgatā । pratiṣedhe punaḥ pratiṣedhyasya akratvarthatvāt
ākhyātena ca kartrabhidhānāt kartureva pratīyate । na ca tatsaṃbandhā-
vagatirviruddhā । kratorapi puruṣārthatvāt upanayanottarakālabhāvi-
tvācca tadarthapratipatteḥ siddho'nuvāda ityuktam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b826"/>
<p>atrocyate---syādetadevaṃ yadyākhyātānāṃ kartā'bhidheyaḥ syāt,
na punarākhyātānāṃ kartrabhidhānaśaktiḥ śakyate kalpayitum ।
kriyābhidhānādeva sarvakārakāvagateḥ । kathaṃ tarhi bhagavataḥ pāṇineḥ
sūtraṃ laḥ karmaṇi ca bhāve cākarmakabhyaḥ cakārāt kartari ceti । saṅkhyā-
vidhānārthametaditi pradarśitam । saṅkhyāviśeṣavidhānāśrayaṃ ca yak
śabiti ca । anyakārakasaṅkhyābhidhānamidānīṃ kimiti na bhavati ?
tulye'vagamyamānatve । na lokaḥ paryanuyok‍tuṃ śakyate । durjayo
hi mahājanaḥ; laukikaprayogamūlaṃ cedaṃ śāstraṃ bhagavataḥ pāṇineḥ
﻿<pb n="b827"/>
prayuktasya hi niyamamācaṣṭe । nāprayuktasyābhidhānam । tasmāda-
paryanuyogo'yam । ataḥ kratvarthapadārthamātrapravṛttyāśrayamevedaṃ pratiṣedha-
śāstram । nanu ca pratiṣedhyagatā pravṛttiḥ na kratvarthatyuktam । aco-
ditatvāt । naiva tādarthyena coditatvaṃ saṃbandhahetuḥ upakārakatayāpi
saṃbandhitopapadyata eva । saṃbandhini ca vidhiḥ kratvartho bhavatītyuktaṃ
payo brataṃ brāhmaṇasyetyevamādiṣu । nanu copakārakaviṣayatayā
pratiṣedhasya kratvarthapuruṣārthayorna kaścidviśeṣaḥ । yathāsti viśeṣa-
stathoktam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b828"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="14">।। 5 ।। 1ahīnavatpuruṣadharmastadarthatvāt ।।3-4-14 ।।</ab>
<p>kaḥ punaḥ nivītaṃ manuṣyāṇāmityanena viśeṣaḥ jañjabhyamānasya ?
ayamasti viśeṣaḥ nārthavādāt parihāraḥ saṃbhavati । avākya-
śeṣatvāt । nāpyanuvādo nānṛtaṃ vadeditivat । nāpyatrārthaprāptasya
viṣayatvasaṃbhavo nānṛtaṃ vadeditivat । na hi jañjabhyamānatāṃ
kadācidapi prāp‍noti anṛtavadanavat । tasmājjañjabhyamāna-
mātrasya mantravidhānamidaṃ na prakaraṇe'vasthāpayituṃ śakyate ।
﻿<pb n="b829"/>
nanu caivaṃ sati phalakalpanā syāt । bhavatu vacanāt, ko doṣaḥ ?
ato vākyāt prakaraṇabādhaḥ siddho yathā dvādaśāhīna-
syeti । atrābhidhīyate---na phalakalpanāmarhatyetadvacanam । kutaḥ ?
vākyaṃ hi padārthasaṃbandhamātre prabhavati na kārye । kāryaṃ hi
niyogasamadhigamyameva prakṛtaścāyaṃ dārśapaurṇamāsiko niyogaḥ ।
sarvamevedaṃ viniyogakāraṇam । na ca kāryāntarakalpanā
﻿<pb n="b830"/>
klṛpte sati saṃbhavati iti prakaraṇa eva niveśaḥ । nanu ca jañjabhya-
mānatā na kratvarthatayā'nṛtavadanavat saṃbhavati । mābhūt jañjabhya-
mānatā kratvarthā । kartustu kratvarthatā prakaraṇasaṃbandhe heturbhaviṣyati ।
tasmāt kratoḥ kartuḥ dharmo'yamiti siddham । ahīne punaḥ
kāryatvād‍yuktaḥ utkarṣaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="17">।। 6 ।। 1śaṃyau ca sarvaparīdānāt ।। 3-4-17 ।।</ab>
<p>śaṃyau punaḥ śatena yātayāditi phalaśruteḥ na prakaraṇa-
kalpanā nyāyyā । svavākyasthā hi kāryāvagatiḥ balīyasī
﻿<pb n="b831"/>
tasmāt puruṣamātradharmau'yaṃ na brāhmaṇāyāvagureditivat । nanu
jañjabhyamānepi <q>‘prāṇāpānāvevātman dhatta’</q> iti phalaśravaṇabhastyeva ।
na । dhatta iti vartamānopadeśāt na sādhyatayāvagamyate । iha punaḥ
yātayāta iti bhaviṣyadarthatāṃ liṅavagamayatīti viśeṣaḥ ।
tasmānmūlasmṛteḥ prāptasyānuvāda iti ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b832"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="18">।। 7 ।। prāgaparodhānmalavadvāsasaḥ1 ।। 3-4-18 ।।</ab>
<p>malavadvāsasā saha saṃvādapratiṣedhe sandehaḥ kiṃ kratvarthaḥ saṃvādaḥ
uta puruṣārtha iti । kiṃ prāptaṃ ? nānṛtaṃ vadeditivat kratau saṃbhavāt
kratvartha iti prāpte । ucyate---na prāptatvāt । kratvarthatayā hi
<q>“tāmaparudhya yajeta”</q> । iti prāpta evāyamasaṃvādaḥ। tasmāt
puruṣārthaḥ vākyaṃ ca prakaraṇādvalīya ityuktameva ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b833"/>
<p>nanu puruṣārthatayāpi prāpta evāyamasaṃvādaḥ <q>“nākalyāṃ
nārīmabhiramayenna rajasvalāṃ”</q> iti । asyāḥ smṛteridameva mūlaṃ
bhaviṣyatīti । anuvādo vā sarvathā tāvat kratvarthatā
nāsti । nanu ca saṃvādamātrapratiṣedho'yam । ucyate--<q>‘nāsyā
annamadyāt abhyañjanaṃ vāva striyā annaṃ”</q> ityupagamanapratiṣedha
evāyamiti ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b834"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="28">।। 8 ।। aprakaraṇe tu taddharmastato viśeṣāt ।। 28 ।।</ab>
<p><q>‘hiraṇyaṃ bhāryaṃ’</q> ityanārabhyavādāt puruṣārtho'yam । na hyatra
kratussannihito'vagamyate । tasmātpuruṣārthaḥ । nanu ca prayojanavataḥ
saṃskāro, na niṣprayojanasya saṃskāryatā yuktā dvitīyānirdeśācca
hiraṇyasaṃskāra evāyaṃ yuktaḥ saṃskṛtaṃ kratorupakariṣyatīti ।
atrābhidhīyate---syādetadevaṃ yadi saṃskṛtasya hiraṇyasya karmārthatā
upapadyate---na tāvat prakṛtaṃ karmāsti । na ceha karmacodanā, dravya-
devatāsaṃyogābhāvāt । tasmāt dravyasaṃskārānarthakyāt puruṣa-
dharme'yam । nanu cātra phalaṃ kalpayitavyam ? niyogānāṃ
kāryārthatvāt prakṛtasya kāryāsyāvidyamānatvāt na doṣaḥ kalpanāyām ।
﻿<pb n="b835"/>
tasmāddhiraṇyadhāraṇaṃ karturdharmaścodyata iti sthitam । yadi kartṛ-
saṃskāratvena phalaṃ kalpyate kimiti dravyasaṃskāratayā kratūpakāro na
kalpyate । ayamasti viśeṣaḥ ekavākyāvagatena hyarthavādena
kartṛsambandhe phalakalpanā upapadyate na punaraprakṛtena kratunā artha-
viprakarṣāt । ayaṃ cāparo viśeṣaḥ sarvatra draṣṭavyaḥ kartṛsambandhe
hyadhikārasiddhiḥ adhikṛtasya ca phalakalpanā nyāyyā । na punaḥ
dravyasambandhe prayojanakalpaneti sak‍tuṣu darśitam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b836"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="31">।। 9 ।। śeṣo'prakaraṇe'viśeṣāt sarvakarmaṇāt ।। 31 ।।</ab>
<p>yena karmaṇertset iti aviśeṣāt sarvakarmārthateti pūrvapakṣavādī
manyate । nanu cānāhitāg‍nerāhavanīyābhāvāt nāyaṃ homaḥ
saṃbhavati anāhavanīya evāyaṃ bhaviṣyati pradhānānurodhāt । na
guṇānurodhena pradhānasyāṅtyāgo yuktaḥ । guṇa eva hi tattyāgaḥ
﻿<pb n="b837"/>
pradhānānurodhenetyaṅgavido manyante । satyamevaitat । kintvatra ayaṃ
nyāyo na saṃbhavati । kasmāt ? vaidike tāvadāhavanīyabādho
nopapadyate । na ca laukikasyaivāṅgamiti śakyate vak‍tuṃ tvayaivoktama-
viśeṣāditi । ato bhāvābhāvayorvirodhāt bhāvata eva viśeṣā-
vadhāraṇaṃ yuktam na punaḥ abhāvataḥ । anavagame hetuḥ asau । na punaḥ
viśeṣāvagame hetuḥ । tasmādvaidika eva jayāhoma iti siddham ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="34">।। 10 ।। doṣāttviṣṭirlaukike syāt śāsrāddhi vaidike na doṣaḥ syāt1 ।। 34 ।।</ab>
﻿<pb n="b838"/>
<p>pauṇḍarīke śrūyate---yāvato'śvān pratigṛhṇīyāt iti । kiṃ
laukike'śvapratigrahe iyamiṣṭiḥ uta vaidika iti saṃśayaḥ । laukike
dośadarśanāt śūdrādanyasmādvā pāpakarmaṇaḥ kṛte doṣo bhavatīti ।
<q>“1na doṣasaṅkīrtanaṃ prāyaścittaviṣayaviśeṣaṇam । kintu prāyaścittastu-
tyarthena”</q> iti । kimidaṃ prāyaścittaviṣayaviśeṣaṇaṃ kiṃ vā stutyartheneti़
idamidam । asyārthasyāpanuttaye yadā prāyaścittaṃ tadā viṣaya-
viśeṣaṇam । yadā tu kāryāntarārthaṃ tadā stutyarthena doṣa-
nirghātārthaṃ cedam । tasmāt laukike bhavitumarhati । <q>“2nanu
vaidikepi apratigrāhyāt pratigṛhṇato doṣo'styeva । ucyate ।
﻿<pb n="b839"/>
bhavedetadenaṃ yadi pratigrahasya karturiṣṭirbhavet । sā khalu
yathā hetukartuḥ tathā uttare'dhikaraṇe vakṣyāmaḥ”</q> । asambandha-
midaṃ bhāṣyam । yadi laukike pratigrahīturiṣṭiḥ na bhavati tataśca
vaidike'pi aśvaṃ apratigrāhyāt pratigṛhṇato doṣo'stīti satyapi
doṣanirghātārthe prāyaścitte kasmāllaukika eva pratigrahītuḥ prāyaścittā-
śaṅkā । atha upakramāvagatārthavādadarśanāt dāturiṣṭirityucyate
laukike'pi tulyam । atha laukike pratigrahapakṣepi dāturevetyabhiprāyaḥ
śūdrādanyasmādvā pāpakarmaṇaḥ iti bhāṣyaṃ asambaddham । kathaṃ voparitane-
'dhikaraṇe pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । vedo vā prāyadarśanādityupakrameṇopasaṃhārāva-
dhṛtteḥ । atrābhidhīyate-nedamasaṃbaddham । ayamabhiprāyaḥ pūrvapakṣavādinaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b840"/>
laukike'śvapratigrahe doṣaśravaṇaṃ viṣayaviśeṣaṇatayaivopapatteḥ । yasmā-
dasmin pakṣe pratigrahītureveṣṭiḥ । dāturyadīyamiṣṭiḥ syāt tato
dānasyāṅgaṃ vā kalpayitavyaṃ phalāntaraṃ vā । dānāṅgatā tāvanna saṃbhavati
nimittatvenāsyopakṣayāddānasya । atha viparivṛttyā punaraṅgitvaṃ
dānasya tadā idamevāyuktam । guṇavādenāpyarthavādopapatteḥ । pāpa-
pramocanasya phalatayā vā vākyenāvagateḥ । na ca dātuḥ pāpaṃ
śakyate kalpayitumiti । tasmālaukike pakṣe pratigrahītureveṣṭiḥ
﻿<pb n="b841"/>
coditatvālloke vede ca dānasya । rāddhāntavādī tu yathāśrutasya
pāpasyāśvapratigraho na nidānatayā pramāṇāntareṇa prasiddhaḥ । nāpi
vacanāt । vākyabhedaprasaṅgāt । tasmāt pāpamātravacanamidaṃ
vaidikepyupapadyata eva, rakṣaṇapoṣaṇādinā duḥ khadarśanāt । phalaṃ
ca na kalpayitavyaṃ bhavati karmāṅgatayopapatteḥ । prakaraṇaviniyojyatayā
karturvā bhavatu pratigrahīturvā ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b842"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="30">।। 11 ।। acoditaṃ ca karmabhedāta1 ।। 30।।</ab>
<p>yuktaṃ tāvat yadā kartuḥ tadā karmāṅgaṃ; yadā pratigrahītuḥ tadā
kathaṃ ? upakramopasaṃhāravaśāt pratigrāhayeditivat vipariṇāmāt
kalpyatām । ṛtvijo yājanīyāḥ upavāsavat ।</p>
<p>yatpunaridamuk‍taṃ---kathaṃ punaḥ vedo vā prāyadarśanāditi
sthite'dhikaraṇe uparitane'dhikaraṇe pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । doṣapradarśanādeveti
manyate । arthavādabhūto'pi doṣaḥ pratigrahīturevāñjasyenopapadyate ।
upakramo'pi laukikapakṣavata dāturapi tāvat aśvapratigrahe doṣaḥ
kiṃ punaḥ pratigrahīturiti vyākhyāyate । rāddhāntavādī tu avaśyaṃ
﻿<pb n="b843"/>
tāvat nirvāpayediti vipariṇāmaḥ kalpyaḥ । tasmādvaramupakrama-
darśanāt pratigrāhayedityevaṃ manyate । ato nedaṃ punaruktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="32">।। 12 ।। pānavyāpacca tadvat1 ।। 32 ।।</ab>
<p>tadvadityātideśiko'pi viśeṣaḥ । ayaṃ viśeṣaḥ doṣadarśanam ।
nanu ca pūrvasminnadhikaraṇe doṣadarśanādeva laukika ityuktam ।
satyamanupapattistatroktā doṣasya । iha tu glānirvamanādupapadyata
evendriyāṇāmityadhikāśaṅkā । ata eva vamanārthaṃ taditi parihṛtam ।
﻿<pb n="b844"/>
glānyarthameva yat na tasya glānirdoṣatvena śakyate kalpayitumiti ।
tasmāt pūrvavadevedaṃ karmaphalakalpanābhayāt coditasomapānavamana-
nimittakamityarthaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="34">।। 13।। tatsarvatrāviśeṣāt1 ।। 34 ।।</ab>
<p>kiṃ yāvantassomavāminaḥ tāvatāṃ vamane etatprāyaścittaṃ uta
svāmina eveti । aviśeṣāt sarvārthamiti prāpte । ucyate
---svāmina evedaṃ prāyaścittam । kutaḥ ? na yajamānasya ṛtvijāṃ
caikā codanā saṃbhavati । ekatra yajeteti codanā anyatra yājayediti
﻿<pb n="b845"/>
na caikasmin vākye ubhayametat bhavati । kasmāt ? avipariṇatā eṣā
codanā । sā ca svābhivamana evāvagamyate । tasmāt phalavatsanni-
dhāvaphalaṃ tadaṅgamiti bhavati tadidamuktam । nānyadīyo yāgo'nyasyo-
pakarotīti । tasmānna ṛtvigvamananimittamiti । na hyanyasya
coditamanyasyopakārotītyarthaḥ । ataḥ svāmivamananimittameveti
siddham ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="37">।। 14 ।। 1sarvapradānaṃ haviṣastadarthatvāt ।। 3-4-37 ।।</ab>
﻿<pb n="b846"/>
<p>ihedānīṃ sandihyate । <q>‘āg‍neyo'ṣṭākapāla’</q> iti kiṃ kṛts‍nasya
haviṣastyāgaḥ uta dvirhaviṣo'vadyatīti tāvanmātrasyaiva tyāga iti ।
nanu cātra sandeha eva nopapadyate āg‍neyo'ṣṭākapāla iti pari-
samāptā codanā । dvirhaviṣo'vadyatīti saṃskāracodanā haviṣaḥ
agnestṛṇānyapacinotītivat । nanu ca juhotītyapi śrūyate
haviṣo'panītasya pratipattirbhaviṣyati । yathā yāgottarakālaṃ
sviṣṭakṛdādayaḥ । atrābhidhīyate---naitadevam । juhotiḥ yāgāśca
saṃbandhidravyasādhyāḥ । sakalasya ca parityāge homo
yāgāśca sviṣṭakṛdādayaḥ nopapadyante ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b847"/>
<p>aṣṭākapālaviṣayāścodanāḥ । ata upapadyate saṃśayaḥ ।
asmiṃśca saṃśaye kasya pakṣasyādhyavasānaṃ yuk‍taṃ ? pūrvapakṣavādī
tāvanmanyate---apratipakṣatvādāgreyacodanāyāḥ tatsavyapekṣatvāccotta-
rāsāṃ pūrvaiva balīyasīti । tadidamuktam । <q>“sarvapradānaṃ haviṣasta-
darthatvāt”</q>। kathaṃ tarhi caturavattaṃ juhotīti sviṣṭakṛte sama-
vadyatīti । gauṇo vā yajyartho juhotyarthaśca grahītavyaḥ, taddharmakaṃ vā
dravyāntaramutpādyam । dvirhaviṣo'vadyati havirdharmakādavadyatītyarthaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="40">kṛtatvāt‍tu karmaṇaḥ sakṛtsyāt dravyasya guṇabhūtatvāt।। 3-4-40।।</ab>
<p>atrābhidhīyate---satyamevaṃ yathā bhavānāha। yadi
āgneyo'ṣṭākapāla iti tyāgaparyantastaddhitaḥ syāt।
﻿<pb n="b848"/>
sāsya devateti saṃbandhimātratayā'vagateḥ ekadeśatyāgādapyupapadyata
eva saṃbandhitā । tadidamuktam---<q>“akṛts‍nasaṃbandhepi taddhitasaṃbandha-
syopapattiḥ darśitastato grahītavyamiti saṃbandhaḥ"</q>। sati caivamāgneya-
codanāyāmupapannāyāṃ na caturavattaṃ juhoti sviṣṭakṛte samavadyati iti
gauṇī vṛttiḥ śakyate kalpayitum । havirdharmakasya vā dravya-
syotpādaḥ । tathā caturavattenaiva kṛtaḥ śāstrārthaḥ āg‍neyo'ṣṭāka-
pāla iti sviṣṭakṛdādidarśanaṃ copapannam । yatpunaridamāśaṅkitaṃ
dva‍yavadānasya saṃskāratvānna sarvaparityāge virodha iti tadidamāśaṅkā-
mātrameva haviṣo yāgārthatvādityuktam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b849"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="42">।। 15 ।। aprayojakatvādekasmātkriṃyeran śeṣasya guṇabhūtatvāt ।। 42 ।।</ab>
<p>iha śeṣakarmāṇyudāharaṇaṃ---kiṃ sakṛt kṛtvoparantavyam uta
yāvaccheṣamāvṛttiḥ iti । pūrvapakṣavādī kṛtatvācchāstrārthasya sakṛ-
tkaraṇaṃ manyate । nanu pratipradhānaṃ guṇā āvartanta iti śeṣasyā-
prādhānyādāvṛttikevātrāvagamyate । ayamabhiprāyaḥ pūrvapakṣavādinaḥ
---pradhānopakārāya hi śeṣasya saṃskāraḥ, sakṛt kṛtena ca kṛtaṃ kāryamiti
nāvṛt‍tiṃ manyate । na hi śeṣatvāt saṃskāryatvam । nanu ca
grahādāvapyevameva prāpnoti । prāpnotyeva yadyatra na samādhīyate । tatra
tarhi kā cintā ? ekatvasyāvivakṣetyuktam । atrābhidhīyate
---yāvaccheṣamāvṛt‍tiḥ । nanu ca kṛtatvācchāstrārthasya sakṛt ityuktam
﻿<pb n="b850"/>
ucyate । śeṣasaṃskāradvāraṃ hi pradhānasyopakāryatvamuktam । na ca
śeṣe viśeṣo'vagamyate । ayamayaṃ ayaṃ veti । ato'guhyamāṇa-
viśeṣāt, pratipradhānamāvṛt‍tiḥ liṅgāni darśitāni ca bhāṣye ।
yatpunaraprayojakatvāt śeṣāṇāmiti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ tadevedaṃ na śeṣatvāt
saṃskāryatvamiti yaduk‍taṃ, na punarguṇabhāvaṃ śeṣasya manyate । na hi
śeṣasya prayojakatvamaprayojakatvaṃ copapadyate । tasmāt sa eva pūrvaḥ
pakṣaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="46">।। 16 ।। ekasmāccedyārthākāmyamaviśeṣāt ।। 46।।</ab>
<p>pūrvādhikaraṇapūrvapakṣe anuṣṭhānacinteyam । atrāviśeṣādyataḥ
kutaściṃditi pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b851"/>
<p>mukhya eva nimit‍te saṃbhavati na naimit‍tikopaghātaḥ śakyate
kartumiti rāddhāntaḥ । jaghanyānāṃ tu kṛtatvāt naimit‍tikasya
(nimittāvagatiḥ) yuk‍taivākriyā śeṣakāryāṇām । iti ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="48">।। 17 ।। bhakṣāśravaṇāddānaśabdaḥ parikraye ।। 48 ।।</ab>
<p>idaṃ brahmaṇa iti dvyavadānopasaṃhārādyāgasya śeṣeṇa parikrayaṃ
manyate pūrvapakṣavādī । rāddhāntavādī tu tasyāvadeyayogyatayaivotpat‍teḥ
yāgārthataiveti nārthāntare viniyogamarhatīti । kathaṃ tarhi
sviṣṭakṛdādiyāgaḥ ? atyaktatvāccheṣasya vacanāccopapadyate ।
﻿<pb n="b852"/>
nanu ca dānamapi vacanādbhaviṣyati । satyam---yadi vacanamasti ।
ta tvatra dānaṃ śrūyate tādarthyaśrutistūpakārādapyupapadyata evetyupa-
kāro darśitaḥ । śeṣabhāvastu viparīta evetyanavada‍yam ।</p>
<trailer>iti bṛhatyāṃ tṛtīyasyādhyāyasya caturthaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>
﻿<pb n="b853"/>
</section>
<section>
<head>tṛtīyādhyāyasya pañcamaḥ pādaḥ ।।</head>
<ab type="sutra" n="1">।। 1 ।। ājyācca sarvasaṃyogāta1 ।। 3-5-1 ।।</ab>
<p>yāvaddhaviḥ kiñciccoditaṃ sarvasmāccheṣādavadyatīti sthitam ।
upāṃśuyāje saṃśayaḥ---kiṃ dhruvāsthādaviśeṣādaṅgapradhānasādhāraṇādana-
vadeyaṃ sviṣṭakṛte utāṅgapradhānaśeṣamapi pradhānaśeṣamityavadeyaṃ gṛhītā-
dvā jauhavāt camasavat । aviśeṣādavadeyamiti prāpte । na sādhāraṇe,
śeṣatvābhāvāt । śiṣṭamapi hi tatsādhāraṇameva । pradhānaśeṣācca
sviṣṭakṛdavadānam । na ca tatkevalapradhānaśeṣa iti śakyate vak‍tuṃ
﻿<pb n="b854"/>
sādhāraṇatvādeva । yat‍tu gṛhītasyaiva pratipattiścamasavaditi
tadayuk‍taṃ, caturavattaṃ juhotīti śravaṇāt śeṣayitavye pramāṇābhāvāt ।
sviṣṭakṛdavadānavacanameva pramāṇamiti cenna । aprayuk‍te śeṣe'rtha-
vatvāt । yat‍tu camasavadityuk‍taṃ, tanna । anuvaṣaṭkāraśruterananya-
viṣayatvāt (na sviṣṭakṛdavadānam । na ca tatpradhānaśeṣa iti
śakyateṃ vak‍tum) camasasya grahaṇamātraśruteḥ । darśanaṃ pratyuktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="13">।। 2 ।। sākaṃ prasthāyye sviṣṭakṛdiḍaṃ ca tadvat1 ।। 13 ।।</ab>
<p>kena viśeṣeṇāyamatideśaḥ ? prakṛtivaditi
prāpteḥ kāryārthatayā śeṣaṃ manyate pūrvapakṣavādī ।
﻿<pb n="b855"/>
vacanāt kāryaṃ balavaditi rāddhāntaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="14">।। 3 ।। sautrāmaṇyāṃ ca graheṣu1 ।। 14 ।।</ab>
<p>sautrāmaṇyāṃ <q>‘ucchinaṣṭi na sarvahutaṃ juhoti’</q> iti punarapi
śeṣāśaṅkāyāṃ sviṣṭakṛdi़ḍaṃ manyate pūrvapakṣavādī । tasyānyatra
viniyogāditi rāddhāntaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="16">।। 4 ।। 2dravyaikatve karmabhedāt pratikarma kriyeran ।। 16 ।।</ab>
<p>sarvapṛṣṭhe tu pratipradhānaṃ śeṣasaṃskārādāvṛttiṃ manyate ।
﻿<pb n="b856"/>
agṛhyamāṇaviśeṣatayā kṛtaḥ śāstrārtha iti rāddhāntaḥ । nanu
sādhāraṇe naiva sviṣṭakṛdastītyuktam । satyaṃ, akṛtatvātkāryāntarāṇāṃ
guṇaprādhānyācceti viśeṣaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="18">।। 35 ।। aindravāyave tu vacanāt pratikarma bhakṣaḥ syāt1 ।। 18 ।।</ab>
<p>nanu cātra pūrvapakṣa eva nāsti vacanāt ।
na hi pūrvapakṣe vacanasyānyārthatā śakyate vak‍tum ।
atocyate । ayamabhiprāyaḥ pūrvapakṣavādinaḥ somasaṃskārārtha-
tvādbhakṣasya dviriti prayogāntarāpekṣo'nuvādo bhaviṣyati ।
﻿<pb n="b857"/>
rāddhāntavādī tu vacanātkāryakalpaneti vacanādityuktavān ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="19">।। 6 ।। 1some'vacanādbhakṣo na vidyate ।। 19 ।।</ab>
<p>some śeṣabhakṣo'sti nāstīti saṃśayaḥ । nanu saṃśaya
evāyamayuktaḥ somasya śeṣabhāvāt । yuktaṃ puroḍāśādīnāṃ
dvirhaviṣo'vadyati iti vacanāt tatra yāgopasaṃhārāt śeṣavattvam
tasya ca bhakṣaḥ । iha tu tadabhāvāt bhakṣaśaṅkaiva nāsti । kathaṃ
tarhi vacanānyetāni <q>‘ dviraindravāyavasya bhakṣayati’</q> <q>‘sarvataḥ parihāramā-
śvinaṃ’</q> <q>‘anuvaṣaṭa‍karoti’</q> iti ca । atrāpi ca bhavāneva praṣṭavyaḥ atha
vā bhavantvarthakarmāṇi । kathaṃ tarhi <q>‘aindravāyavasya’</q> ‘āśvinaṃ iti ca ।
﻿<pb n="b858"/>
taddharmalakṣaṇārtho bhaviṣyati । tasmādanupapannamevedaṃ somebhakṣo-
vidyate uta neti । athaitebhyo'pi vacanebhyaḥ śeṣayitavyaṃ
iti kalpyate । na, aprayojakatvāccheṣāṇām । saṃskāryapradhānaṃ hi
saṃskārakarma bhavati । na cāpradhānaṃ prayuṅk‍te । tasmāt vaktavyo'tra
nyāyaḥ । ucyateḥ---nātra sarvahome pramāṇamasti । aindravāyavādiṣu
hi tādarthyena grahaṇam । gṛhītasyaikadeśenāpi kṛte kṛtaivaindravāyavatā,
kimiti sarvasya homaḥ । nanu ca sarvasya yāgārthatā śrūyate <q>‘somena
yajeta’</q> iti । tatrāpi ekedeśainaiva somenetyupapannatvāt । tathā
﻿<pb n="b859"/>
ca asya grahaṇaṃ ṛjīṣādeśca tyāgaḥ । yadyevaṃ kimiti <q>‘dvirhaviṣo-
'vadyati’</q> ityetasmādevopasaṃhāraḥ । yathakathaṃcit tatrāpyupasaṃhāra-
siddheḥ । niyamārthaṃ taditi cet । sarvapradānaṃ tarhi pūrvapakṣavādino na
ghaṭate kiñca ekadeśenāpyupapadyata iti naitāvatā sarvaṃ na hotavyam ।
sarvahomenāpyupapadyata eva । tasmādvaktavyo viśeṣaḥ ।</p>
<p>ayamabhidhīyate---kṛte śāstrārthe punaḥ karaṇaṃ tāvanna vidyate । eka-
deśena kṛtaḥ śāstrārtha iti pradarśitam । kathaṃ tarhi sarvapradānāśaṅkā ?
﻿<pb n="b860"/>
avakhaṇḍyāvakhaṇḍyadātavyamiti vacanārthavagamāt । na yāgārtha-
tvāt dravyasyetyupasaṃhāraḥ । ataḥ ekadeśena niyama evāyam ।
ata eva laukikāḥ pāyasādi devatoddeśena kṛtvā tata uda‍dhṛtya
kiñcit devatoddeśena tyak‍tvā śeṣaṃ yatheṣṭaṃ viniyuñjate । tasmā-
dupapadyate saṃśayaḥ---kiṃ bhakṣaṇenaiva śeṣapratipattiḥ uta neti । vacanā-
bhāvāt na bhakṣaṇeneti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । bhakṣaṇaviśeṣavidhānāt astīti
dvitīyaḥ । anyathā hi viśeṣavidhānaṃ nopapadyate । yadi viśeṣavidhānaṃ
nopapadyate kāmaṃ mopapādi, na punarvacanādṛte bhakṣaḥ śakyate pratipat‍tum
yadā bhakṣayati tadā dviriti evamevopapatteḥ, evaṃ tarhi tānyeva
vacanānīti rāddhāntaḥ yāvadvacanaṃ vacanam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b861"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="22">।।7।। 1camaseṣu samākhyānāt saṃyogasya tannimittatvāt ।। 22 ।।</ab>
<p>camaseṣu idānīṃ vacanābhāvānnāstīti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । taccamasa-
taivānyathā nopapadyate । ayamasya camasa iti vacanaṃ yathaiva viśeṣa-
vidhānamanyathā nopapadyata iti pūrvatra । dravyāntaracamanaṃ takṣaṇādi
ca na kalpanāmarhati iti pradarśitaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="8">।। 8 ।। udgāṃtṛcamasamekasya śrutisaṃyogāt2 ।। 8 ।।</ab>
﻿<pb n="b862"/>
<p>prodgāṃtṝṇāmityatra kiṃ punaḥ kāraṇaṃ na gānaṃ lakṣayati samā-
khyaiva kimiti lakṣayati ? ucchabdasyāvivakṣā prāpnoti gānakāriṣu
lakṣyamāṇeṣu । tathā ca darśitam---anyadeva gānaṃ anyadevodgānamiti ।
samākhyāne tu nāyaṃ doṣaḥ । nanu codgānaṃ nāma gānameva nāsti
﻿<pb n="b863"/>
bhaktirhi sā । sā codgīthavācyā । yaḥ punarudgāyedityeva-
mādiṣu prayogaḥ udgīthaṃ gāyediti tatrārthaḥ । ucchabdo hi
tatra bhaktilakṣaṇārthaḥ । gānaṃ tu gānameva । tasmādudgātetyṛ-
tvigviśeṣanāmaivaitat । na punaḥ udgānasya kartā udgātā । ata
eva samākhyaivātra lakṣayituṃ prabhavati na gānakriyeti rāddhāntitam ।
ata eva apasubrahmaṇyavādino'pi apanyāyavādina eva । nātra
﻿<pb n="b864"/>
stutyādiśravaṇamiva saṅkocakapramāṇamasti । nanu prodgātṝṇāmiti
triṣveva bahuvacanopapatteḥ kimiti samubrahmaṇyānāṃ bhakṣa iti ?
yadi bahuvacanopapattyarthaṃ satyameva । atrodgātṛśabdaḥ tadarthakāriṣu
vartata ityuktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="27">।। 9 ।। grāvastuto bhakṣo na vidyate'nāmnānāt1 ।। 27 ।।</ab>
<p>uk‍taṃ vacanāt samākhyānācca bhakṣaṇam । idānīṃ vacanārtha-
vipratipattau sampratipattyarthametānyadhikaraṇānyārabhyante । sarve hāri-
yojanasyānte lipsinta iti camasināmeveti pūrvapakṣa-
﻿<pb n="b865"/>
vādinā śaṅkitam । vākyaśeṣāt । asandigdhatvāt prakṛta-
vacanatayā sarvaśabdasya nopaṃsahāro yukto vākyaśeṣāditi rāddhāntaḥ
pakṣaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="31">।। 10 ।। vaṣa‍ṭakārācca bhakṣayet1 ।। 31 ।।</ab>
<p>atra vaṣaṭa‍kartuḥ prathamabhakṣa iti guṇaśravaṇāt na bhakṣa-
vidhānamiti āśaṅkya viśiṣṭavidhānāditi rāddhāntaḥ । nanu
cātra viśiṣṭavidhānaṃ nāsti । na hi prāthamyaṃ nāma bhakṣaṇasya
kārakaṃ yena yāgaviśiṣṭā kriyā vidhīyeta ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b866"/>
<p>ata eva pūrvapakṣavādī na viśiṣṭavidhānamatra saṃbhavatītyāśaṅkatavān ।
kathaṃ tarhi rāddhāntaḥ? prathamabhakṣa iti padadvayasya caikārthyābhidhā-
nāt abhihitavidhānāccaikārthyaṃ manyate । tadayuktam ।
samāsepi hi tada‍bhūtādhikaraṇanyāyāt apagatirnāsti । satya-
mevaṃ, tathāpi pūrvottarapadasaṃbandhāyattā samāse ca padārthāntarasaṅgatiḥ
﻿<pb n="b867"/>
iti yuktamuk‍taṃ samāse ca vidadhato nānekaguṇavidhānaṃ duṣkara-
mityataḥ siddhamatna viśiṣṭavidhānam।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="32">।। 11 ।। hāmābhiṣavābhyāṃ ca1।। 32 ।।</ab>
<p>abhiṣutya hutvā bhakṣayati ityapi bhakṣavidhānam। homābhiṣavayoḥ
prāptatvāt।</p>
﻿<pb n="b868"/>
<p>aṅgatayā ca vidhānānupapatterbhakṣa eva vidhātavyaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="33">।। 12 ।। pratyakṣopadeśāccamasānāmavyak‍taśśeṣe1 ।। 33 ।।</ab>
<p>hotṛcamasa ityevamādyābhiḥ śrutibhiḥ samākhyābhiḥ sakala-
camasasaṃbandhāvagateḥ abhiṣutya hutvetyanyatra camasebhyo bhakṣa iti
manyate । evaṃ prāpte ucyate । abhiṣavahomanimitto bhakṣaścamaseṣu
bhavatyeva । nanu ca hotṛcamasa iti sakalacamasāvagatirityuktam ।
satyamuk‍taṃ na punarabhiṣavanimittatāṃ bādhitumarhati । prāpakāṇyetāni
vacanāni na hotṛcamasa ityasyāṃ saṃbandhāvagatau saṃbandhāntaranivṛttiḥ
śakyate'vagantum । prāptimātrāvagateḥ । prāptau hi satyāṃ kasye-
damiti vivakṣāyāṃ anyanivṛttiḥ pratīyate । yathā āgneya ityuk‍te
﻿<pb n="b869"/>
naindrāgnasyāvagatiḥ । iha punaḥ prāptiphalatvādvākyasya nānyanivṛttiḥ
śakyate'vagantum । nanu ca prāptāvapi sakalāvagatervirodho vidyata
eva । satyaṃ yadi samākhyayā prāptiḥ iha punaḥ praituhotuścamasaḥ iti
vacanāt । kalpyaṃ caitat abhiṣutya hutvetyanena ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="36">।। 13 ।। ekapātre kramādadhvaryuḥ pūrvo bhakṣayet1 ।। 36 ।।</ab>
<p>sthitaṃ camasino'bhiṣotāro hotāraśca bhakṣayanti iti ।
atredānīṃ kaḥ prathamaṃ bhakṣayediti vicāryate । adhvaryuḥ
bhakṣayati hastagatatvāt yasya haste sa jayatīti nyāyāt ।
﻿<pb n="b870"/>
nanu vaṣaṭa‍kartuḥ prathamabhakṣa iti । vacanāt kathamadhvaryorbhakṣaḥ ? bhakṣa-
mātravidhānādapi vaṣaṭa‍kartureva prathamaṃ bhakṣa iti manvānasya
punaridamadhikaraṇam । pradarśitaṃ ca prāthamyādvaṣaṭa‍kārasyeti । vaca-
nāccetyupasaṃhṛtam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="40">।। 14 ।। vacanādanujñātabhakṣaṇam1 ।। 40 ।।</ab>
<p>kiṃ anujñātetaiva bhakṣayitavyaṃ uta ananujñāteneti prāptidarśa-
nārthamidamadhikaraṇam । asati vacane'niyamaḥ । vacanāt‍tu niyama
﻿<pb n="b871"/>
eva । niyame sati kiṃ laukikena śabdenānujñāpanaṃ uta vaidikeneti ।
mantrānāmnānāt vaidikeneti niyamaḥ । idamapi mantraprāpti-
darśanārthameva ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="42">।। 15 ।। tatrārthāt prativacanam1 ।। 42 ।।</ab>
<p>idānīṃ prativacane saṃśayaḥ kiṃ mantreṇa prativacanaṃ uta lauki-
kena śabdeneti । kathaṃ punarupahūta iti mantrāmnānāt sandehaḥ
upahrayasvetyasyaiva śeṣaṃ manvānasya । na hyanujñāpanāt pūrvapaṭhitaṃ
prativacanasamarthamapi prativacanāyālaṃ bhavatītyabhiprāyaḥ । rāddhānta-
vādī tu pūrvataivātra bādhyata iti rāddhāntitavān ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b872"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="43">।। 16 ।। tadekapātrāṇāṃ samavāyāt1 ।। 43 ।।</ab>
<p>paṭhite jñāpane prativacane ca kimekapātrāṇāmevānujñāpanaṃ utā-
viśeṣeṇeti । avidhānādaviśeṣaṃ manyate pūrvapakṣavādī । dṛṣṭārtha-
tayā tu rāddhāntaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="44">।। 17 ।।yājyāpanayanenāpanīto bhakṣaḥ pravaravat2 ।। 44 ।।</ab>
<p>yājyāmātrāpanayanaṃ manvānasya pūrvapakṣavādino hotureva bhakṣa
ityabhiprāyaḥ । kimanavānaśrutiḥ niṣadya yajatītivat vacanaṃ na
paśyati । na na paśyati, yājyāmātre । evametada‍dvayamapyupapadyata
﻿<pb n="b873"/>
ityabhiprāyaḥ । yājyābhidhānena yajeḥ kartṛtvamupapadyata ityarthaḥ ।
rāddhāntavādī tu manyate । satyamupapadyate na punarvaṣaṭa‍kārāpanaye kiñcana
pramāṇamasti iti savaṣaṭa‍kārameva yājyāprayogamātrepyupapadyata iti
vyāpāramaṅgīkṛtya kartṛtvaṃ yuktamiti । yat‍tu pravaro nāpanīyata iti
tadatraupadeśikatvāt yathā pravaro nāpanīyate tathā pradarśitam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="47">।। 18 ।। phalacamaso naimittiko bhakṣavikāraḥ śrutisaṃyogāt ।। 47 ।।</ab>
<p>kiṃ phalacamaso bhakṣavikāra utejyāvikāra iti । asmin
saṃśaye brūmaḥ naivātra saṃśayaḥ tamasmaibhakṣaṃ prayacchet iti bhakṣasaṃba-
﻿<pb n="b874"/>
ndhitvena vidhānāt । bhakṣe somaṃ vikāroti na yāge । na ca
yāgavikāraḥ śakyate vak‍tum । utpattiśiṣṭatvāt somasya ।
vidhīyamāne tu karmāntarāpattiḥ । tataśca bhakṣavikāro'pi na syāt
dūre ijyāvikāratā । atrābhidhīyate---nejyāvikāramantareṇa bhakṣaṃ
vikartuṃ samarthaḥ phalacamasaḥ । ijyāśeṣasya hi somasya bhakṣaḥ । na
cāśeṣabhūte bhakṣyamāṇe sa vikṛto bhavati । tasmādijyāśeṣataiva phala-
camasasyāpi mantavyā । nanu cotpattiśiṣṭatvāt somasya yāge vidhānaṃ
na saṃbhavatītyuktam । yāgānuvādena vidhāne hi apratyabhijñāna-
﻿<pb n="b875"/>
muktam । na punaḥ kāryeṇāpi saṃbandhe । kāryata evāyaṃ saṃbandhaḥ ।
nanu ca bhāṣyakāreṇa yāgasaṃbandhābhāvaṃ codayitvā yāja-
yediti saṃbandha uktaḥ yajinā । yāgānvayapradarśanārthaṃ taduktam
na punaranūdya vidhānāyetyadoṣaḥ । bhakṣaṃ kuryāditi copasaṃhāraḥ
imamevārthaṃ prakaṭīkaroti । tasmādijyāvikāraḥ phalacamasa iti
siddham । guṇavidhānāni ca pradarśitāni ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="52">।। 20 ।। anuprasarpiṣu sāmānyāt1 ।। 52 ।।</ab>
<p>daśadaśa ekaikaṃ camasamanuprasarpantīti vidhānāt śataṃ brāhmaṇāḥ
somān bhakṣayantītyanuvādaṃ manvānasya nābhakṣo rājeti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b876"/>
satyamevaṃ yadyanuvādaḥ syāt । na cānuvṛtte rājani anuvādaḥ
śakyate vak‍tum । ayathārthānuvādaprasaṅgāt । nanu cānuvāde
ayathārthatvaṃ adoṣaḥ bhūyastvena lakṣaṇā bhaviṣyati । satyaṃ yadye-
kāntato'nuvādaḥ iha punarvidheyatayāpyupapadyata eveti nāyathārthatvaṃ
śakyate । tasmāt dvayamapyetadvidhīyate śataṃ brāhmaṇāḥ daśa ekaikaṃ
camasaṃ iti ca । nanu ca <q>‘samaṃ syādaśrutatvāt’</q> iti nyāyena śate
vibhajyamāne ekaikatra daśadaśaprāpteḥ daśa daśa ekaikaṃ camasamanu-
prasarpanti ityanuvādaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b877"/>
<p>na ekaikatra śataprāpteḥ pratyuddeśaṃ vākyasamāpteḥ । tasmāda-
bhakṣo rājā brāhmaṇavidhānāditi । yatpunaratra śataṃ brāhmaṇāssomān
ityanekārthavidhānaṃ manyate, tadayuktaṃ, yasmāt karmāntaravidhānenāpi
prākṛtakāryārthatāṃ daśame vakṣyāmaḥ ।</p>
<trailer>iti bṛhatyāṃ tṛtīyasya
pañcamaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>
﻿<pb n="b878"/>
</section>
<section>
<head>bṛhatyāṃ</head>
</section>
<section>
<head>tṛtīyādhyāyasya ṣaṣṭhaḥ pādaḥ ।।</head>
<ab type="sutra" n="1">।। 1 ।। sarvārthamaprakaraṇāt1 ।। 1 ।।</ab>
<p>kiṃ punaratra kāraṇaṃ pakṣadvayopanyāsasya । kasya pakṣadvayopanyā-
sasya ? । codakādanārabhyavidhiḥ balīyān sāmānyatodṛṣṭatvācceti ।
prathamasya tāvatpakṣasya idaṃ prayojanaṃ naivātra dviruktatā vidyate ।
upadeśātideśābhyāṃ prakṛtivikṛtyoḥ sruksaṃbhavān । evaṃ tarhi
sāmānyato darśanena prakṛtyarthateti । aparasya pakṣasyopanyāsaḥ prāya-
﻿<pb n="b879"/>
darśanavat । ayaṃ tāvadanantaraḥ pakṣo nirākriyate । na sāmā-
nyato dṛṣṭaṃ śabdārthāvagatau hetuḥ । nāpi prāyadarśanam ।
prakṛtāviva vikṛtāvapi saṃkṣepavistāropadeśadarśanāt । idānī-
maparasya pakṣasya nirasanaṃ codakāpekṣaścet anārabhya vidhiḥ ।
prakṛtau pūrvamupadeśo'pekṣaṇīyaḥ upadeśāpekṣatvādatideśasya ।
upadeśena cedupasaṃhṛto'nārabhyavidhiḥ nātideśamapekṣate ।
﻿<pb n="b880"/>
kāryata eva vikṛtau prāptatvāt । ato dviruktatā'saṃbhavāt advirukta-
tvāditi sthito hetuḥ । yastu yāgasaṃbandhopanyāsaḥ1 asāvavaśyaṃ
bhāvī codaka iti pradarśayitum । avaśyaṃbhāvitve cādviruktatvasya
siddhiruktā ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="1">।। 2 ।। prakaraṇaviśeṣāt‍tu vikṛtau virodhi syāt2 ।। 1 ।।</ab>
<p>nanu cānārabhyādhītaṃ sāptadaśyaṃ, yacca prakaraṇādhītaṃ
pāñcadaśyaṃ ubhayamapi śrutyaiva sāmidhenīsaṃbandhitayā
﻿<pb n="b881"/>
codyate । ko'ya prakaraṇopanyāsaḥ । naivātra(yotra) prakaraṇaṃ vini-
yojakaṃ yena prakaraṇavidhirbalīyān bhavati । athāyamabhiprāyaḥ
prakaraṇasavyapekṣā eva śrutyādayo viniyojakāḥ iti । satyaṃ grāha-
kalakṣaṇaprakaraṇasavyapekṣāḥ na tu viniyojakamapekṣante । grāhakasa-
vyapekṣā cānārabhyavidherapi tulyaiva । ato'trāpi dvirukterasaṃbhavāt
prakṛtāveveti yuktam ।</p>
<p>astyatra viśeṣaḥ । prakṛtatve hi pāñcadaśyasya grāhakapratyabhi-
jñānaṃ saṃbhavati । avyavāyāt । anārabhyavidheḥ punaḥ kāryato
grāhakāvamarśaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b882"/>
<p>evaṃ ca sati na klṛpte kalpanā saṃbhavati iti na prakṛtau
niveśaḥ । pratipattyavirodhinī hi kalpanā na pratipannopamardinī ।
tasmādvikṛtāvanārabhya vidhānamiti sūktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="10">।। 3 ।। naimittikaṃ tu prakṛtau tadvikāraḥ saṃyāgaviśeṣāta1 ।। 10 ।।</ab>
<p>kathaṃ punaratra pūrvapakṣāśaṅkā । itthamāśaṅkā kratvarthe bādhyamāne upa-
deśaḥ pīḍito bhavati । nacopadeśāśādṛte prakṛtau sāda‍guṇyāvagatirbhavati ।
﻿<pb n="b883"/>
vikṛtau punaḥ kāryata eva sāda‍guṇyāvagatiḥ ityekakārya-
tvāt puruṣārthenāpi kratoḥ sāda‍guṇyaṃ śakyate vak‍tuṃ kārya-
viśeṣāt । tasmāt puruṣārthānāṃ vikṛtau niveśaḥ । satyamevaṃ
yadi prakṛtāvapi kāryaviśeṣo na syāt । iha tu dṛṣṭārthatvādupadeśasya
tulyaḥ kāryaviśeṣaḥ । (kārya)viśeṣāvagamācca sāmānyato balīyastvaṃ
viśeṣopadeśasyeti prakṛtāveva niveśaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="11">।। 4 ।। iṣṭyarthamagnyādheyaṃ prakaraṇāt1 ।। 11 ।।</ab>
<p>kathaṃ punaratreṣṭeḥ prakaraṇaṃ ? iṣṭerapi naivādhikāraśrutirasti ।
﻿<pb n="b884"/>
ādhānasyaiva hi sādhikārasya vidheḥ prakaraṇam । tasmānneṣṭeḥ prakaraṇaṃ
iti śakyate vak‍tum । kathaṃ tarhi pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ? bhavato vā
ko'bhiprāyaḥ । na kiñcitpratibhāti । atrābhidhīyate---dvayamapya-
trodāharaṇam । kimādhānaṃ uteṣṭaya iti । dvayoḥ prādhānyamayukta-
miti manvānasya iṣṭeścāṅgabāhulyāt prādhānyāropeṇa pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।
rāddhāntastu dvayorapyadhikārābhāvāt । agnyarthatayā ca
viniyogopapatteḥ dvayoragnyarthatvam । tathā ca liṅgadarśanam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b885"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="14">।। 5 ।। tatprakṛtyarthaṃ yathā'nye'nārabhyavādāḥ ।। 14 ।।</ab>
<p>kimidānīṃ prakṛtyarthamādhānaṃ uta sarvārthamiti । etaduk‍taṃ
bhavati---kiṃ kratvarthanāmag‍nīnāmādhānaṃ uta āhitānāṃ kratvarthateti ।
kaścātra viśeṣaḥ ? ayamasti viśeṣaḥ---yadi kratvarthānāmādhānaṃ tataḥ
parṇamayītvavat prakṛtigāmitvamādhānavidheḥ । atha tu āhitānāṃ
kratvarthatā tadā homādimātraśeṣatayā'g‍nīnāṃ sarvārthamādhāna-
mityucyate । kiṃ punaratra yuktam ? parṇatādivat kratusaṃbandhānāmevāgrī-
nāmādhānamiti । āhitāg‍neradhikārāt āhitānāṃ kratvarthateti ।
﻿<pb n="b886"/>
yathā vā āhitāgnerādhikārastathā ṣaṣṭhe vakṣyāmaḥ । vasantādikāla-
vidhiścaivamupapanno bhaviṣyati ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="16">।। 6 ।। tāsāmagniḥ prakṛtitaḥ prayājavat1 ।। 16 ।।</ab>
<p>kathaṃ punaḥ pavamāneṣṭiṣu pavamāneṣṭisaṃskṛtā agnayaḥ āśaṅkya-
nte । yā api hi tāḥ agnyarthā iṣṭayaḥ tā api
pavamāneṣṭaya eva । tasmādanāśaṅkanīyamevedamāśaṅkitam । atrocyate
---idamevātra cintyate । kimayamatideśaḥ prakṛtau yāva-
dupakārakaṃ tāvadatidiśati uta yathākāryamatideśa iti ।
﻿<pb n="b887"/>
tatra pūrvapakṣavādino'bhiprāyaḥ । yāvadupakārakaṃ tāvadati-
diśatīti । rāddhāntavādī punaḥ yathākāryamati-
deśaḥ । upadeśetu viparītam । tasmānnaitadupadeśavad
draṣṭavyam । upadeśaviśeṣapradarśanārthaṃ caitadupadeśalakṣaṇe cintitam ।
﻿<pb n="b888"/>
anyathā hi anvārambhaṇīyādhikaraṇenaiva gatam syāt । agnyartha-
tayā ca pavamāneṣṭīnāṃ upadeśānyatve yatnaḥ iti viśeṣaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="18">।। 7 ।। tulyaḥ sarveṣāṃ paśuvidhiḥ prakaraṇāviśeṣāt1 ।। 18 ।।</ab>
<p>kathaṃ punaridamadhikaraṇaṃ prārabdham । yathaiva bhāṣyakāreṇa । na tathā
śakyate vak‍tum । tasmādyadi tāvadidaṃ jyotiṣṭomākhyaprakaraṇaṃ tadā
﻿<pb n="b889"/>
śrutyādībhireva paśuyāgasaṃbandhāt viśasanādīnām । kimidaṃ
prakaraṇaviśeṣāditi sarvārthatocyate । atha prakaraṇe aviśeṣaḥ
paśūnāmityaviśeṣatocyate kathaṃ tarhi sūtraṃ---asti tu prakaraṇe viśeṣa
iti । nacāvāntaraprakaraṇaṃ nāma kiñcidasti jyautiṣṭomikamahāprakaraṇe ।
prakaraṇāntare cābhyupagamyamāne('rthe) na tāvatprakaraṇamagrīṣomīyā-
derupapadyate । kimityeva hi tadā jyotiṣṭomasaṃbandho'bhyupagataḥ
syāt । evaṃ ca dīkṣaṇīyāderitikartavyatābhāva eva hīyeta ।
﻿<pb n="b890"/>
﻿<pb n="b891"/>
darśapūrṇamāsayośca prayājāderitikartavyatāprasaṅgaḥ prakaraṇaviniyo-
jyatayā ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b892"/>
<p>tataśca <q>‘avyaktāsu tu somasye’</q>ti somikī itikartavyatā
prāpnoti dīkṣaṇīyāderiva dārśapūrṇamāsikī । kimiti vā na bhavati ?
﻿<pb n="b893"/>
uktamavāntaraprakaraṇābhāvāditi । na hyekasmin prayogavacane
nānākimityāṅkṣā saṃbhavati । ekaścāyaṃ prayogavacanaḥ setikarta-
vyatākasya prayogasyaikaśabda‍yāditi vakṣyati ।</p>
<p>kathaṃ tarhi dīkṣaṇīyāderātideśikā dharmāḥ ? mā bhūvan,
na punaḥ kimityākāṅkṣādvayamekasmin prakaraṇe saṃbhavati ।
﻿<pb n="b894"/>
evaṃ sthite yadidamucyate prakaraṇātsavanīyasyeti sthānāccāgnīṣo-
mīyasyeti sarvamidamandhapadam । tasmāt mahatā prayat‍nenātra bhāṣyaṃ
vyākhyeyam । atrābhidhīyate---prakaraṇaṃ tāvadidaṃ jyotiṣ‍ṭomasya ।
aupavasathye'hani dharmāścodyante । na ca paśavastasminnahani sarve
sannihitāḥ sannihitavacanaṃ coddeśakaṃ padam । ataḥ kasyāyamuddeśaka
iti cintyate viśasanādividhiṣu । tatra prakaraṇāviśeṣāt sarve
paśavo jyotiṣṭomārthatayā prakṛtā iti sarvārthatāṃ manyate ।</p>
<p>apareṇa pūrvapakṣiṇā ahassāmānyasannidhānāt‍tu (sannikṛṣṭa iti)
sannidhiviśeṣo vidyata iti asti tu prakaraṇaviśeṣa ityuktam ।
﻿<pb n="b895"/>
prakṛtalakṣaṇaṃ ca prakaraṇamatrābhipretam । ataḥ sthānādag‍nīṣomīyasyeti
yuktam । (siddham) । aprakṛtasiddha‍yarthaṃ ca sautye'hani vidhānaṃ
savanīyasyetyevamāda‍yupapannam । nanu sannidhānaviśeṣeṇāg‍nīṣomī-
yārthatve siddhe jyotiṣṭomaprakaraṇe cāmnānasyārthavatve tasminneva
prakaraṇe paśudvayasyātideśaḥ । na hyekaḥ prayogavacanaḥ upadeśena
atideśena ca tāneva dharmān gṛhṇāti । asya codyasya parihāraṃ
atideśa eva vakṣyāmaḥ kṛts‍navidhānādapūrvaḥ soma ityatra । asmin
﻿<pb n="b896"/>
punaradhikaraṇe upadeśaviśeṣo nirūpitaḥ । upadeśaviśeṣatvāccheṣa-
lakṣaṇasya । kaḥ punaḥ aupavasathye'hani savanīyeṣu vidhīyamāneṣu
āśvinakāle vākyabhedaḥ? nanvidaṃ pūrvapakṣī codayati । kathaṃ ca
sautyehani savanīyeṣu vidhīyamāneṣu vākyabhedaṃ rāddhāntavādī
codayati । kiñca ubhayatra vākyabheda eva coditaḥ । ucyate ।
anekaguṇavidhānameva vākyabhedaṃ pūrvapakṣavādī manyate । rāddhānta-
vādyapi vapāpracāramātrotkarṣaṃ manvānaḥ punarālambhavidhāne ca vākya-
bhedameva coditavān । āg‍neyyaudāsīnyamuktavān ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b897"/>
<p>kiṃ punaranayorvākyabhedayordūṣaṇam । rāddhāntavāda‍yuktameva
dūṣaṇam । aparihāryaṃ hi tatra vākyāntaratvam । pūrvapakṣavāda‍yuktasya
tu viśiṣṭavidhānādapi siddhiḥ <q>“saṃskāro'yaṃ paśuyāgaprayuktaḥ
na jyotiṣṭomaprayukta”</q>1 iti । kimidaṃ jyotiṣṭomaprayuktaṃ iti ?
nanu ca sarvamevedaṃ jyotiṣṭomaprayuktam । tatprakaraṇāmnānāt ।
ucyate । viniyogābhipnāṃyo'yaṃ granthaḥ । na punaḥ prayojyābhiprāyaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b898"/>
na prakaraṇaviniyojyatayā prayuktiḥ(ityarthaḥ) । kiṃ tarhi ? śrutyaiva
viniyoga । <q>‘prakaraṇavantaśca’</q> iti । śaknoti hi svasthānepi
prayogavacanaḥ prayok‍tumiti darśayati । ata eva ca prakaraṇasthāne
api prakṛtābhiprāyeṇaivetyuktam । darśanācchidrāpidhāne pratyuk‍te ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="28">।। 8 ।। 1dohayoḥ kālabhedādasaṃyuk‍taṃ śrṛtaṃ syāt ।। 28 ।।</ab>
<p>pūrvavadatrāpi sannidhānaviśeṣamaṅgīkṛtya pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ।
﻿<pb n="b899"/>
rāddhāntastu naiva dadhipayasoḥ kālabhedena vidhānamasti । yadi paraṃ
krame kālabhedaḥ sa ca prakaraṇe pratyarthini na viniyojaka
ityuktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="30">।। 9 ।। 1tadvat savanāntare grahāmnānam ।। 30 ।।</ab>
<p>atrāpi pūrvavadeva sannidhānaviśeṣāśaṅkā pūrvapakṣavādinaḥ ।
rāddhāntastu na dharmāṇāṃ savanaviśeṣe vidhānamiti sarvārthatā ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b900"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="31">।। 10 ।। 1raśanā ca liṅgadarśanāt ।। 31 ।।</ab>
<p>raśanāyāstvagnīṣomīyaprakaraṇa2 eva vidhānamiti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।
rāddhāntastu satyaṃ tatprakrame vidhānaṃ yūpastveka iti sarvārthato raśanā-
yāstaddharmāṇāṃ ca । tathā ca liṅgamuktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="32">।। 11 ।। 3ārācchiṣṭamasaṃyuktamitaraissannidhānāt ।। 32 ।।</ab>
<p>aṃśvadābhyayostu prakaraṇe avidhānāt uddeśakasya ca sannihita-
vacanatvāt na taddharma iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । rāddhāntastu na sanni-
hitamātravacanamuddeśakaṃ prayojanavatsannihitavacanaṃ hi tat ।
﻿<pb n="b901"/>
abhinnaṃ cātna prayojanam । prakṛtānāmaprakṛtānāṃ ca grahaṇām । tasmāt
prayojanābhedāta prayojanāvacchinnagrahajātīye grahaśabdo na prakṛtatvena
saṅakocamarhati । maitrāvaruṇe tu nirdeśāt yuktam । iha tu viparīto
nirdeśa ityapi darśitam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="35">।। 12 ।। agnyarthamaprakaraṇe tadvat ।। 35 ।।</ab>
<p>kaḥ punaranayoradhikaraṇayorviśeṣaḥ ? ayamasti viśeṣaḥ ।
tatra hi ekadravyasaṃbandhitvād‍yukto viśeṣaḥ। iha punaḥ ekaikeṣṭakā-
vyāpārasaṃbandhitayāpi dharmavidhayo'rthavanto bhavanti । tadayuktam ।
﻿<pb n="b902"/>
tatrāpi hi ekaikagrahavyāpārabhedo vidyata eva । evaṃ tarhi citi-
bhedāt abhyadhikāśaṅkā । rāddhāntastu yadyapi citibhedaḥ tathāpi
citau dharmāṇāmapratiṣṭhitatvāt ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="36">।। 13 ।। naimittikamatulyatvādasamānavidhānaṃ syāt ।। 36 ।।</ab>
<p>idamidānīṃ cintyate---kiṃ naimittikānāṃ dharmavidhayaḥ samānā
uta kāryavanto bhavantīti । tatra tulyatvāt prakaraṇasya samānā dharma-
vidhaya iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । satyaṃ tulyaṃ prakaraṇam dharmavantastu nityāḥ
﻿<pb n="b903"/>
naimittikāśca godohanādayaḥ । tad‍dvāraṃ ca prakaraṇasya grāhakatvamiti
sthitam । naimittikaṃ ca nityakāryāpannaṃ bhavati । ataḥ kāryataḥ
siddheḥ na punarupadeśamarhati iti । dviruktatādoṣaścoktaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="37">।। 14 ।। pratinidhiśca tadvat ।। 37 ।।</ab>
<p>athedānīṃ pratinidhau kā vārtā । tatra kāryataḥ prāptiriti pūrva-
pakṣavādī manyate kāryeṇākṣipratvātpratinidheḥ । atrābhidhīyate---satyaṃ
kāryeṇākṣiptaḥ pratinidhiḥ upadeśasaṃpadā tulyaḥ, nānyasādhyatayā,
﻿<pb n="b904"/>
tasmādaupadeśika eva dharmasaṃbandhaḥ na kāryasādhanatayā dravyāntaraṃ
nīvārāḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="40">।। 15 ।। niyamārthā guṇaśratiḥ ।। 40 ।।</ab>
<p>yatra punaḥ śrūyate pratinidhiḥ tatra śrutāśaṅkatayā pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।
śrutopapattyartho'yaṃ niyama iti rāddhāntaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="41">।। 16 ।। saṃsthāstu samānavidhānāḥ prakaraṇāviśeṣāt ।। 41 ।।</ab>
<p>nanu cedaṃ phalacamasena gatamevādhikaraṇam । na naimitti-
kasya dharmā bhavantyupadeśata iti । ucyate---astyatrādhikā---
﻿<pb n="b905"/>
śaṅkā । kā punarasau ? iyamasau । ukthyādayo hi grahaṇa-
viśeṣāḥ । te ca saṃskārāḥ svayamitikartavyatābhūtāḥ na ceti-
kartavyatā itikartavyatayā saṃbadhyate । kiṃ tarhi ? yāgena ।
﻿<pb n="b906"/>
sarvagrahaṇasaṃskāryadravyakaścāyaṃ sa eva yāgaḥ somena
yajeteti । nānyotpattirvidyate । sa cedyāgaḥ grahaṇāntare-
ṣvapi itikartavyatāpi saiva । na ca grahaṇaviśeṣo
yāgasyetikartavyatāprāptau nimittaṃ; kiṃ tarhi prayoga-
codanaiva । na ca grahaṇāntareṣu prayogāntaracodanā yāgasya ।
guṇānāmeva hi tatra phalāya codanā na yāgasya, yathā
godohanena paśukāmasya praṇayediti na darśapūrṇamāsayoḥ
﻿<pb n="b907"/>
prayogaścodyate । tasmādbhavantu grahaṇāni grahaṇadharmopadeśaśūnyāni phala-
camasavat na punaryāgo'pi yāgadharmaśūnya iti śakyate vak‍tum । 
sarvasaṃskāreṣvekaprayogasya coditatvāt । prayogagrāhyatvācceti-
kartavyatāyā ityuktam । ata eva cāgniṣṭomagrahaṇaṃ samuccayaśca
pradarśitaḥ । paśūnāmadṛṣṭārthatayā samuccaya eva nyāyyaḥ । atrocyate
-savanīyasamākhyayā sarvapaśūnāṃ tulyakāryāvagamāt । atrābhidhīyate
---satyamevaṃ syādyadi saṃsthantāreṣu ukthyādiṣu prayogacodanayaiva
labhyate । yathā godohanena darśapūrṇamāsayoḥ । iha tu agniṣṭoma-
﻿<pb n="b908"/>
paryantaiva yāgasya prayogacodanā । ata ūrdhvaṃ grahā ukthyādaya
eva codanāmākṣipanti yathā grahāḥ āvṛttim nimitte । evaṃ
cenna yāgacodanayā dharmāḥ śakyante grahītuṃ ukthyādiṣu । ataḥ
phalacamasavat nityānityasaṃyogavirodho yuktaḥ । kāryataśca dharmaprāptiḥ
tasmāt samuccayagrahaṇaṃ vacanāt bhaviṣyati । agniṣṭomaśabdaścānu-
vādaḥ । tathā homādīnāmabhāvadarśanamupapannaṃ bhavati ।</p> 
<trailer>iti bṛhatyāṃ tṛtīyādhyāyasya
ṣaṣṭaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>
<pb n="b909"/>
﻿<pb n="b910"/>
</section>
<section>
<head>tṛtīyādhyāyasya saptamaḥ pādaḥ ।।</head>
<ab type="sutra" n="1">।। 1 ।। prakaraṇāviśeṣādasaṃyuk‍taṃ pradhānasya ।। 1 ।।</ab>
<p>barhirdharmāśca kimaṅgapradhānārthā uta pradhānārthā eveti sandehe
prakaraṇāt pradhānārthā ityuk‍tvā upakārakatvenāṅgapradhānārthatāmāha ।
tadayuktam । śrutyādimirhi tādarthyamavagamyate nopakāreṇa ।</p>
<p>ucyate---śrutyādaya evopanyastā barhiṣi havīṃṣyāsādayatīti ।
upakārakagrahaṇaṃ tarhi kimarthaṃ ? kadācit tadabhāvāt śruteḥ saṅkocaḥ
syāt । asti cāsāvekarūpa upakāro nāmeti tadabhidhānam ।
﻿<pb n="b911"/>
evaṃ tarhi vākyenaiva śeṣāvagatiḥ । kimiti tarhi barhirmātre(ṇa)
na bhavati ? grāhakatve sati śeṣatvamityuktam । grāhakaśca dārśapaurṇa-
māsikaprayogavidhiḥ sannidhānāt । liṅgadarśanamuktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="2">।। 2 ।। phalasaṃyogātsvāmiyuktaṃ pradhānasya 2 ।। 2 ।।</ab>
<p>iha purūṣasaṃskārā udāharaṇam । te kiṃ karkṛbhūtasya utādhi-
kṛtasyeti । kartṛbhūtasya । evaṃ karmāṅgatopapadyata iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b912"/>
kimityaṃśopanipātinī itikartavyateti saptamādye vakṣyāmaḥ ।
ākāṅkṣādvayasya tatprasūteḥ । tatra yadarthaḥ kartṛbhāvaḥ saṃskāro'pi
tadartha eva yuktaḥ । adhikāraniṣpattyarthatvācchāstrasya । tasmādadhi-
kṛtasyasaṃskāra iti yuktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="7">।। 3 ।।cikīrṣayā ca saṃyogāt1 ।। 7 ।।</ab>
<p>barhirdharmādhikaraṇena kimatrānyatvaṃ yenedamādhikaraṇamārabhyate ।
﻿<pb n="b913"/>
pradhānacikīrṣāṃ dhurvapakṣavādī manyate । yadarthā cikīrṣā tadarthā-
nyaṅgānītyabhiprāyaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="8">।। 4 ।। tathābhidhānena1 ।। 8 ।।</ab>
<p>abhimarśane tu sākṣātpradhānaśabdasaṃyogāt pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । satyaṃ,
pradhānaṃ cikīrṣyate । tat‍tu sāṅgaṃ adhikāranirvṛttāviti rāddhāntaḥ ।
evamabhimarśanamapi adhikārasādhanasyaiveti ubhayoraṅgapradhānārthatā ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b914"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="5">।। 6 ।। dīkṣādakṣiṇaṃ tu vacanātpradhānesya1 ।। 11 ।।</ab>
<p>dīkṣādakṣiṇamapi sāṅgādadhikāranirvṛt‍teḥ sāṅgasyetyāśaṅkya
vacanātpradhānasyeti rāddhāntaḥ । yuk‍taṃ tāvat vacanāt dīkṣā
prādhānasya । dakṣiṇā punaḥ yadā pradhānasyaiva kathamapi tadā
kathamaparikrītairaṅgāni kriyante । kena vok‍tamaparikrītairaṅgāni kriyanta
iti prākṛtamānatikāraṇaṃ bhaviṣyatyeva । yadyevaṃ na tarhi prasaṅgaḥ ।
yathā prasaṅgaḥ tathā prasaṅgalakṣaṇa eva vakṣyāmaḥ । darśanamuk‍tam ।</p> 
<ab type="sutra" n="13">।। 6 ।। tathā yūpasya vediḥ2 ।। 13 ।।</ab>
<p>ardhamantarvedīti kiṃ vediḥ yūpāṅgamuta neti saṃśaye
﻿<pb n="b915"/>
śruteraṅgamiti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । bahirvedipadaikavākyatvāt na śrutyartha-
vidhānaṃ saṃbhavatīti deśalakṣaṇā । ubhayavidhāne vākyabheda-
prasaṅgāt ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="15">sāmidhenīstadanvāhuriti havirdhānayorvacanātsāmidhenīnām1 ।। 15 ।।</ab>
<p>kaḥ punaḥ pūrveṇāsyādhikaraṇasya viśeṣaḥ ? ayamasti viśeṣaḥ
padāntarāsaṃbaddhaṃ hyatra havirdhānaṃ śrūyate nāntarvedivat bahirvedipada-
saṃbaddham । tasmādaṅgāṅgibhāva iti pūrvapakṣavādī manyate śruteḥ
﻿<pb n="b916"/>
vijñānaviparītaṃ hi virūddhamabhidhīyate । rāddhāntavādītu ubhayo---
ranyārthatvāt deśalakṣaṇasaṃbandha eva nyāyya iti manyate । tathā
ca <q>‘havirdhānaṃ’</q> <q>‘sāmidhenya’</q> iti ca samākhyāpi na pīḍitā syāt ।
anyathāhi havirdhānaṃ sāmidhenīnāṃ sāmidhenyo vā havirdhānasyeti
devadattasyedaṃ yajñadattasyeti yathaitadasaṃbaddhaṃ tathedamapi syāt । tasmāda-
trāpi pūrvavat deśaviśeṣalakṣaṇaiveti yuktam । āgneyyadhikaraṇavacca
sāmānyaviśeṣasaṃbandhe vākyabhedaḥ syāt ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="18">śāstraphalaṃ prayok‍tari tallakṣaṇatvāt tasmātsvayaṃ prayoge syāt1 ।। 18 ।।</ab>
<p>kathaṃ punaratra parikrayādiṣu śrūyamāṇeṣu saṃśayaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b917"/>
ayamabhiprāyaḥ kartṛgāmikriyāphalamatra śrūyate । atastadvirodhāt
gauṇaṃ adṛṣṭārthaṃ vaha manyate । kathaṃ tarhi samākhyāḥ ādhvaryavamityeva-
mādyāḥ ? granthasaṃyogādupapannā bhaviṣyanti । tasmātsvayaṃ kartṛ-
taiva nyāyyeti pūrvapakṣavādī manyate । aniyamavādī tu parīkrītairapi
kriyamāṇaṃ tenaiva kṛtaṃ bhavati । sa hi teṣāṃ prayoktā । prayok‍tuśca
kartṛtvasmaraṇam । na punarāhatyaiva kartṛtvam । utsargastu svadravya-
tyāgalakṣaṇatvāt svayameva kartavyaḥ । evaṃ kartṛtve upapanne na
parikrayasya gauṇatā, adṛṣṭārthatā vā kalpayituṃ śakyate । samā-
﻿<pb n="b918"/>
khyāśca mukhyārthāḥ na granthadvārikāḥ kalpitā bhaviṣyanti । na hi
adhyetāro'dhvaryuśabdavācyāḥ adhyayanakāle । kathaṃ punaraniyamaṃ
manyate । ayamabhiprāyaḥ yadā svayamanutsāhī tadā parikrayaḥ yadāsau
parikrayaḥ tadā anyaireveti manyate । rāddhāntavādī tu manyate
nityavadānnānāt parikrayasya yadā svayaṃ na śak‍nuyāt tadā
parikrayeṇeti na śakyate kalpayitum । nanu ca sāmarthyādbhaviṣyati
lokavata । na hi śrutau pratyarthinyāṃ sāmarthyaṃ prabhavatītyuktam ।
loke tu dṛṣṭārthatvāt yathārthamiti yuktam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b919"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="9">।। 9 ।। 1tatrārthāt kartṛparimāṇaṃ syodaniyamo'viśeṣāt ।। 21 ।।</ab>
<p>evaṃ sthite parikrītakartṛtve anyatrotsargāt aniyamaṃ
saṅkhyāyāḥ pūrvapakṣavādī manyate । ekasminnapi samākhyāvaraṇayo-
rupapatteḥ । rāddhāntavādī tu utpattau tāvat samākhyāto bhedaṃ manvānaḥ
na punareka eva saṃjñī । codanāvagamyatvāt saṃjñānām, codanā-
bhedācca yāvaccodanaṃ saṃjñibhedaniyamamuktavān । evaṃ darśapūrṇamā-
sādiṣvapītyuktam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b920"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="25">।। 10 ।। 1camasādhvaryavaśca tairvyapadeśāt ।। 25 ।।</ab>
<p>camasādhvaryavaśca kiṃ ṛtviksaṅkhyāsaṅkhyeyāḥ uta saṅkhyāntara
paricthedyāḥ । nanu ca hotṛkāṇāṃ camasādhvaryava iti vyapadeśāt
anyairbhavitavyam । parasparavyapadeśādapyetadupapadyata iti pūrvaḥ
pakṣaḥ । na hi ṣaṣṭha‍yantānāṃ parasparasaṃbandho vidyata iti rāddhāntavādī
vyatirik‍taṃ manyate । utpattau ca saṃjñābhedāt । tasmādanye te
iti ।</p> 
<ab type="sutra" n=" ">।। 11 ।। 2utpattau ca bahuśruteḥ ।।</ab>
<p>idamidānīṃ sandihyate---kimaniyatā uta bahava iti
﻿<pb n="b921"/>
prātipadikārthasiddheraniyatā iti । aniyame'pi bahuvacanopapatteḥ ।
na, nityavadvahuvacanasya śrūyamāṇatvāt । utpattau ca bahuvacanasya
vivakṣitatvāt । asiddhārthalakṣaṇaṃ hi prātipadikaṃ na vacanama-
pekṣate । notpādyavacanam । tasmādvahavaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="27">।। 12 ।। 1daśatvaṃ liṅgadarśanāt ।। 27 ।।</ab>
<p>sthite bahutve kimaniyamaḥ uta niyataiva kācit bahuvacanā-
bhidheyā saṅkhyā uta tritvasaṅkhyaiveti । kapiñjalādhikaraṇena tri-
saṅkhyaiveti prāpte darśanāda‍daśapeye, svāmidaśatvācca daśaiveti niyamaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b922"/>
anyatrāpi śrūyamāṇā niyatā saṅkhyā aniyatopadeśaṃ niyantumarhati
avirodhāt । tathā coktaṃ kāraṇādatikrama iti ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="28">।। 13 ।। 1śamitā ca śabdabhedāt ।। 28 ।।</ab>
<p>evaṃ sthite śabhitāpi śabdabhedāt camasādhvaryuvadbhidyate ।
saṃjñābhedaścopapanno bhavati । evaṃ prāpte'bhidhīyate-nātra bhedaḥ utpatti-
nibandhano hi bheda uktaḥ । na cāsyotpattirasti । kathaṃ tarhi saṃjñānyatvaṃ ?
﻿<pb n="b923"/>
naiveyaṃ saṃjñā asya, virodhāt । kiṃ tarhi ? yaugikābhidhānameva ।
evaṃ cādhvaryavamiti samākhyopapannā bhaviṣyati ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="30">।। 14 ।। 1upagāśca liṅgadarśanāt ।। 30 ।।</ab>
<p>kena punarviśeṣeṇāyamadhikaraṇātideśaḥ ? ayaṃ viśeṣaḥ
upagā iti gānakāriṇāṃ saṃbandhāt camasādhvaryava iva hotra-
kāṇāmiti pūrvapakṣavādī manyate । utpatteraśravaṇādityatidiṣṭo
rāddhāntaḥ । liṅgamuktam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b924"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="31">1vikrayī tvanyaḥ karmaṇo'coditatvāt ।। 31 ।।</ab>
<p>somavikrayī punaḥ kaḥ ? teṣāmevānyatama iti manyate । nanu
cācodito vikrayaḥ । coditasya ca ṛtvijaḥ kartṛtvenopādīyante ।
krayopādānaśeṣatvaṃ vikraye manvānasya pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । rāddhāntavādī tu
lobhādevākṣepasiddheḥ dravyārjanavanna śeṣaṃ manyate । tasmādanā-
rtvijametat । ato'nya iti rāddhāntitam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="32">।। 16 ।। karmakāryāt sarveṣāmṛtviktvamaviśeṣāt ।। 32 ।।</ab>
<p>nanu cātra rāddhānto na ghaṭate । kathaṃ na ghaṭate ?
﻿<pb n="b925"/>
utpattāvapi hi parisaṅkhyaiva prāpnoti । camasādhvaryūṇāmapyutpatti-
śravaṇāt । atha parisaṅkhyaiveṣṭā, ṛtuyajananimittanirasanamanarthakaṃ
syāt । atrocyate---utpattau naiva parisaṅkhyā prāpnoti । ekaikatra
udgātrādiśabdatulyatvāt ṛtvika‍śabdasya nātrāpahnavanīyaṃ kiñci-
dasti । ṛtuyajananimitte punarapahnavaḥ prāp‍noti । na cāsau
śakyate । evaṃ coparitanamadhikaraṇamupapannaṃ bhavati ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b926"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="36">।। 17 ।। 1niyamastu dakṣiṇābhiḥ śrutisaṃyogāt ।। 36 ।।</ab>
<p>ke ta iti । ṛtvigbhyo dakṣiṇāṃ dadātīti prakramya yān
saṃkīrtayati te ta iti rāddhāntaḥ । tathā ye yajamānāsta ṛtvija
iti darśitam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="37">।। 18 ।। 2svāmisaptadaśāḥ karmasāmānyāt ।। 37 ।।</ab>
<p>saptadaśa ṛtvija iti śrūyate । tatra kiṃ saha yajamānen saptadaśa
uta yajamānavyatiriktā anye saptadaśeti karmakarasaṅkhyaiṣā । na ca
svāmī karmakaraḥ । ekadharmayuktānāṃ cāvāntarasaṅkhyopapadyate ityanya
eveti yuktam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b927"/>
<p>atrocyate---svāmisaptadaśāḥ saptadaśaḥ svāmī yeṣāṃ te
tayoktāḥ । nanu ca karmakarasāmānyaprayuk‍taivaiṣā'vāntarasaṅkyā ।
kena vok‍taṃ neti । kathaṃ tarhi svāmisaptadaśāḥ saptadaśa । na
svāmitayā yajamānaḥ saptadaśaḥ । kiṃ tarhi ? kartṛtayaiva । yajamānā-
pekṣaiṣā saṅkhyā nādhikāritayā । nanu ca sadasyaṃ vṛṇīta iti
varaṇotpat‍tibhaṅgīkṛtya eṣāṃ saṅkhyā, na ca yajamāna utpadyate ।
ucyate---ṣoḍaśānāmeva varaṇenotpat‍tiḥ । nanu ca sadasyaṃ vṛṇīta iti
sadasyaḥ saptadaśo bhaviṣyati yadi brahmaṇyevāyaṃ sadasyaśabdo vartate ।
﻿<pb n="b928"/>
tasmāt svāmisaptadaśāḥ parigṛhyante । atha kasmādekaścama-
sādhvaryuḥ na parigṛhyate ? na te yajamānena varitavyā ityuktam ।
tasmāt karmakaraṇasāmānyāt yajamāna evetyuktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="39">।। 19 ।। 1te sarvārthāḥ prayuktatvādagnayaśca svakālatvāt ।। 39 ।।</ab>
<p>idamidānīṃ sandihyate---kiṃ sarvārthā ṛrtvijaḥ yāvatpuruṣakāryaṃ
yajamānasya tāvattaiḥ kriyate uta yāvadvacanamiti । <q>“agnayaśca
svakālatvā”</q>diti । kimidaṃ ? nanu cādhānasya sarvārthatāṃ vadatā
agnīnāṃ sarvārthatvamuktam । kimidaṃ punaḥ sarvārthatocyate ? saiveyaṃ
﻿<pb n="b929"/>
sarvārthatā'tra sādhyate svakālatvāditi । nanu ca svakālatvāt
yāvadagnikāryaṃ tatsarvamagnimirityucyate yathā yāvatpuruṣakāryaṃ tatsarva-
mṛtvigbhiriti । tataḥ kim ? tadeva nopapadyate samadhigatametat
agnayaśca svakālatvāditi । na hi svakālatvādyāvadagni-
kāryaṃ tadarthatā siddha‍yati । kiṃ tarhi ? svakālatvena
sarvakarmārthatā siddha‍yati na hi pratikarmotpattirbhavatītyarthaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b930"/>
evaṃ tarhi bhavataivok‍tam । yasmādyasyaiva hetuḥ sa eva pratijñātārthaḥ ।
tasmāt sūtradvayamevaitat । ādhastyasūtrasya parihāro'yamucyate ।
idaṃ tu sthitameva । na hyatra vacanāni nityānuvādatayā kalpyante ।
tasmādyavadvacanamevaitat ṛtvijāṃ kāryam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="41">।। 21 ।। 1tasyopadeśasamākhyānena nirdeśaḥ ।। 41 ।।</ab>
<p>idamidānīṃ cintyate । yadyena samākhyāyate tat
tenaiva kartavyaṃ uta kiñcidanyenāpi iti । eṣa tāvadutsargaḥ
yadyena samākhyāyate tattena kartavyamiti । ucyate---vacanāt
﻿<pb n="b931"/>
samākhyānācca apavādaḥ । kathaṃ tarhi samākhyāḥ ? brāhmaṇagrāma-
vadityadoṣaḥ । darśanamuktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="43">।। 22 ।। 1praiṣānuvacanaṃ maitrāvaruṇasyopadeśāt ।। 43 ।।</ab>
<p>maitrāvaruṇaḥ preṣyati cānucāheti kiṃ praiṣamātraṃ anuvacanamātraṃ
maitrāvaruṇena kartavyaṃ, uta saṃyuktameveti । saṃyuktasya vidyamāna-
tvānnāsaṃyuk‍taṃ parigṛhyate । caśabdaścaivaṃ samarthito bhavati ।
darśanamuktam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b932"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="46">।। 23 ।। 1camasāṃścamasādhvaryavassamākhyānāt ।। 46 ।।</ab>
<p>kiṃ camasaiścamasādhvaryavo juhvati utādhvaryureveti । samākhyai-
vānyathā nopapadyata iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । rāddhāntastu---adhvaryuśabda-
syotpat‍tinimittatvāt । adhvaryuriva camaseṣu bhavantīti cama-
sādhvaryavaḥ tasmādadhvaryurjuhotīti । kathaṃ tarhi adhvaryuriva bhavati ?
anyatra vyāpṛte tasmin tatkāryakaratvāt । darśanamuktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="50">।। 24 ।। 2vedopadeśāt pūrvavadvedānyatve yathopadeśaṃ syuḥ ।। 50 ।।</ab>
<p>śyenavājapeyāvudāharaṇam । kiṃ śyenaḥ udgātrā kartavyaḥ
samākhyānāta adhvaryuṇā ca vājapeyaḥ uta ṣoḍaśabhirapīti ।
﻿<pb n="b933"/>
viśeṣasamākhyānāta udgātrā'dhvaryuṇā ceti prāpte upakāradarśanāt
ṣoḍaśabhirapīti vadāmaḥ । klṛpto balīyānityuktau hetuḥ ।</p>
<trailer>iti bṛhatyāṃ tṛtīyādhyāyasya
saptamaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>
﻿<pb n="b934"/>
</section>
<section>
<head>tṛtīyādhyāyasya aṣṭamaḥ pādaḥ ।।</head>
<ab type="sutra" n="1">।। 1 ।। 1svāmikarma parikrayaḥ karmaṇastadarthatvāt ।। 1 ।।</ab>
<p>samākhyayā ādhvaryavamiti prāpte adhikāraśrutivirodhāt
yājamānamiti rāddhāntaḥ । vacanādanyeṣāmṛtvijāmapi parikrayaḥ
syāt ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="2">।। 2 ।। saṃskārastu puruṣasāmarthye yathāvedaṃ karmavadva‍yavatiṣṭheran ।।</ab>
<p>vapanādīnāṃ samākhyayā nādhikāro virudhyata iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b935"/>
rāddhāntavādī tu puruṣasaṃskāraṃ manvāno na saṃskartuṃ puruṣāḥ pari-
krīyante । kiṃ tarhi kārayitum, ataḥ sāmarthyāt samākhyābādhaṃ
manyate । yatra punaḥ śrutyaiva saṃskāraścodyate na tatra sāmarthyā-
nnivṛttiḥ yathopavāsaṃ vakṣyati । athobhayānugrahāya samānavidhānaṃ
kasmānna bhavatīti cet ? ṛtvikṣu kriyamāṇo yajamānena kṛtaḥ
kārito vā na bhavati ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b936"/>
<p>kimiti na kṛtaḥ kārito vā ? 1sādhāraṇyādeva । nanu ceḍā-
bhakṣaṇavat svayaṃ ca karoti kārayati ca । na । tatra kartṛtvenā-
viśeṣāt । iha tu prādhānyāviśeṣādanupapattiḥ । tasmādyājamāna-
iti siddham । vacanādvā yajamānapañcamā iti ।</p>*****
<ab type="sutra" n="9">।। 3 ।। 2tapaśca phalasiddhitvāllokavat ।। 9 ।।</ab>
<p>kimatrātidiśyate ? rāddhāntaḥ । kā punaratra pūrvapakṣā-
śaṅkā ? iyamasti kleśarūpatvāt tapasaḥ । parikrayaśca
kleśāpanuttaye dṛṣṭārtho bhavati ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b937"/>
<p>na saṃskārasāmānyāditi rāddhāntaḥ । darśanamuktam । upa-
vāsaśca vacanādityetadapyuktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="12">।। 4 ।। 1guṇatvācca vedena na vyavasthā syāt ।। 12 ।।</ab>
<p>hiraṇyamālyādiṣu tu guṇatvādeva padārthasya na samākhyayā
kartṛtvaṃ niyamyata iti sarvartvijāṃ pratipradhānāvṛttyā guṇo bhavitu-
marhati । yatra punaḥ kartṛtayaiva saṃbandhaḥ yathokthyādiṣu tatroktaḥ
samākhyayā niyamaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b938"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="13">।। 5 ।। 1tathākāmo'rthasaṃyogāt ।। 13 ।।</ab>
<p>kāmasaṃyoga idānīṃ śrūyamāṇaḥ kimārtvijo bhavatu guṇaphala-
saṃbandheṣu uta yājamāna iti । kiṃ yuktam ? ārtvijaḥ ।
kutaḥ ? ṛtvika‍padārthāśritatvāt guṇaphalasaṃbandhasya kāmasaṃyogo'pi
ṛtvijāmeva । ato guṇakāmeṣu ṛtvijāmadhikāra iti । atro-
cyate । yajamāna evādhikriyate sāṅge karmaṇyadhikṛtatvāt । nanu
cāsāvārtvijapadārthaḥ । neti brūmaḥ । tatkartṛko hi saḥ na punaḥ
tasya saḥ । yasya ca karma tadāśritamapi tasyaiveti yajamāna
evādhikriyate । evaṃ cātmanepadābhidhānamupapannaṃ bhavati ।
﻿<pb n="b939"/>
