yatra ca punaḥ vacanādārtvijo'dhikāraḥ tatrānyadīyapadārthāśritepi
guṇe vyāpṛtasya phalaṃ bhavati iti kalpyate ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="15">।। 6 ।। 1mantrāścākarmakaraṇāstadvat ।। 15 ।।</ab>
<p>idānīmāśīrmantrā udāharaṇam । kiṃ yājamāna utārtvijā
iti । ārtvijāssamākhyayeti prāpte brūmaḥ---liṅgādyājamānā iti ।
liṅgaṃ hi samākhyāto balīya ityuktam । proṣitasamidādhānadarśanaṃ
ca liṅgam । nanu ca mama yajamānasyetyevamādi liṅgamupapadyate ।
﻿<pb n="b940"/>
ayameva doṣaḥ yadutādhyāhāro nāma । tasmādvak‍tureva mametyupapannaṃ
bhavati ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="17">।। 7 ।। dva‍yāmnāteṣūbhau dva‍yāmnānasyārthavattvāt ।। 17 ।।</ab>
<p>kecinmantrāḥ yājamāne cādhvaryane cāmnātāḥ । tatra saṃśayaḥ kiṃ
dvābhyāṃ vaktavyāḥ utādhvaryuṇaiveti । kathaṃ punaḥ dva‍yāmnānāta dvābhyāṃ
ca samākhyātāḥ ekena vaktavyā iti । ekakāryatvānmantrāṇā-
miti pūrvapakṣavādī ekaprayojyatāṃ manyate । rāddhāntavādī tu
ekasyānuṣṭhānasmaraṇādanyasya ca pratyavekṣaṇāt āmnānadvayasyāpi
arthavattvāt dvābhyāmapi prayoktavyāḥ । samākhyādvayaṃ cānugṛhītaṃ
bhaviṣyati ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b941"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="18">।। 8 ।। 1jñāte ca vacanaṃ na hyavidvān vihito'sti ।। 18 ।।</ab>
<p>k‌lṛptīryajamānaṃ vācayatīti śrūyate । kiṃ vidvāneva vācayi-
tavyaḥ utāvidvānapīti saṃśayeḥ । kathaṃ punaḥ viduṣo'dhikārasiddheḥ
aviduṣo'dhikārāśaṅkā ? vācayatītyetasmādeva hi na viduṣo
vācayatīti dṛṣṭārthatā saṃbhavatīti । evaṃ tarhi aviduṣa eva vācanaṃ
bhavatu । bhavatu ko doṣaḥ ? viduṣo'dhikārahāniḥ prāpnoti ।
nādhikāraṃ nivārayāmaḥ aviduṣo'pyastīti । idaṃphalamidamadhi-
karaṇam । atrocyate---nādhikāramākṣep‍tumidaṃ vacaḥ । bruvantameva
hi vācayatīti bravīti । nābruvataḥ pravṛttimāha । viduṣaśca
﻿<pb n="b942"/>
prakṛtyarthe pravṛttiḥ nāviduṣaḥ śrutaḥ । ato yathādhikāraṃ vācanamiti
siddham ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="19">।। 9 ।। 1yājamāne samākhyānāt karmāṇi yājamānāni syuḥ ।। 19 ।।</ab>
<p>iha dvandvānyudāharaṇam । kiṃ yajamānena kartavyāni utādhva-
ryuṇeti saṃśayaḥ । ekatra padārthāmnānāt । anyatra samabhyā-
śīkaraṇāt । tatra viśeṣasamākhyayā yājamānāni । padārtha-
pūrvakatvāt samabhyāśasya । atrocyate । padārthāstāvadādhvaryavā eva
﻿<pb n="b943"/>
akriyamāṇe padārthe na yajamānena samabhyāśaḥ śakyate kartumiti
ādhvaryava eva । viśeṣasamākhyāpravṛttistu darśitā ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="21">।। 10 ।। 1vipratiṣedhe karaṇaḥ samavāyaviśeṣāt itaramanyarateṣāṃ
yato viśeṣaḥ syāt ।। 21 ।।</ab>
<p>ṛtvigantarakāryopadeśe kimātmīyaṃ karma karotu uta ati-
diṣṭamiti saṃśaye atidiṣṭaṃ pratyakṣavidhānāditi siddham ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="23">।। 11 ।। 2praiṣeṣu parādhikārāt ।। 23 ।।</ab>
<p>praiṣapraiṣārthau kimekena kartavyau uta dvābhyāmiti ।
﻿<pb n="b944"/>
prāptakālabhrāntyā ekeneti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । yuṣmadarthaparityāga-
kāraṇābhāvāditi rāddhāntaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="23">।। 12 ।। 1adhvaryuśca darśanāt ।। 23 ।।</ab>
<p>idānīṃ kimadhvaryuḥ praiṣārthaṃ karotu utānya iti saṃśayaḥ । artha-
vādadarśanādanya iti prāptam । mantraliṅgadarśanāt samākhyānārtha-
saṃbhavāccādhvaryuḥ । arthavādastu guṇavādena parihṛtaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b945"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="25">।। 13 ।। 1ṛtvikphalaṃ karaṇerṣvathavattvāt ।। 25 ।।</ab>
<p>kaḥ punarāśīrmantrairasya viśeṣaḥ ? samākhyātaḥ sthite'dhvaryu-
kartṛtve agnyanvādhānasya śratyā mantravidhānam । na ca guṇānu-
rodhena pradhāna (kartṛtva)bādhaḥ śakyate vak‍tum । tasmādādhvaryavo mantra
iti sthite kasyāśīriti cintyate । liṅgādadhvaryoḥ । vaktā hi
uttamapuruṣeṇa saṃbadhyate । nanu karmasaṃbaddhaphalasaṅkīrtanāt karmārthatā
mantrāṇām । na । karmaprayuktayaśaḥ prakāśayataḥ upapannaiva karmārtha-
teti pūrvapakṣavādī manyate । rāddhāntavādī tu yaścārthādartho na sa
codanārtha iti manvānaḥ karmasaṃbaddhameva phalaṃ prakāśayan mantraḥ
﻿<pb n="b946"/>
karmortho bhavati । yajamānasaṃbaddhameva phalam । yajamānasya mameti
mantrārthaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="28">।। 14 ।। 1karmārthaṃ tu phalaṃ teṣāṃ svāminaṃ pratyarthavattvāt ।। 28 ।।</ab>
<p>yatra punaḥ dṛṣṭārthameva tat kimṛtvijāmeva uta atrāpi karma-
phalameveti । uk‍tena nyāyena karmaphalameveti vadāmaḥ । atrocyate ।
yaścārthādartho na sa codanārtha iti anupakāramaṅgīkṛtyaitaduktam । yat
punaḥ karmaṇa upakaroti tadupādānaśeṣatayā bhavatyeva karmārthamiti
nākarmārthatā mantrāṇām ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b947"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="29">।। 15 ।। vyapadeśācca ।। 29 ।।</ab>
<p>yatra ca vyapadiśyata eva tatra bhavatyeva phaladarśanam---tannau
saheti ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="30">।। 16 ।। dravyasaṃskāraḥ prakaraṇaviśeṣāt ।। 30 ।।</ab>
<p>vedirvedidharmāścetyuktamuttaravivakṣayeti ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="31">।। 17 ।। nirdeśāt‍tu vikṛtāpūrvasyānadhikāraḥ ।। 31 ।।</ab>
<p>sthitamaṅgapradhānārthaṃ prakṛtau barhiriti । vikṛtāvidānīṃ
cintyate---kimatrāpi aṅgapradhānārthe barhiṣi dharmā bhavanti
codakena uta prākṛtakāryaprayukta eveti । tatra prakṛtivadvikṛtā-
vapoṃti pūrvapakṣavādī manyate ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b948"/>
<p>rāddhāntavādī tu kāryamukhenāṅgapradhānārthasaṃbandhitayā sāmānyena
prakṛtivadvikṛtāviti dharmāṇāṃ vikṛtau nirūpaṇam । na yathā
prakṛtisaṃvandhitayā । saṃbandhasāmānyena hi sarvatropadeśaḥ
syāt । tataścohadarśanaṃ nopapadyate । tasmātsiddhaṃ na yūpabarhiṣi
dharmāḥ kartavyāḥ । añjanājye na ājyadharmāḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="32">।। 18 ।। 1virodhe ca śrutiviśeṣādavyaktaḥ śeṣe ।। 32 ।।</ab>
<p>anekatra śeṣabhāvo na nyāyyaḥ iti paribhojanīyādanyat
kartavyam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b949"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="33">।। 19 ।। 1ayanayastvekadeśasya ।। 33 ।।</ab>
<p>pūrvādhikaraṇanyāyenānekatra śeṣabhāvo na nyāyya iti manvānasya
pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । dvayavadānopasaṃhārāt pratipatteśca rāddhāntaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="34">।। 20 ।। 2vikṛtau sarvārthaḥ śeṣaḥ ।। 34 ।।</ab>
<p>idānīṃ vikṛtābupāṃśutvādayo dharmāścintyante । kiṃ
tatrāpi prakṛtivat aṅgapradhānārthatā dharmāṇāṃ uta neti
saṃśayaḥ । prakṛtivadaṅgapradhānārthatā dharmāṇāmiti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b950"/>
naupadeśikātideśikaiḥupadeśaḥ saṃbadhyata iti । upadeśāpekṣa-
tvādatideśasya sāpekṣatvaṃ rāddhāntaḥ । kiṃ punaḥ kāraṇaṃ na
saṃbadhyata iti ? upadeśāpekṣatvādatideśasya sāpekṣanirapekṣayoḥ
nirapekṣaṃ balīya iti nyāyavidaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="36">।। 21 ।। 1sannidhānaviśeṣādasaṃbhave tadaṅgānām ।। 36 ।।</ab>
<p>śyene tvaupadeśikasaṃbandhābhāvāt ātideśikaireva saṃbandha iti
viśeṣaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b951"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="39">।। 22 ।। 1tatkāle vo liṅgadarśanāt ।। 39 ।।</ab>
<p>idānīṃ liṅgadarśanabhrāntyā sutyākālānāmevātra vidhānamiti
pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । aviśeṣāt sarveṣāmiti rāddhāntaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="42">।। 23 ।। māṃsa tu savanīyānām ।। 42 ।।</ab>
<p>tarasāḥ savanīyāḥ puroḍāśā bhavantīti । atra savanīya-
puroḍāśayoḥ vivakṣāyāṃ vākyabhedaprasaṅgāt kasyāyathārthatvamiti ।
dṛṣṭavyabhicārāt puroḍāśasya ayathārthatvamiti rāddhāntitam ।</p>
<trailer>iti bṛhatyāṃ tṛtīyādhyāyasya
aṣṭamaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>
﻿<pb n="b952"/>
﻿<pb n="b953"/>
</section>
<section>
<head>caturthādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pādaḥ ।।</head>
<ab type="sutra" n="1">।। 1 ।। 1athātaḥ kratvarthapuruṣārthayorjiṃjñāsā ।। 1 ।।</ab>
<p>kratvarthapuruṣārthayorjijñāsā kimiti pṛthak pratijñāyate ?
aidamarthyalakṣaṇameva hi śeṣatvam; śeṣaḥ parārthatvādityuktam । kratvartha-
tāpi tadantaḥpātinī pratijñātaivāthātaḥ śeṣalakṣaṇamityanena ।
tasmāt punaḥ pratijñāyāḥ prayojanaṃ na vidmaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b954"/>
<p>atha mataṃ na śrutyādibhiḥ puruṣārthatā'vagamyate tasya lipsārtha-
lakṣaṇeti vakṣyati । kratvarthagrahaṇaṃ tarhi pratyuktam । na ceyamapi
puruṣārthatālakṣaṇā śakyate vak‍tum । na ca śabdādṛte yāgaḥ svargārtha
iti jñānamutpadyate । na ca tatsādhyaḥ svargaḥ puruṣārtha iti svato'ya-
mapyasamādhiḥ । yadapi śrutyādīnāṃ saṅkīrtanaṃ tadapi kasmai prayojanā-
yeti na vidmaḥ । śrutyādibhiśśeṣalakṣaṇaṃ nānyena pramāṇena । ataḥ
śeṣalakṣaṇamityetāvataiva tathā । tataḥ śrutyādisaṅkīrtanaṃ mandaprayo-
janamiva pratibhāti । yadapi kratvarthapuruṣārthayoḥ prayojakāprayo-
jakādīnantarbhāvayan pratijñātān kathayati tadapyasamañjasa iva ।
kutaḥ ? antarbhāvo hi svarūpato lakṣaṇataḥ kāryato bhavati ।
﻿<pb n="b955"/>
trayamapyatra nāsti । svarūpaṃ tāvat pṛthagabhidhānādeva bhinnam ।
lakṣaṇamapi svarūpabhedādeva bhinnam । lakṣaṇabhedādṛte na svarūpabhedaḥ
kāryamapi yaddarśitaṃ bhāṣyakāreṇa tadayuktam । pradeśāntaraviruddha-
ścārthavādastāvat stutyarthaḥ prādhānyamapi upakāryopakāranibandhanam ।
prayojakamapi prayojyaṃ prati prādhānyamātmanaḥ pratipādayati । na
punarātmanaḥ parārthatām । tadidaṃ rātriprayāṇamivādeśakaṃ bhāṣyaṃ
vyāmohamupajanayati ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b956"/>
<p>atrocyate---dvayamapyetad‏yuk‍taṃ bhedopanyāso'ntarbhāvaśca yathā
tatra । yatpunaḥ tādarthyaṃ śeṣatve heturiti satsu śrutyādiṣu
tadityuktam । nanu caivaṃ sati kratvarthatā pratyuk‍tetyapyuktam ।
bhavedetadevaṃ yadi vainiyogikamucyate । iha tu upādānanibandhana-
meva pratijānāti । kimupādānaṃ nāma ? niyogākṣepa upādānam ।
tatkṛtaṃ ca prokṣaṇādeḥ kratvarthatvam । viniyogāt punaḥ vrīhyarthataiva ।
﻿<pb n="b957"/>
bhedārthapratijñānaṃ tarhi kimiti ? kimitivā'ntarbhāvaḥ । avagati
hetubhedādbhedaḥ upakārasāmānyādantarbhāvaḥ । prayojakaḥ kaścit
puruṣārtha iti kaścid‌grahaṇaṃ kiñcitprayojakasyāpyapuruṣārthatājñāpanārthaṃ
yathā---kasya ? ācāryakaraṇavidheḥ svādhyāyasya ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="2">1yasmin prītiḥ puruṣasya tasya lipsārthalakṣaṇāvibhak‍tatvāt ।। 2 ।।</ab>
<p><q>“tasya lipsārthenaiva bhavati na śās‍treṇa”</q> iti viruddhamuktam ।
﻿<pb n="b958"/>
na śāstrādṛte svargaḥ sādhyatayā pratīyate । kartṛgāmitayā ca ।
saṃbandhaśāstramaṅgīkṛtyaitaduktam । arthaśca niyogasiddhiḥ taccopādāna-
mityuktam । nanu ca kratvarthatāpyupādānenaivoktā । viniyoge-
satītyuktam । arthādeva hi puruṣārtha iti viśeṣaḥ ।
kimidamavibhāgāditi ? puruṣasya kratusaṃbandhāvibhāgādityarthaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b959"/>
etacca ṣaṣṭhe nipuṇataramupapādayiṣyāmaḥ । pariśeṣādviniyoge satīti
kratvarthatoktā bhavati ।</p>
<p>evaṃ vā । nanu guṇaphalacodanā etā ityuktam । ko'yaṃ
punarvicāraḥ ? ucyate---pradarśitamasmābhiḥ viniyogatastaduktamiti ।
iha punarupādānato dṛṣṭaprayojanasaṃbhavāt nādṛṣṭaṃ prayojanaṃ saṃbhavati
iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।</p>
<p>na, yathāviniyogaṃ kāryāvagateḥ । viniyuktasyaiva hi kārya-
kalpanā nāviniyuktasyeti rāddhāntaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b960"/>
<p>ato viniyogataḥ upādānataśca puruṣārthataiva guṇaphalacodanā-
sviti sthitam । bādarigrahaṇaṃ punarupakārapradarśanārtham । na punaḥ
parārthatvāditi śeṣahetunivṛttyartham । kathaṃ ? viniyoge hi sa
uktaḥ । nanu bādariṇāpi viniyoga evāsāvupanyastaḥ । ata
evāsau nirākṛtaḥ । iha punaḥ kāryata evopādānamityupanyastam ।
﻿<pb n="b961"/>
ayathāviniyogatayā nirasyata ityavirodhaḥ । evaṃ vā । iha
dravyārjananiyamā udāharaṇam । tatra pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । niyamaniyo
mānāmadhikāraśūnyatvāt kāmaśrutiniyogenaikavākyatvāt adhi-
kārasiddheḥ । evaṃ ca kṣāmavatyādīnāmapi spaṣṭaiva karmārthatopapannā bhavati
iti । tasmādanadhikāriṇe vidherānarthakyaṃ mābhūditi kratvarthatā ।
nanu kratvarthatve svatvameva na bhavatīti yāga eva na saṃvarteteti
pralapitamidaṃ kenāpi ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b962"/>
<p>ārjanaṃ svatvaṃ nāpādayatīti vipratiṣiddham । kathaṃ tarhi
kratvarthatā ? vanīvananavat tadarthaṃ svatvamityabhiprāyaḥ ।</p>
<p>atrocyate---neme adhikāraśūnyā niyamavidhayaśśakyante
vak‍tum । jīvanāya pravṛttā adhikṛtā bhaviṣyanti ।
﻿<pb n="b963"/>
na ca śabdādevādhikāraḥ adhikārādeva [hyadhikāraḥ] sa tu kvaci-
cchabdāvagamyaḥ kvacit pramāṇāntarāvagamyaḥ । ataḥ svatvasyā-
viśeṣāt sarvapuruṣārthanirvṛttau na viśeṣaśśakyate'vadhārayitum ।</p>
<p>1api ca yadi śāstrāt karmārthaṃ dravyaṃ tannānyatra viniyujyeta,
tathā''rjitaṃ, tatra sarvatantraparilopaḥ syāt2 । ko'rthaḥ ? kimidaṃ
tantram ? jīvanamiti cet aniyamāttarhi jīviṣyati । niyamasya
kratvarthatvāt । atha kratvantarāṇi tantraśabdābhidheyānyabhipretāni
tathāpi pratikratu niyamānna lopaḥ ।</p>
<p>atrocyate---kratvantarāṇyeva tantraśabdābhidheyānyabhipretāni ।
﻿<pb n="b964"/>
nacārjanasya viśeṣopādānatve pramāṇamasti । na ca sarvatantraṃ sarveṇa
dravyeṇa śakyate kartuṃ iti tantraparilopaḥ sarvakarmaṇām, ayaṃ
cāparo doṣaḥ nānyasya tantre pratate anyattantraṃ pratāyate iti darśanaṃ
nopapadyate । atha naivedaṃ kasyacidekasyāṅgamiti । evaṃ tarhi naivedaṃ
prayogavacanena gṛhyate, anupāttaprayogavacanasyāṅgataiva nāsti ।
asatyaṅgatve yasya kila aṅgatā nāsti tasyāprayogeṇānupa-
kārakatvamiti so'yamaṅgatā'bhāva evānupakārakatvena darśitaḥ1 ।
﻿<pb n="b965"/>
na cādhānavadbhavitumarhati । na ca dravyārthamevedamārjanaṃ ādhāna-
vadagnyarthameva bhavitumarhati, jīvanāya pravṛttasyādhikārāvagamāt ।
ataḥ puruṣārthamevedamārjanam । tasmāt kratvarthatve tantraparilopaḥ
sthito doṣaḥ । kṣāmavatyādīnāmāhitāgneradhikārāvagamāt bhavatu
kratvarthatā phalaṃ kalpayitum । puruṣārtha eva vā naimittiko'stu ।
tasmāt puruṣārthā dravyārjananiyamā iti sthitam । ato niya-
mātikramaḥ puruṣasyānarthaḥ na kratoḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="3">।। 3 ।। tadutsarge karmaṇi puruṣārthāya śāstrasyānatiśaṅkyatvāt
na ca dravyaṃ cikīrṣyate tenārthenībhisambandhāt kriyāyāṃ puruṣaśrutiḥ ।। 3 ।।</ab>
﻿<pb n="b966"/>
<p>yasmin prītiḥ puruṣasya tasya lipsā arthalakṣaṇetyuktam ।
iha tu prīteraśravaṇāt arthataśca śravaṇādanavagamāt adhikāri-
śūnyatā vidheḥ । na cānadhikāraṃ puruṣārthaṃ bhavati iti tasya kratvartha-
syaivekṣaṇasyāyaṃ pratiṣedhaḥ niyamo vā । atrābhidhīyate---prītyu-
tsargepyetaduktam । adhikārāśravaṇepi adhikāro yuktaḥ kalpayitum
na punaḥ kratusaṃbandhakalpanā । kaḥ punaratra viśeṣaḥ ? ayamasti
viśeṣaḥ । yathaivādhikāre śrūyamāṇe gamyamānatatkartṛtaiva nyāyyā ।
﻿<pb n="b967"/>
evaṃ gamyamānakartravagamāt adhikārakalpanaiva nyāyyā । kathaṃ tarhi
kartradhikaraṇam ? tatra hi viniyogo'dhikārakalpanāyāḥ
pratipakṣaḥ । iha tu apratipakṣā'dhikārakalpaneti । kiṃ bhūtaḥ
punaratrādhikriyate ? <q>“etāvatā hainasā viyukto bhavati”</q> iti
śravaṇāt jīvata eva vā'dhikāraḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b968"/>
<p>ato nityo'yaṃ jauvanānupālanīyo niyamaḥ svadharmatayā । nanu
ca prasajyapratiṣedho nyāyyaḥ । satyam, tasya vratamityanvayāvagate-
rlakṣaṇaiva nyāyyā । ādhānavadapyatra naiva dravyārthatā saṃbhavati ।
aviniyuktadravyasaṃyogāt । dṛṣṭasya ca saṃskārasyāvidyamānatvāt ।
kiṃ dṛṣṭārthatā śakyate vak‍tum ? bāḍhaṃ śakyate darpaṇapramārjanavat
loka evopayogadarśanāt । tasmāt puruṣārtho niyam iti yuktam ।
dṛṣṭārthāsaṃbhavena ca karkarīkarṇādayo'pi puruṣārthā ityuktam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b969"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="7">।। 4 ।। dravyoṇi tvaviśeṣeṇānarthakyāt pradīyeran ।। 7 ।।</ab>
<p>uktaṃ <q>‘spha‍yaśca kapālāni ca’</q> <q>‘spha‍yenoddhanti’</q> ityetayoḥ
kiṃ viniyojakamiti । tatra pūrvapakṣavādī <q>“spha‍yenoddhanti”</q>
ityevamādibhirvākyaiḥ sākṣāt yajñasaṃbandhānavagamāt yajñā-
yudhānīti vidhyantaraṃ manyate । nanu vājapeyasya yūpa itivat
praṇāḍyāpi saṃbandha upapadyate । yuktaṃ yūpābhāvātkratostatra ।
﻿<pb n="b970"/>
iha punaḥ kiṃ nopapadyata ityabhiprāyaḥ । evaṃ prāpte'bhidhīyate---yajñā-
yudhānīti tāvat lakṣaṇā । lakṣaṇā cet sākṣādva‍yavadhāne ca na
kaścidviśeṣa pramāṇāntarānusāriṇī hi lakṣaṇā । na ca vidyamāne
pramāṇe pramāṇāntarakalpanā śakyā । spha‍yenoddhantītyubhaya
siddhatvāt । evaṃ ca vikalpadoṣaḥ parihṛto bhavati । liṅgaṃ cāpyupapannaṃ
bhavati ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b971"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="11">।। 5 ।। tatra caikatvamayajñāṅgamarthasya guṇabhūtatvāt ।। 11 ।।</ab>
<p>ekatvaṃ viniyogābhāvānna yajñāṅgamiti pūrvapakṣavādino'bhi-
prāyaḥ । kathaṃ punarekatvaṃ na viniyujyate ? vibhaktayo hi prāti-
padikārthasya svārthasaṃbandhamabhidadhati । tasmādekatvaṃ karaṇatvaṃ ca
prātipadikārthasyaiva । naikatvasya karaṇabhāvaḥ । karaṇasaṃbandhe sati
prātipadikārthasaṃbandho na syāt । yathā <q>‘arūṇayā’</q> iti na
dravyeṇa ataḥ pratīyamānamapyetanna kriyayā saṃbadhyate yathā pūrvo
dhāvatītyaparapratyayaḥ । liṅgadarśanāni caivamupapannāni bhavanti ।
evaṃ prāpte ucyate---na viniyogādeva kriyāṅgatā, kiṃ tarhi ?
﻿<pb n="b972"/>
upādānādapi hi śeṣatābhavati । yathaiva hi karaṇībhūtasyai-
vopādānaṃ evamekatvayuktasyāpi । na hyakārakasyopādānamasaṅkhyā-
yuktasyāpi saṃbhavati । tathā ca laukikāḥ gāmānayetyevamādiṣu
tathaiva pratipadyante । tadidamuktaṃ <q>“na śrutirbrūte (pramite)
vākyārtho nāsti”</q> iti1 । na viniyogo brūte upādānaṃ
nāstītyarthaḥ । nanu <q>‘na śrutirbrūte vākyārtho nāsti’</q> iti
anya evārthaḥ pratīyate । ko'rthaḥ ? ayamarthaḥ pratīyate ।
na śrutyā vākyārthasya virodho'stīti । śrutyarthāparityāgena
vākyāt kratvarthatāvagamyate । virodhe na daurbalyamuktam ।
﻿<pb n="b973"/>
uktamasmābhiḥ viniyogo na saṃbhavatīti karaṇasyevaikatvasyeti ।
kathaṃ tarhi vākyaśabdaḥ ? samabhivyāhāraparyāyo'yaṃ na viniyo-
jakaparyāyaḥ । tasmātsiddhamupādānataḥ śeṣatvaṃ saṅkhyāyā liṅgasya
ca । evaṃ darśanānyupapannāni pūrvapakṣadarśanaṃ cānuvādaḥ ।</p>
<p>evaṃ vā । liṅgādhikaraṇam punaḥ evaṃ veti
vadataḥ ko'bhiprāyaḥ aparicchedakatvaṃ liṅgasya pūrvapakṣavādī
manyate । paricchedikā hi saṅkhyā dravyasya parimāṇamācaṣṭe
﻿<pb n="b974"/>
śravaṇāviśeṣālliṅgamapyupādīyata iti rāddhāntaḥ । nanu cāpari-
māṇāpādakatvālliṅgaṃ nopādātavyamityuktam । nātra parimāṇa-
mupādāne upayujyate । viśeṣaniṣṭhatvādupādānasya । yathā'nuṣṭhāna-
viśeṣākāṅkṣā tathā kārakaviśeṣākāṅkṣāpi । atassaṅkhyāvadupādāna-
miti siddham । śeṣaṃ pūrvavat ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="18">।। 7 ।। 1āśrayiṣvaviśeṣeṇa bhāvo'rthaḥ pratīyeta ।। 18 ।।</ab>
<p>ihāśrayiṇaḥ padārthā udāharaṇam । nanu bhāṣyamayuktaṃ
kiṃ yajimātraṃ saṃskāro devatāyā uta yajinā'dṛṣṭaṃ
devatāyāṃ kriyata iti yasmātsaṃskāramātramadṛṣṭa[ma]kurvadanarthakam ।
﻿<pb n="b975"/>
dvividhamākhyātamuk‍taṃ paraprāptaniyogānuvādakam । avahantītyāg‍ne-
yādicodanāvagataniyogānuvādakaṃ svaniyogasaṃbandhitayā'dhikāra-
sādhanaṃ ca । ihedānīṃ sandihyate---kiṃ paraprāptaniyogānuvādātmakaṃ
uta svaniyogasaṃbandhitayādhikārasādhanamiti । kutaḥ saṃśayaḥ ?
aṃśena dṛṣṭasya saṃbhavaḥ aṃśenādṛṣṭasyeti pūrvapakṣavādī dṛṣṭe
saṃbhavatyadṛṣṭakalpanā na nyāyyeti paraprāptānuvādaṃ manyate । nanu
yajyartho'tra na niṣpadyate । anuṣṭhānād‌dṛṣṭopapattyartho
('dṛṣṭo)bhaviṣyatītyabhiprāyaḥ । atrābhidhīyate---dṛṣṭopapattyarthataiva
na ghaṭate । kasmāt ? niyogasiddheravivakṣitatvāt ।
﻿<pb n="b976"/>
niyogāddhi niyogārthe pravṛttiḥ । atha tadarthamutpattiniyogo
vivakṣyate siddhamapūrvārthatvam । paścādadhikāraniyogārthatve yāgasya
---nirūpaḍhe'ṅgasaṃbandhe sati tad‌dvāreṇa dravyadevatāgatadṛṣṭasaṃskāraniṣpa-
ttyarthamityanumanyata eva । na ca tṛtīyaprakāro'yaṃ niyoganiṣpatte-
stulyatvāt samidādivat । prayojanaṃ tu dṛṣṭamadṛṣṭaṃ vā bhavatu ।
prayojanavaśācca anuṣṭhānamananuṣṭhānaṃ vā bhavatu । sarvathā sidhyati
svaniyogārthatā ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b977"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="21">।। 8 ।। 1arthe samavaiṣamyamato dravyakarmaṇām ।। 21 ।।</ab>
<p><q>‘atikrāntastṛtīyaviṣayaḥ’</q> iti । ko'yaṃ tṛtīyaviṣayaḥ ?
pārārthyapratipattiḥ । sā'tikrāntā । idānīṃ punaḥ sthite pārārthye
kevalamupādānameva cintyate kena prayojanenopādānaṃ kena neti ।
nanu ca prāgapyasmāt prayojanakṛtaivopādānacintā । kena viśeṣeṇa-
damucyate idamidānīmiti । satyaṃ---kintu pārārthyamapi tannimitta-
kameva, na (vi)niyoganimittakam । ata idamuk‍taṃ tṛtīyaviṣaya
iti । tṛtīyasyāyaṃ viṣayaḥ na punaḥ tārtīyaiḥ pramāṇaiḥ śakyate-
'vagantum । ato vidhinimittakamevāsya pārārthyamiti caturthe
cintitam । etacca vyākhyātam---na śrutyādibhiḥ sarvasya
﻿<pb n="b978"/>
pārārthyaṃ śakyate pratipādayitumiti । etadevātra kathyate । tathā ca
yāgaphalayoradhikārāt pārārthyaṃ vakṣyati । ata eva vādarereṣā
bhrāntiḥ dravyaguṇasaṃskāreṣveva śeṣatvamiti । śrutyādīnāṃ tatra
dravyādau saṃbhavāt upādānādhikārayoḥ sāmarthyamapaśyato'va-
dhāraṇāt । ata evedaṃ lakṣaṇāntaramucyate śeṣāvagamatulyatvepi ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="12">।। 9 ।। ekaniṣpatteḥ sarvaṃ samaṃ syāt ।। 12 ।।</ab>
<p>ataḥ prabhṛtīdānīṃ kevalopādānavyāpāra eva cintyate ।
śeṣatā tu viniyogata eva । nopādānataḥ । pūrva-
pakṣavādī tu kevalopakāradarśanādevopādānamāha, na śeṣatā-
'pekṣaṇīyeti manyate । yathaivopādānaśeṣeṣu paś‍vekatvādiṣu ।
﻿<pb n="b979"/>
tasmādubhayaṃ prayojakamiti । atrābhidhīyate---nātra prayojakatvaṃ
vājinasya । kutaḥ ? śeṣabhūtasya hi prayojanākāṅkṣā । sā ca
yasya śeṣabhūtā tenaiva prayojanena nivṛtterna prayojanāntaraṃ prayoja-
katvenāpekṣate । kathaṃ tarhi aśeṣabhūtasyopādānaśeṣatvaṃ, ekatvādeḥ
aśeṣabhūtasya prayojanākāṅkṣaiva nāstīti । aśeṣatve upādāna-
syaivānupapatteḥ । atrocyate---śeṣasyāvagamāt anyathānavagamāt
avagamapūrvakatvāccopādānasya । kiṃ ca śeṣabhūtasya prayojyatvānya-
thānupapatteḥ । na hyanavacchinnamupādātuṃ śakyata ityuktam ।
﻿<pb n="b980"/>
yatpunarna śeṣabhūtaṃ na ca śeṣasthamavagamyate na śeṣopādānenā-
pekṣyate na tat prayojyaṃ bhavitumarhati । yathā na dadhyānayanaṃ
na vājinaśeṣabhūtaṃ tathā pradarśitaṃ bhāṣye । tathā ca liṅgaṃ
pradarśitam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="25">।। 10 ।। padakarmāprayojakaṃ nayanasya parārthatvāt ।। 25 ।।</ab>
<p>kaḥ punarādhastyenādhikaraṇenāsya viśeṣaḥ ? ayamasti
viśeṣaḥ tatra hi dadhyānayanaṃ āmikṣānirvṛttisamakālameva
vājinamanuniṣpādayati । ato yuk‍taṃ vājinaniṣpatteḥ na
kāraṇāntarāpekṣā । iha punaḥ saptamaṃ padaṃ ityuk‍te bhavatyā-
kāṅkṣā kasyeti । prakṛtatvādekahāyanyā iti gamyate ।
﻿<pb n="b981"/>
tasmādubhayārthāmekahāyanīṃ manyate । evaṃ prāpte'bhidhīyate---satyaṃ
yadi kasyetyākāṅkṣopapadyate anirjñātasaṃbandhāntare saṃbandhinyu-
padiśyamāne bhavatyākāṅkṣāpūrvikā prajñā । yatra punassaṃbandhyantarapūrvaka
evopadeśaḥ । tatra yathānirjñātasaṃbandhipurassara evopadeśaḥ iti
darśitamaśvapratigrahe । ataḥ krayārthaivaikahāyanī saptamapadasaṃbandhinīti na
prayujyate । atra bhāṣyam---<q>‘prasaṅgamupajīvatā’</q> iti । nanu cedaṃ prayojana-
lakṣaṇam । kaḥ prasaṅgasyāvasaraḥ ? vidyamāne hi prayojakatve prasaṅga
uktaḥ । iha tu prayok‍tṛtaiva nāstīti । ucyate---śās‍traprasaṅga-
maṅgīkṛtyaitaduktam । na prayogaprasaṅgamityadoṣaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b982"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="26">।। 11 ।। 1arthābhidhānakarma ca bhaviṣyatā saṃyogasya tannimittatvāt
tadartho hi vidhīyate ।। 26 ।।</ab>
<p><q>‘puroḍāśakapālena tuṣānupavapati’</q> iti nātra śāstra-
prasaṅgaḥ saṃbhavatīti prayok‍tṛtvaṃ pūrvapakṣavādī manyate
tuṣopavāpasyāpi na ca nāntarīyakaḥ śakya upavāpo vak‍tum
vājinavat । tasmādubhayaṃ prayojakamiti । atrābhidhīyate
---satyaṃ viniyoge nāsti śāstraprasaṅgaḥ । nāpi nāntarīyaka-
﻿<pb n="b983"/>
bhāvaḥ । kintūpāttasyāyaṃ viniyoga iti nopādānakalpa-
nā kramate । tadidamuktam---<q>“bhaviṣyatā saṃbandho'yaṃ na bhūtavartamānā-
bhyāṃ”</q> iti । yadi punaḥ bhūtavartamānābhyāṃ saṃbandhaḥ kimupādānaṃ
syāt ? ucyate---na bhūtasya, tasya bhaviṣyadarthatayā anupātta-
syaiva pālanaṃ bhaviṣyati । pālanabhūtamevopādānaṃ yataḥ । vartamāna-
syāpi yaḥ saṃbandhī tasyānyatra viniyogo na saṃbhavatītyarthādanya-
dupādeyam । bhaviṣyadarthatve punaḥ anyārthamevopāttasya viniyogaḥ
saṃbhavatīti siddhamaprayojakatvam । tuṣopavāpastu kartavyo na
kartavya iti nāsyādhikaraṇasyāyaṃ viṣayaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b984"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="17">।। 12 ।। paśāvanālambhāllohitaśakṛtorakarmatvam ।। 27 ।।</ab>
<p>āsminnadhikaraṇe hṛdayādyavadānavacanaṃ lohitaśakṛtsaṃpravyādha---
vacanaṃ ca tulyam । prakṛtapaśuviṣayatayā <q>‘agnīṣomīyaṃ paśumālabheta’</q>
iti dvayorapi prayojakatāṃ manyate pūrvapakṣavādī ।</p>
<p>atrābhidhīyate---<q>‘hṛdayasyāgre'vadyapi’</q> iti yāgo-
pasaṃhṛtiriyam । aṅgaistṛtīyasavana iti śravaṇāt ।
﻿<pb n="b985"/>
śakṛtsaṃpravyādhastu tāvanmātraparyavasāyitvāt prakṛtāśrayatvācca ।
pratipattiśca na prayojikā । na pratipādyaṃ pratipattyarthamupādīyata
iti nyāyāt । ato na prayojakaṃ paśoḥ śakṛtādīti ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="28">।। 13 ।। ekadeśadravyaṃ cotpattau vidyamānasaṃyogāt ।। 28 ।।</ab>
<p>nanu cātraṃ pūrvapakṣa eva nopapadyate । upāttadravyaviṣayatvāt
iśukhaṇḍavaccheṣāvagateḥ । satyamevaṃ, kintvatra puroḍāśasyānyārtha-
tvāt nānyatra kāryāntare viniyoga upapadyata iti ।
﻿<pb n="b986"/>
ato dravyāntaramupādeyamiti pūrvapakṣavādī manyate । rāddhāntavādī tu
na dva‍yavadānamātropasaṃhāraḥ dvayavadānamātreṇaivāg‍neyayāganirvṛttimupa-
saṃhāramanyatra viniyogopapattyarthamuktavān । yadyanyasmai dīyate
dīyamānaṃ hi tadā saṃpradānārthamiti tannopapadyate । tasmānna yāga-
kāryādanyatra viniyogassaṃbhavati । yāgakāryatayā punaḥ nānyārthatā
śakyate vak‍tum । ato nāg‍neyādicodanāyā viroṃdhaḥ । tasmāda-
pratipakṣekṣukhaṇḍanyāyenānupādānaṃ siddham śeṣadarśanāt tathā samava-
dānaśrutirityuktaṃ bhāṣye ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n=" ">।। 14 ।। 1abhidhāraṇe viprakarṣādanuyājavatpātrabhedaḥ syāt ।।</ab>
﻿<pb n="b987"/>
<p>kiṃ punaḥ puroḍāśakapālenātra viśiṣyate ? dravyopādānaṃ
tāvat tadvannāstīti sthitameva । dhāraṇasya tūpādānaṃ haviṣaḥ
prādhānyānnānyārthatayā virudhyata iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । kathaṃ
punaḥ haviṣaḥ prādhānyaṃ dvitīyāśravaṇādabhidhāraṇasya tadarthatvāt
prayājaśeṣasya ca puroḍāśakapālavat tadarthatvāt ।
siddhāntastu na prādhānyaṃ haviṣāṃ dṛṣṭārthatayā''jyasyaiveti yuktam ।
﻿<pb n="b988"/>
tasmāt pratipattireveyaṃ prayājaśeṣasyeti । kathaṃ tarhi havīṃṣya-
bhidhārayatīti bahuvacanaṃ ekena haviṣā'bhidhāraṇanirvṛtteḥ । agṛ-
hyamāṇaviśeṣatvāt bahuvacanamaviruddham । ato dravyopādānavat
dhāraṇopādānamapi na yuk‍taṃ sannihita eva haviṣi pratipattisiddheḥ
iti ।</p>
<p>nanu dvitīyātṛtīyayoranyārthatā grahītuṃ na śakyā yathārthatayāpi
vacanāvirodhāt । satyaṃ, yadyavirodhī vacanasya syāt । iha tu
﻿<pb n="b989"/>
prayājaśeṣaśabdena virudhyate pratipat‍tau punaḥ nāyaṃ virodha iti
prātipadikārthānurodhinī guṇabhūtārthavādinī vibhaktiriti yuktam ।
atrāpyanyārthataiva nyāyyā dvayoḥ karmaṇorekasmin vākye saṃbandhānu-
guṇaḥ saptamyartho draṣṭavyaḥ । darśanamuktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="40">।। 15 ।। 1samānayanaṃ tu mukhyaṃ syālliṅgadarśanāt ।। 40 ।।</ab>
<p><q>‘atihāyeḍo barhiḥ prati samānayate’</q>
ityatra sandehaḥ---kimuparitanaprayājadvayārthamevedaṃ samānayanaṃ
﻿<pb n="b990"/>
tattaścaupabhṛtasyājyasya prayājānūyājārthasya taddharbhāṇāṃ ca prayojakam ।
uta miśrīkaraṇārthamevedaṃ jauhavasaṃskārārtham । tataśca paraprayukta-
dravyasādhyatvāt aprayojakamājyasya dharmāṇāṃ ceti । tatra pūrva-
pakṣavādī samānayanamātraśravaṇāt miśrīkaraṇamātraṃ manyate । aṣṭā-
vupabhṛti gṛhṇātīti ca sarvaprayājārthatāṃ manyate । kutaḥ ?
viśeṣāśravaṇāt । tasmādadṛṣṭārthamevedaṃ samānayanamiti ।</p>
<p>evaṃ prāpte'bhidhīyate---prayājadvayasādhanārthamevedaṃ samānayanam ।
kutaḥ ? evaṃ dṛṣṭārthatā samānayanasya bhavatiupabhṛti ca
prayājārthasya grahaṇasya ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b991"/>
<p>nunu cāviśeṣeṇa tadaupabhṛtaṃ sarvārthaṃ śrūyate । śrutānu-
sāreṇa cādṛṣṭārthatā nyāyyā । nāviśeṣaśrutiḥ sāmarthyena viśeṣe-
'vasthāpyamānā śabdārthatāṃ jahāti । tasmāt śabdasyāpratirodhi---
tvāt dṛṣṭe saṃbhavati adṛṣṭakalpanā na nyāyyeti rāddhāntadarśana-
muktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="42">।। 16 ।। tatrotpattiravibhaktā syāt ।। 42 ।।</ab>
<p>kaḥ punaratra pūrvapakṣavādino'bhiprāyaḥ ? ubhayamubhayārthamiti
vadataḥ iti । ayamabhiprāyaḥ aviśeṣeṇa śravaṇāt---caturjuhvāṃ
gṛhṇātīti, viśeṣataśca kāryasiddheḥ prayājagrahaṇamanūyāja-
vannityānuvādaṃ manyate jauhave ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b992"/>
<p>atrocyate---yadyupādānata eva prāptiḥ syāt syādetadevaṃ
upādānamātrādubhayārthatāpratīteḥ । evaṃ tarhi anūyājamātrārtha-
mevaupabhṛtaṃ bhavatu । kevalānūyājārthaśravaṇāt । ucyate---prāptārtha-
tvādasya viniyojakasya kevalānūyājasaṃbandhino'nuvādaṃ manyate ।
kutaḥ prāptiḥ ? prayājānūyājabhyastadgṛhṇātītyubhayārthatvāt ।</p>
<p>nanu samānayanādhikaraṇe sthite kathamidānīmāśaṅkyate । tatra
hi uparitanaprayājārthamaupabhṛtaṃ samānīyata iti vadatā ubhayārthatva-
muktam । kathaṃ kevalānūyājārthatā āśaṅkyate । ucyate---sthite
etasmin tadbhavati anyathā'dṛṣṭārthameva samānayanaṃ saṃskāramātraṃ
syāt ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b993"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="46">।। 17 ।। 1tadaṣṭasaṅkhyaṃ syāt ।। 46 ।।</ab>
<p>aṣṭāvupabhṛti gṛhṇāti iti śrūyate । atra saṃśayaḥ kiṃ dve
ete caturgṛhīte utāṣṭagṛhītamekamevedamiti । nanu samānayanādhi-
karaṇa idamuktam dvauṃ prayājau yaṣ‍ṭumekamidaṃ caturgṛhītaṃ samānīyata
iti । kayā yuktyā ? evaṃ ca dṛṣṭārthatā bhaviṣyatītyanayā yuktyetyarthaḥ ।
tadevedamākṣipyate । aṣṭasaṃṅkhyāśravaṇāt । dṛṣṭārthatā ca samānayana-
syopapadyata eva āghāre prācīne prayājatraye ca vyāpṛtasya jauhavasyā-
jyasya svakāryaṃ pratyaśak‍tasyānugrahāya samānīyata iti । ato'tra
﻿<pb n="b994"/>
pūrvapakṣavādī śrutatvādaṣṭasaṅkhyākameva grahaṇamiti manyate ।
rāddhāntastu bhinnaviṣayatvāt catussaṅkhyāṣṭasaṅkhyayoḥ nānya-
tarasyāprāptiḥ śakyate varṇayitum avirodhāt । kathaṃ punaraṣṭasaṃkhyā
catussaṅkhyāṃ niṣyādayati home ? yasmād‍dve ete caturgṛhīte saṃyo-
ginī, prayājānūyājebhya ityubhayārthatvena viniyogāt । ubhayośca
dvābhyāṃ caturgṛhītābhyāṃ prayojanamaṣṭagrahaṇena saṃpādyate aṣṭāvupabhṛti
gṛhṇātīti । dve ete caturgṛhīte iti darśanaṃ ca pūrvavat samarthitaṃ
bhavati । catugṛhītānyājyāni bhavantīti hetuvannigadaśca
samarthito bhavati ।</p>
<trailer>iti bṛhatyāṃ caturthādhyāyasya
prathamaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>
﻿<pb n="b995"/>
﻿<pb n="b996"/>
</section>
<section>
<head>caturthādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ ।।</head>
<ab type="sutra" n="1">।। 1 ।। svarustvanekaniṣpattiḥ svakarmaśabdatvāt ।। 1 ।।</ab>
<p>ekamatrādhikaraṇaṃ vākyāntarābhiprāyeṇa varṇitam । dvitīya-
ntvekavākyamaṅgīkṛtya । yuktayaścaikavākyavicāre vākyāntarā-
pekṣiṇyāṃ ca mīmāṃsāyāṃ tulyā iti pradarśitam । yuktiśca
śrutyā vidhānam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b997"/>
﻿<pb n="b998"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="7">।। 2 ।। śākhāyāṃ tatpradhānatvāt ।। 7 ।।</ab>
<p>kimarthamidamadhikaraṇamasmin prayojakāprayojakalakṣaṇe ?
nātra vidhitaḥ pūrvapakṣo rāddhānto vā'vagamyate ।
atrocyate---vidhita eveyaṃ cintā । kiṃ vṛkṣaprāgde-
śāt śākhopādānamuta vihāraprāgdeśādānayanopādānamiti ।
﻿<pb n="b999"/>
viniyogavadabhidhānamanuvartate upādānamiti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।
rāddhāntastu---aparihāryalakṣaṇamidamābhidhānamiti śākhaivopādeyā
prācīnānayanameva deśaviśiṣṭam । ayaṃ cāparo viśeṣaḥ ।
avaśyopalakṣayitabyā śākhā pakṣadvayepītyayameva pakṣo nyāyyaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="7">।। 2 ।। śākhāyāṃ tatpradhānatvāt ।। 7 ।।</ab>
<p>atra parivāsanopādānaṃ śākhopādānaṃ vā cintyate, avi-
﻿<pb n="b1000"/>
śeṣāt । kiṃ punaratra yuktam ? ubhayaṃ parivāsanasya
prayojakaṃ mūlamagraṃ ca dvayorapi śākhābhidhānatvāt । nanu
ca kriyādvayamatra śrūyate parivāsayati karoti iti ca ।
tataḥ kim ? idaṃ tataḥ bhavati । śākhāparivāsanasya karma
karoterupaveṣaḥ । tasmānnopaveṣaḥ karmakārakasya prayoktā । ucyate
---śākhāśabdaḥ samūlamagramācaṣṭa ityuktamasmābhiḥ । tatra mūlamupaveṣaṃ
karoti । agramapi kāryāntare viniyuktamiti dvayoḥ prayojakatvam ।
﻿<pb n="b1001"/>
atrocyate---syādetadevaṃ yadi mūlamupaveṣaṃ karotīti saṃbandhaḥ । kathaṃ
tarhi saṃbandhaḥ ? upaveṣaṃ karotīti mūlata iti । kimato yadyevaṃ ?
etadato bhavati । anyato niṣpannānmūlādupaveṣa iti । tasmāt
yadyapi samūlamagraṃ śākhāśabdenocyate tathāpi na parivāsanamupa-
veṣārthaṃ iti siddham ।</p>
<p>kiṃ ca śākhāśabdābhidhānaṃ ca kāryāntareṣu agra
eva prayuk‍taṃ śākhayā vatsānapākaroti iti । ato viniyo-
gāta mūlaparivāsanārtho'yamagre śākhāśabdaḥ prayukta iti ।
﻿<pb n="b1002"/>
tasmānnopaveṣaḥ prayojakaḥ । prayojanamuktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="10">।। 3 ।। 1haraṇe tu juhotiryogasāmānyāt ।। 10 ।।</ab>
<p>nanu cedaṃ haraṇaṃ prastarapratipattyarthameva; yadyapi haratiḥ yajatyartho
māntravarṇiko devatāvidhiḥ tathāpi pratipattikarmaivaitat yathottamaḥ
prayājaḥ । pratipattau ca na dravyasya guṇabhāvaḥ । nanu ca yathottamaprayāje
ājyaṃ pratipattāvapi guṇabhūtaṃ tathātra śākhāpi bhaviṣyatīti cet ।
﻿<pb n="b1003"/>
naivam । dravyasyātra pratipattiḥ । tatra punardevatāsmaraṇārtho
yāga iti yukto dravyasya guṇabhāvaḥ ।</p>
<p>nanu cottamaprayājo naiva pratipattiḥ dravyaṃ hi yatra pratipādyate
tatpratipattikarma । kenedamuk‍taṃ kārakārtho yo yāgaḥ pratipattikarme-
tyucyate kvaciddeśavirecanāt saṃskāraḥ, kvacit smaraṇamiti ।
prayojanaviśeṣā hyete । ato na śākhā guṇabhūteti śakyate pūrva-
pakṣayitum । ucyate---pratipattāveva tṛtīyāśravaṇāt guṇabhāvaṃ pūrva-
pakṣavādī manyate, nāvaśyaṃ pratipattau sarvameva pradhānaṃ bhavati । yadyathā
śrūyate tattathaiva bhavitumarhati yathā juhvā juhotīti guṇabhūtaiva juhūḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1004"/>
<p>atrābhidhīyate । bhavedetadevaṃ yadyatra sahaśabdo na śrūyate ।
sahaśabdaśravaṇe tu tulyayogitvaṃ prastareṇa saha śākhāyā avagamyate ।
tasmācchākhāpi pratipādyata eva । anyathā hi tulyayogo na syāt ।
ataśśākhāyāmapi dvitīyārtha eva prastaravad‌draṣṭavyaḥ । kathaṃ tarhi
tṛtīyā ? na ceyaṃ kārakalakṣaṇā kiṃ tarhi sahayogalakṣaṇārthā ।
prasiddhena ca sahayogo lakṣyata iti vibhaktivyatyaya uktaḥ ।
prasiddhatvāt prastarasya praharaṇe । śeṣamuktam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1005"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="14">।। 5 ।। 1utpattyasaṃyogātpraṇītānāmājyavadvibhāgaḥ syāt ।। 14 ।।</ab>
<p>apaḥ praṇayatīti kāryadvayāsaṃbandhamapāṃ praṇayanamutpannam ।
paścātkāryadvayaṃ śrutamityaviśeṣeṇa dvayoḥ prayok‍tṛtāṃ manyate । nanu
ca <q>‘apo ninayati’</q> iti dvitīyā śrūyate । anīpsitatvāt
kārakamātre bhaviṣyatītyabhiprāyaḥ । atocyate---nānīpsitatve
heturasti । kṛtaprayojanamapi hi tat pratipādyatayā iṣyata eva ।
﻿<pb n="b1006"/>
na cepsite saṃbhavati anīpsitāśrayaṇamupapadyate tatpurassarā-
vagateḥ । tasmāt saṃyavane kṛtārthānāmapāṃ pratipattireva ninayanam ।
iti siddhamaprayok‍tṛtvam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="16">।। 6 ।। 1prāsanavanmaitrāvaruṇāya daṇḍapradānaṃ kṛtārthatvāt ।। 16 ।।</ab>
<p>maitrāvaruṇāya daṇḍaṃ prayacchatīti pratipattirapāmiveti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।
nanu ca karmaṇā yamabhipraiti sa sampradānamiti siddho guṇabhāvaḥ
﻿<pb n="b1007"/>
sasaṃpradānake karmaṇi । sampradānagaprītyutpādakatayaiva karmaṇo
guṇabhāvaḥ na punaḥ karmāntarasādhyatayā karmabhāvānupapatteḥ । kathaṃ
tarhi <q>‘daṇḍī praiṣānanvāha’</q> ityādidarśanam saṃpradāne yadṛcchayā
prāptasyāyamanuvādaḥ ityabhiprāyaḥ ।</p>
<p>atrābhidhīyate---maitrāvaruṇāya daṇḍaṃ iti vyapadeśāt daṇḍī
praiṣānanvāha ityevamādi ca darśanāt । arthakarmaivedaṃ na pratipattiḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b1008"/>
nanu ca yadṛcchayā prāptasyāyamanuvāda ityuktam । ayameva doṣaḥ
pākṣikatvaprasaṅgāt । kathaṃ tarhi dvitīyā ? tathā yuk‍taṃ cānīpsita-
mityuktam । tadayuktamiva pratibhāti । anupādeyaṃ hi tatrodā-
haraṇam ahiṃ laṅghayati iti । tathā ca sak‍tuṣu vibhaktivyatyaya
uktaḥ upādeyatvādanīpsitatvaṃ na bhavatīti । ucyate---suṣṭhūk‍taṃ
sak‍tuṣu homārthaṃ tatropādānam । iha tu na prayacchatyarthamupādānaṃ
upāttameva hi prayacchatīti । atastathāyuktamevedaṃ karmeti śakyate
vak‍tum nepsitatamam । nāpi vibhaktyantarayogyam tasmādartha-
karmeti sūktam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1009"/>
<p>kiṃ punaratra dhāraṇameva prayujyate utotpat‍tipīti cintāntara-
metat । asti tāvat prayok‍tṛtvamiti rāddhāntaḥ । adhikaraṇā-
ntaramuktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="20">।। 8 ।। 1saumike ca kṛtārthatvāt ।। 20 ।।</ab>
<p>kaḥ punaratra prayājaśeṣeṇa viśeṣaḥ ? nanu ca prayājaśeṣeṇeti
﻿<pb n="b1010"/>
prayājārthatā'vagamyate । somalipteneti karmārthatā(vagatiḥ) kimiti
na viśeṣaḥ । ucyate---somaliptenetyapi somayāgārthatayaiva soma-
saṃbandhaḥ । evaṃ tarhi avabhṛthaśruteḥ karmāntarayogaṃ somaliptasya
manvānaḥ śeṣabhāvaṃ manyate ।</p>
<p>atrocyate---karmāntarayogepi nānyaśeṣo'nyaśeṣatayā
pratipat‍tuṃ śakyate anyatra vyāpṛta ivānyatra । tasmātkarma-
śabdo lakṣaṇayaiva pratipattavyaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1011"/>
<p>yantīti ca prakṛtyartho'ntarṇītaṇijartho vihito bhavati ।
anyathā'nuvādamātraṃ dhātvarthaḥ syāt । tadidamuktam---<q>“śrutiśca
vākyādbalīyasī”</q> iti ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="23">।। 9 ।। kartṛdeśakālānāmacodanaṃ prayoge nityasamavāyāt ।। 23 ।।</ab>
<p>nanu cānuvādakatvapakṣe apratipādakatvāt vākyānarthakyameva
prāpnoti । na brūmo viniyoge ānarthakyamiti । viniyoge itthameva
anvito vākyārthaḥ pratīyate । prayok‍tṛtvaṃ tu na saṃbhavati । kathaṃ
na saṃbhavati ? nityaprāptatvāt kārakagrāmasya । dravyasya hyatra niyamaḥ
﻿<pb n="b1012"/>
kriyate na kārakāṇām । na cākārakasya prayok‍tṛtvaṃ
saṃbhavati । tasmādviniyoga evāyaṃ(niyama) viṣayaviśeṣo'vagamyate
na prayok‍tṛvyāpāra iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।</p>
<p>atrocyate---yadi dravyādanyat kārakatayā'vagamyate
tato yathā bhavānāha । iha tu dravyameva kāraka-
tayā'vagamyate । tasyābhidhānādvibhaktyutpat‍teḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1013"/>
<p>nanu ca kārakaṃ hi kriyāprayuktyaiva prayujyate । na ca kārakaśūnyaṃ
karmāsti । satyaṃ na kārakaśūnyaṃ karma na punaḥ sāmānyaṃ kiñcidasti
kārakaṃ nāma । yadeva hi vibhaktyā dravyaṃ guṇo vā samarpyate
tadeva kārakam । tasmādviniyogāt prayok‍tṛtvepi niyamaḥ
saṃbhavati । uktaṃ ca viniyogānusārī niyogaḥ sati saṃbhave
iti ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="25">।। 10 ।। 1tathā dravyeṣu guṇaśrutirutpattisaṃyogāt ।। 25 ।।</ab>
<p>yuktaṃ tāvat dravyasyopādānaṃ vibhaktibhistasya kārakatayā-
﻿<pb n="b1014"/>
'vagateḥ guṇastu tadviśeṣaṇamātrameva ś‍vetādiṣu । yatra punararuṇayeti
vibhaktyaiva kārakatvenāvagatiḥ tatra pūrvādhikaraṇenaivāvagatam । ato
dravyopādānārthatvāt guṇajātyoravivakṣeti pūrvapakṣavādī manyate ।
atrocyate---satyaṃ dravyopādānārthamidam । tadeva tu dravyaṃ tadrahitaṃ
na śakyate tadviśiṣṭamupādātumiti guṇajātyorapi dravyavadupādāna
siddhiḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="26">।। 11 ।। 1saṃskāre ca tatpradhānatvāt ।। 26 ।।</ab>
<p>saṃskāre punaḥ ko viśeṣaḥ ? ayaṃ viśeṣaḥ । adhikāraśūnyo
hi saṃskāravidhirbhavati saṃskāryārthatvāt saṃskārasya, nātrādhikārārthaṃ
﻿<pb n="b1015"/>
karmāvagamyate । tasmādavivakṣaiveti pūrvābhyāṃ viśeṣaḥ । atrocyate
---satyamadhikāro nāvagamyate । adhikṛtadravyārthatayā tu pratīyate ।
tataḥ kim ? idaṃ tato bhavati ? saṃskāraviśiṣṭadravyaṃ adhikāra-
vidhiviśeṣaṇatayā'vagamyate । tataśca guṇavat tadapi adhikāra-
vidhinaivopādīyata iti tadvadityucyate । tatpradarśitamevaṃ satyaṅga-
vidhiranuvāda iti ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="27">।। 12 ।। 1yajati codanādravyadevatākriyaṃ samudāye kṛtārthatvāt ।। 27 ।।</ab>
﻿<pb n="b1016"/>
<p>ke punaste'dhikāraviṣayāḥ ? yāgadānahomāḥ । <q>“svargakāmo
yajeta,”</q> <q>“āyuṣkāmo hiraṇyaṃ dadyāt”</q> saubhāgyakāmo juhuyāt”
ityevamādayaḥ । etaccopalakṣaṇamātram । anyepi ye kāmaśruti-
saṃyuktāḥ । kaḥ punastyāgātmakatve sati yāgadānahomānāṃ parasparaṃ
viśeṣa ityāśaṅkānivṛttyarthaṃ svarūpavarṇanamityuktam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1017"/>
﻿<pb n="b1018"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="29">।। 14 ।। vidheḥ karmāpavargitvādarthāntare vidhipradeśaḥ syāt ।। 29 ।।</ab>
<p>kaḥ punarasyopādānalakṣaṇena saṃbandhaḥ ? eṣa saṃbandhaḥ । kimu-
pāttasyātithyārthaṃ dhāraṇamātraṃ dvābhyāṃ prayujyate, uta niriṣṭakasya
punarupādānam, uta pṛthagevopādānaṃ, dharmamātrātideśakamidaṃ
vacanaṃ, uta sādhāraṇametadevopādānamiti । anyaśeṣasyānyatra-
﻿<pb n="b1019"/>
viniyogo nāsti[yathā] anyatra vyāpṛtasyaivānyatra vyāpāraḥ
ityuktam । viniyogānusārī co(no)pādānamityetadapyuktam ।
tasmānnātithyopāttasya upasadagnīṣomābhyāṃ dhāraṇaṃ prayujyata iti
ghaṭate । niriṣṭakopadeśaśca śiṣṭācāravirodhānna bhavati । lakṣaṇā-
śrayaṇaṃ ca nopapadyate । evaṃ dharmātideśo'pi lakṣaṇābhayādeva
tyajyate । tasmātsādhāraṇāvagatireva śrutyopapannā bhavatīti
sādhāraṇamupādānamiti siddham ।</p>
<trailer>iti bṛhatyāṃ caturthādhyāyasya
dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>
﻿<pb n="b1020"/>
</section>
<section>
<head>caturthādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ ।।</head>
<ab type="sutra" n="1">।। 1 ।। 1dravyāsaṃskārakarmasu parārthatvāt phalaśrutirarthavādaḥ
syāt ।। 1 ।।</ab>
<p>uktamadhyāyādau sarvatra niyogavyāpāra eva cintyata iti । ihe-
dānīṃ kiṃ phalasaṃbandhitayā puruṣasya vidhivyāpārassaṃbhavati neti ci-
ntyate । puruṣaphalasaṃbandhāsaṃbhave kathaṃ prāmāṇyaṃ saṃbhavati iti pramāṇa-
lakṣaṇe cintitam । yo'pi tatra pūrvapakṣaḥ asāvapi kriyākāraka-
saṃbandho'vagamyamānaḥ kathaṃ kriyāntaraviṣayaṃ niyogaṃ pratipādayatī
﻿<pb n="b1021"/>
tyasyārthasya nirākaraṇāya । iha tu svaviṣayo niyogo na saṃbhavatīti
cintā । kathaṃ ? yasyetyevamādīnāmadhikāriviśeṣaṇatayā'saṃbhavāt ।
kathamasaṃbhavaḥ ? tatsaṃbandhasya niyogasyānupapatteḥ kimiti ? siddha-
vadupadeśāt । yathā devadattaḥ odanaṃ pacati iti puruṣopalakṣaṇatā
pratīyate । na puruṣeṇodanaḥ paktavya iti । nāyaṃ śabdārthaḥ yasya
parṇamayī juhūrbhavati na sa pāpaṃ ślokaṃ śṛṇoti iti । pratyayāntarā-
﻿<pb n="b1022"/>
vagamyatvādasyārthasya । na ca tatpratyayāntaramasti prathamalakṣaṇokta
evāyamartha iti sthitaṃ evaṃbhūtānāmarthavādatvamiti ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="4">।। 2 ।। 1naimittike vikāratvāt kratupradhānamanyat syāt ।। 4 ।।</ab>
<p>kathaṃ punaratra dva‍yarthaṃ vākyamupanyasyate । yatrāpi tāvadarthadvaye
viśeṣo nāvagamyate tatrāpyekārthenaiva vākyena bhavitavyam । prakaraṇā-
dibhistu viśeṣo'vagantavyaḥ । kiṃ punaratra viśeṣa evāvagamyate ।
﻿<pb n="b1023"/>
dva‍yarthatā cābhidhānasya pramāṇalakṣaṇa eva nirākṛtā । tasmāta-
saṃbhavātpūrvapakṣamevedamadhikaraṇaṃ pratibhāti ।</p>
<p>atrocyate---evamevaitadekārthatvameva anvitābhidhāne । prayojana-
dvayaṃ tu atra saṃbhavatīti kratvarthatāmapi pūrvapakṣavādī manyate । saṃbandhā-
nusāri copādānamityuktam । nanu ca viniyogānusārītyuktaṃ na saṃba-
ndhānusārī । naivaṃ, viniyogo hi saṃbandhahetutayoktaḥ, na punarviniyoga-
﻿<pb n="b1024"/>
taivāśrīyate । tasmāt dvayamupādāpakaṃ, saṃbandhadvayāvagamāt
na kriyāsaṃbandhatyāgena dravyādeḥ puruṣārthatā'vasīyate ।
atrābhidhīyate । naitad‍yuk‍taṃ yaduk‍taṃ saṃbandhamātrānusāryu-
pādānamiti śabdopapāditasaṃbandhānusāryupādānaṃ na saṃbandhānu-
sārī śabdācca puruṣārthatayaivānvayo'vagamyate । nanu kriyayāpya-
nvayo'vagamyate । satyam gamyate puruṣārthaupayikatayā ।
﻿<pb n="b1025"/>
tasmāt tadevopādāpakaṃ yadarthamevānvayāvagamaḥ । yatpunaridaṃ bhāṣya-
kāreṇok‍taṃ viśeṣānavagamāt dviṣṭhaṃ vākyamalambusānāṃ 1yāteti
tat prakaraṇādyasaṃbhave anirṇayāyaiva na punaḥ śabdāt dvaya
avagantuṃ śakyate । iha tu viśeṣāvaṇamānnānirṇaya ityarthaḥ ।
nanu na kiñcidvihitamastīti paricodya sāmānyavidhānopanyāsaḥ
sāmasādhyastutyapekṣayā nābhivartaparatayetyadoṣaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1026"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="5">।। 3 ।। 1ekasya tūbhayatve saṃyogapṛthaktvam ।। 5 ।।</ab>
<p>kaḥ punaḥ pūrvaparkṣiṇa āśaṅkāhetuḥ ? ayamāśaṅkāhetuḥ yathā
<q>‘agnihotraṃ juhoti’</q> <q>‘agnihotraṃ juhuyāt svargakāma’</q> iti ca na pṛthak
prayok‍tṛtvamasti svargakāmapadānvayepi homānvayāvagateḥ । evamatrāpi
<q>‘dadhnā juhoti’</q> <q>‘dadhnendriyakāmasya juhuyāt’</q> iti kāmasaṃyogepi
dadhihomāvagateḥ puruṣārthasyaiva prayok‍tṛtvaṃ manyate[pūrvavādī]evaṃ prāpte-
'bhidhīyate । naitad‍yuktam kratorapyatra prayok‍tṛtvamavasīyate kraturapi
hi sādhikāraḥ । na guṇaphalasaṃbandhaḥ āśraye aidamarthyamapekṣata
﻿<pb n="b1027"/>
ityuktam । tasmāt <q>‘dadhnā juhoti’</q> iti homārtha evāyaṃ
viniyogaḥ <q>‘dadhnendriyakāmasya’</q> ityeva puruṣārthaḥ । yaduk‍taṃ <q>‘agnihotraṃ
juhoti’</q> <q>‘agnihotraṃ juhuyāt svargakāmaḥ’</q> ityekaḥ prayok‍teti yuk‍taṃ
adhikārāntarāśravaṇāt upādāturevādhikārakalpanā । iha tu
adhikāradvayaṃ nityaṃ naimittikaṃ cāstīti yukto viśeṣaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="8">।। 4 ।। 1dravyāṇāṃ tu kiyārthānāṃ saṃskāraḥ kratudharmaḥ syāt ।। 8 ।।</ab>
<p>iha tu prāṇadhāraṇārthatvādvratasya puruṣārthatāṃ manyate pūrvapakṣa-
vādī niyamasyaiva prāṅmukho'nnānibhuñ‍jīta iti vat pratigraha-
niyamavacca ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1028"/>
<p>atrocyate---nāyaṃ niyamaniyogo'dhikārakalpanāṃ sahate ।
sannihitaśca kratvadhikāraḥ । sākṣāt śrutādhikārasannidhau yadaśrūya-
māṇādhikāraṃ tata tadarthamevābhidhānena pratibhāti । tādarthyenaiva ca
niyamasya niyojyasaṃbandhalābhāt nādhikārāntarāpekṣā'sti । yaduktaṃ
pratigrahādiniyamavat bhavitumarhatīti । yuk‍taṃ tatrādhikārāśravaṇāt
iha punaḥ tadviparītaṃ iti darśitam । ataḥ kratuprayojya eva dravya-
niyama iti sthitam । kratvadhikāraprayojyamityuk‍taṃ bhavati ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="10">।। 5 ।। 1codanāyāṃ phalāśruteḥ karmamātraṃ vidhīyeta na hyaśabdaṃ
pratīyeta ।। 10 ।।</ab>
﻿<pb n="b1029"/>
<p>ihādhikāraśūnyā vidhaya udāharaṇam । kiṃ teṣāmadhikāra-
kalpanā uta tāvatyeva paryavasānamiti saṃśayaḥ । nanu ca <q>‘saphalaṃ’</q>
<q>‘aphalaṃ’</q> ityatra sandeho bhāṣye śrūyate । ucyate---adhikārādṛte
phalaṃ nāstīti svargakāmādhikaraṇe <q>‘tasmātsiddho'dhikāra’</q> iti vadatā
pradarśitam । anyathā hi siddhaṃ svargasya prādhānyamityupasaṃhāraḥ
syāt । tasmāta sādhikāraniradhikāracintaiveyam ।</p>
<p>kiṃ tāvatprāptam ? yāvadvacanaṃ vacanamiti kartavya-
tāparyavasāyyeva niyogo nādhikāraparyanto bhavitumarhati ।
nanu ca niyoga evādhikārādṛte na nirvartyate ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1030"/>
<p>kena vā uktamadhikārādṛte na niyogo niṣpadyata
iti adhikṛtasya niyogaḥ na punaḥ niyogata evādhi-
kāraḥ । nanu cādhikārādṛte'nanuṣṭheyatvāt niyogāvagati-
rbādhyeta । nāvagateḥ kaścidbādhaḥ । anadhikṛtāstu na kurvate
kimāyātamavagateḥ । taduk‍taṃ bhāṣyakāreṇa <q>‘kṣemyo'yaṃ panthāḥ gacchatu
bhavān anena’</q> iti । tasmānnātra kasyacidadhikāraṃ paśyāmaḥ ।
adhyāhriyamāṇepyadhikāre kasyādhikāro'dhyāhriyeta yasmānna niyogā-
﻿<pb n="b1031"/>
dviśeṣākṣepaḥ saṃbhavati । na cāparipūrṇa vākyamityatra pramāṇamasti ।
<q>‘paṭobhavati’</q> ityetāvadeva vākyam । <q>‘raktaḥ paṭobhavati’</q>
ityapi bhavati । tasmāt padāntaraśravaṇanibandhana eva
vākyeṣu arthāntarāvagamaḥ । na punaḥ aśrūyamāṇa evārthāntara-
kalpanāpramāṇamasti । kathaṃ tarhi <q>‘vasantāya kapiñjalānālabhate’</q>
grīṣmāya kalaviṅkān iti agṛhyamāṇaviśeṣatvāditi tatro-
ktam । loke tarhi kathaṃ <q>‘dvāraṃ’</q> <q>‘dvāra’</q> mityevamādiṣu ।
﻿<pb n="b1032"/>
yuktaṃ kārakāṇāṃ kriyāpekṣatvāt na punarniyogo'dhikārama-
pekṣata ityuktam । tasmādyāvadvacanaṃ vacanaṃ iti । atrā-
bhidhīyate---kārakamiva kriyāpekṣaṃ niyogamapyadhikārāpekṣaṃ
vadāmaḥ । kutaḥ ? loke tathā darśanāt devadattagāmabhyāja śuklāṃ iti ।
na hi anapekṣitaviśeṣaṃ loke vaktāro bhavanti iti devadattaṃ
yajñadattaṃ vā'dhikṛtya liṅādayaḥ prayojyāḥ । nanu ca devadattādayaḥ
kartṛviśeṣaṇam । yathā na kartṛviśeṣaṇaṃ tathā ṣaṣṭhe vakṣyāmaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b1033"/>
adhikārāddhi kartṛtvaṃ sthāsyati na kartṛtvādadhikāra-
tasmāt śrutyekadeśaḥ sa ucyate---yatpunaratra bhāṣyakāreṇok‍taṃ
<q>“evaṃ laukiko'dhyāhāraḥ prāpnoti”</q> iti parihṛtaṃ ca <q>“vaidikamevādhyāha-
riṣyāma”</q> iti, vyavadhānaṃ cāśaṅkya <q>‘api paśyasi’</q> iti dṛṣṭāntā-
bhidhānaṃ sarvamidaṃ asamañjasamiva pratibhāti yanniyogādavagamyate
kathaṃ tadavaidikaṃ ? vyavadhāne ca kathamanuṣaṅga ? yadapyuk‍taṃ <q>‘api
paśyasi dhāvantaṃ’</q> iti । asaṃbandhipadavyavāyāt naivāyaṃ vyavāyaḥ
yogyapadasaṃbaddhaṃ vyavahitamityucyate । atrocyate---vaidikamevādhyā-
hariṣyāmaḥ iti । etaduk‍taṃ bhavati । na kārakatayā'dhyāhriyate ।
﻿<pb n="b1034"/>
kathaṃ tarhi ? adhikārimukhenaiveti । kārakatayā hi phalasaṃbandho
laukiko bhavati pramāṇāntarāpekṣatvāt dṛṣṭānto'pi yathā na
padavyavadhānamātrādva‍yavahitaṃ bhavati kintu yogyapadasaṃbaddhaṃ vākyā-
ntaravyavahitaṃ vyavahitaṃ bhavati । tasmānnādhikārādhyāhāre vya-
vadhānam । api paśyasīti ca sūktam । ato'śrūyamāṇādhi-
kārāṇyapi sādhikārāṇīti siddham ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="13,15">।। 6 ।। 1tatsarvārthamaviśeṣāt sa svargaḥ sarvān pratyaviśiṣṭa-
tvāt ।। 13, 15 ।।</ab>
<p>sthitaṃ niyogo nādhikāraśūnya iti । kenādhi-
﻿<pb n="b1035"/>
kāreṇeti na jñāyate । ato'gṛhyamāṇaviśeṣatvāt sarvārthibhiḥ
saṃbadhyata iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । atrocyate---bahubhiḥ saṃbandhe niyatamekena
saṃbandhaḥ bhavati । ekena cedupapanno niyogaḥ nādhikārāntarasaṃbandhe
pramāṇamasti । nanu cāgṛhyamāṇaviśeṣatvānnāsau nirūpayituṃ śakyata
ityuktam । satyaṃ yadi na gṛhyate viśeṣaḥ । iha tu sarvān pratyaviśi-
ṣṭatvāt svargakāmasyaivādhikāro'trāvagamyate । sāmānyakalpanāyāṃ hi
viśeṣāvagamahetvabhāvāt । tadidamuktaṃ---<q>“sa svargaḥ syāt sarvān
﻿<pb n="b1036"/>
pratyaviśiṣṭatvāt”</q> iti ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="17">।। 8 ।। kratau phalārthavādamaṅgavat kārṣṇājiniḥ ।। 17 ।।</ab>
<p>sthitamaśrūyamāṇādhikāreṣu sarvān pratyaviśiṣṭatvāt svargo-
'dhikāravidhiheturiti । yatra punaḥ viśeṣābhidhāyino'rthavādāḥ
śrūyante yatra saṃśayaḥ---kiṃ atrāpi svarga evādhikārahetuḥ । atha
vā'rthavādābhihitaṃ vastviti । pūrvapakṣavādī niyogādyadavagamyate
tadeva yuktamiti manyate । arthavādastvarthavāda eva ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1037"/>
<p>atrocyate---arthavādābhihitameva phalaṃ yuktam । kutaḥ ?
evamarthastutyaiva stutyartha upapanno bhavati । nanu ca niyogāt
svargārthataivāvagamyata ityuktam । sandigdhe ca vākyaśeṣānnirṇayaḥ
uktaḥ । atrocyate---satyaṃ saṃśayo nāsti । niścayo'pi naiva
vidyate । ataśca vākyaśeṣādyo'rtho'vagamyate sa eva
vākyārthaḥ । na cāpratipanne vākyārthe kevalānniyogāt
kiñcitpratipadyate । tasmātsūktamarthavādābhihitamevādhikāraheturiti ।
﻿<pb n="b1038"/>
yatpunarbhāṣyakāreṇoktaṃ---vibhaktimātraṃ kalpyate sa sahadhātvarthena
prayogavacano vidhāsyatīti । pakṣe kārye kāraṇaviśeṣakalpanā[nāya]
na khedanīyaṃ mana ityabhiprāyaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="1">।। 9 ।। 1kāmye karmaṇi nityaḥ svargo yathā yajñāṅge kratvarthaḥ ।। 20 ।।</ab>
<p>idamidānīṃ cintyate---yadi punarniyogāt svargādhikāraḥ ।
padāntarayogāccopādhayaḥ kalpyante śākamapyāharetivat ko doṣa
﻿<pb n="b1039"/>
syāt । na khalu kaściddoṣaḥ । kintu aniścitāt sāmānyādhikārāt
viśeṣa upādhiriti tu duśśakaṃ vak‍tum । kāṣṭhasaṃyuktamiva śākā-
haraṇam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="21">।। 10 ।। 1sārvakāmyamaṅgakāmaiḥ prakaraṇāt ।। 21 ।।</ab>
<p>sarvebhyaḥ kāmebhyo darśapūrṇamāsāviti kimayamanuvādaḥ । atha-
vā'yamapi vidhiriti prāptārthatvādanuvāda iti manyate । kathaṃ
prāptiḥ ? kiñcidaṅgadvāreṇa kiñcitsvata iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b1040"/>
nanu pradhānasaṃbandhitayaivaitacchrūyate kathamaṅgāpekṣo'nuvādaḥ । aṅga-
dvāramapi hi pradhānena vyapadiśyate yūpavat ।</p>
<p>atrābhidhīyate---pramāṇāntarāvagamyamidaṃ yadutānyasaṃbandhī
anyena vyapadiśyata iti । siddhe cānuvāde pramāṇāntaragamyatā,
pramāṇāntaragamyatāyāṃ cānuvāda itītaretarāśrayatvam । tasmānnira-
pekṣācchabdānniyoga eveti manyāmahe । yūpe punararthāntaravidheyatvāt
pramāṇāntaraprameyatā yuktā ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="17">।। 11 ।। 1tatra sarve'viśeṣāt ।। 17 ।।</ab>
﻿<pb n="b1041"/>
<p>idamidānīṃ cintyate---sakṛtsarvakābhāvāptiḥ uta yāvatkāmaṃ
prayoga iti । sarvakāmanimittatayā śravaṇāt na prayoge viśeṣā-
vadhāraṇā śakyā । ekatvāditi pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । nanu ca sarvakāmo nāma
naiva kaścidastyadhikārī anadhikārācca phalotpatterasaṃbhavaḥ । ucyate
---yadi kāmanā aṅgaṃ syāt anutpannā satī nāṅgabhāva upapadyata iti
bhavati kāmanānāmanutpādaḥ sakṛtprayoge sarvaphalānutpattau hetuḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b1042"/>
iha tu sarvakāmairyuktasya kāmino'dhikāra iti na prayoga-
kāle kāmanotpāda upayujyate । tasmānnanimitte sati naimitti-
kasya vyāghāto bhavitu marhati । atrocyate---yāvatkāmaṃ
prayoga iti । evamadhikārasiddhirupapannā bhavati । na hi
akāminaḥ phalādhikāro'stīti ṣaṣṭhe vakṣyāmaḥ । nanu
ca prayogakāle kāmanotpādo'naṅgatvānnopayujyata ityuktam ।
﻿<pb n="b1043"/>
kena voktaṃ prayogakāle utpādo heturiti । adhikārāvagatāveva
sarvakāmitā yugapanna saṃbhavatītyuktamasmābhiḥ । asaṃbhave ca yugapat
sarvaniyogānupapattiḥ । tasmāt pratikāmamadhikāraḥ । yadvā
yathoddiṣṭakāmābhiprāyamiti bhāṣyakāreṇoktam anirdiṣṭānāmava-
gamābhāva ityabhiprāyaḥ । ato nirdiṣṭāpekṣī sarvaśabdaḥ sarvaṃ
kṛtamitivat । ataḥ siddhaṃ pratikāmaṃ prayoga iti । ata eva
ca viruddhānāmapi phalānāmadhikāraḥ siddhobhavati । sakṛtprayoge
hi maraṇāyuṣoranutpattiḥ syāt । tasmādyogasiddhirveti
sūktam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1044"/>
<p> evaṃ vā ।।</p>
<p>asminnadhikaraṇe niyogasya phalaṃ prati kiṃ śarīragrahaṇapūrvakaḥ
prayojakabhāvaḥ uta yāvacchrutaṃ prayok‍tṛtvamiti । tata pūrvapakṣavādī
śarīragrahaṇasya kāraṇāntarādarśanāt paśvādīnāṃ ca kāraṇāntareṇo-
papatteḥ śarīragrahaṇapūrvakaḥ phalākṣepa iti manyate । paśvādīnāṃ kāraṇaṃ
pratigrahādi pratyakṣaṃ bhaviṣyatīti । rāddhāntavādī tu yāvacchrutaṃ prayo-
k‍tṛtvaṃ manyate । kasmāt ? kevalaśravaṇāvagamyatvāt prayok‍tṛbhāvasya ।
﻿<pb n="b1045"/>
sarvāviśeṣāt । na hi gamyate viśeṣaḥ ihaiva amutraiva veti
kāmaśrutisāmānyāt ।</p>
<p>atra bhāṣyakāro'nantarādarśanamupanyasya pratyakṣānumānābhyāṃ
nopalabhāmahe śabdādavagamyata ityuktavān । tadayuk‍taṃ, śabdādapi
hi nānantaryamupalabhyata ityuktam । ayamabhiprāyaḥ bhāṣyakārasya
---sāmānyāvagamāt ihāmuṣminniti ca viśeṣānavagamāt śabdato
na pramāṇāntarābhāvaḥ ānantaryaṃ vihantīti । liṅgamuktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="19">।। 12 ।। 1samavāye codanāsaṃyogasyārthavattvāt ।। 19 ।।</ab>
<p>vājapeyeneṣ‍ṭvā bṛhaspatisavena yajeta’ iti lakṣaṇe ktyāpratya-
﻿<pb n="1046"/>
yotpattau kālaśravaṇāt kālārthaḥ saṃyoga iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।
samānakartṛkyordhātvarthayoḥ anvayāvagateḥ dhātusaṃbandha evāyam ।
sa ca aṅgāṅgibhāvādṛte na saṃbhavatīti aṅgāṅgitaiveti rāddhāntaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="32">।। 13 ।। 1ubhayārthamiti cet ।। 32 ।।</ab>
<p>paurṇamāsīṃ saṃsthāpyeti parisamāptivacanatvāt saṃsthāśabdasya
nāṅgāṅgibhāvaḥ paurṇamāsyāṃ saṃbhavatīti prakaraṇāt darśapūrṇamāsāṅgataiva
vaimṛdhasyeti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="1047"/>
<p>atrābhidhīyate---yadi samāptivacanatvāt saṃsthāśabdasya
nāṅgitvaṃ paurṇamāsyāḥ prakaraṇādapi naivāṅgitvaṃ saṃbhavati । atha
saṃsthāpyeti pūrvavihitāṅgakalāpaparisamāp‍tyabhiprāyo'yaṃ saṃsthā-
śabdaḥ evaṃ tarhi vākyāt paurṇamāsyaṅgataiva vaimṛdhasya । na ca
niyogaikye kaścidviśeṣaḥ asyāpyadhikārasaṃbandhāt । atassiddhaṃ
paurṇamāsyaṅgaṃ vaimṛdha iti ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="36">।। 14 ।। anutpattau tu kālaḥ syāt prayojanena sambandhāt ।। 36 ।।</ab>
﻿<pb n="1048"/>
<p>nirjñātaparāṅgabhāvayoḥ saṃbandhe niyogaḥ kālavidhānaparyavasāyyeva
karmaṇaḥ pratyabhijñānāt tasmāt kālārtho niyogaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="37">।। 15 ।। utpattikālaviśaye kālaḥ syādvākyasya tatpradhāna-
tvāt ।। 37 ।।</ab>
<p>darśapūrṇamāsābhyāmiṣṭvā somena yajena’ ityatrākarmavidhānāt
kālārtho niyoga ityuktam । tatpunaridamayuktam । vājapeyeneṣṭvā
bṛhaspatisavena yajetetyanenāviśeṣāt tenātrāpi kālārthena niyogena
bhavitavyam । ubhayatra vā karmārthatvaṃ niyogasya । vaktavyo vā
﻿<pb n="1049"/>
viśeṣaḥ । atra kaiścidanārabhya vidhānaṃ viśeṣa uktaḥ । kaḥ punaranāra-
bhyavidhānena viśeṣa upalabhyate ? ayaṃ viśeṣaḥ---karmadvayavidhānaṃ
tāvanna saṃbhavati aneneṣṭvā anena yajetetyevamādiṣu । anārabhya-
vidhāne ca naikamapi karma prakṛtamasti । tasmānnāmataḥ prasiddha-
karmopādānaṃ kālaniyogārtham । uktaṃ ca nāmadheyamapi guṇaphalopabandhe-
nārthavat iti । vājapeye punaḥ prakṛtatvādvājapeyasya karmāntara-
vidhānaṃ śrutyopapadyate । nāma ca taddharmātideśārthaṃ bhaviṣyati
prakaraṇāntare prayojanānyatvamiti nyāyāt । anārabhyavidhāne
punaḥ prakaraṇāntarābhāvāt dvayorapi (akarmārthatvaṃ yuktam)
﻿<pb n="1050"/>
karmāntaratvamayuktam । yeṣāṃ punaḥ darśapūrṇamāsaprakaraṇa evaitatpaṭhyate
tatra kā kathā bhavatu । tatrāṅgāṅgibhāvaḥ kā no bādhā ? atha vā pari-
hṛtamevaitat śākhāntarādhikaraṇe sarvaśākhāpratyayamekaṃ karmeti vadatā ।
kathaṃ parihṛtaṃ ? tadevedaṃ śāstramiti yuktam । bhavatvevaṃ tathāpi na
vidmaḥ kiṃ anārabhyavādasya yo'rthaḥ tena śās‍traṃ pratyabhijñāyatāṃ uta
prakaraṇe'pi yo'rthaḥ iti । avirodhādanārabhyavādena pratyabhijñānaṃ bheda-
vido manyante । tasmātsūktamiha kalārthaḥ saṃyoga iti । darśana-
muktam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="1051"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="38">।। 16 ।। phalasaṃyogastvacodite na syādaśeṣabhūtatvāt ।। 38 ।।</ab>
<p>atra saṃśayaḥ kiṃ yasya niyogaḥ tasya phalaṃ uta anyasya
niyogo'nyasya phalamiti । adhikārī ca niyujyate । yadarthaṃ
karma so'dhikārī sa eva niyujyate । yadarthaṃ karma so'dhikārī sa
eva niyujyate । anadhikāre ca pituḥ nāsya niyojyatā syāt ।
tasmādbhavati saṃśayaḥ । kiṃ yuktam ? niyojyasya pituḥ phalamiti ।
kutaḥ ? adhikārasidhyartho niyogaḥ na saṃbandhamātrāvagamyaḥ
tasmāt pituridaṃ phalaṃ putraphalānvayasya stutyā'nvayo bhavatu ।
lakṣaṇayā'dhikṛtaviśeṣaṇam । tathā ca kratusaṃbandhinimitte
﻿<pb n="1052"/>
niyojyasyaiva phalaṃ na kratunā saṃbadhyate । atrocyate
---yasya phalānvayaḥ tasyaiva phalaṃ nimittatayāpyadhikāra-
siddheḥ । itarasya putrajanmanā nimittenāpi puruṣārthatā'stī-
tyadhikārasiddhiḥ । kathaṃ tarhi phalapadaṃ ? na karma viśeṣaṇaṃ, nāpyadhi-
kāropanipāti । ucyate---bhaviṣyatyadhikāropanipāti । katha-
mevaṃvidhasya putrajanmano'dhikāriviśeṣaṇatvena śravaṇāt । tasmādyasya
niyogastasyaiva phalamiti aviruddhametat prītyāpyadhikārasiddheḥ ।
yaduk‍taṃ kratusaṃbandhe niyojyasyaiva phalamiti, yuktamadhikārānu-
﻿<pb n="1053"/>
praveśānnimittasyeti ṣaṣṭhe vakṣyāmaḥ ।</p>
<p>evaṃ vā ।।</p>
<p><q>‘putre jāte’</q> iti śrūyate । tatra saṃśayaḥ---kiṃ jananānantarameva
naimittikaṃ bhavatu utāṅgopasaṃhāramapekṣate prakṛtivadabhiprāptamiti ।
yadyevaṃ kimiti kumārasya prāṇadhāraṇamutkarṣahetutvenopanyasyate ।
ekamevedamadhikaraṇamastu । sāṅgasya naimit‍tikatvāt na nimittāna-
ntaraṃ prayogaḥ saṃbhavati iti svakāla eva kartavyaḥ । na cānantarye-
'sati nimittatvavyāghātaḥ bhūtapratyayayogānnimittasya । na ca
pratīkṣaṇe bhūtatvamapaiti । tasmāt pṛthagadhikaraṇaṃ niṣprayojanamiva
pratibhāti ।</p>
﻿<pb n="1054"/>
<p>atrābhidhīyate---nimittānantaraṃ naimit‍tikamityautsargiko
nyāyaḥ na kāraṇādṛte kālotkarṣo'vagamyate । nanu ca kāraṇamuk‍taṃ
sāṅgasya naimit‍tikatvam । etadeva na vijānīmaḥ kiṃ nimittakāle
niyogāvagamāt viniyogāvagamyamaṅgaṃ tyajyatāṃ uta niyogakāla-
syotkarṣa iti । niyogārthatvādviniyogasyāṅgatyāgaṃ viniyoga-
vido manyante । yathā rajasvalādisparśanena pūrvāhṇādikālaḥ vihita
upekṣyate । ata etadbādhanārthaṃ pūrvamadhikaraṇam । yadi hi
niyogakāla evānuṣṭhānaṃ kriyate yadartho niyogastadeva hīyate ।
﻿<pb n="1055"/>
tasmānniyogakālāvagatirevotkraṣṭavyā । utkṛṣṭā cet svakāla
eva syānnāṅgatyāge pramāṇamastīti dvitīyamadhikaraṇaṃ
likhitam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="40">।। 17 ।। pradhānenābhisaṃyogādaṅgānāṃ mukhyakālatvam ।। 40 ।।</ab>
<p><q>‘vājapeyeneṣṭvā bṛhaspatisavena yajeta’</q> ityatra
saṃśayaḥ---kimeko niyogaḥ uta niyogadvayamiti । nanu
niyogadvitve'ṅgāṅgibhāvo nopapadyate । asti cāṅgāṅgitvaṃ,
tasmānna prayogabhedaḥ । bāḍhamupapadyate । viniyogādaṅgāṅgitā
﻿<pb n="1056"/>
prayogānyatvena viniyogānyatvam । nanu ca niyogānyatve śāstra-
bhedaḥ prāpnoti । bhavatu prayogāpekṣayā na kaściddoṣaḥ । viniyogā-
pekṣayā tvekamevedaṃ śāstram । kathaṃ punarekatve śāstrasya prayogabhedaḥ ?
kena vāryate vidhānabhedavat anubandhanimittakam । yadyathaivānu-
badhyate tat tathaiva tantraṃ bhinatti । iha tu prayogānubandhabhedāta
prayogabhedaḥ prāpnoti । bhavatu prayogabhedāpekṣayā na doṣaḥ ।
tasmānna śāstrāntarāpattiḥ kevalaṃ prayogabhedaḥ । yathā ca
prayogabhedastathā darśitam ।</p>
<trailer>iti bṛhatyāṃ caturthādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>
﻿<pb n="1057"/>
</section>
<section>
<head>caturthādhyāyasya caturthaḥ pādaḥ ।।</head>
<ab type="sutra" n="1">।। 1 ।। 1prakaraṇaśabdasāmānyāccodanānāmanaṅgatvam ।। 1 ।।</ab>
<p>nanu ca nāmadheyavicāre yajisāmānādhikaraṇyānnāma bhavatī-
tyuktam । kathaṃ punarayajyarthasyāpyetadabhidhānaṃ śaṅkyate ?
ataḥ pūrvapakṣa evāyaṃ nopapadyate । ucyate---iha tu
niyogaikyād‍yugapadabhidhānaṃ dhātvarthasya । niyogaikyaṃ ca
prakaraṇāyattamiti sarvaprakṛtābhidhāyī dhāturiti pūrvapakṣavādī manyate ।
﻿<pb n="1058"/>
evaṃ prāpte'bhidhīyate---satyaṃ prakaraṇānniyogaikyaṃ na punaḥ śrutānu-
bandhaparityāge kāraṇamasti । kathaṃ ? itikartavyatāpi hi
niyogaikyaṃ naiva viruṇaddhi । tathābhūtopadeśāditi vakṣyāmaḥ ।
ato yāgavyatiriktamaṅgamiti siddham ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="2">।। 2 ।। 1madhyasthaṃ yasya tanmadhye ।। 2 ।।</ab>
<p>nanu cātrāpi kramāt prakaraṇa balīya ityetadevodāhṛtam ।
﻿<pb n="1059"/>
sthitaṃ ca sarvārthatvaṃ tṛtīye । ucyate---satyaṃ viniyogāt sthitam ।
idānīṃ tu pṛthak prayojyatvādabhiṣecanīyaniyogasya tasya ca
sannidhānāt tenaivaikya yuktamiti manyate pūrvapakṣavādī । na viniyoga-
virodhaḥ ; pratyekasaṃbandhahetutvāta prakaraṇasya । ataḥ sannidhi-
viśeṣasyātikramo nopapadyate । atrocyate---sthitamaikaśabdyamadhi-
kāravidheḥ । tataḥ kiṃ ? idaṃ tato bhavati । yasyaiva prayogānubandha-
bhedaḥ tasyaiva pṛthak prayogo'vasīyate svenetikartavyatā-
kālāpena । yasya punaraṅgasyādhikāravidhireva prayogaṃ jñāpayati
na tasyāvāntaraprayogaḥ śakyate jñāpayitum । tasmāt
kramāt taddeśasyaiva anuṣṭhānamadhikāravidhisamadhigamyameva ।
﻿<pb n="1060"/>
prakaraṇāvirodhastvayaivoktaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="1">।। 3 ।। 1prakaraṇāvibhāge ca vipratiṣiddhaṃ hyubhayam ।। 5 ।।</ab>
<p>purastādupasadāṃ saumyena pracarantīti । kaḥ khalvāgnimārutā-
dūrdhvamanūyājaiścarantītyanenāsya viśeṣaḥ । na khalu kaścidviśeṣaḥ ।
kimityadhikaraṇāntaraṃ saumyādīnāṃ anyadadhikaraṇāntaram । kā no
bādhā ? । na khalu kaścidbhavato bādhā । adhikaraṇānarthakyaṃ tu
bhavati । ayaṃ tarhi viśeṣaḥ । prakaraṇāt sarvasya prādhānyaṃ iti-
kartavyatātvaṃ vā rājasūye । asaṃyuk‍taṃ ca prakaraṇādityuktam ।
﻿<pb n="1061"/>
tasmādvākyādupasadaṅgameveti pūrvapakṣavādino'bhiprāyaḥ । api ca
sannidhānaviśeṣeṇopasadaṅgataiva yuktā, adhikāraniyogāt ।</p>
<p>atrābhidhīyate---na tāvadupasadāṃ prakaraṇamasti adhikāra-
nibandhanatvāt prakaraṇasya । nanu ca vākyādupasadaṅgatvamityuktam
nobhayapadasaṃbandhābhāvāt vākyaṃ saṃbhavati । tasmāt
purastādupasadāmityeva saṃbandhaḥ । atha kasmādupasadāṃ saumyenetyeṣa
saṃbandhaḥ na bhavati । purastādityananvayaḥ prāpnoti
﻿<pb n="1062"/>
purastāditi saṃbandhe kālavidhānāt saumyena carantītyaviruddham ।
tasmādidamapi āgnimārutādityanenāviśiṣṭam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="7">।। 4 ।। 1phalavadvok‍tahetutvāditarasya pradhāna syāt ।। 7 ।।</ab>
<p>sāṅgrahaṇyāṃ tu phalavatsannidhau aphalaṃ tadaṅgamiti siddhepyanu-
ṣaṅganivṛttyarthamidamadhikaraṇam । darśitaṃ ca ।</p>
﻿<pb n="1063"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="8">।। 5 ।। 1dadhigraho naimittikaḥ śrutisaṃyogāt ।। 8 ।।</ab>
<p>anityadoṣanirharaṇārthasaṅkīrtanāt naimittikaṃ manyate pūrvapakṣa-
vādī । khadiravadubhayārthatāmācāryadeśīyaḥ । nityatve sati jyeṣṭha-
śabdopapattiriti manyate । rāddhāntastu nimittasaṃyogābhāvāt
na doṣanirharaṇārthatayā naimittikatvamasya śakyate kalpayitum ।
kimiti na śakyate naimittikadoṣanirharaṇānyathānupapattyā
tasyāpi naimittikatvaṃ bhavitumarhati । satyaṃ yadyanyathā
nopapadyate । arthavādatayā tūpapadyata eveti na kalpanāmarhati ।
﻿<pb n="1064"/>
sārūpyādyuktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="12">।। 6 ।। vaiśvānaraśca nityaḥ syānnityaiḥ samānasaṅkhyatvāt ।। 12 ।।</ab>
<p>anityadoṣanirharaṇārthavādatayāpyupapadyata iti yadyu-
cyeta vaiśvānare'pi nityatā bhavatīti pūrvapakṣavādino'bhimānaḥ ।
rāddhāntastu na brūmo doṣanirharaṇānnaimittikatvam nimitta-
saṃyoga evātra śrūyate । na ca nimittaśrutirarthavādatayā śakyate
vyākhyātum । śrutyarthe saṃbhavati nārthāntarakalpanopapadyate ।
darśanamuktam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="1065"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="14">।। 7 ।। 1ṣaṭ‌citiḥ pūrvavattvāt ।। 14 ।।</ab>
<p>ṣaṣṭhīṃ citimiti pūraṇapratyayāvagamāt nimittaśrutiḥ artha-
vādatayā varṇayituṃ nyāyyeti pūrvapakṣavādino'bhiprāyaḥ kutaḥ ?
vidheyānurodhāt adhikārakalpanā nyāyyeti manyate ।</p>
<p>rāddhāntastu satyamevaṃ yadi virodhaḥ syāt na tvatra virodhaḥ,
upadeśavivakṣayāpi pratyayārthopapatteḥ nāvaśyama(rthā)nuṣṭhānāpekṣayaiva
bhagavataḥ pāṇineḥ pūraṇasūtraṃ śakyate varṇayitum । tasmāda-
﻿<pb n="1066"/>
virodhaḥ । avirodhe ca na nimittaśratiḥ tyak‍tuṃ pāryate ।
tasmānnaimittikatvaṃ siddham । darśanopanyāsaparihārāvuktau ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="19">।। 8 ।। 1pitṛyajñaḥ svakālatvādanaṅgaṃ syāt ।। 19 ।।</ab>
<p>phalakalpanāto varaṃ lakṣaṇeti pūrvapakṣavādino'bhiprāyaḥ ।
darśādhikārānupraveśe sati nādhikārāntaraṃ śakyate kalpayitu-
mityuk‍taṃ bhavati । tasmādaṅgataivāmāvāsyāyāḥ pitṛyajñasya ।
atrocyate-naikaniyogatā saṃbhavati amāvāsyāyāmiva kālasaṃyogā-
﻿<pb n="1067"/>
viśeṣāt piṇḍapitṛyajñasya । nāmāvāsyāyāṃ śrautaḥ piṇḍapitṛyajñe
ca lakṣaṇeti viśeṣo'vagamyate । ubhayatra kālasaṃyogasya saṃbhavāt ।
tasmātpūrvāparaśrutistatkālalakṣaṇetyavirodhaḥ । prayojanamuktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="21">।। 9 ।। paśvaṅgaṃ raśanā syāt tadāgame vidhānāt ।। 21 ।।</ab>
﻿<pb n="1068"/>
<p>atrāpi ktvāpratyayasya kriyāntarāpekṣitvāt ekaniyoga-
tāṃ pūrvapakṣavādī manyate । tatra ca paśvarthataiva prāpnoti yūpasyāpi
tadarthatvāt । rāddhāntavādī tu samānakartṛkatāmātraṃ ktvāpratyayāda-
vagamyate na niyogaikyamiti yūpasyaḥ punaḥ dvitīyātaḥ prādhānyameva
yuktamiti rāddhāntitavān ।</p>
<p>nanu caikaniyogādṛte samānakartṛkataiva na saṃbhavati । satyaṃ
na saṃbhavati kintu adhikāraikyāt siddhaṃ samānakartṛkatvam ।
﻿<pb n="1069"/>
nanu ca kālalakṣaṇā naivātra saṃbhavati । uccāraṇakālavibhāgo hi
ktvāpratyayotpattau heturityuktam । satyamuktaṃ, sa evoccāraṇakālo-
'nuṣṭhānepi lakṣaṇayocyate । sarvatra ca kālavidhāviyameva prati-
pattirloke vede ca । samānakartṛkatāpi naiva tatrādriyate kāla-
niṣṭhatvānniyogasya । ata eva ca darśapūrṇamāsābhyāmiṣṭvā somena
yajeteti samānakartṛkatācodyaṃ parihṛtaṃ bhavati । prayojanamuktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="15">।। 10 ।। 1svaruścāpyekadeśatvāt ।। 15 ।।</ab>
<p>yūpasya svarupamiti svarumān yūpa iti gomānitivat
tādarthyaṃ manyate pūrvapakṣavādī । dṛṣṭo hi tādarthye sati
﻿<pb n="1070"/>
matvarthaḥ । evamatrāpītyabhiprāyaḥ । rāddhāntavādī tu yavamatītye-
vamādiṣu anaikāntyāt paśumanak‍tītī dvitīyānirdeśāt dṛṣṭārthaḥ-
tvācca paśvarthataiveti । ṣaṣṭhī tūtpat‍tisaṃyogepyupapannā cetyadoṣaḥ ।
prayojanamuktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="29">।। 11 ।। darśapūrṇamāsayorijyāḥ prādhānyaviśeṣāt ।। 29 ।।</ab>
﻿<pb n="1071"/>
<p>sthitaṃ rājasūyādhikaraṇe anijyā vyudasyante । yajiśabda-
saṃyogenādhikāraśravaṇāt । yatraiva ca dhāturvartate tatraivaupapadaṃ
nāmatayā vartata iti nāmadheyavicāre sthitam । ataḥ pūrvapakṣavādī
yāgamātra'vacano'yaṃ yajiḥ yatra yajiḥ tatraivopapadaṃ vartata iti
manvāno dvivacanāntasarūpamevedamabhidhānaṃ manyate । yatpunaḥ
<q>‘prayāje prayāje kṛṣṇalaṃ juhoti’</q> iti vikṛtiṣu darśanaṃ tat katha-
﻿<pb n="1072"/>
masmin pakṣe bhaviṣyati ? pramāṇāntaraṃ mṛgyaṃ yatreti vā,
vyāmoho vā, karmāntaraṃ vā nāmataśca dharmagrahaṇaṃ bhaviṣyati । yatpunaḥ
ya evaṃ vidvānamāvāsyāṃ yajata iti tat prakṛtasamudāyadvayaṃ kimiti
na parigṛhyate dvivacanayogāt । uktaṃ ca dhātvarthānusāryupapadamiti ।
darśaśabdāccānyatvāvagateḥ । tasmādrājasūyavadanijyaivātrāṅgamiti
sthitam । atrocyate---satyamidaṃ dhātvarthānusāryupapadamiti
﻿<pb n="1073"/>
tathāpi samudāyadvayasya prakṛtatvāt dvivacanasya cārthāntarānupapat‍teḥ ।
saṃbhavati ca svārthe sarūpakalpanāyā asaṃvāt । dhātvarthānusāri-
tāyāṃ cāvirodha upapadasya । kathaṃ ? naivedamupapadaṃ adhātvarthe pravṛttaṃ,
dhātvarthapravṛttau satyāṃ na nāmārthaparityāga upapadyate । kaścāsyārthaḥ
prakṛtasamudāyadvayavacanatā । evaṃ ca tadanusāritve upapanne
nārthāntarakalpanāyāṃ pramāṇamasti । nanu ca prakṛtayāgaparityāge
nāsti pramāṇaṃ ghātoḥ; kena vā uk‍taṃ aparityāge pramāṇamastīti
kintūpapadārthavirodhābhidhāne nāsti pramāṇamityuktamasmābhiḥ ।
﻿<pb n="1074"/>
yacca darśaśabdaśravaṇāt na prakṛtapratyabhijñānamastīti parihṛtaṃ
tadvākyaśeṣeṣvekārthatvadarśanāditi । śakyatvācca darśaśabde-
nāpi tadarthābhidhānasya । tasmātsūk‍taṃ phalavatsannidhāva-
phalaṃ tadaṅgamiti । yatpunaridamuk‍taṃ kasmānnānuṣaṅgo bhavatīti codyaṃ
parihṛtaṃ tadanuṣaṅgato vara[mitikartavyatā]kāṅkṣāparipūraṇamiti ।
anyathā tvanavasthaivākāṅkṣāyā iti । yadyavaṃ kimiti vyavā-
yānnānuṣajyete iti sāṅgrahaṇyāṃ darśitaṃ tatrāpyayameva nyāyo yuktaḥ
vaktavyo vā viśeṣaḥ ।</p>
<p>ayamabhidhīyate---yuk‍taṃ tatra prakṛtivaditikartavya-
tāyāṃ sthitāyāṃ nirākāṅkṣatvāt vyavāyādevānuṣaṅga-
niṣedhaḥ । iha punaraparyavasitatvāditikartavyatārthitāyāṃ sthitāyāṃ
﻿<pb n="1075"/>
pūraṇenaivaikaniyogatvaṃ yuktam । na punaradhikārāntarakalpaneti
sūktam । darśanāni coktāni । aṅgavatstutayaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="39">।। 12 ।। jyotiṣṭome tulyānyaviśiṣṭaṃ hi kāraṇam ।। 39 ।।</ab>
<p>iha tu dvivacanādyabhāvāt na yāgamātrapratipattiḥ
śakyate vārayitum । [jyotiṣṭomaśabdasya ca nāmadheyatvāt
pravṛttau nimittaṃ abhidheyaṃ nānvayītyuk‍taṃ nāmadheyavicāre] ।
﻿<pb n="1076"/>
nanu ca nāmataivātra hīyate viśeṣaṇamevaitattadā bhavati kiṃ na
śchinnam । tathāpi rāddhāntaḥ siddha eva । kintu viśeṣaṇa-
padamapi etannāmaiva arthāntarānupapatteḥ yajyarthasya viśeṣaṇa-
mātrāvagamahetutvāt । (tadetad‍‌dvitvamapi) । ato'nvitamapi
viśeṣaṇaniṣṭhamiti nāmaiva, arthāntarānupādānāt । stutidarśanaṃ
coktam ।</p>
<trailer>iti bṛhatyāṃ caturthādhyāyasya
caturthaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>
﻿<pb n="b1077"/>
﻿<pb n="b1078"/>
﻿<pb n="1079"/>
</section>
<section>
<head>atha bṛhatyāṃ</head>
</section>
<section>
<head>pañcamādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pādaḥ ।।</head>
<ab type="sutra" n="1">।। 1 ।। 1śrutilakṣaṇamānupūrvyaṃ tatpradhānatvāt ।। 1 ।।</ab>
<p>nanu kratvarthapuruṣārthacintāpi tatra vṛttā kimidaṃ prayojakā-
prayojakalakṣaṇaṃ vṛttamiti । ucyate---kramacintāyāmasyaivopayogāt
vakṣyamāṇaupayikatayā vṛttaṃ saṅkīrtyate na vṛttatayā । ekaprayogaprayuktanāṃ
hi kramo bhavati nāprayuktānāmiti prayojakāprayojakasaṅkīrtanam ।
﻿<pb n="1080"/>
yadi(prayojakāprayojaka)prayuktānāṃ kramaścintyate । avidheyastarhi
kramaḥ vihitaṃ hi prayujyate nāprayuktasya vidhānam ।
kena voktaṃ kramovidhīyata iti । vihitavitānamevātra
cintyate kiṃ yathāpratipannavihitavitānamanuṣṭheyaṃ utā-
niyameneti । kathaṃ punarayathāpratipannānuṣṭhānamāśaṅkyate ।
﻿<pb n="1081"/>
viniyogaśūnyatvādvihitavitānāvagamasya । nāntarīyako hi vidheyā-
vagatau vitānapratyayaḥ । ato yaścārthādartho na sa codanārtha iti
manvānaḥ pūrvapakṣavādī aniyamaṃ manyate । nanu ca <q>‘adhvaryurgṛhapatiṃ
dīkṣayitvā’</q> ityatra kramavidhānamevopanyastaṃ bhāṣyakāreṇa
vidheyāntarābhāvāditi vadatā । yadyevamayuktabhidam । astyevātra
vidheyāntaraṃ anenāmī dīkṣitavyā iti kartṛviśeṣavidhānam ।
﻿<pb n="1082"/>
adhvaryuvidhāvapi niyamaḥ eva । kiṃ heyamevedaṃ bhāṣyam ?
neti vadāmaḥ । yadi ktveti paurvāparyamabhidhāne
gamyate kartṛvidhau, tadanuṣṭhānaupayikatayaiva kartṛvidhāvupa-
yujyate na saṃbandhividhāviti tanniṣṭhā śrutirityuktam ।
﻿<pb n="1083"/>
aprayuktasyāvidheyatvameva heturuktaḥ । evaṃ tarhi hṛdayasyāgre'vadyati
atha jihvāyā atha vakṣasa ityetadapyudāharaṇaṃ atra syāt ।
﻿<pb n="1084"/>
neti brūmaḥ । pāṭhāvagatasyāyamathaśabdo'nuvādaḥ । kartṛviśeṣavidhau
punarnānyataḥ kramo'vagantuṃ śakyate ktvāpratyayāt iti
sūktam । kiṃ punaḥ kāraṇaṃ nāntarīyako'yaṃ niyamaḥ ādriyate ।
na hyacodanālakṣaṇasya codanālakṣaṇanirvṛttāvaṅgatopapadyate । satyaṃ
nopapadyate; ata eva ca nānuṣṭhīyate kintvarthaprāptameva
kramāntaraṃ niruṇaddhi tasyānavagamādityucyate । ato'napekṣatva-
mivā'vidhīyamānamapyupakārāyaiva bhavatīti na doṣaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="1085"/>
punaruktyādyāśaṅkā tūktā ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="2">।। 2 ।। 1arthācca ।। 2 ।।</ab>
<p>evaṃ tāvat ananyaparākṣaratayā niyamitaḥ kramaḥ । idānīṃ
kāryānurodhena kramo'pi niyamyate । tatparatvādanuṣṭhānasya । tatra prada-
rśitānyudāharaṇāni । kiṃ pāṭhakramasya bādho'yaṃ neti cintyate । neti
brūmaḥ । idamapi kramaniyamahetukāraṇaṃ na kasyacidvirodhitayā pradarśyate
﻿<pb n="1086"/>
balābalacintāyāṃ tu virodhe balīyastvaṃ ca । iha punaḥ
svarūpapratipattyarthamevedamupanyastam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="3">।। 3 ।। 1aniyamo'nyatra ।। 3 ।।</ab>
<p>yatra kramaniyamapramāṇaṃ nāsti uktaṃ vakṣmāṇaṃ vā tatrāniyama
eva । yathā śākhāntarīyāṅgavidhānaṃ śākhāntare upasaṃhriya-
māṇam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="4">।। 4 ।। 2krameṇa vā niyamyeta kratvekatve tadguṇatvāt ।। 4 ।।</ab>
<p>yatra punastātparyamakṣarāṇāṃ nāsti yathā adhvaryurityādau
na ca kāryato virodhaḥ । tatra kā kathā ? tatrāpi
﻿<pb n="1087"/>
pāṭhaniyamaḥ । nanu ca pāṭhakramāvagatirnirmūlā । na tasyāḥ
kiñcidavagatinimittamasti padānāṃ vākyārthāvagatihetutvāt ।
nirmūlā cāvagatirna pramāṇam । pūrvo dhāvatītyatra parānvaya iva ।
tasmādyatheṣṭamatra kramaparigrahaṇaṃ manyāmahe । ucyate---maivaṃ vocaḥ ।
vākyakrama iva vākyārthe kramo'pi śabdanibandhana eveti ।
yathā na śabdādṛte śabdakramo'vagamyate nārthādṛte'rthakramaḥ । yasmiṃśca
satyeva yadavagamyate'vyabhicārāt tat tasya nimittamiti
vadāmaḥ । tasmānnaidaṃ nimittam । ata eva ca niyamakramamadhyayanaṃ
﻿<pb n="1088"/>
dṛṣṭārthameva bhavati । anyatra kāryaviśeṣāt । ata eva ca
laukikāḥ pāṭhakrameṇa dhūpādiṣu vyutkramābhidhāne pratiṣedhaṃ kurvate ।
adṛṣṭārtheṣvapi darśitam । tasmādatrāpi na kramāntarakalpanā
yuk‍teti yuktam । ata eva ca <q>‘adhvaryurgṛhapatiṃ dīkṣayitvā’</q>
ityevamādiṣu tātparyamātrāt kramasiddhiḥ । nimittatvamātraṃ
hi atra parigṛhyate । tasmāt sanimittā pratipattiḥ pramāṇamityuktaṃ
pramāṇaparīkṣāyām । ato yāvatī sanimittā pratipattiḥ sā sarvaiva
kramāvadhāraṇe anyatra vā vedārthānuṣṭhānopakāriṇī pramāṇamiti
mantavyam । darśanamuk‍tam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="1089"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="8">।। 5 ।। 1pravṛttyā tulyakālānāṃ guṇānāṃ tadupakramāt ।। 8 ।।</ab>
<p>kimaparaṃ kāraṇaṃ kramaniyame ? pravṛttiriti brūmaḥ ।
pravṛttyāpi hi kramabuddhirupajāyate । kathaṃ punavaidikatvam ?
tadarthāśrayāt । tasmāt pravṛttirapi niyamahetuḥ । yatpunaridaṃ
bhāṣyakāreṇok‍taṃ <q>“evaṃ pradhānapratyāsat‍tirbhavati”</q> iti tathā
sauryādibhiśca sāmyamāśaṅkya punarvaiṣamyamupanyastaṃ kastasyo-
payogaḥ ? nātīva kramāvadhāraṇe upayujyate । astyatropayogaḥ
pravṛt‍tirnāma kramanirapekṣaṃ kvacidanuṣṭhānaṃ nirapekṣaṃ cedanuṣṭhānaṃ pravṛt‍taṃ na
﻿<pb n="1090"/>
punarapekṣāyāṃ (pramāṇaṃ)prayojanaṃ astīti manvānasyedamuttaraṃ
---pradhānapratyāsat‍tiḥ sahacodanāto'vagatā vaiṣamyāt pīḍitā
bhavati । sāmye punaḥ yathābhyanujñātaiva bhavati । tatsiddha‍yarthaṃ
niyamo'bhyupagantavyaḥ । sa ca prathamapravṛt‍tipūrvaka
iti tayaiva vyākhyāyate । sauryādidarśanamidānīṃ kimartham ?
﻿<pb n="1091"/>
yadi kramāvagatimātratayaiva krama ādriyate sauryādiṣu kaḥ
pradveṣaḥ । na khalu kaścit । anuṣṭhānānaupayikatayā tu pratītamapi
tyajyate varṇasvarūpamiva padeṣu (vākyeṣu) ekatvamiva graheṣu
ubhayatvamiva haviṣvu naitāvatā aupayikasyāpi tyāga upapadyate ।
﻿<pb n="1092"/>
ato'pekṣitaṃ pratipannamādriyate । pratipannamapyanapekṣitamu-
pekṣaṇīyameva । nanu caivaṃ sati pratipattiranarthikā prāpnoti । kena
vok‍taṃ pratipattera(na) rthavattvaṃ arthavatpratipattirevārthavattve hetuḥ na
pratipattimātraṃ, nāpratipattiḥ pratipattiparyantaiveti sūktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="13">।। 6 ।। 1sthānāccotpattisaṃyogāt ।। 13 ।।</ab>
<p>atra bhāṣyakāreṇa triṇavādiṣvadarśanāt samāmnāya[krama]sya
vidyamānasyāpyaviṣayatāṃ manvānaiḥ idamudāhṛtamityaviṣayatāṃ matveda-
mudāhṛtaṃ saha paśūnālabhata iti ।</p>
﻿<pb n="1093"/>
<p>atra ca adhikaraṇāntarasiddhamarthamupādāya sahapaśūnā-
labhata iti savanīyasthāne sahatvamiti sthite kaḥ kramaniyama
iti cintyate kimatrāpi pravṛt‍tireva nimittaṃ uta
nimittāntaramastīti । tatra pūrvapakṣavādī avaśyaṃbhāvini
krame yadi pravṛt‍tirneṣyate pūrvāvagatapāṭhādeva niyama iti
manyate । rāddhāntavādī tu sahavacanena sthānasyābādhi-
tatvāt savanīyasyaiva pūrvamanuṣṭhānaṃ nyāyyamityuktavān ।
﻿<pb n="1094"/>
yadyevamagnīṣomīyānubandhyayoḥ kā vārtā ? kathaṃ paurvāparyaṃ atra ।
kimanayā'nupanyastayā cintayā ? yadvā sthānavat kālabādho'pya-
yukta iti agnīṣomīya eva pūrvam । yadyevaṃ savanīyādapi tarhi
pūrvatvaṃ bhavitumarhati । na । vihitatvāt savanīyakālasya pracayā-
vagamyatvādagnīṣomīyakālasya । vidhānārthatvācca pracayasya vihitaṃ
balīyaḥ । evaṃ tarhi balābalacinteyam (na pramāṇasyārthānniyamo
yuktaḥ) । naivaṃ, sthite pramāṇāntaratve balavadabalatvamiti sūktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="14">।। 7 ।। 1mukhyakrameṇa cāṅgānāṃ tadarthatvāt ।। 14 ।।</ab>
﻿<pb n="1095"/>
<p>yatra yaugapadyena codanā sārasvatau bhavati iti tatra kiṃ
pramāṇāntaramasti kramaniyamasya aṅgānāṃ uta yatheṣṭā pravṛt‍tiriti ।
tantreṇoccāraṇācchās‍trasya na kramaḥ pratīyate ityabhiprāyaḥ ।</p>
<p>evaṃ prāpte'bhidhīyate---mukhye kramadarśanāt aṅgeṣvapi kramo
yuktaḥ । evaṃ ca sati yāvadanujñātaṃ vyavadhānaṃ bhaviṣyati ।
aniyame hi anujñātātikramaḥ । kramabādho na yukta iti ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="15">।। 8 ।। 1 prakṛtau tu svaśabdatvādyathākramaṃ pratīyeta ।। 15 ।।</ab>
<p>idānīṃ pāṭhamukhyayorvirodhe cintyate । tatra mukhyā-
﻿<pb n="b1096"/>
rthatvādaṅgānāṃ mukhyakramo balīyāniti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । evaṃ ca
prayogacodanānugrahaḥ pratyāsat‍teḥ । atrābhidhīyate---na pratītasya
bādho yuktaḥ pāṭhācca nirapekṣāt kramo'vagato'ṅgānāṃ nānyāpekṣayā
bādhituṃ yuktaḥ । nanu ca pratyāsat‍teḥ prādhānyācca balavat‍toktā ।
satyamuktā---ayuktā tu sā । yathāpratītaṃ hi prayogavacano gṛhṇāti ।
na prayogavacanādaṅagāvagatiḥ । aṅgaṃ sat prayogavacanena gṛhyata
ityuk‍tam । tasmāt yathāvagamaṃ pratyāsattiḥ । na pratyāsāt‍terava-
gamo'ṅgānāṃ, ataḥ pāṭho balīyāniti yuktam । uktaṃ ca
svaśabdatvāditi ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1097"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="16">।। 9 ।। 1mantratastu virādhe syāt prayogarūpasāmarthyāt tasmā-
dutpattideśaḥ saḥ ।। 16 ।।</ab>
<p>mantrabrāhmaṇapāṭhavirodhe kiṃ balīya iti । aniyama iti prāpte
ucyate---mantrakramo balīyāniti । kutaḥ ? pāṭhasyānanyaparatvāt ।
prayojyatvānmantrāṇām । nanu brāhmaṇepyananyapara eva pāṭhakramaḥ ।
yatpunaḥ (kramotpattiḥ)karmotpattiḥ prayojanamityuk‍taṃ, vākyasya
tatprayojanaṃ na pāṭhakramasya । ucyate---utpattyarthaḥ sa pāṭhakramaḥ,
na prayogārtha ityuktaṃ bhavati । mantre punaḥ prayogārthaḥ kramo bhavatīti
balavattvam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1098"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="17">।। 10 ।। 1tadvacanādvikṛtau yathā pradhānaṃ syāt ।। 17 ।।</ab>
<p>kiṃ mukhyakramādvikṛtau kramaḥ uta pāṭhakramāt prakṛtau yathā
nirjñāto'ṅgakramaḥ vikṛtāvapi tathaiva prayok‍tavya iti । kiṃ yuk‍taṃ ?
prayogārthatvāt kramasya vikṛtau prayogāvagamāt yathāvikṛti
prayoga iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।</p>
<p>rāddhāntastu na nirjñātakramaṃ prayogavacano bādhitumarhati ।
nirjñātasya hi prayogo aṅgānāmiva kramasya(āha) । anirjñāte hi
hetvantarakalpanā na niścite । tasmādyathā prakṛtau tathā vikṛtā-
vapyaṅgānāṃ prayoga iti ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1099"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="18">।। 11 ।। vikṛtiḥ prakṛtidharmatvāt tatkālā syāt yathā-
śiṣṭam ।। 18 ।।</ab>
<p>sadyaskāladvayahakālacintā । keyaṃ kramacintāyāṃ ? krama-
sidhyartheti brūmaḥ । sadyaskālatāyāmanyathā kramo bhavati । dvayaha-
kālatāyāṃ cānyathā । tasmād‌yukto vicāraḥ । tatra prakṛtivaditi
dvayahakālatāṃ manyate pūrvapakṣavādī । aharantarepi savanaśrutera-
viśeṣāt । rāddhāntī tu kālāntaraśravaṇāt na prākṛtaṃ kālamapekṣata
iti sadyaskālatāṃ manyate । savanāni caikāhaḥ saṃbandhānyeva śrutyā'va-
gamyamānāni na kāraṇādṛte'harantarāpekṣāṇi yuktāni kalpayitum ।
﻿<pb n="b1100"/>
darśanamuktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="12">।। 12 ।। aṅgānāṃ mukhyakālatvādyathoktamutkarṣe syāt ।। 23 ।।</ab>
<p>aśrūyamāṇānāmutkarṣavākye'pakarṣavākye ca kimityutkarṣāpa-
karṣau । satyaṃ śrutasya padārthasya utkarṣo'pakarṣo vā śrūyate na
punaruparitanamādhastyaṃ vā'kṛtveti । na cedidamavagamyate kramāda-
vagatamanuṣṭhānaṃ kena vāryate । ataḥ kimatrotkarṣavākye'śrutatvaṃ
kariṣyati । anyataḥ siddheḥ । tasmāt yuktamuk‍taṃ---tadādi
vā'bhisaṃbandhāt tadantamapakarṣe syāditi ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1101"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="25">।। 13 ।। 1pravṛttyā kṛtakālānām ।। 25 ।।</ab>
<p>kimalaṅkaraṇādayo dharmāḥ praiṣottarakālaṃ kartavyā uta pāṭhādevā-
vagatāḥ saumikā iti । tatra vacanabalāt nirvāpamātrameva madhye
kartavyaṃ, ato'niyama iti prāpte abhidhīyate---prokṣaṇādayaḥ kartavyāḥ
anirjñātakartavyatā hi pāṭhānniyamyate । na punaḥ nirjñātakartavyatāṃ
niruṇaddhi pāṭhaḥ । praiṣāt praiṣārthakartavyatā vijñāyate । ataḥ paraṃ tu
pāṭhānniyamaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1102"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="27">।। 14 ।। 1asaṃyogāt‍tu tadeva pratikṛṣyeta ।। 27 ।।</ab>
<p>dīkṣāsu yūpaṃ chinattītyapakarṣaḥ śrūyate tatra tadantāśaṅkā-
nivṛttyarthamidamadhikaraṇam । abhisambandhābhāvāt । yāvadvacana-
mapakarṣa iti ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="28">।। 15 ।। 2prāsaṅgikaṃ ca notkarṣedasaṃyogāt ।। 28 ।।</ab>
<p>prāsaṅgikepyayaṃ tulyo heturiti prāsaṅgikaṃ ca notkarṣedityuktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="29">।। 16 ।। 3tathā'pūrvam ।। 29 ।।</ab>
﻿<pb n="b1103"/>
<p>paurṇamāsyāṃ pāṭhakramāt kramasaṃbandho nirjñāta iti
tadapakarṣa iti tadantāpakarṣaṃ manyate pūrvapakṣavādī । rāddhāntavādī
tu na paurṇamāsīprakṛtikamāmāvāsyaṃ karmeti manvānaḥ apakarṣottara-
kālameva kramo niyamyate śeṣāṇāmiti yāvadvacanamapakarṣamuktavāt ।
kāryavirodhaścābhyuccayaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="30">।। 17 ।। 1sāntapanīyāṃ tūtkarṣedagnihotraṃ savanadvaiguṇyāt ।। 30 ।।</ab>
<p>parārthamuddhṛte'gnau prasaṅgādṛte nāgnihotraṃ hotavyaṃ
iti manvānaḥ pūrvapakṣavādī utkarṣamuktavān ।
﻿<pb n="b1104"/>
rāddhāntavādī tu nimittatvātkālasyānutkarṣaṃ manyate । kathaṃ punaḥ
kālo nimittaṃ ? tasmin sati prayogāt na punaḥ adhikāri-
viśeṣaṇatvāt ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1105"/>
<p>ato nimitte sati naimittikena bhavitavyamityarthāt
prasaṅgasiddhiḥ । ato'nutkarṣaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="35">।। 18 ।। ṣoḍaśī cokthyasaṃyogāt ।। 35 ।।</ab>
<p>ṣoḍaśinyapyaṅgakālavirodhāta kādācitkatvāccotkarṣasya anu-
tkarṣaṃ manyate pūrvapakṣavādī । rāddhāntavādī tu avaśyaṃbhāvitvā-
cchāstrātikramasya varaṃ aṅgaśāstrātikrama ityuktavān ।</p>
<trailer>iti bṛhatyāṃ pañcamādhyāyasya
prathamaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>
﻿<pb n="b1106"/>
</section>
<section>
<head>bṛhatī</head>
</section>
<section>
<head>pañcamādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ ।।</head>
<ab type="sutra" n="1">।। 1 ।। 1sannipāte pradhānānāmekaikasya guṇānāṃ sarvakarma
syāt ।। 1 ।।</ab>
<p>nanu ca pravṛttyā kramo niyataḥ । kimidamekaikasya kṛts‍namiti ।
ucyate---sthita etasminnadhikaraṇe tat । iha punaḥ pūrvapakṣavādī
manyate sakalapadārthānuṣṭhānenāpi sahatvamupapadyata eva । kimiti
kālavyavadhānaṃ kalpyate । evamevānujñātamupapannaṃ bhavati ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1107"/>
<p>rāddhāntavādī tu sahatvacodanādekaikasya padārthasya sahānuṣṭhāna-
mavagamyamānaṃ na śakyate tyak‍tum । atastadanurodhena vyavadhānānu-
jñānaṃ na tatparityāgeneti padārthānusamayamuktavān । adhikaraṇāntaraṃ
veti kāryavirodhāt sahatvāvagamatyāgaḥ pāṭhavat ।</p>
