<ab type="sutra" n="4">।। 3 ।। 1muṣṭikapālāvadānāñjanābhyañjanavapanapāvaneṣu caikena ।। 4 ।।</ab>
<p>asminnadhikaraṇe anāvṛttenāpi muṣṭyādinā kṛtaṃ
śāstrārthaṃ manyamānaḥ pūrvapakṣavādī padārthānusamayamuktavān ।
﻿<pb n="b1108"/>
rāddhāntavādī tu codanātaḥ padārthādhyavasānaṃ vaidikeṣu ca na lokavat
pramāṇāntarāvaseyam । ekaṃ cedaṃ śās‍traṃ caturo muṣṭhīnnirvapatīti
dvirhaviṣo'vadyatīti ca । tasmācchāstrārthānusamayo nyāyya iti
manyate ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="6">।। 4 ।। 1saṃyukte tu prakramādaṅgaṃ syāditarasya tadarthatvāt ।। 6 ।।</ab>
<p>yadi śāstrādanusamayo dvirhaviṣo'vadyatīti ekatvā-
cchāstrasya etāvataivānusamaya eva nyāyyaḥ iti pūrvapakṣaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b1109"/>
tasmāt pradānāntamevānusametavyamiti siddham ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="7">।। 5 ।। 1vacanāt‍tu parivyāṇāntamañjanādi syāt ।। 7 ।।</ab>
<p>arthādyūpadhāraṇamiti pūrvapakṣavādī padārthānusamayaṃ manyate ।
śāstrabhedāt śāstrārthānāṃ saha codanāt । rāddhānta-
vādī tu vihitopapattyarthatvātkramasya kāṇḍānusamayaṃ manyate ।
nanu ca dṛṣṭārthatvādanyenāpi tat kriyata ityuktam ।
﻿<pb n="b1110"/>
satyaṃ yadyarthād dṛṣṭārthatā syāt । vidhau tu sati dṛṣṭepyarthe na
śāstrārtho vyatikramituṃ śakyate । darśitametat ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="10">।। 6 ।। 1paśugaṇe tasya tasyāpavarjayeta paś‍vekatvāt ।। 10 ।।</ab>
<p>atrāpi śāstrabādhaṃ manvānaḥ kāṇḍānusamayaṃ manyate
pūrvapakṣavādī । rāddhāntavādī tu padārthānusamayepyabādhaṃ manvānaḥ
sahacodanānugrahāya padārthānusamaya eva nyāyya ityuktavān ।
﻿<pb n="b1111"/>
man‍troccāraṇatan‍tratā ca sahatve liṅgam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="13">।। 7 ।। 1nānābījeṣvekamulūkhalaṃ vibhavāt ।। 13 ।।</ab>
<p>kaḥ punaratra viśeṣo'vadānādihomaparyantānusamaya ityanenādhi-
karaṇena । na khalu kaścidviśeṣaḥ । kimarthaṃ tarhīdamadhikaraṇaṃ ?
vidhānāt padārthāvacchedo bhavatīti pūrvapakṣavādino'bhimānaḥ ।</p>
<p>rāddhāntavādī tu vidheyānyatvena vidhānopapattau na padārthā-
vacchedāya prabhavo'stīti pūrvok‍ta eva nyāyyaḥ । anena ca
﻿<pb n="b1112"/>
viśeṣeṇa tadapyatrodāharaṇam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="16">।। 8 ।। 1vikāre tvanūyājānāṃ pātrabhedā'rthabhedāt syāt ।। 16 ।।</ab>
<p>kaḥ punarayaṃ kramacintāyāṃ pātrabhedopanyāsaḥ । kramasiddha‍yarthaṃ
iti brūmaḥ । bhedābhede kramānyatvadarśanāt । tatra pūrvaḥ pakṣo-
dravyavikāraśaṅkyā pātravikāraśaṅkyā ca । kālānyatvena
copapatteḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1113"/>
<p>rāddhāntastu dravyavikārāpatteḥ kālānyatve ca grahaṇayoḥ
sahāvagamabādhāt tadanuguṇaḥ pātrabhedo nyāyya iti siddham ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="17">।। 9 ।। 1prakṛteḥ pūrvoktatvādapūrvamante syāt na hyacoditasya
śeṣāmnānam ।। 17 ।।</ab>
<p>vaikṛtānāṃ pāṭhakramaḥ prākṛtairvyavadhīyate neti cintā । vyavadhī-
yata iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । padārthānuṣṭhānena vyavadhānāvagamāt ।</p>
<p>rāddhāntastu vaikṛtaprayogavacanāt prākṛtapadārthāvagamāt (a)
vyavadhānam । atassūk‍taṃ ante tu bādarāyaṇa iti ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1114"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="21">।। 10 ।। 1kṛtadeśāt‍tu pūrveṣām sadeśaḥ syāt tena pratyakṣa-
saṃyogāt nyāyamātramitarat ।। 21 ।।</ab>
<p>rājasūyepi videvanādayo vaikṛtena pāṭhena viruddha‍yamānā
nānte'nuṣṭhānamarhanti । nyāyamātramitaraditi ।</p>
<p>etaduk‍taṃ bhavati---nānte'nuṣṭhānaṃ kenacitkrameṇāvagamyate ।
kiṃ tarhi ? pūrvāvagamavirodhāt ante'nuṣṭhānamiti nyāyamātra-
mityucyate ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1115"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="22">।। 11 ।। 1prākṛtācca purastāt ।। 22 ।।</ab>
<p>atrāpi prākṛtakramāvagamāt prayogacodanāta eva ante'nu-
ṣṭhānaṃ manyate pūrvapakṣavādī । punaḥ śrutistu ananyārthā kramamevā-
vagamayatīti rāddhāntaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="23">।। 12 ।। 2sannipātaścedyathoktamante syāt ।। 23 ।।</ab>
﻿<pb n="b1116"/>
<p>atrāpi dīkṣaṇīyāsaṅkīrtanaṃ pūrvavat kramārthaṃ manyate pūrvapakṣa-
vādī । tat‍tu pūrvapadārthakramaparatayaivoktamiti(vopayuktamiti) ।
rāddhāntavādī tu parastādyathok‍taṃ nyāyyaṃ manyate । kiṃ punaḥ kāraṇaṃ
pūrvasminnevopayujyate na punaḥ parasminnapīti । atrocyate---parato'na-
nyatvāvagamāt pūrvasmiṃścānyatvāvagateḥ yuktamuktam ।</p>
<trailer>iti bṛhatyāṃ pañcamasya
dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>
﻿<pb n="b1117"/>
</section>
<section>
<head>bṛhatyāṃ</head>
</section>
<section>
<head>pañcamādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ ।।</head>
<ab type="sutra" n="1">।। 1 ।। 1vivṛddhiḥ karmabhedāt pṛṣadājyavattasya tasyopadiśyeta ।। 1 ।।</ab>
<p>kramārtha eva pratyekasamudāyasambandhaścintyate । pratyekasambandhe
hi vyavadhānamahatvaṃ samudāyasambandhe tvalpatvam । tasmād‍yuktā
cintā । kiṃ punaryuk‍taṃ ? pratyekamabhisaṃbandha iti । pratipradhānaṃ guṇā
āvartanta iti nyāyāt । nanu ca pṛthaktvaniveśinī saṅkhyetyuktam ।
satyamuktaṃ vidhānavaśāt‍tu yathopapadyate tathopakalpanīyam ।
﻿<pb n="b1118"/>
ata eva <q>‘pañcadaśānyājyāni’</q> iti ca pratyekamabhisaṃbandhaḥ ।
atrocyate---na vidhānaṃ padārthamanyathā kartumutsahate ।
padārthānurodhī hi vidhiḥ na vidhyanurodhinaḥ padārthāḥ । <q>‘agninā
siñcet’</q> ityevamādiṣu darśitam । tasmāt yāvatpṛthaktvaṃ
tāvadabhyāsakalpanā na sambhavatīti samudāyābhisambandhaḥ ।
pṛṣadājye tvetadviparītaṃ iti pratyekamabhisaṃbandhaḥ । yadapyuk‍taṃ
pañcadaśānyājyānīti āvṛttau ḍapratyayaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="3">।। 2 ।। 1svasthānāt‍tu vivṛddha‍yeran kṛtānupūrvyatvāt ।। 3 ।।</ab>
﻿<pb n="b1119"/>
<p>saṅkhyāsampattyarthamabhyase prāpte idaṃ cintyate---kiṃ daṇḍakalita-
vadabhyāsaḥ uta svasthāna iti । samudāyābhisambandhāt daṇḍakalita-
vadabhyāsammanyate pūrvapakṣavādī । pūrvapratītakramānurodhāt svasthāne
yukta iti rāddhāntaḥ । samudāyasaṃbandhasya tūbhayathāpyavirodhaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="1">।। 3 ।। 1samidhyamānavatīṃ samiddhavatīṃ ka cāntareṇa dhāyyāḥ syuḥ
dyāvāpṛthivyorantarāle samarhaṇāt ।। 4 ।।</ab>
<p>nanu vacane sati pūrvapakṣa eva na sambhavati । arthavādapūrvakaṃ
tadvacanamiti pūrvapakṣavādī nyāyānusāreṇāpi gacchatyeveti manyate ।
﻿<pb n="b1120"/>
rāddhāntastu nāyathārthagrahaṇe pramāṇamastyarthavādasya iti na śabdārthaṃ
nyāyo niruṇaddhi iti nyāyamātraṃ tadityuktam । ato yathārtha-
vādamevedaṃ vidhānaṃ nyāyyaṃ, dhāyyāśabdanirūpaṇaṃ tu prāsaṅgikam ।
pradarśitaṃ ca tat ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="7">।। 4 ।। 1stomavivṛddhau bahiṣpavamāne purastāt paryāsādāgantavaḥ
syuḥ tathāhi dṛṣṭaṃ dvādaśāhe ।। 7 ।।</ab>
<p>nyāyamātraṃ vacanaṃ bādhituṃ na kṣamata ityuktam । vacanaṃ
cedaṃ vṛṣaṇvantastṛcā bhavanti tṛca uttamaḥ paryāsa iti ।
nanu dvādaśāhe etadvacanaṃ, atadvikāreṣu keyamāśaṅkā ।
﻿<pb n="b1121"/>
uttamaśabdaśravaṇāt1 । kimidamuttamaśabdaśravaṇāditi ? uttamaḥ
paryāso bhavatīti padārthāṅgatāṃ manyate pūrvapakṣavādī । nanu ca
padārthāṅgatve ānarthakyamuktam । na tat paryāse bhavitumarhati ।
sarvasya paryāsasyārthavattvāt kratusaṃbandhinī hi paryāsasaṃjñā
udgīthavata । tasmād‍yuktamuktam । dvādaśāhavikṛtiṣvapi nirā-
karaṇīya evāyamartha ityupanyāsaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1122"/>
<p>atrābhidhīyate-nāyaṃ padārthadharmaḥ । kastarhi ? kratudharmaḥ । kathaṃ ?
prakaraṇāt dvādaśāhaniyogaikyamavagamyate । na kratvantaraniyogai-
kyam । nanu ca padārthānusārī niyogaḥ । padārthānusārepyatrā-
virodhāt । tasmānna kratvantarasaṃbandhakalpanāyāṃ pramāṇamasti ।
dvādaśāhavikāreṣvevaitat syāt । na vā tatrāpi । atha vā
vṛṣaṇvatāṃ dharmaḥ । nanu ca padārthadharmo na bhavatītyuktam, satyamuktaṃ,
﻿<pb n="b1123"/>
na punaḥ kratvarthāparityāgeneti । tasmātsūk‍taṃ tadvikāreṣvapi na
bhavatīti ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="13">।। 5 ।। 1ante tūttarayordadhyāt ।। 13 ।।</ab>
<p>kathamatra pūrvapakṣo yuktaḥ, vacanamadṛṣ‌ṭvetyayuktamidam । adhīta-
vedasya hi dharmajijñāsā । ayaṃ tarhi pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । idamapi dvādaśāha
eva vacanam atra viśeṣāgrahaṇāt tadvikāreṣu bhavatu ata-
dvikāreṣu mābhūditi pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1124"/>
<p>atrocyate---āvāpanibandhanametadvacanaṃ yāvadāvāpaṃ bhavitu-
marhati । kathaṃ tarhi prakṛtaniyogaikyaṃ ? na, kāryāśritatvādasya
vidheḥ vṛṣaṇvatsūpadeśāśraya ityuktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="15">।। 6 ।। 1graheṣṭakamaupānuvākyaṃ savanacitiśeṣaḥ syāt ।। 15 ।।</ab>
<p>atrāpyaṅgāṅgicintā kramārthaiva । kathamatra pūrvapakṣaḥ ?
﻿<pb n="b1125"/>
atrocyate---kāryānupraveśitvānniyogārthasya niyogasya । citi-
savananiṣpattyā cānupraveśasya । tasmāccitisavanaśeṣo'yamiti
pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।</p>
<p>atrocyate---upadeśasiddha‍yarthaṃ hi kāryaṃ na kārya-
siddha‍yartha upadeśaḥ yāgāgrisaṃbandhaścāyaṃ upadeśaḥ । nanu
ca nyāyapaunaruktyamidaṃ aruṇayā krīṇātīti darśitam ।
﻿<pb n="b1126"/>
tatrāsambhavādapi bhavantīti pūrvapakṣavādī manyate । tannirā-
karaṇārthamidam । prayojanamuktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="17">।। 7 ।। 1ante syuravyavāyāta ।। 17 ।।</ab>
<p>nanu vacane sati atra pūrvapakṣo nopapadyate । na
nopapadyate । sarvā brāhmaṇavatya ityanuvādaṃ manyate । evaṃ
sati anyā anyā iti darśanamupapannaṃ bhavati
﻿<pb n="b1127"/>
iti । evaṃ prāpte abhidhīyate । brāhmaṇavatyaḥ śrutiviniyuk‍tāḥ pari-
gṛhyante । kimiti---mantraviniyojyatvāccheṣāṇām । samākhyā
punarlaukikyevetyuktam । tasmānmadhyamāyāṃ citāvupadhātavya
iti । nanu ca mantreṇāpi viniyujyamānāḥ brāhmaṇenaiva viniyuktā
na svatantraliṅgapramāṇamityuk‍tam । viśeṣābhiprāyeṇedamuktam
vacanasyārthavattvāyetyadoṣaḥ । darśane tu mantrābhiprāyeṇānyatvaṃ
varṇanīyam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="20">।। 8 ।। 1prāglokaṃ pṛṇāyāstasyāssampūraṇārthatvāt ।। 20 ।।</ab>
<p>nanu cānte vādarāyaṇa iti nopapadyate, lokaṃpṛṇāpi
brāhmaṇavatyeva ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1128"/>
<p>nanu ca mantravidhānārthaṃ tadvacanam । nanu ca sarvā eva
mantradvāṃreṇa codyante । satyaṃ; tathāpīṣṭakābhidhānapradhāno'yaṃ nirdeśaḥ
<q>‘citriṇīrupadadhāti’</q> ityevamādiṣu । iha punaḥ <q>‘lokaṃ pṛṇa chidraṃ
pṛṇa’</q> iti mantrapradhāno'yaṃ nirdeśa iti laiṅgikyeveyam । ante tu
bādarāyaṇa iti yuk‍tam । rāddhāntastu mantrārthavādānyathānupapatteḥ
laiṅgikā api prāgeva brāhmaṇavatya iti yuk‍tam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1129"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="21">।। 9 ।। saṃskṛte karma saṃskārāṇāṃ tadarthatvāt ।। 21 ।।</ab>
<p>āhitāgneradhikāraśravaṇāta ādhānena cāgnīnāmutpatteḥ
bhavatyanantaramadhikāra iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । ādhānānantarakramasiddhiścā-
nena prakāreṇok‍tā । yathā <q>‘āhitāgnirnaklinnaṃ dārvabhyādadhyāta’</q>
ityevamādīnām । evaṃ prāpte'bhidhīyate---ubhayamapyagnyarthamityuk‍tam
āhavanīyādimukhenāhitāg‍neradhikāraḥ । na ceṣṭibhirvinā''havanī-
yo bhavati iti na karmasvadhikāraḥ । darśanaṃ punaḥ agnyarthasyaiva
homasya ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1130"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="26">।। 10 ।। 1sañcite tvagnicid‍yuktaṃ prāpaṇānnimittasya ।। 26 ।।</ab>
<p>ihāpi cayanānantaraṃ vrataprāptiṃ manyate pūrvapakṣavādī ।
atrocyate---nedamāhitāgninā tulyam । tatra hi agnyarthamādhānam
iha punaḥ agnikāryārthaṃ cayanaṃ, prokṣaṇamiva vrīhikāryārtham । kāryaṃ
ca kṛts‍nakratuprayogasādhyamiti kratusamāptāvevāg‍niciditi । na
cāg‍nicayananimittā hyete niyamāḥ kratoravagamyante bhedanahomavat
﻿<pb n="b1131"/>
kṛtaprayogasyāg‍nicidabhidhānāt । tasmātkratvante niyamā iti
siddham ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="29">।। 11 ।। 1pareṇāvedanāddīkṣitaḥ syāt sarvairdīṃkṣābhisambandhāt ।। 29 ।।</ab>
<p>atrāpi dīkṣitapadārthakramasiddha‍yarthamidaṃ cintyate । kiyadbhi-
rdīkṣito bhavati iti । yāvatā dīkṣābhisambandhaḥ tāvadbhirdīkṣito
bhavatīti pūrvapakṣavādī manyate । sarveṣāmutpattyarthatvāt yathā''dhānena
pavamāneṣṭibhiścāgnayaḥ । anyathā hi vikalpaḥ syāt
pratyekaṃ dīkṣābhinirvṛtteḥ । ata evābhidhānamapyuttarakāla-
meva । atrocyate---dīkṣiṣyamāṇa ityadhikāripadamidam ।
﻿<pb n="b1132"/>
na cādhikārāniṣpatterviṣayasiddhiriti ṣaṣṭhe vakṣyāmaḥ । tasmādiṣṭereva
dīkṣitatvasiddhiḥ । samuccayaścaivamupapanno bhavati । utpattisaṃskāra-
bhedāt । sarveṣāmutpasyarthatvāta anapekṣaśravaṇācca । kathaṃ tarhi
ādhānapavamāneṣṭīnāṃ samuccayaḥ ? prayojanāntarābhāvāt na tatra
tayorgrāhakaṃ kiñcidasti । iha punarjyotiṣṭomavidheḥ vikalpaḥ
tulyarthānām । tasmādasmatpakṣa eva samuccayasiddhiḥ । na
cābhidhānābhāvādarthābhāvaḥ śakyate vak‍tumiti darśitam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1133"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="32">।। 12 ।। 1aṅgavatkratūnāmānupūrvyama ।। 32 ।।</ab>
<p>nanu cāvaśyaṃbhāvini krame pāṭhānniyama uktaḥ । kratvantaravaditi
ca vyatireko varṇitaḥ bhinnaprayogavacanatvānnaiṣāṃ krama upapadyata
iti । kathamatra pūrvapakṣaḥ ? ucyate---anekānuṣṭhānanibandhano'yaṃ
kramaḥ । anekaṃ ca kāmyaṃ kurvataḥ kāminaḥ yuktaḥ kramaniyama iti
pūrvapakṣavādī manyate । kathaṃ tarhi sarvasvāre pāṭhakramaḥ ? arthā-
dbādho bhaviṣyatītyadoṣaḥ । atrābhidhīyate---vidhivitāna-
cinteyam na puruṣecchāvitānacintā, acodanālakṣaṇatvāttasya
﻿<pb n="b1134"/>
ekasya cādhikāravidheraṅgavidhivitānasaṃbandho nādhikāramapekṣate
saṃbandhābhāvāt । asaṃbandhasya ca śābdataiva na śakyate vak‍tum ।
na ca sarvakāmasyādhikāraḥ yogasiddha‍yadhikaraṇe pratyuktatvāt ।
arthasya sambandhaviṣayatvāta । tasmāta kāmyeṣvaniyamaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1135"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="37">।। 13 ।। ya etenetyagniṣṭomaḥ prakaraṇāt ।। 37 ।।</ab>
<p>uparitanasyādhikaraṇasya viṣayapradarśanārthamidamadhikaṇam ।
agniṣṭomapradarśanādityuktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="39">।। 14 ।। 1athānyeneti saṃsthānāṃ sannidhānāt ।। 39 ।।</ab>
<p>ya etenetyagniṣṭomasaṃsthasyāvamarśāt anyeneti saṃsthāntarāva-
marśaṃ manyate pūrvapakṣavādī । rāddhāntavādī tu eṣa vāva prathamo
yajño yajñānāmiti yajñaśabdaśruteḥ yajñāntaramevānyaśabdena
﻿<pb n="b1136"/>
pratīyata ityuktavān । ag‍niṣṭomasaṃsthasya nityatvāt ya etene-
tyucyate । tathā cāpattivihārāvupapannau bhavataḥ । āpattyākṣepa-
samādhānaṃ ca darśitam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="43">।। 15 ।। 1ekastobhe vā kratusaṃyogāta ।। 43 ।।</ab>
<p>ekastomānāṃ vākyaśeṣādanyeneti grahaṇam । na cānyenetya-
nyatvamātrāvagateḥ । nanu ca vākyaśeṣādviśeṣāvagatirityuktam ।
﻿<pb n="b1137"/>
sandigdheṣu vākyaśeṣānnirṇaya ityuktam । iha tu asandigdhaiva
jyotiṣṭomādanyeṣvavagatiriti arthavādamātrametata ।</p>
<trailer>iti bṛhatyāṃ pañcamādhyāyasya
tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>
﻿<pb n="b1138"/>
</section>
<section>
<head>bṛhatyāṃ</head>
</section>
<section>
<head>pañcamādhyāyasya caturthaḥ pādaḥ ।।</head>
<ab type="sutra" n="1">।। 1 ।। 1kramakopo'rthaśabdābhyāṃ śrutiviśeṣādarthaparatvācca ।। 1 ।।</ab>
<p>atra balābalacintā । pūrvapakṣavādino'bhiprāyaḥ avidheya-
tvātkramasya avagateśca tulyatvādvikalpa iti । rāddhāntastu
vidheyavirodhādavagaterevātulyatvamiti śrutyarthayoreva tu balavattvam ।
atra śrutyarthayorvirodhe kathaṃ ? naivodāharaṇamasti । artha eva
﻿<pb n="b1139"/>
balīyān । kāryaṃ hyatrārthaśabdenocyate । kāryārthaśca kramaḥ । ataḥ
śrutimapabādhate kāryaviṣayatvāttasyāḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="2">।। 2 ।। avadānābhidhāraṇāsādaneṣvānupūrvyaṃ pravṛttyā syāt ।। 2 ।।</ab>
<p>atrāpi balābalacintaiva । pravṛtteḥ pūrvapravṛttatvāta pravṛtti-
rbalīyasīti pūrvapakṣavādī manyate । kāryārthatvātkramasya avadānasya ca
pradānopakramatvāt mukhyakramo balīyāniti rāddhāntaḥ । darśana-
maktam ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="5">।। 3 ।। 1vacanādiṣṭipūrvatvam ।। 5 ।।</ab>
﻿<pb n="b1140"/>
<p>atrāpyakṣaraparaṃ kramamaṅgīkṛtya cintā । tatra pūrvapakṣavādī
somena yakṣyamāṇa’ iti nākṣaraparatā kramasya sambhavatīti manvānaḥ,
iṣṭipūrvatāmevāha । kathaṃ punarna saṃbhavati ? ādhānavidhānaparatvā-
dvākyasya । darśapūrṇamāsāviṣ‌ṭveti tu kālavidhānātsiddhiḥ । atrā-
bhidhīyate---yeyamadyatanī vibhaktiḥ sā nādhānānantaryādṛte
sambhavatītyarthāt atrāpi kramasiddhiḥ somādhānayoḥ । kva
punariyaṃ na sambhavati ? adhikāre । adhikārāyattañca vidhānaṃ
﻿<pb n="b1141"/>
ityādhānavidhānepyarthāta kramākṣepaḥ । abhyuccayo darśitaḥ ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="10">।। 4 ।। 1utkarṣādvā brāhmaṇasya somaḥ syāt ।। 10 ।।</ab>
<p>asminnadhikaraṇe pūrvādhikaraṇārthasya viṣayaviśeṣe avasthā-
panam । yadanyattatprāsaṅgikameva । yaḥ punarayamantarāgarbhiṇyupanyāsaḥ
sa kimarthaḥ ? evamartho'sau । yadyanantaraṃ somādhānaṃ tadā
brāhmaṇasya kalpadvayaṃ sambhavati । anyasya vā svakāle
punariṣ‍ṭipūrvakatvamevati niyamyate ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1142"/>
<p>kathaṃ punaridamavagamyate brāhmaṇasyaiva kalpadvayamiti
rāddhāntastu iṣ‍ṭipūrvatve haviṣa utkarṣāt tasmāt somā-
dhānaṃ tasyaiva । anyathā hi brāhmaṇasyaivotkarṣe'napekṣitārtha-
vidhānaṃ syāt । śeṣamuktam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b1143"/>
<ab type="sutra" n="19">।। 6 ।। 1puroḍāśastvanirdeśe tad‌yuk‍te devatābhāvāt ।। 19 ।।</ab>
<p>ekasya haviṣa utkarṣa iti sthite tadviśeṣāvadhāraṇāyedama-
dhikaraṇam । uktaṃ ca ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="12">।। 7 ।। vikṛteḥ prakṛtikālatvāt sadyaskālottarā vikṛtiḥ
tayoḥ pratyakṣaśiṣṭatvāt ।। 12 ।।</ab>
<p>pūrvaṃ nyāyato'sambhavamuktvā tasminnevāhani samāp‍tyupakramau
darśitavān sambhavārtham ।</p>
﻿<pb n="1144"/>
<p>sadyaskālataiva vikṛtīnāmityuktavān ।</p>
<ab type="sutra" n="25">।। 8 ।। sānnāyyāgnīṣomīyavikārāḥ ūrdhvaṃ somāt prakṛtivat ।। 25 ।।</ab>
<ab type="sutra" n="26">।। 9 ।। tathā somavikārāḥ darśapūrṇamāsābhyās ।। 26 ।।</ab>
<p>ihādhikaraṇadvayepyadhikārādṛte kālalakṣaṇā na sambhavatīti
kṛtādhikārasyaiva kramasyādhikāra iti tadvikārāṇāmapyevameveti
yuktam । kimarthaṃ tarhi adhikaraṇadvayam ? pūrvatra kartṛtānirdeśāt
nāsomayājīti somayāgasya kartā sānnāyye kartṛtayā'bhidhīyate
﻿<pb n="1145"/>
dvitīyādhikaraṇe tu darśapūrṇamāsābhyāmiṣṭveti punarāśaṅkitavān
kartṛnirdeśābhāvāt । kathaṃ tarhi rāddhānte nyāyatulyatā ? nādhi-
kārādṛte kālalakṣaṇā sambhavatīti tulyatoktā ।</p>
<trailer>iti bṛhatyāṃ pañcamādhyāyasya
caturthaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>
